
-----title
杭州 (出生地)
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='38b57820daf348c7809bd74f15f4e796_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("38b57820daf348c7809bd74f15f4e796");'><span id='38b57820daf348c7809bd74f15f4e796_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1072&endYear=1074')">1072-1074年</a>，1-3岁</div><div id='38b57820daf348c7809bd74f15f4e796' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1072&endYear=1072')">1072年4月4日</a>　四月四日，苏过生，奶名“似叔”。生母王闰之，字季章，封同安郡夫人。时父苏轼因与王安石政见不合，出任杭州通判。是时，长兄苏迈十四岁，仲兄苏迨三岁。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1073&endYear=1073')">1073年</a>　苏过随父在杭州。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1074&endYear=1074')">1074年9月</a>　熙宁七年五月苏轼奉命知密州，九月离杭州，十一月到任。熙宁九年十一月移知河中府，十二月离密州。苏过随行。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='1818325c1226401a80423aa54449bf77_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("1818325c1226401a80423aa54449bf77");'><span id='1818325c1226401a80423aa54449bf77_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1089&endYear=1090')">1089-1090年</a>，18-19岁</div><div id='1818325c1226401a80423aa54449bf77' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1089&endYear=1089')">1089年7月3日</a>　三月，苏轼被命知杭州，四月末离京，七月三日到杭州。苏过随父自京至杭。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1089&endYear=1089')">1089年</a>　舅父王箴（元直）自蜀来杭，苏过始识之。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1089&endYear=1089')">1089年</a>　苏过与秦觏游，常为父检书摘典。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1090&endYear=1090')">1090年</a>　春，王箴归蜀，苏轼作诗送之，苏过兄弟皆次其韵。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1090&endYear=1090')">1090年10月</a>　十月，苏迨、苏过赴礼部试，参寥子以诗送之。<br /></div>
-----end



-----title
诸城
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='39650448a4c1466b9109b29c7015d6a7_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("39650448a4c1466b9109b29c7015d6a7");'><span id='39650448a4c1466b9109b29c7015d6a7_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1074&endYear=1076')">1074-1076年</a>，3-5岁</div><div id='39650448a4c1466b9109b29c7015d6a7' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1074&endYear=1076')">1074-1076年</a>　熙宁七年五月苏轼奉命知密州，九月离杭州，十一月到任。熙宁九年十一月移知河中府，十二月离密州。苏过随行。<br /></div>
-----end



-----title
开封
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='d2fca9dd1d484d44bfcf09b250a0ea65_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("d2fca9dd1d484d44bfcf09b250a0ea65");'><span id='d2fca9dd1d484d44bfcf09b250a0ea65_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1077&endYear=1077')">1077年</a>，6岁</div><div id='d2fca9dd1d484d44bfcf09b250a0ea65' class='detail'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>苏轼赴河中府，苏辙自京师来迎，抵陈桥驿，告下徙知徐州，不得入国门，寓郊外范镇东园。苏过随行。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='899e7ac1e1b34519a2793624614d4daa_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("899e7ac1e1b34519a2793624614d4daa");'><span id='899e7ac1e1b34519a2793624614d4daa_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1085&endYear=1089')">1085-1089年</a>，14-18岁</div><div id='899e7ac1e1b34519a2793624614d4daa' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1085&endYear=1085')">1085年12月</a>　十二月，到京师。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1086&endYear=1086')">1086年闰2月6日</a>　闰二月六日，苏轼书苏辙梦中诗付苏过。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1086&endYear=1086')">1086年9月</a>　九月丁卯，苏轼自试中书舍人为翰林学士、知制诰。苏过兄弟相从，得天伦之乐。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1087&endYear=1087')">1087年</a>　随父在京师。苏过卧听父轼夜读。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1088&endYear=1088')">1088年7月</a>　七月，苏轼馆伴北使于都亭驿，苏迨、苏过、苏远往省，令同作诗。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1088&endYear=1088')">1088年11月6日</a>　十二月六日，苏轼作《评诗人写物》付苏过。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1089&endYear=1089')">1089年4月</a>　三月，苏轼被命知杭州，四月末离京，七月三日到杭州。苏过随父自京至杭。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='e4da62f8904842549dab6f337b5be2a3_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("e4da62f8904842549dab6f337b5be2a3");'><span id='e4da62f8904842549dab6f337b5be2a3_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1091&endYear=1091')">1091年</a>，20岁</div><div id='e4da62f8904842549dab6f337b5be2a3' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1091&endYear=1091')">1091年</a>　春，苏迨、苏过应礼部试，下第。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1091&endYear=1091')">1091年5月</a>　二月二十八日，苏轼被召还朝，三月离杭，五月到京，任翰林学士，家于京师阊阖白家巷。苏过娶妻范氏，乃范镇（蜀忠文公）之孙、范百嘉之女。八月，苏轼出知颍州，苏迨、苏过皆随行。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='dd77c0a822cd46ca862302ee14d5b23c_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("dd77c0a822cd46ca862302ee14d5b23c");'><span id='dd77c0a822cd46ca862302ee14d5b23c_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1092&endYear=1093')">1092-1093年</a>，21-22岁</div><div id='dd77c0a822cd46ca862302ee14d5b23c' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1092&endYear=1092')">1092年9月</a>　三月十六日，抵扬州。八月，苏轼复以兵部尚书召还朝，九月至京。苏过恩授右承务郎。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1092&endYear=1092')">1092年</a>　是年，叔父苏辙为门下侍郎。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1093&endYear=1093')">1093年8月1日</a>　八月一日，母王闰之病逝于京师。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1093&endYear=1093')">1093年9月27日</a>　八月，苏轼被命知定州。九月三日，高太后卒，哲宗亲政。苏轼九月二十七日离京，十月二十三日到达定州。苏迨、苏过随行。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='bb738a837cc74f71b37e0ed1bf06bd04_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("bb738a837cc74f71b37e0ed1bf06bd04");'><span id='bb738a837cc74f71b37e0ed1bf06bd04_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1102&endYear=1102')">1102年</a>，31岁</div><div id='bb738a837cc74f71b37e0ed1bf06bd04' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1102&endYear=1102')">1102年</a>　春，苏过扶苏轼灵柩自淮入汴，至陈留登陆西行。四月，苏辙遣苏迈往京城迁王闰之及苏迨亡妻欧阳氏灵柩，至郏县待葬。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='55820033b8b64840a1244753910b4757_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("55820033b8b64840a1244753910b4757");'><span id='55820033b8b64840a1244753910b4757_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1116&endYear=1116')">1116年</a>，45岁</div><div id='55820033b8b64840a1244753910b4757' class='detail'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>苏过至中都，叹一切变古，以醉寄慨，超然于当世之外。<br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>在开封，郾城县知县任上。在京师，苏过题蔡致君藏书目。作品：《夷门蔡氏藏书目叙》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《斜川集校注》卷九。）</span><div id='poem_1215253' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1215253' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1215253?labeling=true' target='_blank'>夷门蔡氏藏书目叙</a><span class='authorDate'>（1116年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31323, "北宋", "苏过", "poem_title_1215253")'>苏过</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1215253_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1215253'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1215253'>自书契三代以来，礼乐文章，播在方册，皆藏于<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_0_1215253", 1215253, "Clauses/3/Comments/0")'>王府</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1215253_comment'></div>老聃为柱下史，实主其藏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1215253_comment'></div>虽列国诸侯，莫得而与；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1215253_comment'></div>当世学士大夫，盖得观其书者，鲜矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1215253_comment'></div>故韩宣子适鲁，见《易象》与《鲁春秋》，曰：「周礼尽在鲁矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1215253_comment'></div>楚左史倚相，能读《三坟》、《五典》、《八索》、《九丘》，则国人皆尊之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1215253_comment'></div>孔子，圣人也，然犹问礼于老聃，学官名于郯子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1215253_comment'></div>季札，蛮夷也，聘于齐鲁，然后获观先王之乐，而闻大国之风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1215253_comment'></div>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1215253_comment'></div>读其书，论其世，想见其人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1215253_comment'></div>凛然于千载之上，修身立言，可以垂训于百世之后，岂有不因载籍之有考乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1215253_comment'></div>是以有国有家者，尝刻意于此，而孝悌忠信，必由是而出。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1215253_comment'></div>古之人躬行不逮者多矣，余不复论。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1215253_comment'></div>比游京师，有为余言：「吾里有蔡致君，隐居以求志，好古而博雅，闭门读书，不交当世之公卿，类有道者也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1215253_comment'></div>余矍然异之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1215253_comment'></div>一日造其门，见其子，从容请交焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1215253_comment'></div>其子为余言：「吾世大梁人，业为儒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1215253_comment'></div>吾祖、吾父皆不事科举，不乐仕宦，独喜收古今之书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1215253_comment'></div>空四壁，捐千金以购之，常若饥渴然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1215253_comment'></div>尽求善工良纸，手校而积藏之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1215253_comment'></div>凡五十年，经、史、百家、《离骚》、风雅、儒、墨、道德、阴阳、卜筮、技术之书，莫不兼收而并取，今二万卷矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1215253_comment'></div>且吾父有德不耀，常畏人知，弃冠冕而遗世故久矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1215253_comment'></div>必不能从子游」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1215253_comment'></div>余怅然自失，悠然而返。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1215253_comment'></div>予惟古之逸民，未尝以一艺自名于世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1215253_comment'></div>虽不求人知，而人自知之，以其所践履者，绝乎流俗故也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1215253_comment'></div>庞德公隐于鹿门，妻子躬耕，或疑其不仕，以为何以遗子孙也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1215253_comment'></div>庞公曰：「我遗子孙以安，不为无所遗也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1215253_comment'></div>今居士口不谈世之爵禄，身不问家之有无，所付子孙者，独书耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1215253_comment'></div>庞公之意，殆无以过此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1215253_comment'></div>居士之子，敏而文，学日富。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1215253_comment'></div>人不知其所以然者，抑所谓不见异人，必得异书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1215253_comment'></div>中郎为有子矣！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1215253_comment'></div>余将负笈而请观焉，乃持其总目三卷，为叙而归之，庶几附托于斯，与藏书者终始。</div><div id='poem_sentence_33_1215253_comment'></div></div></div><br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>苏过曾客高俅馆，赵鼎臣有诗相戏。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='07c41391f45840288a3ca6b2c4afbaf9_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("07c41391f45840288a3ca6b2c4afbaf9");'><span id='07c41391f45840288a3ca6b2c4afbaf9_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1122&endYear=1122')">1122年</a>，51岁</div><div id='07c41391f45840288a3ca6b2c4afbaf9' class='detail'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>苏过尝至京师，为徽宗画画壁。<br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>苏过在京师尝与赵夔游，夔访以东坡诗事。<br /></div>
-----end



-----title
商丘
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='b842acf6048a4c8184b7b274bce4edd1_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("b842acf6048a4c8184b7b274bce4edd1");'><span id='b842acf6048a4c8184b7b274bce4edd1_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1077&endYear=1077')">1077年</a>，6岁</div><div id='b842acf6048a4c8184b7b274bce4edd1' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1077&endYear=1077')">1077年4月</a>　四月，苏轼兄弟谒张方平于南都，同月二十一日到徐州任所。苏过随至。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='6815d1d982a04c72bebf6bfba83860c8_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("6815d1d982a04c72bebf6bfba83860c8");'><span id='6815d1d982a04c72bebf6bfba83860c8_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1079&endYear=1079')">1079年</a>，8岁</div><div id='6815d1d982a04c72bebf6bfba83860c8' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1079&endYear=1079')">1079年</a>　七月二十八日，苏轼因乌台诗案被逮入都，苏迈随行。王适、王遹兄弟送苏过母子于南京（商丘）苏辙处。苏过兄弟与王适游，文章人品皆受其影响。十二月二十九日案结，苏轼谪黄州，苏辙坐贬筠州。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='1cc0d8ff46d54be1af3b562bfa9de00f_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("1cc0d8ff46d54be1af3b562bfa9de00f");'><span id='1cc0d8ff46d54be1af3b562bfa9de00f_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1085&endYear=1085')">1085年</a>，14岁</div><div id='1cc0d8ff46d54be1af3b562bfa9de00f' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1085&endYear=1085')">1085年2月</a>　二月，苏过一家至南都（商丘），告下，许常州居住。三月，神宗去世。四月发南都。五月二十二日，至常州。六月苏轼起知登州。九月抵楚州，至淮口遇大风。<br /></div>
-----end



-----title
徐州
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='eb41010caf994e48814de6dc186dd7c0_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("eb41010caf994e48814de6dc186dd7c0");'><span id='eb41010caf994e48814de6dc186dd7c0_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1077&endYear=1079')">1077-1079年</a>，6-8岁</div><div id='eb41010caf994e48814de6dc186dd7c0' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1077&endYear=1077')">1077年4月21日</a>　四月，苏轼兄弟谒张方平于南都，同月二十一日到徐州任所。苏过随至。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1078&endYear=1078')">1078年</a>　苏过随父在徐州。苏过兄弟幼年，厌弃轩华，崇尚隐逸。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1079&endYear=1079')">1079年3月</a>　三月，苏轼改知湖州，四月二十九日到任。苏过随行。<br /></div>
-----end



-----title
黄冈
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='22694d0b2604458bb2311300d6df4b66_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("22694d0b2604458bb2311300d6df4b66");'><span id='22694d0b2604458bb2311300d6df4b66_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1080&endYear=1084')">1080-1084年</a>，9-13岁</div><div id='22694d0b2604458bb2311300d6df4b66' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1080&endYear=1080')">1080年5月20日</a>　五月二十日，苏辙赴筠州贬所，绕道送苏过母子到黄州。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1080&endYear=1080')">1080年10月</a>　养视苏过三兄弟之苏轼乳母任氏卒，十月葬之。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1081&endYear=1081')">1081年</a>　苏过随父在黄州。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1082&endYear=1082')">1082年</a>　苏迈与弟迨、过，从父系统习作诗文，当在此时。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1083&endYear=1083')">1083年1月</a>　正月，巢谷自蜀来，遂留，苏迨、苏过从谷学于雪堂。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1083&endYear=1083')">1083年3月</a>　三月，参寥来访，苏过始识之。留弥年乃归。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1083&endYear=1083')">1083年9月27日</a>　九月二十七日，弟苏遯生，未期年而夭。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1083&endYear=1083')">1083年</a>　冬，巢谷辞归眉山。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1084&endYear=1084')">1084年4月</a>　三月，苏轼奉命迁汝州，四月离黄州，苏过等随行。<br /></div>
-----end



-----title
高安
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='6a072cbe7a7a4c26ad0f85b5024fdb17_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("6a072cbe7a7a4c26ad0f85b5024fdb17");'><span id='6a072cbe7a7a4c26ad0f85b5024fdb17_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1084&endYear=1084')">1084年</a>，13岁</div><div id='6a072cbe7a7a4c26ad0f85b5024fdb17' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1084&endYear=1084')">1084年5月5日</a>　五月，苏过与父绕道筠州看望苏辙。与苏辙子迟、适、远端午出游。留十日，别去。苏辙为诗盛赞苏过兄弟。<br /></div>
-----end



-----title
当涂
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='f3a328e8f5af46ebb8e336fea8f45f02_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("f3a328e8f5af46ebb8e336fea8f45f02");'><span id='f3a328e8f5af46ebb8e336fea8f45f02_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1084&endYear=1084')">1084年</a>，13岁</div><div id='f3a328e8f5af46ebb8e336fea8f45f02' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1084&endYear=1084')">1084年7月</a>　七月，舟行至当涂，苏轼以天石砚付苏迨、苏过。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='c04104a0af354c3fab901804398ae34b_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("c04104a0af354c3fab901804398ae34b");'><span id='c04104a0af354c3fab901804398ae34b_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1094&endYear=1094')">1094年</a>，23岁</div><div id='c04104a0af354c3fab901804398ae34b' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1094&endYear=1094')">1094年6月25日</a>　六月二十五日，抵当涂，告下，苏轼以诋斥神宗罪，诏谪惠州。苏轼令苏迨亦归宜兴，书生平所作六赋付之。独与幼子过赴贬所，苏过妻小亦随迨归阳羡。<br /></div>
-----end



-----title
南京
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='8200e4a9ed424fa097cb9342dbcf0c66_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("8200e4a9ed424fa097cb9342dbcf0c66");'><span id='8200e4a9ed424fa097cb9342dbcf0c66_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1084&endYear=1084')">1084年</a>，13岁</div><div id='8200e4a9ed424fa097cb9342dbcf0c66' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1084&endYear=1084')">1084年7月28日</a>　七月二十八日，幼弟苏遯夭折于金陵。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='ccf409f128f64ea088f450dc1814e04d_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("ccf409f128f64ea088f450dc1814e04d");'><span id='ccf409f128f64ea088f450dc1814e04d_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1094&endYear=1094')">1094年</a>，23岁</div><div id='ccf409f128f64ea088f450dc1814e04d' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1094&endYear=1094')">1094年6月</a>　六月，至金陵。苏迈与父分别，率家人赶赴宜兴。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='8d6b5c539c6d4f329dedcb036483d070_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("8d6b5c539c6d4f329dedcb036483d070");'><span id='8d6b5c539c6d4f329dedcb036483d070_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1101&endYear=1101')">1101年</a>，30岁</div><div id='8d6b5c539c6d4f329dedcb036483d070' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1101&endYear=1101')">1101年5月</a>　五月抵金陵。苏过与父本欲归宜兴，因苏辙乞归许昌，苏轼命迈、迨往宜兴收拾变卖家产，以备北迁。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1101&endYear=1101')">1101年</a>　苏轼作书李廌（方叔），赞苏迨、苏过不废学。<br /></div>
-----end



-----title
仪征
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='ab22b200506a408bb7e8f53da5d3b739_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("ab22b200506a408bb7e8f53da5d3b739");'><span id='ab22b200506a408bb7e8f53da5d3b739_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1084&endYear=1084')">1084年</a>，13岁</div><div id='ab22b200506a408bb7e8f53da5d3b739' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1084&endYear=1084')">1084年8月</a>　八月至仪真，九月渡江至京口。苏迨奉父命持钱往宜兴购田宅。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='f9f017a8243046cf97e8f4b5ea9b5f7b_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("f9f017a8243046cf97e8f4b5ea9b5f7b");'><span id='f9f017a8243046cf97e8f4b5ea9b5f7b_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1101&endYear=1101')">1101年</a>，30岁</div><div id='f9f017a8243046cf97e8f4b5ea9b5f7b' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1101&endYear=1101')">1101年5月</a>　五月下旬，至仪真，与程之元（德孺）等会于金山。闻政局有变，苏轼决计归常州，并计划遣苏迈注官，自己与迨、迈闭门终老。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1101&endYear=1101')">1101年</a>　舟中热不可胜，苏轼常夜间露坐，且饮冷过度，中夜暴下，苏过晓夜扶持。过诵米芾（元章）《宝月观赋》，轼悦而致书米芾。<br /></div>
-----end

-----title
扬州
-----detail

-----title
盱眙
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='39c9568254b24c6d922ebff04b9b643a_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("39c9568254b24c6d922ebff04b9b643a");'><span id='39c9568254b24c6d922ebff04b9b643a_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1084&endYear=1084')">1084年</a>，13岁</div><div id='39c9568254b24c6d922ebff04b9b643a' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1084&endYear=1084')">1084年12月</a>　十月至扬州，苏轼上表求常州居住。十二月抵泗州。苏过随行。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='d78d0e4e82d34ca792957e64bbb3c645_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("d78d0e4e82d34ca792957e64bbb3c645");'><span id='d78d0e4e82d34ca792957e64bbb3c645_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1102&endYear=1102')">1102年</a>，31岁</div><div id='d78d0e4e82d34ca792957e64bbb3c645' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1102&endYear=1102')">1102年</a>　春，苏过扶苏轼灵柩自淮入汴，至陈留登陆西行。四月，苏辙遣苏迈往京城迁王闰之及苏迨亡妻欧阳氏灵柩，至郏县待葬。<br /></div>

-----title
常州
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='26c4a925719e492ea5877bddbfd7c019_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("26c4a925719e492ea5877bddbfd7c019");'><span id='26c4a925719e492ea5877bddbfd7c019_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1085&endYear=1085')">1085年</a>，14岁</div><div id='26c4a925719e492ea5877bddbfd7c019' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1085&endYear=1085')">1085年5月22日</a>　二月，苏过一家至南都（商丘），告下，许常州居住。三月，神宗去世。四月发南都。五月二十二日，至常州。六月苏轼起知登州。九月抵楚州，至淮口遇大风。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='38b33494afa54c958c98d6ac7fdc047f_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("38b33494afa54c958c98d6ac7fdc047f");'><span id='38b33494afa54c958c98d6ac7fdc047f_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1101&endYear=1101')">1101年</a>，30岁</div><div id='38b33494afa54c958c98d6ac7fdc047f' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1101&endYear=1101')">1101年</a>　六月十五日，发舟赴毗陵，至，寓于孙馆。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1101&endYear=1101')">1101年7月</a>　七月立秋，苏过代父轼写书与米芾。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1101&endYear=1101')">1101年7月28日</a>　苏轼病危，令苏迈、苏迨、苏过侍侧。七月二十八日，苏轼卒于常州。<br /></div>
-----end



-----title
淮安
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='eec679b6ed2944f4ac48608e7905ac9b_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("eec679b6ed2944f4ac48608e7905ac9b");'><span id='eec679b6ed2944f4ac48608e7905ac9b_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1085&endYear=1085')">1085年</a>，14岁</div><div id='eec679b6ed2944f4ac48608e7905ac9b' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1085&endYear=1085')">1085年9月</a>　二月，苏过一家至南都（商丘），告下，许常州居住。三月，神宗去世。四月发南都。五月二十二日，至常州。六月苏轼起知登州。九月抵楚州，至淮口遇大风。<br /></div>

蓬莱
-----detail

-----title
阜阳
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='1e4835867c4c480f8e4d5b24b6f9e585_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("1e4835867c4c480f8e4d5b24b6f9e585");'><span id='1e4835867c4c480f8e4d5b24b6f9e585_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1091&endYear=1092')">1091-1092年</a>，20-21岁</div><div id='1e4835867c4c480f8e4d5b24b6f9e585' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1091&endYear=1091')">1091年8月</a>　二月二十八日，苏轼被召还朝，三月离杭，五月到京，任翰林学士，家于京师阊阖白家巷。苏过娶妻范氏，乃范镇（蜀忠文公）之孙、范百嘉之女。八月，苏轼出知颍州，苏迨、苏过皆随行。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1092&endYear=1092')">1092年2月</a>　二月，苏轼罢颍州任，改知扬州。三月三日赴扬州途中，苏迨、苏过与父轼同游涂山、荆山。<br /></div>
-----end

-----title
定州
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='0fbec111dc8f47e791d92f1401fb7448_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("0fbec111dc8f47e791d92f1401fb7448");'><span id='0fbec111dc8f47e791d92f1401fb7448_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1093&endYear=1094')">1093-1094年</a>，22-23岁</div><div id='0fbec111dc8f47e791d92f1401fb7448' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1093&endYear=1093')">1093年10月23日</a>　八月，苏轼被命知定州。九月三日，高太后卒，哲宗亲政。苏轼九月二十七日离京，十月二十三日到达定州。苏迨、苏过随行。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1094&endYear=1094')">1094年4月3日</a>　四月三日，苏轼以前掌制命，有讥讪神宗之嫌，落职英州。苏迈、苏迨、苏过同行。过临城，苏轼作诗付苏过。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='d4137438ba3048059e54b89ccef82a50_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("d4137438ba3048059e54b89ccef82a50");'><span id='d4137438ba3048059e54b89ccef82a50_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1123&endYear=1123')">1123年</a>，52岁</div><div id='d4137438ba3048059e54b89ccef82a50' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1123&endYear=1123')">1123年</a>　约在安喜，权通判中山府。友人单某以书相庆，苏过作启答之。作品：《回单靖州启》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《斜川集校注》卷九。徽宗政和三年（1113），定州改中山府。）</span><div id='poem_1215236' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1215236' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1215236?labeling=true' target='_blank'>回单靖州启</a><span class='authorDate'>（宣和五年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31323, "北宋", "苏过", "poem_title_1215236")'>苏过</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1215236_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1215236'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1215236'>狐狸未尽，宜雕鹗之横飞；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1215236_comment'></div>骐骥先驱，甘驽骀之在后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1215236_comment'></div>顾蹉跎之无用，虽矍铄以奚为。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1215236_comment'></div>过辱缄题，曲垂存藉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1215236_comment'></div>仰君子之有道，识仁人之用心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1215236_comment'></div>感极成悲，惊定而愧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1215236_comment'></div>恭惟某官才推人杰，名擅国桢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1215236_comment'></div>相有掷笔之虎头，终封定远；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1215236_comment'></div>忠并伏波之马革，不畏蛮溪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1215236_comment'></div>闾里观杨仆之怀黄，道路耸买臣之衣绣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1215236_comment'></div>某忝兹别乘，预切依仁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1215236_comment'></div>方残暑之秋风，多生寒之夜雨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1215236_comment'></div>更祈善摄，以永寿祺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1215236_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_13_1215236_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='2ac2c89d608247e9b25f136f3ccabf4b_label'><a ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1123&endYear=1123')">1123年</a>　在安喜，权通判中山府。苏过与中山帅陈遘登城观猎，作诗。作品：《陪中山帅登城口号》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《斜川集校注》卷六。）</span>《再次韵答陈帅和诗》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《斜川集校注》卷六。）</span><div id='poem_522771' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_522771' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/522771?labeling=true' target='_blank'>诏中山帅登城口号</a><span class='authorDate'>（1123年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31323, "北宋", "苏过", "poem_title_522771")'>苏过</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_522771_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_522771'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_522771'>西风卷雨出群山，晓色朦胧未散烟。<div id='poem_sentence_0_522771_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_522771'>雉堞横空云半隐，旌旂改色日争鲜。<div id='poem_sentence_1_522771_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_522771'>承平不在山河险，卧护何须铁石坚。<div id='poem_sentence_2_522771_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_522771'>卖剑决牛从此始，陪公千骑看秋田。<div id='poem_sentence_3_522771_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_522771'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_522771_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_522772' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_522772' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/522772?labeling=true' "poem_title_522772")'>苏过</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_522772_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_522772'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_522772_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_522772'>收拾风浪开幕府，从容谈笑卧中坚。<div id='poem_sentence_2_522772_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_522772'>愿观横槊诗千首，锋镝消磨变力田。<div id='poem_sentence_3_522772_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_522772'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_522772_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1123&endYear=1123')">1123年</a>　在安喜，权通判中山府。八月，辽萧幹称大奚王，引兵攻破景、蓟二州，遂攻燕。郭药师与战，破之，苏过作诗相庆。作品：《闻郭太尉出师大捷奚人擒契丹酋领四军者来献作长句古调一首》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《斜川集校注》卷六。）</span><div id='poem_522680' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_522680' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/522680?labeling=true' ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31323, "北宋", "苏过", "poem_title_522680")'>苏过</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_522680_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_522680'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_522680'>辽人猖蹶败纪纲，鸟兽惊骇自取亡。<div id='poem_sentence_0_522680_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_522680'>归我五季旧土疆，有如宣宗复河湟。<div id='poem_sentence_1_522680_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_522680'>彼酋假息不自量，网开三面犹跳梁。<div id='poem_sentence_2_522680_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_522680'>爝火乃欲犯太阳，怒臂当车学螳螂。<div id='poem_sentence_3_522680_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_522680'>支天所坏仍鸱张，含沙射影出复藏。<div id='poem_sentence_4_522680_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_522680'>将军义勇冠三光，愿以部曲除螟蝗。<div id='poem_sentence_5_522680_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_522680'>户有三丁一我将，遣汝积愤当少偿。<div id='poem_sentence_6_522680_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_522680'>上马亟持十日粮，长矛短戟舂其吭。<div id='poem_sentence_7_522680_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_522680'>前者披靡后者戕，系累妻子涕泗滂。<div id='poem_sentence_8_522680_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_522680'>将军折北昔未尝，以巧服人尤所长。<div id='poem_sentence_9_522680_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_522680'>勿追穷寇非深防，会遣生致如探囊。<div id='poem_sentence_10_522680_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_522680'>匈奴自古夸豪强，三表五饵称前王。<div id='poem_sentence_11_522680_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_522680'>竟无一日笞中行，昭君远嫁令人伤。<div id='poem_sentence_12_522680_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_522680'>岂知天兵自鹰扬，郅支援首须陈汤。<div id='poem_sentence_13_522680_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_522680'>头颅万里行朔方，遣示藁街听徜徉。<div id='poem_sentence_14_522680_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_522680'>偃兵息民令有常，昔居锋镝今农桑。<div id='poem_sentence_15_522680_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_522680'>百年版籍沦要荒，一日冠盖欣相望。<div id='poem_sentence_16_522680_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_522680'>李白长歌汉道昌，两阶羽舞垂衣裳。<div ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1123&endYear=1123')">1123年9月7日</a>　九月七日，苏过与陈遘等饭于定州天宁寺，过题名。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1123&endYear=1123')">1123年</a>　在安喜，权通判中山府。在中山，苏过曾代人作谢启。作品：《代人谢启》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《斜川集校注》卷九。《斜川集校注》有《代人谢启》同题文多首，此篇首句为“飞刍挽粟”）</span><div id='poem_1215233' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1215233' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1215233?labeling=true' target='_blank'>代人谢启<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其六 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1123年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31323, "北宋", "苏过", "poem_title_1215233")'>苏过</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1215233_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1215233'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1215233'>飞刍挽粟，惭无补于事功；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1215233_comment'></div>说《礼》敦《诗》，辄滥居于谋帅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1215233_comment'></div>况此鲜虞之旧壤，蔚为朔野之雄都。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1215233_comment'></div>素称足食而足兵，何止有民而有社。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1215233_comment'></div>控临胡虏，虽无表里之山河；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1215233_comment'></div>拊循士夫，必赖折冲于樽俎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1215233_comment'></div>而某学不足以经远，才未能以过人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1215233_comment'></div>久玷朝廷之误恩，尚处承明之秘职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1215233_comment'></div>兼收并用，录其薄效于东南；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1215233_comment'></div>舍短取长，姑又责成于燕赵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1215233_comment'></div>此盖某官弼亮元圣，师保万民。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1215233_comment'></div>才全而德不形，任重而道愈远。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1215233_comment'></div>以求贤取士为报国，以养兵息民考治功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1215233_comment'></div>矧燕云抚顺之初，实庙堂宵旰之际。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1215233_comment'></div>昭携怀远，卧鼓灭烽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1215233_comment'></div>既书卫、霍之功，行责龚、黄之政。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1215233_comment'></div>遂因人乏，得冒恩私。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1215233_comment'></div>某谨当益竭空疏，务酬知遇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1215233_comment'></div>轻裘缓带，敢希羊叔子之风；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1215233_comment'></div>积谷屯田，庶收赵充国之效。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1215233_comment'></div>过此以往，未知所裁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1215233_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_21_1215233_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1123&endYear=1123')">1123年10月</a>　十月，从兄苏适下葬，苏迟撰志，苏过为苏适及其夫人黄氏题写志盖。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1123&endYear=1123')">1123年</a>　在安喜，权通判中山府。从兄苏迟得戎州通判，欲归蜀，与朋友唱和，苏过次韵。作品：《和伯充兄唱酬二首一题伯充一寄高仲贻》（其一）<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《斜川集校注》卷六。）</span>《和伯充兄唱酬二首一题伯充一寄高仲贻》（其二）<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《斜川集校注》卷六。）</span><div id='poem_522777' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_522777' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/522777?labeling=true' target='_blank'>和伯充兄唱酬二首一赠伯充一寄高仲贻<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1123年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31323, "北宋", "苏过", "poem_title_522777")'>苏过</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_522777_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_522777'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_522777'>倦客难堪走世尘，空嗟林下见何人。<div id='poem_sentence_0_522777_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_522777'>坐令岁月徂清夜，梦想田园趁食新。<div id='poem_sentence_1_522777_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_522777'>老境已侵无几发，垂堂共爱不赀身。<div id='poem_sentence_2_522777_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_522777'>一官聊为家山往，要看明年濯锦春<span id='poem_sentence_4_522777_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_522778' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_522778' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/522778?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1123年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_522778_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_522778'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_522778'>家风凛凛嗣前尘，元祐庵中老道人<span class='inlineComment2'>（自注：仲贻家庵，自谓老道人。）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_0_522778_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_522778'>形似子綦独枯槁，诗如开府日清新。<div id='poem_sentence_1_522778_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_522778'>功名轩冕真馀事，富贵籧篨误此身。<div id='poem_sentence_2_522778_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_522778'>不有胸中陂万顷，肯教白发负青春。<div id='poem_sentence_3_522778_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_522778'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_522778_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1123&endYear=1123')">1123年</a>　或在安喜，权通判中山府。苏过有《士燮论》文。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《斜川集校注》卷九。此文具体写作时地不详，姑系于此。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1123&endYear=1123')">1123年</a>　或在安喜，权通判中山府。苏过有《代人贺启》文。（其一）<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《斜川集校注》卷一〇。《斜川集校注》有《代人贺启》（一）同题文二篇，此为其中一篇，首句为“伏审拜命宸严”此文具体写作时地不详，姑系于此。）</span>《代人贺启》（其二）<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《斜川集校注》卷一〇。《斜川集校注》有《代人贺启》同题文二篇，此为其中一篇，首二句为“显被明纶，升华内阁”此文具体写作时地不详，姑系于此。）</span><div id='poem_1215237' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1215237' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1215237?labeling=true' target='_blank'>代人贺启<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1123年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31323, "北宋", "苏过", "poem_title_1215237")'>苏过</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1215237_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1215237'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1215237'>伏审拜命宸严，分符外阃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1215237_comment'></div>辍从朝著，作镇全齐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1215237_comment'></div>恭惟欢庆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1215237_comment'></div>窃以历下名城，古称十万户之富；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1215237_comment'></div>汉庭多士，尤重二千石之良。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1215237_comment'></div>将使子惠一方之黎元，岂独谨守三尺之条教。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1215237_comment'></div>山川广袤，鸡犬相闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1215237_comment'></div>民淳而寡求，士美而好学。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1215237_comment'></div>既欲阜安其俗，必资果艺之材。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1215237_comment'></div>用分宵旰之忧，乃荷承宣之寄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1215237_comment'></div>恭惟某官智兼经术，识达古今。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1215237_comment'></div>夙膺黼座之知，屡试盘根之用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1215237_comment'></div>德星所次，民瘼一消。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1215237_comment'></div>揽辔登车，已获二天之誉；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1215237_comment'></div>期年报政，即闻《五裤》之谣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1215237_comment'></div>某久去乡关，缪持使节。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1215237_comment'></div>未能躬桑梓之礼，姑欲致蘋藻之诚。</div><div id='poem_sentence_16_1215237_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1123&endYear=1123')">1123年</a>　或在安喜，权通判中山府。苏过有《代人谢启》文。（其一）<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《斜川集校注》卷一〇。《斜川集校注》有《代人谢启》（一）同题文二篇，此为其中一篇，首句为“缪膺使指”此文具体写作时地不详，姑系于此。）</span>《代人谢启》（其二）<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《斜川集校注》卷一〇。《斜川集校注》有《代人谢启》（二）同题文二篇，此为其中一篇，首句为“奉使十年”此文具体写作时地不详，姑系于此。）</span>《代人谢启》（其三）<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《斜川集校注》卷一〇。此文具体写作时地不详，姑系于此。）</span>《代人谢启》（其四）<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《斜川集校注》卷一〇。此文具体写作时地不详，姑系于此。）</span><div id='poem_1215232' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1215232' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1215232?labeling=true' target='_blank'>代人谢启<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其五 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1123年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31323, "北宋", "苏过", "poem_title_1215232")'>苏过</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1215232_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1215232'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1215232'>缪膺使指，方愧无功，宠畀漕权，复叨重寄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1215232_comment'></div>自顾才能之谫薄，猥当金谷之转输。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1215232_comment'></div>迁徙有无，乏桑羊之心计；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1215232_comment'></div>重轻殖货，愧刘晏之钱流。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1215232_comment'></div>偶缘岁月之劳，遂玷云天之泽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1215232_comment'></div>迹其忝冒，实自吹嘘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1215232_comment'></div>某官名重搢绅，望隆朝野。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1215232_comment'></div>器藏清庙之瑚琏，材并豫章之楩楠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1215232_comment'></div>治行已著于龚、黄，人物独高于许、郭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1215232_comment'></div>借其馀论，得被甄收。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1215232_comment'></div>愧驰谢之未遑，辱赐书之先及。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1215232_comment'></div>莫报琼瑶之赠，但为箧笥之珍。</div><div id='poem_sentence_11_1215232_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1215230' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1215230' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1215230?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其三 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1123年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1215230_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1215230'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1215230'>奉使十年，愧无功于毫发；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1215230_comment'></div>转输一路，复冒宠于云天。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1215230_comment'></div>自惭燕雀之微，辄厕鹓鸿之列。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1215230_comment'></div>省躬无有，抚己若惊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1215230_comment'></div>惟国家留意于远人，而庙堂责成于使者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1215230_comment'></div>委以观风于千里，考其治行于三年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1215230_comment'></div>内则与主计者任赢虚，外则与牧民者同休戚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1215230_comment'></div>眷兹重寄，宜属异能。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1215230_comment'></div>而某才不逮人，学专为己。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1215230_comment'></div>远惭齐相，素无狱市之容；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1215230_comment'></div>近类绛侯，不知钱谷之对。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1215230_comment'></div>夫何忝冒，下逮庸虚！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1215230_comment'></div>此盖某官杞梓良材，圭璋重器。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1215230_comment'></div>以经术润吏事，以仁义陈王前。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1215230_comment'></div>嘘枯吹生，得育才之三乐；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1215230_comment'></div>绝长补短，无求备于一夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1215230_comment'></div>致此恩荣，尽荷吹借。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1215230_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_17_1215230_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
临城
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='66a76fc80bf94de59c2cef8f6be897eb_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("66a76fc80bf94de59c2cef8f6be897eb");'><span id='66a76fc80bf94de59c2cef8f6be897eb_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1094&endYear=1094')">1094年</a>，23岁</div><div id='66a76fc80bf94de59c2cef8f6be897eb' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1094&endYear=1094')">1094年</a>　四月三日，苏轼以前掌制命，有讥讪神宗之嫌，落职英州。苏迈、苏迨、苏过同行。过临城，苏轼作诗付苏过。<br /></div>
-----end



-----title
汤阴
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='ba5f35713a274798a079af2ba2e6079a_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("ba5f35713a274798a079af2ba2e6079a");'><span id='ba5f35713a274798a079af2ba2e6079a_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1094&endYear=1094')">1094年</a>，23岁</div><div id='ba5f35713a274798a079af2ba2e6079a' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1094&endYear=1094')">1094年</a>　过汤阴，食豌豆大麦粥，苏轼作诗付迈、迨、过。<br /></div>
-----end

-----title
临汝
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='f90562d270e24c3882cc96d1d1600573_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("f90562d270e24c3882cc96d1d1600573");'><span id='f90562d270e24c3882cc96d1d1600573_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1094&endYear=1094')">1094年</a>，23岁</div><div id='f90562d270e24c3882cc96d1d1600573' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1094&endYear=1094')">1094年</a>　苏轼挈家过汝州，苏辙分俸七千，使苏迈就食宜兴。苏过等未免丧，从父南迁，哀毁之情，动于涂人。<br /></div>
-----end



-----title
湖口
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='f39ddb8bb492459b8333e16219539aae_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("f39ddb8bb492459b8333e16219539aae");'><span id='f39ddb8bb492459b8333e16219539aae_link' class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《斜川集校注》（苏过原著、舒大刚等校注，巴蜀书社1996年12月版。下同）卷一。苏轼《壶中九华诗》（并引），见《苏轼诗集》卷三十八。）</span><div id='poem_522673' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_522673' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31323, "北宋", "苏过", "poem_title_522673")'>苏过</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_522673_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_522673'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_522673'>至人寓迹尘凡中，杖头挂壶来何从。<div id='poem_sentence_0_522673_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_522673'>长房俗眼偶澄澈，一笑市井得此翁。<div id='poem_sentence_1_522673_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_522673'>试窥壶中子无物，何处著此千柱宫。<div id='poem_sentence_4_522673'>我闻须弥纳芥子，况此空洞孰不容。<div id='poem_sentence_4_522673_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_522673'>何人误持一嶂出，恍是九华巉绝峰。<div id='poem_sentence_5_522673_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_522673'>令人却信刘郎语，当年霹雳化九龙。<div id='poem_sentence_6_522673_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_522673'>谁将真形写此石，太华女几分清雄。<div id='poem_sentence_7_522673_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_522673'>终当作亭号秋浦，刻公妙句传无穷。<div -----title
赣州
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='f6d7aa09992742c69aa94da58eee2099_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("f6d7aa09992742c69aa94da58eee2099");'><span id='f6d7aa09992742c69aa94da58eee2099_link' href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1094&endYear=1094')">1094年8月</a>　八月，过虔州，苏过与父游郁孤台。苏轼作诗，过亦有《题郁孤台》一篇。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《斜川集校注》卷一。苏轼所作诗为《郁孤台》，见《苏轼诗集》卷三十八。）</span><div id='poem_522713' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_522713' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/522713?labeling=true' target='_blank'>题郁孤台</a><span class='authorDate'>（1094年8月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31323, "北宋", "苏过", "poem_title_522713")'>苏过</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言排律</div></div><div id='poem_title_522713_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_522713'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_522713'>泽国风烟恶，平居念少游。<div id='poem_sentence_0_522713_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_522713'>三冬霜树少，八月火云流。<div id='poem_sentence_1_522713_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_522713'>旅馆那堪暑，危台独觉秋。<div id='poem_sentence_2_522713_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_522713'>远林藏小寺，虚市隔孤洲。<div id='poem_sentence_3_522713_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_522713'>日落山衔碧，江昏蜃吐楼。<div id='poem_sentence_4_522713_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_522713'>云峰连北斗，鸟道绝南州。<div id='poem_sentence_5_522713_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_522713'>丘壑从兹逝，轩裳岂足留。<div id='poem_sentence_6_522713_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_522713'>终当思范蠡，归泛五湖舟。<div id='poem_sentence_7_522713_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_522713'></div><div id='poem_sentence_8_522713_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='b93b9075c6a443cea683877183d37b8d_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("b93b9075c6a443cea683877183d37b8d");'><span id='b93b9075c6a443cea683877183d37b8d_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1101&endYear=1101')">1101年</a>，30岁</div><div id='b93b9075c6a443cea683877183d37b8d' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1101&endYear=1101')">1101年1月</a>　正月渡大庾岭，抵虔州。得孙志举寄书，见苏迟《赠孙志举》诗，苏过与父皆和。作品：《用伯充韵赠孙志举》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《斜川集校注》卷二。苏轼诗为《和犹子迟赠孙志举》，见《苏轼诗集》卷四十五。）</span><div id='poem_522672' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_522672' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/522672?labeling=true' target='_blank'>用伯充韵赠孙志举</a><span class='authorDate'>（1101年1月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31323, "北宋", "苏过", "poem_title_522672")'>苏过</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_522672_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_522672'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_522672'>朱颜染黄茅，自意岭表人。<div id='poem_sentence_0_522672_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_522672'>长恬服世俗，敢愧歠菽贫。<div id='poem_sentence_1_522672_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_522672'>送车反自厓，异獠纷来宾。<div id='poem_sentence_2_522672_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_522672'>蛙蝝与蚔醢，敬我如族姻<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_3_522672_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_522672'>海风吹余舟，夜渡徐闻垠。<div id='poem_sentence_4_522672_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_522672'>往来一沤间，劳生竟非真。<div id='poem_sentence_5_522672_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_522672'>重寻江南游，再款空同闉。<div id='poem_sentence_6_522672_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_522672'>山中有异士，束书来卜邻。<div id='poem_sentence_7_522672_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_522672'>胸中出虹霓，雷袂勇且仁。<div id='poem_sentence_8_522672_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_522672'>索居□枯槁，赖此意少春。<div id='poem_sentence_9_522672_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_522672'>当年老于公，硬语本为民。<div id='poem_sentence_10_522672_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_522672'>终身虽坎壈，谁得疏而亲。<div id='poem_sentence_11_522672_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_522672'>臧孙固有后，仲子先离伦。<div id='poem_sentence_12_522672_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_522672'>不忧廊庙迟，绿发未肯银。<div id='poem_sentence_13_522672_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_522672'>季子又一奇，武库戈矛新。<div id='poem_sentence_14_522672_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_522672'>片言折鹿角，不许枝词谆。<div id='poem_sentence_15_522672_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_522672'>近闻获麟书，还许登成均。<div id='poem_sentence_16_522672_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_522672'>归欤汶上兄，器新人惟陈<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑵</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_17_522672_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_522672'></div><div id='poem_sentence_18_522672_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_522672'><span class='label'>按：</span>以上《斜川集》卷一<br /><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_3_522672_0'>⑴ 自注：南夷风俗，非姻家不得与蛙蛤蚁酱之会。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_17_522672_0'>⑵ 自注：志康兄以《春秋》第一人登第。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_522672_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1101&endYear=1101')">1101年</a>　苏过有《江天上梁文》，当作于虔州。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《斜川集校注》卷八。）</span><div id='poem_1215299' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1215299' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1215299?labeling=true' target='_blank'>江天上梁文</a><span class='authorDate'>（1101年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31323, "北宋", "苏过", "poem_title_1215299")'>苏过</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1215299_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1215299'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1215299'>鄱川泽国，楚地名邦，民物阜藩，有山水禽鱼之乐；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1215299_comment'></div>人情朴愿，无陂池台榭之娱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1215299_comment'></div>谁知隐莽之丘，乃得宽闲之野。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1215299_comment'></div>天怜此老，日逐斯游。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1215299_comment'></div>野处老人年过七旬，仕尝三黜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1215299_comment'></div>黄粱入梦，每惭四禁之清；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1215299_comment'></div>碧瓦照城，坐占两园之胜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1215299_comment'></div>眷兹东圃，实傍北门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1215299_comment'></div>经营不辍于历年，指顾尽谐于佳趣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1215299_comment'></div>呀然成谷，宛一壑之神剜；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1215299_comment'></div>幽处生云，叹三峰之匠巧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1215299_comment'></div>北升高阜，复刱新亭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1215299_comment'></div>阁山蟠踞以南临，芝岭翚翔而后镇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1215299_comment'></div>万家井邑，近列目前。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1215299_comment'></div>百丈桅樯，远从烟际。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1215299_comment'></div>结庐在人境，岂嫌车马之喧；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1215299_comment'></div>恣意买江天，宁复藩篱之限。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1215299_comment'></div>戏裁长句，以侑修梁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1215299_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_1215299'>东，买断江天景不穷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1215299_comment'></div>万树碧桃开未遍，神仙应在此山中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1215299_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_20_1215299'>西，旋凿方塘著淤泥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1215299_comment'></div>种得芳莲千叶盛，他年拟作钓璜溪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1215299_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_22_1215299'>南，春著人间醉欲酣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1215299_comment'></div>天际归舟谁认得，满城烟柳正毵毵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1215299_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_24_1215299'>北，处处亭台共燕息。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1215299_comment'></div>士女如云任意来，芝山自此无颜色。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1215299_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_26_1215299'>上，落絮游丝春骀荡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1215299_comment'></div>寒食清明十日晴，危栏倚遍成高唱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1215299_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_28_1215299'>下，胜事清时无论价。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1215299_comment'></div>只有丹青可作图，范宽老去谁能画。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1215299_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_30_1215299'>伏愿上梁之后，优游卒岁，安乐延年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1215299_comment'></div>酿酒千钟，不怕临川之客；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1215299_comment'></div>种花万本，或招鳌洞之仙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1215299_comment'></div>凡我往来，共兹庆快。</div><div id='poem_sentence_33_1215299_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1101&endYear=1101')">1101年2月</a>　苏过舅父王箴（元直）将访苏过与父于海南，二月卒于途。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1101&endYear=1101')">1101年3月</a>　三月下旬，离虔州。四月，至南康军；十二日，苏过侍父为刘义仲题写墓表。<br /></div>
-----end

-----title
清远
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='41f6ac57c3364cce8a1b4b5f243a0569_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("41f6ac57c3364cce8a1b4b5f243a0569");'><span id='41f6ac57c3364cce8a1b4b5f243a0569_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1094&endYear=1094')">1094年</a>，23岁</div><div id='41f6ac57c3364cce8a1b4b5f243a0569' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1094&endYear=1094')">1094年9月13日</a>　九月十三日，至广州清远峡，苏过侍父游峡山寺。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1094&endYear=1094')">1094年9月</a>　至清远县，苏轼父子见顾秀才，极谈惠州风物之美，游城西天庆观。侍父游广州白云山蒲涧寺、滴水岩诸胜，访安期生旧迹；与蒲涧信长老别，发扶胥口，游南海诸庙，登浴日亭。<br /></div>

-----title
广州
-----detail

id='poem_522554' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_522554' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/522554?labeling=true' target='_blank'>将至五羊先寄伯达仲豫二兄</a><span class='authorDate'>（1100年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31323, "北宋", "苏过", "poem_title_522554")'>苏过</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_522554_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_522554'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_522554'>人皆有离别，我别不忍道。<div id='poem_sentence_0_522554_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_522554'>惟应付梦幻，事已共一笑。<div id='poem_sentence_1_522554_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_522554'>忆昔与仲别，秦淮汇秋潦。<div id='poem_sentence_2_522554_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_522554'>相望一叶舟，目断飞鸿杳。<div id='poem_sentence_3_522554_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_522554'>伯兄阳羡来，万里踰烟峤。<div id='poem_sentence_4_522554_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_522554'>未温白鹤席，已饯罗浮晓。<div id='poem_sentence_5_522554_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_522554'>江边空忍泪，我亦肝肠绕。<div id='poem_sentence_6_522554_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_522554'>崎岖七年中，云海用浩渺。<div id='poem_sentence_7_522554_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_522554'>岂知羌村晚，惊拜杜陵老。<div id='poem_sentence_8_522554_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_522554'>干戈虽事异，欢喜动夷獠。<div id='poem_sentence_9_522554_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_522554'>山川旧悽惨，云物今清好。<div id='poem_sentence_10_522554_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_522554'>不似玄都桃，秋风不堪扫。<div id='poem_sentence_11_522554_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_522554'></div><div id='poem_sentence_12_522554_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1100&endYear=1100')">1100年10月</a>　十月，抵广州，苏迈、苏迨及苏簟、苏符、苏籥等家小皆至。迨告以参寥子编管，复落发事。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1100&endYear=1100')">1100年</a>　在广州，盘桓月余，苏迈、苏迨、苏过等陪父轼遍游羊城名胜。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1100&endYear=1100')">1100年</a>　在广州。谢举廉（民师）来访，赠诗苏过，过次其韵。作品：《次韵谢民师》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《斜川集校注》卷二。谢举廉原诗已佚。）</span><div id='poem_522678' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_522678' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/522678?labeling=true' target='_blank'>次韵谢民师</a><span class='authorDate'>（1100年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31323, "北宋", "苏过", "poem_title_522678")'>苏过</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_522678_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_522678'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_522678'>老鹤过海仍将雏，澹然如将没齿疏。<div id='poem_sentence_0_522678_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_522678'>人生如寄何足道，富贵贫贱隙白驹。<div id='poem_sentence_1_522678_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_522678'>飘流仅以虞夫子，饥坐弦歌古儋耳。<div id='poem_sentence_2_522678_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_522678'>不堪秦岭望家山，敢有玉关生入理。<div id='poem_sentence_3_522678_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_522678'>广文才名三十年，困穷直到寒无毡。<div id='poem_sentence_4_522678_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_522678'>将军夜行遭醉尉，曲逆解衣尝刺船。<div id='poem_sentence_5_522678_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_522678'>岂知雷雨来说渥，归路江山宛如昨。<div id='poem_sentence_6_522678_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_522678'>饥人但觉秕糠美，忧患始知田舍乐。<div id='poem_sentence_7_522678_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_522678'>梦中犹记鱼相濡，庄叟屡困监河枯。<div id='poem_sentence_8_522678_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_522678'>聊因竞病歌归欤，宁复灿烂悲穷途。<div id='poem_sentence_9_522678_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_522678'>知君笃学真为己，不从世好惟耽此。<div id='poem_sentence_10_522678_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_522678'>作诗颇似建安风，取友更同鲍叔义。<div id='poem_sentence_11_522678_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_522678'>我闻得士朝廷尊，搢绅所寄惟斯文。<div id='poem_sentence_12_522678_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_522678'>象犀珠玉本安用，犹使四海争趋奔。<div id='poem_sentence_13_522678_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_522678'>高人处世诚难矣，绝俗惊愚空目眯。<div id='poem_sentence_14_522678_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_522678'>坐令瑚琏废清庙，涧毛何由荐天子。<div id='poem_sentence_15_522678_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_522678'>我羡平生马少游，不愿沟渎容吞舟。<div id='poem_sentence_16_522678_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_522678'>夜光明月请自閟，按剑或恐疑轻投。<div id='poem_sentence_17_522678_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_522678'></div><div id='poem_sentence_18_522678_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1100&endYear=1100')">1100年11月</a>　十一月离廉州，十二月至韶州。<br /></div>

博罗

ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1094&endYear=1094')">1094年9月27日</a>　在归善。九月二十七日，至浮罗山，苏过侍父游浮罗，父子均有诗。作品：《和大人游浮罗山》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《斜川集校注》卷一。苏轼诗为《游浮罗山一首示二子过》，见《苏轼诗集》卷三十八。）</span><div id='poem_522674' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_522674' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/522674?labeling=true' target='_blank'>和大人游罗浮山</a><span class='authorDate'>（1094年9月27日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31323, "北宋", "苏过", "poem_title_522674")'>苏过</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_522674_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_522674'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_522674'>我公阴德谁与京，学道岂厌迟蜚鸣。<div id='poem_sentence_0_522674_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_522674'>世间出世无两得，先使此路荒承明。<div id='poem_sentence_1_522674_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_522674'>谪官罗浮定天意，不涉忧患那长生。<div id='poem_sentence_2_522674_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_522674'>海涯莫惊万里远，山下幸足五亩耕。<div id='poem_sentence_3_522674_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_522674'>人生露电非虚语，在椿固已悲老彭。<div id='poem_sentence_4_522674_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_522674'>蓬莱方丈今咫尺，富贵敝屣孰重轻。<div id='poem_sentence_5_522674_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_522674'>结茅愿为麋鹿友，无心坐伏豺虎狞。<div id='poem_sentence_6_522674_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_522674'>况公方瞳已照座，奕奕神光在天庭。<div id='poem_sentence_7_522674_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_522674'>出青入玄二气换，妙理默契黄庭经。<div id='poem_sentence_8_522674_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_522674'>但愿他时仇池主，不愿更勒燕然铭。<div id='poem_sentence_9_522674_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_522674'>稚川刀圭傥可得，簪组永谢汉公卿。<div id='poem_sentence_10_522674_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_522674'>腹中梨枣晚自成，本无荆棘何所平。<div id='poem_sentence_11_522674_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_522674'></div><div id='poem_sentence_12_522674_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
惠州

href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1094&endYear=1094')">1094年10月2日</a>　十月二日，到达惠州，惠之父老夹道相迎。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1094&endYear=1094')">1094年</a>　初寓居合江楼，继迁嘉祐寺。在惠州，凡苏轼生理所需，过一身任之。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1094&endYear=1094')">1094年</a>　在归善。嘉祐寺旁有松风亭，为苏过父子寓居游观之所，过作有《松风亭词》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《斜川集校注》卷一。）</span><div id='poem_522711' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_522711_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_522711'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_522711'>乱一水兮清泠，绝尘市兮郊坰。<div id='poem_sentence_0_522711_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_522711'>郁松风之参差，忽飞构兮危亭。<div id='poem_sentence_1_522711_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_522711'>悲风来兮号沧溟，寒月出兮款户庭。<div id='poem_sentence_2_522711_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_522711'>听万籁兮发无形，感穷岁兮物彫零。<div id='poem_sentence_5_522711'>二江东来兮势建瓴，千山右绕兮环翠屏。<div id='poem_sentence_5_522711_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_522711'>彼柴门兮昼常扃，屏外物兮返视听。<div id='poem_sentence_12_522711_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_522711'>余师首阳之清德兮，超千古而犹馨。<div id='poem_sentence_13_522711_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' class='authorDate'>（1095年1月2日）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_522645_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_522645'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_522645_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_522645'>百年过隙尔，朝不及谋夕。<div id='poem_sentence_2_522645_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_522645'>吾驾当早回，覆车岂无迹。<div id='poem_sentence_3_522645_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_522645'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_522645_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1095&endYear=1095')">1095年1月24日</a>　在归善。正月二十四日，苏过侍父与王原（子直）等游惠州罗浮道院、栖禅山寺，作诗；苏轼次其韵，寄阳羡苏迈、苏迨。作品：《正月二十四日侍亲游罗浮道院栖禅山寺》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《斜川集校注》卷一。苏轼诗为《正月二十四日与儿子过赖仙芝王原秀才僧昙颖行全道士何宗一同游罗浮道院及栖禅精舍过作诗和其韵寄迈迨一首》，见《苏轼诗集》卷三十九。）</span><div id='poem_522546' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_522546' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/522546?labeling=true' target='_blank'>正月二十四日侍亲游罗浮道院栖禅山寺</a><span class='authorDate'>（1095年1月24日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31323, "北宋", "苏过", "poem_title_522546")'>苏过</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_522546_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_522546'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_522546'>淡云晓葱茏，野水清可揭。<div id='poem_sentence_0_522546_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_522546'>山明草木秀，使里见琐细。<div id='poem_sentence_1_522546_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_522546'>人闲境愈静，地暖春先逝。<div id='poem_sentence_2_522546_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_522546'>桃李已青枝，落花空覆砌。<div id='poem_sentence_3_522546_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_522546'>凉风稍可爱，习习来衣袂。<div id='poem_sentence_4_522546_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_522546'>赤日虽未苦，炎炎逼裘毳。<div id='poem_sentence_5_522546_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_522546'>道人疑有道，羽服襟裳弊。<div id='poem_sentence_6_522546_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_522546'>晨斋爨无烟，含糗聊卒岁。<div id='poem_sentence_7_522546_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_522546'>空阶指荜拨，破屋缘薜荔。<div id='poem_sentence_8_522546_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_522546'>拄杖挑笋蕨，折柳樊兰蕙。<div id='poem_sentence_9_522546_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_522546'>居夷信何陋，即此可遁世。<div id='poem_sentence_10_522546_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_522546'>敢师浴乎沂，不数山阴禊。<div id='poem_sentence_11_522546_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_522546'>人生行乐耳，四海皆兄弟。<div id='poem_sentence_12_522546_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_522546'>何必怀故乡，吾驾随所税。<div id='poem_sentence_13_522546_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_522546'></div><div id='poem_sentence_14_522546_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1095&endYear=1095')">1095年2月11日</a>　二月十一日，苏轼书陶渊明诗付苏过。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1095&endYear=1095')">1095年3月4日</a>　三月四日，苏过诵陶渊明《归园田居》诗，苏轼闻而和之。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1095&endYear=1095')">1095年3月4日</a>　三月四日，苏轼得参寥专使寄书，又得陈慥（季常）书，作书答陈季常，盛赞苏过兄弟。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1095&endYear=1095')">1095年3月7日</a>　三月七日，程之才（正辅）巡按广州，是日至惠州，迎之者即苏过。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1095&endYear=1095')">1095年3月19日</a>　三月十九日，迁居合江楼。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1095&endYear=1095')">1095年3月</a>　在归善。三月末，王原归，苏过父子均有诗赠之。作品：《赠王子直》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《斜川集校注》卷一。苏轼诗为《赠王子直秀才》，见《苏轼诗集》卷三十九。）</span><div id='poem_522670' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_522670' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/522670?labeling=true' target='_blank'>赠王子直</a><span class='authorDate'>（1095年3月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31323, "北宋", "苏过", "poem_title_522670")'>苏过</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_522670_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_522670'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_522670'>南行几万里，亲旧书亦缺。<div id='poem_sentence_0_522670_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_522670'>谁知倾盖交，乃胜白头节。<div id='poem_sentence_1_522670_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_522670'>去国日已远，凄凉瘴烟窟。<div id='poem_sentence_2_522670_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_522670'>未著绝交书，已叹交游绝。<div id='poem_sentence_3_522670_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_522670'>门前空雀罗，巷语纷鴃舌。<div id='poem_sentence_4_522670_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_522670'>怪君一事无，访我此穷发。<div id='poem_sentence_5_522670_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_522670'>自怜甑生尘，每愧羹屡颉。<div id='poem_sentence_6_522670_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_522670'>何以为子娱，江水清可啜。<div id='poem_sentence_7_522670_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_522670'>男儿重志气，勿使变穷达。<div id='poem_sentence_8_522670_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_522670'>宁甘一瓢乐，耻为五斗折。<div id='poem_sentence_9_522670_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_522670'>火急数相聚，回头君欲别。<div id='poem_sentence_10_522670_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_522670'>一榻当再悬，重来为君设。<div id='poem_sentence_11_522670_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_522670'></div><div id='poem_sentence_12_522670_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1095&endYear=1095')">1095年</a>　初夏，淫雨江涨，苏过作《江涨》诗，父轼、叔辙皆有和作。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1095&endYear=1095')">1095年</a>　苏轼致书徐大正（得之），赞苏过。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1095&endYear=1095')">1095年5月</a>　五月，苏轼寄书王巩，赞苏过超然物外。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1095&endYear=1095')">1095年8月1日</a>　八月一日，苏过书《金光明经》成，苏轼作跋，赞其纯孝。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1095&endYear=1095')">1095年</a>　在归善。广州、惠州飓风，毁树拔屋，苏过作《飓风赋》，一时驰名。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此赋见《斜川集校注》卷七。）</span><div id='poem_1215218' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1215218' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1215218?labeling=true' target='_blank'>飓风赋<span class='inlineComment2'>（并叙绍圣二年）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1095年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31323, "北宋", "苏过", "poem_title_1215218")'>苏过</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1215218_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1215218'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1215218'>《南越志》：熙安间多飓风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1215218_comment'></div>飓者，具四方之风也，尝以五六月发。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1215218_comment'></div>未至时，鸡犬为之不鸣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1215218_comment'></div>又《岭表录》云：秋夏间有晕如虹者，谓之飓母，必有飘风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1215218_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_1215218'>仲秋之夕，客有叩门，指云物而告予曰：「海氛甚恶，非祲非祥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1215218_comment'></div>断霓饮海而北指，赤云夹日而南翔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1215218_comment'></div>此飓之渐也，子盍备之」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1215218_comment'></div>语未卒，庭户<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_7_1215218", 1215218, "Clauses/21/Comments/0")'>肃然</span>，槁叶蔌蔌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1215218_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_8_1215218", 1215218, "Clauses/23/Comments/0")'>惊鸟</span>疾呼，怖兽辟易。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1215218_comment'></div>忽野马之决骤，矫退飞之六鹢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1215218_comment'></div>袭<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_10_1215218", 1215218, "Clauses/27/Comments/0")'>土囊</span>之暴怒，持众窍之叱吸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1215218_comment'></div>予乃入室而坐，敛衽变色。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1215218_comment'></div>客曰：「未也，此飓之先驱尔」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1215218_comment'></div>少焉，排户破牖，陨瓦擗屋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1215218_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_14_1215218", 1215218, "Clauses/37/Comments/0")'>礧击</span>巨石，揉拔乔木。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1215218_comment'></div>势翻渤澥，响振坤轴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1215218_comment'></div>疑屏翳之赫怒，执阳侯而将戮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1215218_comment'></div>鼓千尺之涛澜，襄百仞之<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_17_1215218", 1215218, "Clauses/44/Comments/0")'>陵谷</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1215218_comment'></div>吞泥沙于一卷，落崩崖于再触。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1215218_comment'></div>列万马而并骛，溃千车而争逐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1215218_comment'></div>虎豹詟骇，鲸鲲奔蹙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1215218_comment'></div>类钜鹿之战，殷声呼而动地；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1215218_comment'></div>似昆阳之役，举百万于一覆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1215218_comment'></div>予亦为之股慄<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_23_1215218", 1215218, "Clauses/55/Comments/0")'>毛耸</span>，索气侧足。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1215218_comment'></div>夜拊榻而九徙，昼命龟而三卜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1215218_comment'></div>盖三日而后息也，父老来唁，酒浆罗列。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1215218_comment'></div>劳来僮仆，惧定而说。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1215218_comment'></div>理草木之既偃，葺轩槛之已折。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1215218_comment'></div>补茅屋之罅漏，塞墙垣之颓缺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1215218_comment'></div>已而山林寂然，水波不兴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1215218_comment'></div>动者自止，鸣者自停。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1215218_comment'></div>湛天宇之苍苍，流孤月之荧荧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1215218_comment'></div>忽悟且叹，莫知所营。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1215218_comment'></div>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1215218_comment'></div>小大出于相形，忧喜因于所遇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1215218_comment'></div>昔之飘然者，若为巨邪？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1215218_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_36_1215218", 1215218, "Clauses/81/Comments/0")'>吹万</span>不同，果足怖邪？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1215218_comment'></div>蚁之缘也嘘则坠，蚋之集也呵则举。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1215218_comment'></div>夫嘘呵曾不能以振物，而施之二虫则甚惧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1215218_comment'></div>鹏水击而三千，抟扶摇而九万。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1215218_comment'></div>彼视吾之惴慄，亦尔汝之相莞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1215218_comment'></div>均大块之噫气，奚巨细之足辨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1215218_comment'></div>陋耳目之不广，为外物之所变。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1215218_comment'></div>且夫万象起灭，众怪耀炫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1215218_comment'></div>求髣髴于过耳，视空中之飞电。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1215218_comment'></div>则向之所谓可惧者，实邪虚邪？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1215218_comment'></div>惜吾知之晚也。</div><div id='poem_sentence_46_1215218_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1095&endYear=1095')">1095年</a>　重九渐近，苏轼作和陶诗，令苏过同作，寄许昌、高安、宜兴诸兄弟。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1095&endYear=1095')">1095年9月</a>　在归善。九月既望之后，苏轼与客夜游惠州西湖诸胜，赏月，逮晓乃归，作《江月五首》，苏过次韵。作品：《次韵大人五更山吐月》（其一）<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《斜川集校注》卷一。苏轼诗为《江月五首》（并引），见《苏轼诗集》卷三十九。）</span>《次韵大人五更山吐月》（其二）<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《斜川集校注》卷一。）</span>《次韵大人五更山吐月》（其三）<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《斜川集校注》卷一。）</span>《次韵大人五更山吐月》（其四）<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《斜川集校注》卷一。）</span>《次韵大人五更山吐月》（其五）<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《斜川集校注》卷一。）</span><div id='poem_522665' "poem_title_522665")'>苏过</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_522665_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_522665'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_522665'>一更山吐月，鉴影摇空澜。<div id='poem_sentence_0_522665_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_522665'>悬知今夕游，不减蓬瀛看。<div id='poem_sentence_1_522665_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_522665'>净雾扫馀瘴，清飙戒初寒。<div id='poem_sentence_2_522665_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_522665'>行乐不可迟，乃此桂未残。<div id='poem_sentence_3_522665_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_522665'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_522665_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_522666' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_522666' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/522666?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1095年9月）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_522666_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_522666'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_522666'>二更山吐月，玉杯侧清夜。<div id='poem_sentence_0_522666_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_522666_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_522666'>他时罗浮录，父老成佳话。<div id='poem_sentence_3_522666_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_title_522667_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_522667'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_522667'>三更山吐月，半璧沈沈起。<div id='poem_sentence_0_522667_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_522667'>无言三友欢，夜夜仍会此。<div id='poem_sentence_1_522667_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_522668' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/522668?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其四 </span></a><span id='poem_sentence_1_522668_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_522668'>束缊旋乞火，犬号惊夜行。<div id='poem_sentence_2_522668_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence'
