id='poem_sentence_4_522669'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_522669_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1095&endYear=1095')">1095年</a>　苏过在惠州，有《咏三瘦》诗。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《斜川集校注》卷六。）</span><div id='poem_522829' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_522829' class='poemContent' id='poem_content_522829'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_522829'>勿轻三士各鸢肩，气吐虹霓诗涌泉。<div id='poem_sentence_0_522829_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1095&endYear=1095')">1095年</a>　在归善。苏轼作《小圃五咏》，苏过亦作诗，今存二首。作品：《人参》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《斜川集校注》卷六。苏轼《小圃五咏》，见《苏轼诗集》卷三十九。）</span>《枸杞》<span id='poem_sentence_0_522547'>草木异所禀，甘苦分炎凉。<div id='poem_sentence_0_522547_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_522547'>人参独中和，群药敢雁行。<div id='poem_sentence_1_522547_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_522547'>虽微瞑眩力，颇著难老方。<div id='poem_sentence_2_522547_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_522547'>譬之古循吏，有益初无伤。<div id='poem_sentence_3_522547_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_522547'>安神补五脏，自使精魄强。<div id='poem_sentence_4_522547_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_522547'>罗浮仙者居，灵质不自藏。<div id='poem_sentence_5_522547_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_522547'>移根植膏壤，桠叶粲以长。<div id='poem_sentence_6_522547_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_522547'>东南虽异产，辽海谁能航。<div id='poem_sentence_7_522547_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_522547'>誓将北归日，从我涉汉湘。<div id='poem_sentence_8_522547_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_522547_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_522548' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_522548' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/522548?labeling=true' id='poem_sentence_0_522548'>春槃撷新芽，秋篚得红实。<div id='poem_sentence_0_522548_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_522548'>霜根酿我醪，色味两奇绝。<div id='poem_sentence_4_522548_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_522548'>食前得珍蔬，新酿扫故疾。<div id='poem_sentence_5_522548_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_522548_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_522548'>西河安可冀，北归愿如昔。<div id='poem_sentence_8_522548_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_522548'>区区摘苍耳，粗陋非所敌。<div id='poem_sentence_9_522548_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_522548'></div><div id='poem_sentence_10_522548_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1095&endYear=1095')">1095年11月</a>　十一月，朝廷郊赦，独元祐党人不赦，且终身不徙。元祐臣僚，再申严谴，黄庭坚（鲁直）、张耒（文潜）俱坐谪。张耒徙宣州，来书，并传苏迈、苏迨家信。苏轼作答，书中甚赞苏过有干蛊之才。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1095&endYear=1095')">1095年12月19日</a>　在归善。十二月十九日，苏轼生日作诗，苏过次其韵。作品：《次大人生日》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《斜川集校注》卷一。苏轼所作诗已佚。）</span><div id='poem_522679' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_522679' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/522679?labeling=true' target='_blank'>次大人生日</a><span class='authorDate'>（1095年12月19日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31323, "北宋", "苏过", "poem_title_522679")'>苏过</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_522679_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_522679'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_522679'>阴功若以物假人，酬而不酢非所闻。<div id='poem_sentence_0_522679_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_522679'>丙吉于公德在民，皇天有善初无亲。<div id='poem_sentence_1_522679_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_522679'>自我高曾逮公身，奕世载德一于仁。<div id='poem_sentence_2_522679_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_522679'>遇苦即救志劬辛，岂择富贵与贱贫。<div id='poem_sentence_3_522679_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_522679'>久推是心诚而均，可贯白日照苍旻。<div id='poem_sentence_4_522679_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_522679'>譬如农夫耘耔勤，自有丰年穫千囷。<div id='poem_sentence_5_522679_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_522679'>公何屡困蝇与蚊，身虽厄穷道益信。<div id='poem_sentence_6_522679_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_522679'>天不俾之爵禄新，琢磨功行真人邻。<div id='poem_sentence_7_522679_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_522679'>直言便触天子嗔，万里远谪南海滨。<div id='poem_sentence_8_522679_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_522679'>朝夕异引存吾神，两仪入腹如车轮。<div id='poem_sentence_9_522679_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_522679'>罗浮至今馀怪珍，稚川药灶隐荆榛。<div id='poem_sentence_10_522679_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_522679'>飞腾涧谷不可驯，月道或肯来相宾。<div id='poem_sentence_11_522679_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_522679'>区区功名安足云，幸此不为世俗醺。<div id='poem_sentence_12_522679_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_522679'>丹砂傥结道力纯，泠然御风归峨岷。<div id='poem_sentence_13_522679_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_522679'></div><div id='poem_sentence_14_522679_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1095&endYear=1095')">1095年</a>　苏过父子曾欲令侄孙苏彭带苏过一房来，未果。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1095&endYear=1095')">1095年</a>　苏轼与孙勰（志康）书，告以明年苏迈当南来，且携苏过一房同来。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1095&endYear=1095')">1095年</a>　苏过画偃松屏风，苏轼作赞。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1095&endYear=1095')">1095年</a>　在归善。苏轼命苏过作《思子台赋》，并为作叙。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此赋见《斜川集校注》卷七。苏轼所作为《思子台赋》（并引），见《苏轼文集》卷一。此条活动具体时地不详，姑系于此。）</span><div id='poem_1215217' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1215217' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1215217?labeling=true' target='_blank'>思子台赋</a><span class='authorDate'>（1095年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31323, "北宋", "苏过", "poem_title_1215217")'>苏过</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1215217_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1215217'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1215217'>客有自蜀游梁，傃关而东。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1215217_comment'></div>览河华之形胜兮，访秦汉之遗宫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1215217_comment'></div>得岿然之颓基兮，并湖城之西墉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1215217_comment'></div>吊汉武之暴怒兮，悼戾园之悯凶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1215217_comment'></div>闻父老之哀叹兮，犹有归来望思之<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_4_1215217", 1215217, "Clauses/9/Comments/0")'>遗恫</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1215217_comment'></div>吁犬台之<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_5_1215217", 1215217, "Clauses/10/Comments/0")'>谗颊</span>兮，实咀毒而<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_5_1215217", 1215217, "Clauses/11/Comments/0")'>衔锋</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1215217_comment'></div>败赵国于俛仰兮，又将覆刘氏之宗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1215217_comment'></div>闻汉武之多忌兮，谓左右之皆戎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1215217_comment'></div>杀阳石而未厌兮，又瘗祸于宫中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1215217_comment'></div>忸君王之好杀兮，视人命犹昆虫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1215217_comment'></div>死者几何人兮，岂问骨肉与王公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1215217_comment'></div>惑狂傅之浅谋兮，不忍忿忿而杀充。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1215217_comment'></div>上曾不鉴予之无聊兮，实有豕心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1215217_comment'></div>负此名而欲亡兮，天下其孰吾容。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1215217_comment'></div>苟逭死于泉鸠兮，冀稍久而自理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1215217_comment'></div>遘大患于仓猝兮，怀孤愤于永已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1215217_comment'></div>念君老而孰图兮，嗟肉食其多鄙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1215217_comment'></div>独三老与千秋兮，怀爱君之拳拳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1215217_comment'></div>犯雷霆之方怒兮，消积祸于一言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1215217_comment'></div>洗沈冤之无告兮，戮谗人其已晚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1215217_comment'></div>幸曾孙之无恙兮，亦足以慰夫九原。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1215217_comment'></div>虽筑台其何救兮，固知已往之不谏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1215217_comment'></div>魂茕茕其归来兮，盖庶几于复见也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1215217_comment'></div>昔秦之亡也，祸始于扶苏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1215217_comment'></div>眇斯高之羸豕兮，视其君如乳虎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1215217_comment'></div>曾纩息之未定兮，乃敢探其穴而啖其雏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1215217_comment'></div>在晋四世，有君不惠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1215217_comment'></div>孽妇晨雊，彊王定制。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1215217_comment'></div>惟悯怀之遭罹兮，实追踪于汉戾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1215217_comment'></div>顾孱后之何知兮，亦号呼于既逝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1215217_comment'></div>写馀哀于江陆兮，发故臣之幽契。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1215217_comment'></div>仍筑台以望思兮，盖援武以自例。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1215217_comment'></div>呜呼噫嘻！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1215217_comment'></div>可吊而不可哂兮，亦各言其子也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1215217_comment'></div>彼茂陵之雄杰兮，系九戎而鞭百蛮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1215217_comment'></div>笑尧禹而陋汤武兮，盖将与黄帝俱仙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1215217_comment'></div>及其失道于几微兮，狐鬼生于左臂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1215217_comment'></div>如婴儿之未孩兮，易耳目而不知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1215217_comment'></div>甘泉咫尺而不通兮，与式乾其何异？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1215217_comment'></div>既上配于秦皇兮，又下比于晋惠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1215217_comment'></div>君子是以知圣狂之本同，而聪明之不可恃也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1215217_comment'></div>览观古初，孰哲孰愚？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1215217_comment'></div>皆知<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_42_1215217", 1215217, "Clauses/83/Comments/0")'>指笑</span>乎前人，而莫知后之视予。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1215217_comment'></div>方汉武之盛也，肯自比于骊山之朽骨，而况于金墉之独夫乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1215217_comment'></div>自今观之，三后一律，皆以信谗而杀子，昵奸而败国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1215217_comment'></div>各筑台以寄哀，信同名而齐实。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1215217_comment'></div>彼<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_46_1215217", 1215217, "Clauses/94/Comments/0")'>昏庸</span>者固不足告也，吾将以为明主之龟策。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1215217_comment'></div>自建元以来，张汤、主父偃之流，与两丞相、三长史之徒，皆以无罪而夷灭，一言以就诛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1215217_comment'></div>曾无兴哀于既往，一洗其无辜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1215217_comment'></div>独于据也，悲歌慷慨，泣涕踌躇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1215217_comment'></div>呜呼哀哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1215217_comment'></div>莫有以楚灵王之言告者，曰：「人之爱其子也，亦如予乎」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1215217_comment'></div>天道好还，以德为符。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1215217_comment'></div>惟孟德之鸷忍兮，亦嗜杀以为娱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1215217_comment'></div>彼杨公之爱修兮，岂减吾之苍舒？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1215217_comment'></div>恨元化之不可作兮，然后知鼠辈之果无。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1215217_comment'></div>同舐犊于晚岁兮，又何怨于老臞？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1215217_comment'></div>吾将以嗜杀为戒也，故于末而并书。</div><div id='poem_sentence_57_1215217_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1096&endYear=1096')">1096年1月5日</a>　在归善。正月五日，父子出游，俱作和陶诗。作品：《次陶渊明正月五日<游斜川>韵》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《斜川集校注》卷一。苏轼和陶诗为《和陶<游斜川>》，见《苏轼诗集》卷四十二。）</span><div id='poem_522550' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_522550' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/522550?labeling=true' target='_blank'>次陶渊明正月五日游斜川韵</a><span class='authorDate'>（1096年1月5日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: id='poem_sentence_1_522550'>糟床有新注，何事不出游。<div id='poem_sentence_1_522550_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_522550'>春云翳薄日，磻石俯清流。<div ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1096&endYear=1096')">1096年3月</a>　三月，苏过与父在白鹤峰买地筑室，其营造之劳，过一人当之。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1096&endYear=1096')">1096年4月20日</a>　四月二十日，迁居嘉祐寺。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1096&endYear=1096')">1096年</a>　夏，兄苏迈授仁化县令。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1096&endYear=1096')">1096年</a>　苏过与父自种蔬菜，终年饱饫。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1096&endYear=1096')">1096年</a>　在归善。吴复古（子野）绝粒避谷，苏过作诗戏之，僧法芝（芝上人、昙秀）、道士陆惟忠皆和，苏轼亦次其韵。作品：《戏赠吴子野》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《斜川集校注》卷一。苏轼次韵诗为《吴子野绝粒不睡过作诗戏之芝上人陆道士皆和予亦次其韵》，见《苏轼诗集》卷四十；僧法芝、陆惟忠和诗未见。）</span><div id='poem_522827' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_522827' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1096&endYear=1096')">1096年</a>　在归善。苏过有《闻潮阳吴子野出家》诗。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《斜川集校注》卷一。此诗亦题苏轼作，见《苏轼诗集》卷四十七。其时吴复古（子野）并未出家。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1096&endYear=1096')">1096年</a>　在归善。夜雨之后，月色皎然，苏过作诗咏之。作品：《雨后见月》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《斜川集校注》卷一。）</span><div id='poem_522664' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_522664' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/522664?labeling=true' target='_blank'>雨后见月</a><span class='authorDate'>（1096年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31323, "北宋", "苏过", "poem_title_522664")'>苏过</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_522664_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_522664'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_522664'>薰风转亭午，流汗浃絺绤。<div id='poem_sentence_0_522664_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_522664'>隆隆空山雷，跨海飞雨黑。<div id='poem_sentence_1_522664_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_522664'>西家长苦贫，而有好颜色。<div id='poem_sentence_8_522664_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_522664'>终年饭半菽，爱酒无从得。<div id='poem_sentence_9_522664_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_522664'>嗟余不解饮，看尔时举白。<div id='poem_sentence_10_522664_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_522664'>岂不贤老兵，聊慰羁旅夕。<div id='poem_sentence_11_522664_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_522664'></div><div class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《斜川集校注》卷一。）</span><div id='poem_522682' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_522682' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/522682?labeling=true' id='poem_title_522731_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_522731'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_522731'>三年避地少经过，十日论诗喜琢磨。<div ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1097&endYear=1097')">1097年闰2月</a>　闰二月初，苏迈将两房大小到达惠州，来者有苏簟、苏符、苏籥，苏轼作诗咏之。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1097&endYear=1097')">1097年</a>　苏过为子籥、女德孙造佛像，苏轼作赞。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1097&endYear=1097')">1097年</a>　章惇以韶州与惠州地近，苏迈不当为仁化令，迈不得赴任。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1097&endYear=1097')">1097年闰2月</a>　闰二月，元祐党人再申贬斥，苏辙为化州别驾，安置于雷州；苏轼责授琼州别驾，移昌化军安置。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1097&endYear=1097')">1097年4月15日</a>　四月十五日，苏轼书《付过》一文，告以谨言慎行。又自画像，题“元祐罪人书以示过”八字。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1097&endYear=1097')">1097年</a>　四月十七日，责授文告传至惠州，十九日苏轼离惠州，苏过随行；苏迈留处惠州。<br /></div>

-----title
龙川
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='5da370f9e6bb4cb4a5e6b151f59c8827_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("5da370f9e6bb4cb4a5e6b151f59c8827");'><span id='5da370f9e6bb4cb4a5e6b151f59c8827_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1097&endYear=1097')">1097年</a>，26岁</div><div id='5da370f9e6bb4cb4a5e6b151f59c8827' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1097&endYear=1097')">1097年</a>　苏迈授仁化令，搬挈苏过一房来，苏轼遣过迎于循州。苏迨已由宜兴至许昌。<br /></div>
-----end

藤县

class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《斜川集校注》卷二。苏轼诗为《徐元用使君与其子端常邀仆与小儿过同游东山浮金堂戏作此诗》，见《苏轼诗集》卷四十四。）</span><div id='poem_522553' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_522553' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a id='poem_content_522553'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_522553'>滩声已悲秋，涧色犹藏春。<div id='poem_sentence_0_522553_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_522553_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_522553'>风松作鼓吹，迎送长江滨。<div id='poem_sentence_3_522553_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_522553'>尔来乘桴翁，归路物色新。<div id='poem_sentence_4_522553_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_522553'>高情寓箕颍，绝意登麒麟。<div id='poem_sentence_5_522553_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_522553'>三吴有负郭，𥝧稏秋盈囷。<div id='poem_sentence_6_522553_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_522553'>瘴茅喜欲脱，下泽还当巾。<div id='poem_sentence_7_522553_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_522553'>缥缈九疑行，此生定知津。<div id='poem_sentence_8_522553_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_522553'>故人傥见思，尺书凭素鳞。<div id='poem_sentence_9_522553_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_522553'></div><div id='poem_sentence_10_522553_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
雷州
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='8289e0564df64f3ea303502787316e59_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("8289e0564df64f3ea303502787316e59");'><span id='8289e0564df64f3ea303502787316e59_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1097&endYear=1097')">1097年</a>，26岁</div><div id='8289e0564df64f3ea303502787316e59' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1097&endYear=1097')">1097年6月5日</a>　五月十一日，苏轼、苏辙相遇于藤州。六月五日同至雷州。<br /></div>

-----title
徐闻
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='f2e150ef8adc4741a97cbdc462cd61aa_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("f2e150ef8adc4741a97cbdc462cd61aa");'><span id='f2e150ef8adc4741a97cbdc462cd61aa_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1097&endYear=1097')">1097年</a>，26岁</div><div id='f2e150ef8adc4741a97cbdc462cd61aa' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1097&endYear=1097')">1097年6月9日</a>　六月九日至徐闻渡，谒伏波祠，苏过作碑记。作品：《伏波将军庙碑》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《斜川集校注》卷七。）</span><div id='poem_1215277' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1215277' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1215277?labeling=true' target='_blank'>伏波将军庙碑<span class='inlineComment2'>（绍圣四年）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1097年6月9日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31323, "北宋", "苏过", "poem_title_1215277")'>苏过</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1215277_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1215277'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1215277'>功名与五福均，意其为造物者所吝也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1215277_comment'></div>富贵之视贫贱，寿考之方疾夭，固悬绝矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1215277_comment'></div>若夫建不朽之功名，铭之鼎彝，垂之竹帛，使百世之后，想见其遗风馀烈，则与夫没世无闻者，盖不可同年而语矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1215277_comment'></div>得不为造物者所吝乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1215277_comment'></div>虽然，圣人罕言命，以为言命则人事废矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1215277_comment'></div>然有不得不疑于造物者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1215277_comment'></div>汉武帝之喜功，而李广卒不封侯；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1215277_comment'></div>光武之好士，而伏波竟以谗死。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1215277_comment'></div>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1215277_comment'></div>伏波亦长于虑患，而智于出师矣，而壶头一衄，谗人遂入其说，人主一信而不回，岂非命也夫！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1215277_comment'></div>始其策公孙述、隗嚣之必败，南征百粤，指挥而定，岂其智于昔，而愚于今耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1215277_comment'></div>武陵之役，壶头路近而水险，若道于充则路夷而运远。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1215277_comment'></div>夫费日运粮，敌必有备，孰若提必死之士，扼其咽喉，所谓疾雷不及掩耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1215277_comment'></div>此邓艾用以破蜀，李靖所以平江陵也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1215277_comment'></div>使伏波士卒不病，则战有馀矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1215277_comment'></div>而耿舒乃谓不从其言致败！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1215277_comment'></div>夫事固有幸不幸耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1215277_comment'></div>田千秋一言取丞相，卫青平匈奴而致位大将军。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1215277_comment'></div>其智安在？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1215277_comment'></div>故豪杰之士，则庸夫得以藉口，而自信其说。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1215277_comment'></div>岂不悲哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1215277_comment'></div>且从光武定天下，功臣莫不有封，而伏波独以谗夺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1215277_comment'></div>至永平图形灵台，而伏波乃以椒房之故不与。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1215277_comment'></div>是命也夫？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1215277_comment'></div>仆侍亲南迁，踰五岭，将涉大海，过将军祠下，哀将军之身，见诬于千载之上，而叹将军之泽，不斩于百世之后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1215277_comment'></div>岂彼造物者能困其人，而不能困其功名也耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1215277_comment'></div>谨拜手稽首，献其词曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_26_1215277'>维百粤之险阻兮，右渤海而左五岭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1215277_comment'></div>洞庭居其肘腋兮，九疑跨其襟领。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1215277_comment'></div>日翳翳其无光兮，谷幽幽其如井。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1215277_comment'></div>烝毒雾之四塞兮，虽六师其安骋？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1215277_comment'></div>故尉佗之陆梁兮，建黄屋而外屏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1215277_comment'></div>薄苍梧之舜野兮，内啸聚夫不逞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1215277_comment'></div>属孝武之明灵兮，赫王怒之谁梗？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1215277_comment'></div>问将军之安在兮？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1215277_comment'></div>敢有爱其遗境。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1215277_comment'></div>嗟粤人之喜乱兮，每觇吾之不警。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1215277_comment'></div>彼徵氏之狂狡兮，民欲殒于陷阱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1215277_comment'></div>虽不足以辱王师兮，非仁者其谁靖？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1215277_comment'></div>下凌波之楼船兮，惊绝俗之气禀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1215277_comment'></div>势破竹之无几兮，倏迎刃而自定。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1215277_comment'></div>歼渠魁以惩慝兮，释俘囚而伸儆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1215277_comment'></div>布天子之德泽兮，舍盟书而胥命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1215277_comment'></div>誓马革以裹尸兮，敢鸢飞而告病。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1215277_comment'></div>何薏苡之兴谗兮，抱孤忠而不见省。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1215277_comment'></div>昔乐毅之去燕兮，遭孱主之听莹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1215277_comment'></div>悲将军之谁咎兮，死青蝇于主圣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1215277_comment'></div>眷朱勃之何人兮，蹈栾布之前鼎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1215277_comment'></div>虽不能已雷霆之怒兮，亦少慰夫未暝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1215277_comment'></div>仰嘉名于千载兮，伤吾道之不竞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1215277_comment'></div>功未录而罪及兮，掩大德于一眚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1215277_comment'></div>维鴂舌之何知兮，独忠义之所敬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1215277_comment'></div>走千里之粢盛兮，恃德刑于邪正。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1215277_comment'></div>使斯民畏罪而不欺兮，犹将军之威令。</div><div id='poem_sentence_52_1215277_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1097&endYear=1097')">1097年6月11日</a>　六月十一日，与叔父辙相别，苏过与父渡海到海南。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='ff8b8c6454d34ff1bdd5f6eb00689459_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("ff8b8c6454d34ff1bdd5f6eb00689459");'><span id='ff8b8c6454d34ff1bdd5f6eb00689459_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1100&endYear=1100')">1100年</a>，29岁</div><div id='ff8b8c6454d34ff1bdd5f6eb00689459' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1100&endYear=1100')">1100年6月</a>　六月底，苏过与父至海康适合浦，水涨遇险。<br /></div>
-----end



-----title
儋州
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='6be04dda57e64461ab4dcb18570a9679_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("6be04dda57e64461ab4dcb18570a9679");'><span id='6be04dda57e64461ab4dcb18570a9679_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1097&endYear=1100')">1097-1100年</a>，26-29岁</div><div id='6be04dda57e64461ab4dcb18570a9679' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1097&endYear=1097')">1097年7月2日</a>　七月二日，到达昌化军贬所。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1097&endYear=1097')">1097年9月</a>　在宜伦。九月，苏过以椰子冠寄赠叔父辙，并作诗，父、叔皆有和。作品：《椰子冠》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《斜川集校注》卷二。苏辙和诗为《过侄寄椰冠》，见《栾城集·栾城后集》卷二；苏轼和诗为《次韵子由三首·椰子冠》，见《苏轼诗集》卷四十一。）</span><div id='poem_522733' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_522733' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/522733?labeling=true' target='_blank'>椰子冠</a><span class='authorDate'>（1097年9月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: id='poem_content_522733'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_522733'>玉佩犀簪暗网丝，黄冠今习野人仪。<div id='poem_sentence_0_522733_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_522733'>著书岂独穷周<span class='inlineComment2'>（原校：一作庄）</span>叟，说偈还应见祖师。<div id='poem_sentence_1_522733_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_522733'>棕子偶从遗物得，竹皮同使后人知。<div id='poem_sentence_2_522733_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_522733'>平生冠冕非吾意，不为飞鸢跕堕时。<div id='poem_sentence_3_522733_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_522733'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_522733_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1097&endYear=1097')">1097年</a>　在宜伦。叔父作《寓居二首》，咏《东亭》、《东楼》，苏过与父俱有和诗。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《斜川集校注》卷二。苏过《东楼》诗似佚。苏辙《寓居二首》，见《栾城集·栾城后集》卷二；苏轼和诗为《次韵子由三首·东亭》、《次韵子由三首·东楼》，见《苏轼诗集》卷四十一。）</span><div id='poem_522732' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_522732' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/522732?labeling=true' target='_blank'>东亭</a><span class='authorDate'>（1097年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31323, "北宋", "苏过", "poem_title_522732")'>苏过</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_522732_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_522732'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_522732'>闭眼黄庭万想归，此心久已息纷驰。<div id='poem_sentence_0_522732_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_522732'>幽居正喜门罗雀，晨起何妨笏拄颐。<div id='poem_sentence_1_522732_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_522732'>自信丹田足梨枣，不忧瘴雨滞茅茨。<div id='poem_sentence_2_522732_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_522732'>三山咫尺承明远，世路榛芜谁与披。<div id='poem_sentence_3_522732_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_522732'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_522732_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1097&endYear=1097')">1097年</a>　在宜伦。叔父辙居所月季，伐而复生，与苏远作诗，苏过与父皆有次韵。作品：《次韵叔父月季再生》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《斜川集校注》卷二。苏辙所作为《所寓堂后月季再生与远同赋》，见《栾城集·栾城后集》卷二；苏轼次韵诗为《次韵子由月季花再生》，见《苏轼诗集》卷四十一；苏远诗佚。）</span><div id='poem_522839' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_522839' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/522839?labeling=true' target='_blank'>次韵叔父月季再生</a><span class='authorDate'>（1097年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31323, "北宋", "苏过", "poem_title_522839")'>苏过</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_522839_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_522839'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_522839'>瘴海不知秋，幽人忘岁月。<div id='poem_sentence_0_522839_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_522839'>祇记庭中花，几度开还蘖。<div id='poem_sentence_1_522839_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_522839'>忆昔移居时，始是青荑茁。<div id='poem_sentence_2_522839_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_522839'>殷勤主人惠，浸灌寒泉冽。<div id='poem_sentence_3_522839_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_522839'>颜色日鲜好，条枝争秀拔。<div id='poem_sentence_4_522839_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_522839'>意无后人剪，喜托先生苃。<div id='poem_sentence_5_522839_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_522839'>海康接儋耳，云水何田蹑。<div id='poem_sentence_6_522839_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_522839'>俯楹独四顾，怅此波涛匝。<div id='poem_sentence_7_522839_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_522839'>闻道海门松，僵枝出繁叶。<div id='poem_sentence_8_522839_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_522839'>困穷不足道，喜有千人活。<div id='poem_sentence_9_522839_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_522839'>不似玄都花，蔌蔌那容折。<div id='poem_sentence_10_522839_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_522839'></div><div id='poem_sentence_11_522839_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1097&endYear=1097')">1097年12月19日</a>　在宜伦。十二月十九日，苏过作诗祝父生日。作品：《大人生日》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《斜川集校注》卷二。《斜川集校注》有《大人生日》同题诗三首，此为其中之一，首句为“勿惊髀减带围宽”）</span><div id='poem_522738' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_522738' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/522738?labeling=true' target='_blank'>大人生日<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其五 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1097年12月19日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31323, "北宋", "苏过", "poem_title_522738")'>苏过</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_522738_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_522738'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_522738'>勿惊髀减带围带，寿骨巉然正隐颧。<div id='poem_sentence_0_522738_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_522738'>不待期颐祝难老，固知穮蓘自丰年。<div id='poem_sentence_1_522738_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_522738'>僵松再蔚千龄叶，眢井新飞百尺泉。<div id='poem_sentence_2_522738_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_522738'>坐想山神无伎俩，却应造物报其天。<div id='poem_sentence_3_522738_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_522738'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_522738_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1097&endYear=1097')">1097年</a>　在宜伦。冬，苏过作诗怀诸兄弟，以状海南贬居之艰况。作品：《冬夜怀诸兄弟》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《斜川集校注》卷二。）</span><div id='poem_522552' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_522552' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/522552?labeling=true' target='_blank'>冬夜怀诸兄弟</a><span class='authorDate'>（1097年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31323, "北宋", "苏过", "poem_title_522552")'>苏过</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_522552_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_522552'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_522552'>霜风连日恶，霜月连夜苦。<div id='poem_sentence_0_522552_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_522552'>青灯寒无光，翳翳昏复吐。<div id='poem_sentence_1_522552_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_522552'>念我手足爱，相望若秦楚。<div id='poem_sentence_2_522552_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_522552'>两兄寄阳羡，耕稼事农圃。<div id='poem_sentence_3_522552_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_522552'>箪瓢有馀乐，菽水未为窭。<div id='poem_sentence_4_522552_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_522552'>两兄客颍川，耿耿怀去鲁。<div id='poem_sentence_5_522552_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_522552'>近闻营菟裘，稍亦葺环堵。<div id='poem_sentence_6_522552_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_522552'>有弟虽咫尺，相逢犹龃龉。<div id='poem_sentence_7_522552_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_522552'>黄湾隔小海，孤岭度大庾。<div id='poem_sentence_8_522552_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_522552'>今年厄陈蔡，夫子嗟兕虎。<div id='poem_sentence_9_522552_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_522552'>惟我二兄弟，颇亦尝险阻。<div id='poem_sentence_10_522552_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_522552'>忆昔居大梁，共结慈明侣。<div id='poem_sentence_11_522552_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_522552'>晨窗惟六人，夜榻到三鼓。<div id='poem_sentence_12_522552_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_522552'>岂知聚散事，翻手如云雨。<div id='poem_sentence_13_522552_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_522552'>我今处海南，日与渔樵伍。<div id='poem_sentence_14_522552_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_522552'>黄茅蔽涧谷，白雾<span class='inlineComment2'>（赵本作露）</span>昏庭宇。<div id='poem_sentence_15_522552_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_522552'>风高翔鸱枭，月黑号鼯鼠。<div id='poem_sentence_16_522552_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_522552'>舟居杂蛮蜑，卉服半夷虏。<div id='poem_sentence_17_522552_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_522552'>下床但药饵，遣瘴烦樽俎。<div id='poem_sentence_18_522552_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_19_522552'>何须鸢堕时，方念平生语。<div id='poem_sentence_19_522552_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_20_522552'></div><div id='poem_sentence_20_522552_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1098&endYear=1098')">1098年1月15日</a>　正月十五日，苏过赴儋州守张中宴。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1098&endYear=1098')">1098年1月23日</a>　一月二十三日，苏轼书陶渊明形、影、神诗付苏过，并和其韵。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1098&endYear=1098')">1098年</a>　儋守张中常与苏过对弈，轼旁观不以为疲。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1098&endYear=1098')">1098年</a>　在宜伦。叔父辙浴罢，作诗，苏过与父皆和。作品：《次韵叔父<浴罢>》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《斜川集校注》卷二。苏辙所作为《浴罢》，见《栾城集·栾城后集》卷二；苏轼和诗为《次韵子由<浴罢>》，见《苏轼诗集》卷四十二。）</span><div id='poem_522549' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_522549' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/522549?labeling=true' target='_blank'>次韵叔父俗罢</a><span class='authorDate'>（1098年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31323, "北宋", "苏过", "poem_title_522549")'>苏过</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_522549_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_522549'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_522549'>黄门昔万机，下士勤握沐。<div id='poem_sentence_0_522549_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_522549'>今已与世疏，雅志追沂浴。<div id='poem_sentence_1_522549_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_522549'>丹田有宿火，如比阳来复。<div id='poem_sentence_2_522549_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_522549'>辘轳自转水，离坎俱实腹。<div id='poem_sentence_3_522549_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_522549'>谪居使事乏，惟喜薪水足。<div id='poem_sentence_4_522549_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_522549'>时濯西风尘，一寓归鸿目。<div id='poem_sentence_5_522549_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_522549'>勿惊髀肉少，衣褐真怀玉。<div id='poem_sentence_6_522549_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_522549'>明镜虽无垢，新苗良待沃。<div id='poem_sentence_7_522549_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_522549'>雨馀餐岩岫，露重膏松竹。<div id='poem_sentence_8_522549_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_522549'>更观云入山，心与境同熟<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_9_522549_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_522549'>珍重耆城言，妙解何须读。<div id='poem_sentence_10_522549_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_522549'>洁香非外求，清净常返瞩。<div id='poem_sentence_11_522549_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_522549'>物初信可游，傥来非所卜。<div id='poem_sentence_12_522549_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_522549'>益师庄叟言，养生贵缘督。<div id='poem_sentence_13_522549_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_522549'></div><div id='poem_sentence_14_522549_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_522549'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_9_522549_0'>⑴ 自注：道书如雨初晴云入山林之语。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_522549_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1098&endYear=1098')">1098年</a>　在宜伦。杭僧参寥子作诗怀苏迈、苏迨，迈、迨和之，苏过亦次韵。作品：《次韵伯达仲豫二兄和参寥子》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《斜川集校注》卷二。僧道潜诗为《重居夜坐怀苏伯达昆仲》，见《参寥子诗集》卷八。）</span><div id='poem_522702' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_522702' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/522702?labeling=true' target='_blank'>次韵伯达仲豫二兄和参寥子</a><span class='authorDate'>（1098年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31323, "北宋", "苏过", "poem_title_522702")'>苏过</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_522702_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_522702'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_522702'>罗浮插天猿昼号，飞步包顶观云涛。<div id='poem_sentence_0_522702_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_522702'>庶几神药两童赐，日暮空叹西山高。<div id='poem_sentence_1_522702_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_522702'>道人航海曾何劳，久将身世轻鸿毛。<div id='poem_sentence_2_522702_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_522702'>只恐西湖六桥月，无人主此诗与骚。<div id='poem_sentence_3_522702_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_522702'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_522702_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1098&endYear=1098')">1098年</a>　苏过于海泊得长兄寄书，作诗，父轼、叔辙皆和。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1098&endYear=1098')">1098年4月</a>　四月，苏过与父被广西察访使董必所遣小使逐出官房，遂卜居城南污池旁桄榔林下。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1098&endYear=1098')">1098年</a>　在宜伦。有客自颍川来，勉苏过以功名进取，过作《志隐》以述志。苏轼览而嘉之，欲作《广志隐》以极其思。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此赋见《斜川集校注》卷七。）</span><div id='poem_1215219' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1215219' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1215219?labeling=true' target='_blank'>志隐赋</a><span class='authorDate'>（元符元年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31323, "北宋", "苏过", "poem_title_1215219")'>苏过</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1215219_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1215219'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1215219'>苏子居岛夷之二年，客有自许来唁，问其安否，而勉之进取。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1215219_comment'></div>曰：「天之生物，类聚群分。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1215219_comment'></div>蠢动飞走，不相夺伦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1215219_comment'></div>鱼宅于渊，兽伏于榛；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1215219_comment'></div>蚕之于冰，鼠之于焚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1215219_comment'></div>失其所则病，因其性则存。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1215219_comment'></div>且非独虫鱼然也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1215219_comment'></div>楚之橘柚不植于燕代，晋之枣栗不繁于闽越。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1215219_comment'></div>非天地之所私，繄物性之南北。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1215219_comment'></div>况于人乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1215219_comment'></div>余蜀人也，少游三晋之间矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1215219_comment'></div>秋冬之交，朔风萧条。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1215219_comment'></div>山童泽枯，堕指折胶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1215219_comment'></div>阴山之雪，三岁不消。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1215219_comment'></div>故其生实瘠而不窳，畜驷强而不乾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1215219_comment'></div>人亦刚而多勇，寿而硕坚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1215219_comment'></div>肤拆面殷，足胝手胼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1215219_comment'></div>为霜雪之所凝，凛其质之岁寒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1215219_comment'></div>而五岭之南，夷獠杂居。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1215219_comment'></div>天卑地溽，山盘水纡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1215219_comment'></div>恶溪肆流，毒雾蒸嘘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1215219_comment'></div>昼避蝮虺，夜号鼪鼯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1215219_comment'></div>草木冬花，霖潦长濡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1215219_comment'></div>星隐于气，日见于晡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1215219_comment'></div>故其民多重膇之病，寒热中肤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1215219_comment'></div>非耋而伛，非躄而扶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1215219_comment'></div>而儋耳者，又在二广之南，南溟之中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1215219_comment'></div>其民卉服鼻饮，语言不通。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1215219_comment'></div>状若禽兽，既嚚且聋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1215219_comment'></div>海气郁雺，瘴烟溟濛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1215219_comment'></div>而子安之，岂亦有道乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1215219_comment'></div>且夫君子之修身也，病没世而无闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1215219_comment'></div>故其蹑屩而取卿相，脱挽辂而□封君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1215219_comment'></div>季子从成而得印，范叔计行而专秦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1215219_comment'></div>相如进缶而赵重，毛遂奉盘而楚亲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1215219_comment'></div>或刀笔以自奋，或干戈以策勋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1215219_comment'></div>脱颖者富贵，陆沈者贱贫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1215219_comment'></div>希揄扬于鼎彝，耻湮没于埃尘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1215219_comment'></div>古人有言：『岁云暮矣，时不我与』。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1215219_comment'></div>如子之年，鸣钟鼎食者多矣，曷亦有意于世乎」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1215219_comment'></div>苏子曰：「噫！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1215219_comment'></div>若客，殆未达者耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1215219_comment'></div>大块之间，有生同之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1215219_comment'></div>喜怒哀乐，钜细不遗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1215219_comment'></div>蚁蜂之君臣，蛮触之雄雌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1215219_comment'></div>以我观之，物何足疑？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1215219_comment'></div>彭聃以寒暑为朝暮，蟪蛄以春秋为期颐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1215219_comment'></div>孰寿孰夭，孰欣孰悲？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1215219_comment'></div>况吾与子，好恶性习，一致同归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1215219_comment'></div>寓此世间，美恶几希。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1215219_comment'></div>乃欲夸三晋而陋百粤，弃远俗而鄙岛夷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1215219_comment'></div>窃为子不取也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1215219_comment'></div>子知鱼之安于水也，而鱼何择夫河汉之与江湖？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1215219_comment'></div>知兽之安于薮也，而兽何择于云梦之与孟诸？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1215219_comment'></div>松柏之后彫，萑苇之易枯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1215219_comment'></div>乃物性之自然，岂土地之能殊？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1215219_comment'></div>子乃以晋楚之产疑之，过矣！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1215219_comment'></div>虽然，瘴厉之地，子得其详也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1215219_comment'></div>仆亦择其可道者，以释子之惑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1215219_comment'></div>天地之气，冬夏一律。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1215219_comment'></div>物不凋瘁，生意靡息。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1215219_comment'></div>冬絺夏葛，稻岁再熟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1215219_comment'></div>富者寡求，贫者易足。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1215219_comment'></div>绩蕊为衣，蓺根为粮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1215219_comment'></div>铸山煮海，国以富强。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1215219_comment'></div>犀象珠玉，走于四方。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1215219_comment'></div>士独免于战争，民独勉于农桑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1215219_comment'></div>其山川则清远而秀绝，陵谷则缥缈而岪郁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1215219_comment'></div>虽龙蛇之委藏，亦神仙之所宅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1215219_comment'></div>吾盖乐游而忘返，岂特暖席之与黔突也哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1215219_comment'></div>若夫纡朱怀金，肥马轻车，固人情之所欲得也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1215219_comment'></div>而况金石之传，不朽之荣，为主上布德泽于斯民，拊四夷而宾不庭，固非独善其身，老死丘壑者所得拟也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1215219_comment'></div>然功高则身危，名重则谤生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1215219_comment'></div>枉寻者见容，方枘者必憎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1215219_comment'></div>而自古豪杰之士，有不能闾阎之穷，慨然有澄清之志，探虎穴，索骊珠，而得全者，盖无一二也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1215219_comment'></div>彼大人者，窅然观之，颦蹙远引，况以荣为乐耶！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1215219_comment'></div>世非不知得士者昌，失士者危。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1215219_comment'></div>然患难或可以共处，安逸或可以长辞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1215219_comment'></div>子胥不免于属镂，范蠡得计于鸱夷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1215219_comment'></div>萧何缧囚于患失，留侯脱屣于先知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1215219_comment'></div>敌国亡而信烹，刘氏安而勃疑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1215219_comment'></div>故介推避禄于绵田，鲁连辞赏于燕师。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1215219_comment'></div>接舆长歌于凤鸟，庄叟感慨于郊牺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1215219_comment'></div>仆无过人之才，固不足以自媒也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1215219_comment'></div>然马之羁靮，鹰之鞲绁，寒心久矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1215219_comment'></div>方长鸣于冀北，睹皂栈而知惧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1215219_comment'></div>击鲜肥于秋风，又何脔割之足顾哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1215219_comment'></div>盖尝闻养生之粗也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1215219_comment'></div>今置身于遐荒，如有物之初。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1215219_comment'></div>余逃空谷之寂寥，眷此世而愈疏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1215219_comment'></div>追赤松于渺茫，想神仙于有无。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1215219_comment'></div>此天下之至乐也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1215219_comment'></div>而子期我以世人，污我于泥涂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1215219_comment'></div>贪千仞之鷇，轻隋侯之珠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1215219_comment'></div>子以为巧，我知其愚」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1215219_comment'></div>客愧且叹曰：「吾浅之为丈夫也」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1215219_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_96_1215219'>昔余侍先君子居儋耳，丁年而往，二毛而归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1215219_comment'></div>盖尝筑室有终焉之志。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1215219_comment'></div>遂赋《志隐》一篇，效昔人《解嘲》、《宾戏》之类。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_98_1215219_comment'></div>将以混得丧，忘羁旅，非特以自广，且以为老人之娱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_99_1215219_comment'></div>先君子览之，欣然嘉焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_100_1215219_comment'></div>逮今二十年矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_101_1215219_comment'></div>政和丙申来颍水，偶发书箧，得旧稿，怅然感叹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_102_1215219_comment'></div>小儿籥在总角时，逮事先君子者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_103_1215219_comment'></div>惜此篇久亡而今存，请书其事而藏之，庶几不忘在莒云耳。</div><div id='poem_sentence_104_1215219_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1098&endYear=1098')">1098年6月</a>　在宜伦。六月，改元元符，苏过代人作《元符改元奉敕告祭文》两通。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《斜川集校注》卷七。《斜川集校注》有《元符改元奉敕告祭文》同题文二篇，此为其中一篇，首句为“主上钦崇天道”）</span>《元符改元奉敕告祭文》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《斜川集校注》卷七。《斜川集校注》有《元符改元奉敕告祭文》同题文二篇，此为其中一篇，首句为“恭惟国家”）</span><div </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1098年6月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31323, "北宋", "苏过", class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1215286'>主上钦崇天道，敷佑下民；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1215286_comment'></div>躬荐徽称，以严上帝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1215286_comment'></div>濡鸿恩于率土，称元祀于百神。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1215286_comment'></div>乃眷明灵，实参化育。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1215286_comment'></div>名纪载籍，功冒黎元。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1215286_comment'></div>冀昭鉴于德音，益道迎于和气。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1215286_comment'></div>均播厥福，永孚于休。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1215286_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_7_1215286_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1215287' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1215287' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1215287?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1098年6月）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1215287_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1215287'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1215287'>恭惟国家享自天之佑，元日受定命之符。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1215287_comment'></div>眷卜世于万年，霈鸿恩于九有。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1215287_comment'></div>遵依诏旨，并走群祠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1215287_comment'></div>凡有功于斯民，咸称秩于元祀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1215287_comment'></div>神其昭鉴，永孚于休。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1215287_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_5_1215287_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1098&endYear=1098')">1098年</a>　苏辙再贬循州，将家过惠州，留家小于惠，与苏迈同住于白鹤峰新居。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1098&endYear=1098')">1098年</a>　在宜伦。苏过与父既居城南，海南土人夜猎，以肉馈之。过作诗记其事。作品：《夜猎行》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《斜川集校注》卷二。）</span><div id='poem_522676' class='_poem'><div /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_522676_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_522676'><div class='poemSentence' href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1098&endYear=1098')">1098年12月19日</a>　在宜伦。十二月十九日，苏轼生日，苏过作诗为庆。作品：《大人生日》（其一）<span id='poem_sentence_1_522834_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_522834'>欲救微言绝，先惩百氏纷。<div id='poem_sentence_2_522834_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_522834_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_522834'>吾庸亦多矣，奚恤彼狺狺。<div id='poem_sentence_5_522834_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_title_522835_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_522835'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_522835'>天定人难胜，诚哉申子言。<div id='poem_sentence_0_522835_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_522835'>不须占倚伏，久已恃乾坤。<div id='poem_sentence_1_522835_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_522835_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_522736' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_522736' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/522736?labeling=true' id='poem_sentence_4_522736'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_522736_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1098&endYear=1098')">1098年</a>　在宜伦。苏过与父于南海，常与人借书，日以读书、著作为乐，过有《借书》诗一篇。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《斜川集校注》卷二。）</span><div id='poem_522840' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_522840' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/522840?labeling=true' target='_blank'>借书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1098年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31323, "北宋", "苏过", "poem_title_522840")'>苏过</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_522840_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_522840'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_522840'>妙年不可再，白日谁能系。<div id='poem_sentence_0_522840_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_522840'>空惭粱肉索，不悟齿发逝。<div id='poem_sentence_1_522840_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_522840'>季子颇亦困，还家笑奴隶。<div id='poem_sentence_2_522840_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_522840'>经年得揣摩，尚可资游说。<div id='poem_sentence_3_522840_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_522840'>良田初不耕，拱手那望岁。<div id='poem_sentence_4_522840_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_522840'>谁令困不学，斯与草木弊。<div id='poem_sentence_5_522840_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_522840'>海南寡书籍，蠹简仅编缀。<div id='poem_sentence_6_522840_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_522840'>诗亡不见雅，易绝空馀系。<div id='poem_sentence_7_522840_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_522840'>借书如假田，主以岁月计。<div id='poem_sentence_8_522840_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_522840'>常恐遗地力，敢有不敛穧。<div
