id='poem_sentence_12_522840_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1098&endYear=1098')">1098年</a>　在宜伦。苏过手抄《唐书》和《前汉书》。数篇文章与之有关，或作于此期。作品：《书<田布传>后》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《斜川集校注》卷七。此文具体作时不详，姑系于此。）</span>《书<周亚夫传>后》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《斜川集校注》卷七。此文具体作时不详，姑系于此。）</span>《萧何论》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《斜川集校注》卷七。此文具体作时不详，姑系于此。）</span>《记交趾进异兽状》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《斜川集校注》卷七。此文具体作时不详，姑系于此。）</span>《书二李传后》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《斜川集校注》卷七。此文具体作时不详，姑系于此。）</span>《读<楚语>》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《斜川集校注》卷七。此文具体作时不详，姑系于此。）</span>《书<张骞传>后》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《斜川集校注》卷八。此文具体作时不详，姑系于此。）</span>《东交门箴》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《斜川集校注》卷八。此文具体作时不详，姑系于此。）</span><div id='poem_1215257' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1215257' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1215257?labeling=true' target='_blank'>书田布传后</a><span class='authorDate'>（1098年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31323, "北宋", "苏过", "poem_title_1215257")'>苏过</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1215257_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1215257'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1215257'>魏人德田弘正而爱布。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1215257_comment'></div>弘正遇害于镇也，穆宗授布魏博，使讨贼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1215257_comment'></div>而度支饷不继，牙将史宪诚者，因是以怒众。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1215257_comment'></div>众不肯战，曰：「公能行河朔旧事，则生死从公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1215257_comment'></div>不然，不可以战」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1215257_comment'></div>布叹曰：「功不成矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1215257_comment'></div>即为书谢帝曰：「臣观众意，终且负国」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1215257_comment'></div>引刀刺心于几筵，曰：「上以谢君父，下以示三军」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1215257_comment'></div>余读至此，流涕太息，曰：「呜呼哀哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1215257_comment'></div>布能不爱死而不知死所也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1215257_comment'></div>乌喙能杀人，亦能起死者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1215257_comment'></div>今有人寝疾将死，食乌喙而得生者十人而一，不食而死者皆是也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1215257_comment'></div>夫畏乌喙而待尽，岂若庶几于十一者耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1215257_comment'></div>余为儿童时，见长老先生言：淳化中，成都戍卒王钧叛，杀尹据城，将剽诸郡，而蜀之戍卒将与之合。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1215257_comment'></div>蜀守杨怀忠者知之，大会将校，出其二息，辞于众曰：「贼有成都，必窥诸郡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1215257_comment'></div>蜀小而近，必首被兵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1215257_comment'></div>吾当死之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1215257_comment'></div>两稚子不可以污贼，请乘其未至，假手于君等杀之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1215257_comment'></div>然后持吾首归贼，则室家完而身且富贵」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1215257_comment'></div>众泣曰：「吾属独无父母妻子乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1215257_comment'></div>主亡而吾存，赤吾族矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1215257_comment'></div>公独欲为忠臣，使他人为反虏耶」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1215257_comment'></div>怀忠曰：「若然，奈何」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1215257_comment'></div>皆曰：「生死从公」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1215257_comment'></div>于是散府库，发民财，得兵千人，出城一舍伏之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1215257_comment'></div>是暮，贼憩伏所，期以旦攻城。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1215257_comment'></div>士方食，伏起歼之，遂远引兵，壁成都，贼气慑，不敢出累月。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1215257_comment'></div>王师至而贼平，怀忠之力也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1215257_comment'></div>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1215257_comment'></div>惜布不知出此也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1215257_comment'></div>此岂非食乌喙而生者耶！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1215257_comment'></div>何则？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1215257_comment'></div>先人有夺人之心，而反侧者易以义使也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1215257_comment'></div>且布之贵也，本以弘正有恩于魏，使世其官，可以成功耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1215257_comment'></div>魏人以河朔旧事逼之，岂遽有害之之意哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1215257_comment'></div>布若能请于军，曰：「先将军以六州归天子，使汝一方不陷于叛逆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1215257_comment'></div>宣慰之言在耳，今几日而忘之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1215257_comment'></div>布不能从诸君为乱，上负君父，下惧祸不旋踵，以取笑天下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1215257_comment'></div>愿诸君杀布而后反」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1215257_comment'></div>则魏人素德其父，未忍杀其子也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1215257_comment'></div>岂不忠义之两全哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1215257_comment'></div>昔弘正遣布以兵助讨蔡，帝议使人代之，而士卒爱布，愿留，乃止。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1215257_comment'></div>则布亦素有德于魏人也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1215257_comment'></div>其时布部曲必有在者，此辈岂肯从乱哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1215257_comment'></div>郭子仪恩结回纥，而保其不以刃相向。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1215257_comment'></div>夷狄犹能尔，而况父子有恩于魏乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1215257_comment'></div>若以忠义激之，祸福动之，戮一宪诚，军自定矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1215257_comment'></div>然后举兵讨镇，雪弘正之冤，刷朝廷之耻，克融势孤，不戮而擒矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1215257_comment'></div>岂非再造河朔之功乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1215257_comment'></div>万有一死宪诚之手，使朝廷以杀帅之罪讨于魏人，众所嫉恶而弃之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1215257_comment'></div>岂不贤于自经沟渎之为谅哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1215257_comment'></div>惜乎不能已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1215257_comment'></div>河北之再乱者，布之死也。</div><div id='poem_sentence_52_1215257_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1215255' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1215255' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1215255?labeling=true' target='_blank'>书周亚夫传后</a><span class='authorDate'>（1098年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31323, "北宋", "苏过", "poem_title_1215255")'>苏过</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1215255_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1215255'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1215255'>曾子曰：「可以托六尺之孤，可以寄百里之命，临大节而不夺」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1215255_comment'></div>君子之学，亦志于斯而已矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1215255_comment'></div>阅古今而不知成败，见小节而闇于大道，虽学足以通天人，智足以周事物，吾不知其人也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1215255_comment'></div>祸福莫大于死生，利害莫大于安危。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1215255_comment'></div>人能轻千金之躯，以任天下之重，祸福不惧，死生不易，虽曰未学，吾必谓之学矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1215255_comment'></div>天下无事，虽腐儒小生弄刀笔有馀；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1215255_comment'></div>事出意外，又能究其本心、而不失其素志者，寡矣！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1215255_comment'></div>晁错号称「智囊」，本造六国之谋，知吴必反者，宜其遭变而不动，慨然以身任之，乃反以危事委人主，而自处于万全。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1215255_comment'></div>此其智已乱矣！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1215255_comment'></div>错犹若此，而况其下者乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1215255_comment'></div>吾观周亚夫之将也，可谓安静有守而不动者矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1215255_comment'></div>梁孝王日夜请救，而亚夫卒坚壁不出；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1215255_comment'></div>军夜惊，相攻至帐下，而亚夫卒坚卧不起。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1215255_comment'></div>夫不救梁，不过梁亡而诛耳，而汉无可几之道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1215255_comment'></div>军夜惊不起，不过匕首窃发，而军无可乘之隙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1215255_comment'></div>以死生而易安危，亦可谓任重而道远矣！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1215255_comment'></div>至于谏临江之废，拒王信之封，所谓严嫡庶之分；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1215255_comment'></div>守高祖之约，可谓真宰相矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1215255_comment'></div>而太史公独称其用兵而不取其守节，曰：「足智而不学，守节而不逊，卒以穷困」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1215255_comment'></div>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1215255_comment'></div>此为景帝讳也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1215255_comment'></div>景帝不道，至于杀无罪元勋之臣，太史公不能直书其恶，乃讥亚夫之短，以为自取者，可为流涕太息也！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1215255_comment'></div>亚夫之不学，岂其似绛侯厚重少文耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1215255_comment'></div>刘氏微其父子，几亡矣！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1215255_comment'></div>何不学之有哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1215255_comment'></div>亚夫之不逊，岂其以面折廷争，而为庸主所不堪耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1215255_comment'></div>鬻拳惧君以兵，君子犹能与之，而守节者安得以不逊罪之哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1215255_comment'></div>孔子曰：「仁者必有勇」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1215255_comment'></div>勇盖仁者之馀事也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1215255_comment'></div>亚夫独以兵见称，岂不遗其大而录其细耶？</div><div id='poem_sentence_29_1215255_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1215268' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1215268' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1215268?labeling=true' target='_blank'>萧何论</a><span class='authorDate'>（1098年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31323, "北宋", "苏过", "poem_title_1215268")'>苏过</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1215268_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1215268'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1215268'>论曰：萧何请上林苑以与民，高祖大怒而械系之廷尉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1215268_comment'></div>高祖疑其受贾人之金乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1215268_comment'></div>曰：非也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1215268_comment'></div>使真受贾人之金，亦不责也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1215268_comment'></div>陈平请金四万斤，以间疏楚君臣，未尝问其出入，乃疑相国以私乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1215268_comment'></div>萧何强贱买关中田宅以自污，上心乃安，又何责其受金也哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1215268_comment'></div>然则何怒之遽也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1215268_comment'></div>曰：久矣，高祖之欲为此系也！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1215268_comment'></div>其为子孙谋也深矣！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1215268_comment'></div>卢绾与之同里闬，生亦同时，少长相狎，群臣莫与为比。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1215268_comment'></div>然一旦之燕，则以反闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1215268_comment'></div>是群臣举不可信矣！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1215268_comment'></div>而萧何居可疑之地，有可疑之势，特未反耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1215268_comment'></div>其镇抚关中十有馀年，恩德洽于百姓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1215268_comment'></div>而高祖连岁在外，关中之民，知有何而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1215268_comment'></div>缚淮阴如婴儿，脱吕后、孝惠于危死，其智力岂小小哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1215268_comment'></div>帝百岁后，母老子少，得安枕而卧乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1215268_comment'></div>高祖盖以是卜也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1215268_comment'></div>曰：「卜何之反乎」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1215268_comment'></div>何安敢反也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1215268_comment'></div>卜之于是民耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1215268_comment'></div>请苑而不许，又械系之，民德何而怒我也必也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1215268_comment'></div>若匈匈有动摇之情，是刘氏之泽不逮也，得不为子孙之谋哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1215268_comment'></div>故曰：「欲令百姓闻吾过」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1215268_comment'></div>是以此卜也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1215268_comment'></div>不然，岂不知「职事有便于民而请之，真宰相之事也」欤？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1215268_comment'></div>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1215268_comment'></div>功臣之难，自古而然乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1215268_comment'></div>何之必不反，盖自今观之矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1215268_comment'></div>当是时，变起无虚岁，非特君疑臣，臣亦自疑而欲反。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1215268_comment'></div>萧何处于其间，盖亦自危哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1215268_comment'></div>贾生有言：「韩信最强，最先反」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1215268_comment'></div>愚以谓不然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1215268_comment'></div>信之英杰，不能为人下者也，虽居关中，犹欲以囚徒反，岂国大兵彊使然哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1215268_comment'></div>萧何、留侯、韩信皆称人杰，高祖所畏也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1215268_comment'></div>然何以素谨畏得全，虽老，得释犹徒跣入谢，此岂韩信所能效哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1215268_comment'></div>然致是纷纷者，有愧留侯矣。</div><div id='poem_sentence_36_1215268_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1215271' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1215271' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1215271?labeling=true' target='_blank'>记交趾进异兽</a><span class='authorDate'>（1098年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31323, "北宋", "苏过", "poem_title_1215271")'>苏过</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1215271_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1215271'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1215271'>麒麟凤凰，天所生也，虎豹蛇蝎，亦天所生也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1215271_comment'></div>生麟凤矣，必复生虎豹蛇蝎，苍苍者或自有说。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1215271_comment'></div>然天之生麟凤也不数，而虎豹蛇蝎害人之物，往往蕃衍于深山大泽间，耽耽焉，逐逐焉，肆其爪牙之利，以逞其口腹之欲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1215271_comment'></div>宜乎麒麟凤凰，高飞远引，不一游于世也！</div><div id='poem_sentence_3_1215271_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1215258' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1215258' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1215258?labeling=true' target='_blank'>书二李传后</a><span class='authorDate'>（1098年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31323, "北宋", "苏过", "poem_title_1215258")'>苏过</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1215258_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1215258'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1215258'>昔袁盎论绛侯功臣，非社稷臣，此固有为而言也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1215258_comment'></div>然功臣、社稷臣之辨，不可不察也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1215258_comment'></div>淮南王安反，谓大将军可刺，说丞相如发蒙耳，而独惮一汲黯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1215258_comment'></div>仗节死义，其与社稷存亡也审矣！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1215258_comment'></div>愚尝谓社稷臣如腹心，功臣如手足。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1215258_comment'></div>人有断一肢、折一足，未及死也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1215258_comment'></div>心腹之病则为膏肓，不可救已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1215258_comment'></div>李靖、李绩可谓功臣，始终唐之元勋也，而太宗付属委托亦已重矣，然止将帅之材耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1215258_comment'></div>疆埸之事，任之则有馀；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1215258_comment'></div>社稷之寄、安危之机，则两人者有折足渥形之败矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1215258_comment'></div>太宗欲伐高丽，谏者十六七，靖已老矣，而自请将兵，遂坚太宗黩武之志，几为不戢自焚之祸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1215258_comment'></div>高宗欲立武后，举朝为之寒心，而绩以为：「陛下家事，无问外人」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1215258_comment'></div>武氏之祸，戮及襁褓，唐室不绝如线。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1215258_comment'></div>夫二人者，为腹心之病，亦大矣！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1215258_comment'></div>张释之谏啬夫之拜，使文帝终身为长者；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1215258_comment'></div>魏元成折封伦之论，使太宗不失行仁义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1215258_comment'></div>语曰：「一言而兴邦，一言而丧邦」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1215258_comment'></div>亶其然乎！</div><div id='poem_sentence_17_1215258_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_522617' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_522617' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/522617?labeling=true' target='_blank'>予寓洛阳宝坛有僧悟超类有道者与语论事能援古證今盖未祝发时读孔氏之史书涉猎大义为浮屠犹不废今老矣不复读也形骸枯槁真能遗世故而玩死生者送予至龙门陪予游东西两山作此诗别之</a><span class='authorDate'>（1098年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31323, "北宋", "苏过", "poem_title_522617")'>苏过</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_522617_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_522617'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_522617'>我生江海上，性与鱼鸟逸。<div id='poem_sentence_0_522617_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_522617'>端来入世网，竟坐形骸役。<div id='poem_sentence_1_522617_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_522617'>此心本洞然，六月遭怵迫。<div id='poem_sentence_2_522617_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_522617'>常恐忘迹熟，主人不胜客。<div id='poem_sentence_3_522617_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_522617'>道人偶相逢，宿契类畴昔。<div id='poem_sentence_4_522617_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_522617'>巉岩秀眉目，灰槁心木石。<div id='poem_sentence_5_522617_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_522617'>语我学道难，吾徒犹不力。<div id='poem_sentence_6_522617_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_522617'>纷华久风靡，外慕失阃域。<div id='poem_sentence_7_522617_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_522617'>卑之毋高论，遣去身外物。<div id='poem_sentence_8_522617_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_522617'>未能忘饥寒，衣布饭疏粝。<div id='poem_sentence_9_522617_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_522617'>此语君自味，至道在咫尺。<div id='poem_sentence_10_522617_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_522617'>阅人吾虽多，子独无荆棘。<div id='poem_sentence_11_522617_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_522617'>送行聊过溪，共蹑登山屐<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_12_522617_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_522617'></div><div id='poem_sentence_13_522617_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_522617'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_12_522617_0'>⑴ 自注：有为超作紫方袍授之，辄藏而不服，曰吾教有坏色衣，无是服也。予益高之。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_522617_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_1215254' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1215254' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1215254?labeling=true' target='_blank'>书张骞传后</a><span class='authorDate'>（1098年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31323, "北宋", "苏过", "poem_title_1215254")'>苏过</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1215254_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1215254'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1215254'>酒色之害人，甚于毒药；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1215254_comment'></div>博弈之害财，甚于盗贼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1215254_comment'></div>然人知畏毒药而甘心于酒色，知恶盗贼而不厌博弈者，何哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1215254_comment'></div>适于己而忘于害耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1215254_comment'></div>千金之子，破家于声色狗马；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1215254_comment'></div>万乘之主，失德于玩好嗜欲者多矣，岂不信哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1215254_comment'></div>昔明皇引镜不乐，左右曰：「自韩休相，陛下无一日欢，何不逐去之」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1215254_comment'></div>帝曰：「吾虽瘠，天下肥矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1215254_comment'></div>而秦二世曰：「贤人之有天下也，适己而已」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1215254_comment'></div>故不及三年而有望夷之祸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1215254_comment'></div>楚灵王、吴夫差皆如是败。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1215254_comment'></div>此适己之效也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1215254_comment'></div>汉武帝袭文、景之业，内外晏然，家给人足，可谓盛矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1215254_comment'></div>然以一马之故，穷师万里，天下骚动，几及胜、广之乱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1215254_comment'></div>此谁发其端欤？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1215254_comment'></div>盖自张骞一使，睹筇竹、蜀布，大宛、身毒之饶，遂倡通西南夷之说。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1215254_comment'></div>又语以蛮夷贪汉币而多奇物，天子由是欣然，发使治兵，必得所欲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1215254_comment'></div>骞既封侯赐金，贪人自是争言外国利害，以尝天子之意，邀取富贵矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1215254_comment'></div>其后得乌孙、宛马，天子益甘心焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1215254_comment'></div>此贰师之役所以作也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1215254_comment'></div>是时李广利丧师郁成，欲归，天子大怒，使使遮玉门关，曰：「军有敢入者斩」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1215254_comment'></div>益发甲卒十八万，仅能克宛，取贰师善马而归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1215254_comment'></div>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1215254_comment'></div>徇一夫之私欲，竭生民之膏髓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1215254_comment'></div>虽系虏其人而郡县其地，何补疮夷之万一哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1215254_comment'></div>昔隋之亡也，盗起征辽，而征辽之师实倡于裴矩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1215254_comment'></div>裴矩之在张掖，得西域诸胡山川国俗之详，还为炀帝言之，曰：「胡多瑰怪名宝」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1215254_comment'></div>帝由是甘心四夷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1215254_comment'></div>高丽不来，故征辽自此始矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1215254_comment'></div>嗟乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1215254_comment'></div>小人之得君也，必因其所嗜而献其说。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1215254_comment'></div>非独用兵也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1215254_comment'></div>德宗喜财，故裴延龄以裒刻进；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1215254_comment'></div>宪宗既平淮西，稍欲纵意宫室游幸之乐，则皇甫镈以贡羡馀取卿相。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1215254_comment'></div>君臣之间，宁复有志于民也哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1215254_comment'></div>且夫土地非不广也，府库非不实也，宫室台榭非不美也，子女玉帛、羽毛齿革非不备也，食租衣税非不厚也，而皇皇焉外求之不已，何哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1215254_comment'></div>贪人之心，如饥渴然，必欲有其所未有者为富，见其所未见者为宝耳，夫岂有穷哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1215254_comment'></div>昔虞公以宝剑而亡，蒯瞆亦死于吕姜之剃，夫岂有国者，少此粪土耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1215254_comment'></div>然二君以此亡国殒身，世皆知非笑之矣，而不知彼数君之所甘心者，独非粪土乎？</div><div id='poem_sentence_38_1215254_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1215272' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1215272' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1215272?labeling=true' target='_blank'>东交门箴</a><span class='authorDate'>（1098年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31323, "北宋", "苏过", "poem_title_1215272")'>苏过</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1215272_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1215272'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1215272'>汉武帝为窦太主置酒宣室，使谒者引纳董偃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1215272_comment'></div>东方朔以为偃有斩罪三，安得入宣室？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1215272_comment'></div>上为更置酒北宫，而引偃从东司马门入，更其门曰东交门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1215272_comment'></div>而《前史》无讥焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1215272_comment'></div>作《东交门箴》：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_1215272'>上所好恶，民实趋之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1215272_comment'></div>风俗厚薄，君实驱之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1215272_comment'></div>道之以正，民俗罔中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1215272_comment'></div>倡之以淫，实烦有从。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1215272_comment'></div>帝于馆陶，在齐文姜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1215272_comment'></div>矧董外人，干国乱常。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1215272_comment'></div>既不能戮，反以为好。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1215272_comment'></div>予饮予燕，宣室是傲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1215272_comment'></div>伟彼臣朔，辟戟趋陛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1215272_comment'></div>鬻拳是效，刚而有礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1215272_comment'></div>改馆彻馔，北宫东门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1215272_comment'></div>虽曰从谏，东交实存。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1215272_comment'></div>维藩维戚，礼法遂恣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1215272_comment'></div>延及齐民，惟上所使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1215272_comment'></div>昔在季孙，赏盗以邑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1215272_comment'></div>鲁遂多盗，而罔敢诘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1215272_comment'></div>矧兹王宫，奸人是纳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1215272_comment'></div>昭示来世，有惭斯阖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1215272_comment'></div>蒉也扬觯，杜举得名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1215272_comment'></div>殿槛勿辑，直臣是旌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1215272_comment'></div>人孰无过，过而勿贰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1215272_comment'></div>宣室东交，实同而名异耳。</div><div id='poem_sentence_25_1215272_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1098&endYear=1098')">1098年</a>　苏过读《南史》，苏轼论物以人贵。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1098&endYear=1098')">1098年</a>　苏轼曾命苏过作《孔子弟子别传》，未成。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1098&endYear=1098')">1098年</a>　苏过之风义，足以动海民而化夷獠。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1098&endYear=1098')">1098年</a>　海南乏食，苏过取土芋细作，为“玉糁羹”，苏轼誉为天上人间绝味。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1098&endYear=1098')">1098年</a>　佳墨将尽，苏轼书记其事以付苏过。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1098&endYear=1098')">1098年</a>　在宜伦。岁末，苏迈、苏迨作诗怀苏过。过复作诗抒怀。作品：《岁暮见怀》（其一）<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《斜川集校注》卷二。）</span>《岁暮见怀》（其二）<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《斜川集校注》卷二。）</span><div id='poem_522597' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_522597' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/522597?labeling=true' target='_blank'>岁暮见怀<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1098年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31323, "北宋", "苏过", "poem_title_522597")'>苏过</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_522597_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_522597'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_522597'>所愿非富贵，甘苦同友于。<div id='poem_sentence_0_522597_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_522597'>长衾与大枕，共寝从悬弧。<div id='poem_sentence_1_522597_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_522597'>尔来万里别，南北如囚拘。<div id='poem_sentence_2_522597_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_522597'>一夫苟不获，仁圣惟予辜。<div id='poem_sentence_3_522597_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_522597'>而我三兄弟，飘泊海与湖。<div id='poem_sentence_4_522597_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_522597'></div><div id='poem_sentence_5_522597_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_522598' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_522598' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/522598?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1098年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_522598_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_522598'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_522598'>纷纷月挂树，征人念行路。<div id='poem_sentence_0_522598_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_522598'>行路何茫茫，谁为供屝屦。<div id='poem_sentence_1_522598_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_522598'>努力治芜秽，公归定非暮。<div id='poem_sentence_2_522598_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_522598'>东门会祖道，叹息两疏傅。<div id='poem_sentence_3_522598_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_522598'>涤器当自今，归欤不愆素。<div id='poem_sentence_4_522598_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_522598'></div><div id='poem_sentence_5_522598_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1099&endYear=1099')">1099年1月</a>　在宜伦。正月，五色雀见，苏轼作诗并记，苏过亦次韵。作品：《五色雀和大人韵》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《斜川集校注》卷二。苏轼所作为《五色雀》（并引），见《苏轼诗集》卷四十三。）</span><div id='poem_522551' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_522551' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/522551?labeling=true' target='_blank'>五色雀和大人韵</a><span class='authorDate'>（1099年1月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31323, "北宋", "苏过", "poem_title_522551")'>苏过</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_522551_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_522551'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_522551'>神雀来何从，飞鸣自为徒。<div id='poem_sentence_0_522551_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_522551'>尊卑有定分，众色敢乱朱。<div id='poem_sentence_1_522551_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_522551'>与公作新年，禬禳陋桃符。<div id='poem_sentence_2_522551_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_522551'>南迁不见鵩，屡集升平乌<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_3_522551_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_522551'>翩然自灵物，岂惟眷庭梧。<div id='poem_sentence_4_522551_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_522551'>年来翟公门，寂寞谁与娱。<div id='poem_sentence_5_522551_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_522551'>瓜田岂故侯，环堵真前儒。<div id='poem_sentence_6_522551_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_522551'>虽知非天穷，险阻殆切肤。<div id='poem_sentence_7_522551_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_522551'>海南夷獠窟，安得此异雏。<div id='poem_sentence_8_522551_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_522551'>似为三足使，仙子傥见呼。<div id='poem_sentence_9_522551_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_522551'>定知隐几人，嗒焉非昔吾。<div id='poem_sentence_10_522551_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_522551'>不愿宴西瑶，东华返旧都。<div id='poem_sentence_11_522551_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_522551'></div><div id='poem_sentence_12_522551_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_522551'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_3_522551_0'>⑴ 自注：柳仲郢每迁官，必乌集升平，第五日乃散。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_522551_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1099&endYear=1099')">1099年1月15日</a>　上元夜，苏轼与海南书生出游，归，与苏过论人生得失。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1099&endYear=1099')">1099年4月15日</a>　四月十五日，苏轼得《十八大阿罗汉图》，命苏过易其装轴。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1099&endYear=1099')">1099年4月19日</a>　四月十九日，海南乏粮，苏轼书龟息法付苏过。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1099&endYear=1099')">1099年</a>　苏轼与侄孙苏元老书，夸赞苏过文章峻壮。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1099&endYear=1099')">1099年</a>　在宜伦。葛延之来访，月余归，苏过作诗送之，兼寄诸兄弟。作品：《送人泛海北归兼寄诸兄弟》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《斜川集校注》卷二。）</span><div id='poem_522677' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_522677' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/522677?labeling=true' target='_blank'>送人泛海北归兼寄诸兄弟</a><span class='authorDate'>（1099年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31323, "北宋", "苏过", "poem_title_522677")'>苏过</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_522677_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_522677'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_522677'>冥冥天水吞为一，夜依北斗占南北。<div id='poem_sentence_0_522677_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_522677'>危楼时吐蛟蜃气，半山忽隐长鲸脊。<div id='poem_sentence_1_522677_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_522677'>起看樯头雉尾转，一帆千里日未足。<div id='poem_sentence_2_522677_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_522677'>此身何止轻鸿毛，到家始觉是真肉。<div id='poem_sentence_3_522677_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_522677'>怪君胡为冒此险，象犀珠玉非所役。<div id='poem_sentence_4_522677_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_522677'>凛然风义照古人，尺书为我通消息。<div id='poem_sentence_5_522677_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_522677'>我似当时常校尉，掘鼠餐毡从属国。<div id='poem_sentence_6_522677_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_522677'>茫茫海阔雁不到，长欲系书空悯默。<div id='poem_sentence_7_522677_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_522677'>凭君为语诸季孟，耐事忍惭真子职。<div id='poem_sentence_8_522677_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_522677'>面唾勿嫌解自乾，盗金却偿安用诘。<div id='poem_sentence_9_522677_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_522677'>杜门只作田舍子，地往江乡乘下泽。<div id='poem_sentence_10_522677_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_522677'>三吴想见稻如云，舶还时救陈蔡厄。<div id='poem_sentence_11_522677_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_522677'></div><div id='poem_sentence_12_522677_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1099&endYear=1099')">1099年</a>　苏轼又与苏元老书，称赞苏过之超然物外；裁书寄许下，托元老转致。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1099&endYear=1099')">1099年11月8日</a>　在宜伦。冬至日，儋人携具邀苏过与父饮，过作诗怀惠、许兄弟，极言海南异况。父轼次其韵。作品：《己卯冬至儋人携具见饮既罢有怀惠许兄弟》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《斜川集校注》卷二。苏轼次韵诗为《用过韵冬至与诸生饮酒》，见《苏轼诗集》卷四十二。是年冬至日为十一月初八日。）</span><div id='poem_522720' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_522720' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/522720?labeling=true' target='_blank'>己卯冬至儋人隽具见饮既罢有怀惠许兄弟</a><span class='authorDate'>（1099年11月8日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31323, "北宋", "苏过", "poem_title_522720")'>苏过</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言排律</div></div><div id='poem_title_522720_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_522720'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_522720'>寂寞三冬至，飘然瘴海中。<div id='poem_sentence_0_522720_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_522720'>不嫌羁寓远，屡感岁华穷。<div id='poem_sentence_1_522720_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_522720'>父老怜匏系，肴蔬盛簋饛。<div id='poem_sentence_2_522720_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_522720'>一欢为子寿，百福与君同。<div id='poem_sentence_3_522720_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_522720'>已惯鸢飞堕，真忘马首东。<div id='poem_sentence_4_522720_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_522720'>南间行自变，重译不须通。<div id='poem_sentence_5_522720_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_522720'>椰酒醍醐白，银皮琥珀红<span class='inlineComment2'>（自注：海南有银皮酒。）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_6_522720_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_522720'>伧狞醉野獠，绝倒共邻翁。<div id='poem_sentence_7_522720_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_522720'>藷芋人人送，囷庖日日丰。<div id='poem_sentence_8_522720_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_522720'>瘴收黎母谷，露入菊花丛。<div id='poem_sentence_9_522720_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_522720'>海蜑羞蚶蛤，园奴馈韭菘。<div id='poem_sentence_10_522720_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_522720'>槟榔代茗饮，吉内御霜风。<div id='poem_sentence_11_522720_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_522720'>怅望怀诸阮，遥知忆小冯。<div id='poem_sentence_12_522720_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_522720'>客身虽岭峤，逸想在瀛蓬。<div id='poem_sentence_13_522720_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_522720'>介阶惟偕母，庞团独侍公。<div id='poem_sentence_14_522720_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_522720'>故山千万里，此意托飞鸿。<div id='poem_sentence_15_522720_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_522720'></div><div id='poem_sentence_16_522720_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1099&endYear=1099')">1099年12月19日</a>　在宜伦。十二月十九日，苏轼生日，苏过作诗。作品：《大人生日》（其一）<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《斜川集校注》卷二。《斜川集校注》有《大人生日》（一）同题诗三首，此为其中之一，首句为“未试凌云白日仙”）</span>《大人生日》（其二）<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《斜川集校注》卷二。《斜川集校注》有《大人生日》（二）同题诗三首，此为其中之一，首句为“昔将直道破群纤”）</span><div id='poem_522735' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_522735' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/522735?labeling=true' target='_blank'>大人生日<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1099年12月19日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31323, "北宋", "苏过", "poem_title_522735")'>苏过</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_522735_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_522735'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_522735'>未试陵云白日仙，此声固已速邮传<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_0_522735_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_522735'>阴功何止千人活，法眼要求一大缘。<div id='poem_sentence_1_522735_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_522735'>枕上轩裳真昨梦，腹中梨枣是归田。<div id='poem_sentence_2_522735_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_522735'>他时汉殿观遗鼎，犹记曾陈柏寝年。<div id='poem_sentence_3_522735_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_522735'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_522735_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_522735'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_0_522735_0'>⑴ 自注：公在海南，四方传有白日上升事。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_522735_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_522736' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_522736' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/522736?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其三 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1098年12月19日）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_522736_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_522736'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_522736'>昔将直道破群纤，出走宁逃此日谗。<div id='poem_sentence_0_522736_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_522736'>塞马未还非叟病，莫邪偶弃岂铅铦。<div id='poem_sentence_1_522736_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_522736'>长生有道因辞宠，造物无私独与谦。<div id='poem_sentence_2_522736_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_522736'>从此轩裳真敝屣，世间出世固难兼。<div id='poem_sentence_3_522736_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_522736'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_522736_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1099&endYear=1099')">1099年</a>　在宜伦。苏过作文论海南黎事，提出“拊循其民”的和夷主张。作品：《论海南黎事书》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《斜川集校注》卷七。）</span><div id='poem_1215246' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1215246' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1215246?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论海南黎事书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1099年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31323, "北宋", "苏过", "poem_title_1215246")'>苏过</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1215246_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1215246'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1215246'>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1215246_comment'></div>天下之利害，县官未始得十四五也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1215246_comment'></div>天子不过得之左右大臣，左右大臣不过得之方伯部使者，方伯部使者不过得之守令；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1215246_comment'></div>守令能得之于民者，特利害之似耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1215246_comment'></div>今天下号称能吏者，直以簿书期会，洁身奉己而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1215246_comment'></div>尤异者，使民尊之如鬼神，畏之如雷霆，可谓能矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1215246_comment'></div>然上之情不可知，下之情不能达，所谓利害之实，从何而得之哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1215246_comment'></div>昔然明欲毁乡校，子产弗许，以为郑人朝夕游焉，以议执政之善否。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1215246_comment'></div>夫民至愚而神者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1215246_comment'></div>国家之善恶，法令之得失，官吏之贤不肖，未尝不窃议于下也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1215246_comment'></div>而况其一方之利害，耳目所见，父兄所传，日夜讲之，可谓熟矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1215246_comment'></div>古之君子建一事，出一令，未尝不参之于民言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1215246_comment'></div>而执事者不求之于斯人，而斯人者未尝以实告，岂上下之情有间而然耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1215246_comment'></div>某窃见海南黎人一事，议者纷然，利害未决。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1215246_comment'></div>此虽朝廷疮疥之病，不足以置齿牙，然一夫不获，亦君子之所耻也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1215246_comment'></div>异时论者，或欲覆其巢穴而夷其地，或欲羁役其人而改其俗，或欲绝其通市以困其力。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1215246_comment'></div>然皆不得其要，徒使震詟警扰，戕我官吏，虏吾民人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1215246_comment'></div>而执事者又熟视而不敢谁何，上下相蒙，使死者无所告，生者无所芘，甚可哀也！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1215246_comment'></div>岂议者未得利害之本末，而斯人未有实告者耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1215246_comment'></div>仆侍亲海南，实编于民，所与游者，田父野老，闾阎之民耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1215246_comment'></div>道不足以相休戚，而言之者又忘其忌讳，故所得为最详。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1215246_comment'></div>若默而不言，孰为执事者论之？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1215246_comment'></div>议者曰：「黎人之居，非有重门击柝之固，甲盾剑戟之利，特若鸟兽，聚散于山林溪谷之閒耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1215246_comment'></div>若以锐师出其不意，焚其聚落，一举可灭也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1215246_comment'></div>执事者以为信然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1215246_comment'></div>何则？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1215246_comment'></div>按图观之，方寸之地耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1215246_comment'></div>不过选士数千，一将可办也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1215246_comment'></div>仆以为不然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1215246_comment'></div>闻之父老曰：黎人之居，山林重复，鸟道上下，骑不能骋也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1215246_comment'></div>而健者常伏于其閒，以阻行旅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1215246_comment'></div>吾乃陈以待之，鼓而攻之，彼不吾角也，然必狼狈而走山林，以邀吾归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1215246_comment'></div>一夫鸱张，虽贲、育无所施其勇，六师无所用其众。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1215246_comment'></div>是岂一将可睥睨也哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1215246_comment'></div>议者又曰：「不克，且济师」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1215246_comment'></div>此又非策也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1215246_comment'></div>贼闻吾之大举也，必尽族而来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1215246_comment'></div>兽穷则搏，无虑精兵万人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1215246_comment'></div>吾乃曳甲胄之士，践不测之域，以所短，校所长，非三万人不可胜也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1215246_comment'></div>且不可以一举得之也，期以三岁取之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1215246_comment'></div>夫濒海瘠卤之地，屯三万人，且三岁粮，民何以堪之乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1215246_comment'></div>且既得地，必郡县之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1215246_comment'></div>而深山穷谷之中，豺狼魑魅之所凭，水土疾疫之为厉，岂华人之所能安也哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1215246_comment'></div>不然，既得之而且复失之矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1215246_comment'></div>议者又曰：「黎人所以慢边吏而侮吾民者，法不惩耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1215246_comment'></div>今杀人者止于输牛羊，是何足创哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1215246_comment'></div>若屯师于境，而许以自新，易之衣冠，使之内属，法令徭赋，一均吾民，则易治矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1215246_comment'></div>执事者以为信然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1215246_comment'></div>何则？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1215246_comment'></div>以其怖死而必从吾，又不血刃而得方千里之地，自是无疆埸之患，省屯师之费矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1215246_comment'></div>仆以为不然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1215246_comment'></div>夷狄之性如犬豕然，其服可变而性不可改也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1215246_comment'></div>其纾死听命，愿为吾民者，未知异日之患也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1215246_comment'></div>法令之烦苛，调敛之无时，官吏之贪求，能保其无乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1215246_comment'></div>闻之父老曰：往者罢庸而取直，吾民皆欲弃冠服而椎髻，舍坟墓而逃山林。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1215246_comment'></div>此岂有他哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1215246_comment'></div>趋所乐也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1215246_comment'></div>而欲使黎人弃彼取此，不亦难乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1215246_comment'></div>譬之养虎狼于陷阱，置蝮虺于几席，谓其驯扰不螫，亦误矣！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1215246_comment'></div>议者又曰：「黎人处不毛之地，盐酪、谷帛、斤斧、器用，悉资之华人，特以沈香、古贝易之耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1215246_comment'></div>吾焉用此藉寇兵而资盗粮哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1215246_comment'></div>宜饬边吏，谨视商贾之出入，彼自困矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1215246_comment'></div>执事必以为信然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1215246_comment'></div>何则？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1215246_comment'></div>以为真能困彼而不能困我也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1215246_comment'></div>仆以为不然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1215246_comment'></div>濒海郡县，所以能鸠民置吏，养兵聚财者，恃商人耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1215246_comment'></div>商人轻风涛之虞，涉不测万里之险，而岁岁必集者，贪倍蓰之息尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1215246_comment'></div>若绝黎人之欢，商人不来，我自困矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1215246_comment'></div>关市之征，岁入不足，一困也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1215246_comment'></div>兵吏廪赐，无所从出，二困也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1215246_comment'></div>衣食不足，饥寒从之，三困也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1215246_comment'></div>而黎人必将齧草木，饮血茹毛，以求生生之理，又焉能困彼哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1215246_comment'></div>医之治疾也，攻其所病之体，未有攻其未病者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1215246_comment'></div>疽之生于首则治其首，生于足则治其足，未有疾在首而砭其背，在足而穴其胸也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1215246_comment'></div>今黎人特小小边盗耳，议者乃欲起争桑、毁瓶之隙，忘一炬燎原之戒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1215246_comment'></div>岂非攻其所未病者哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1215246_comment'></div>父老曰：黎人虽众，不能入寇也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1215246_comment'></div>何则？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1215246_comment'></div>非有君长酋豪为之谋，赏罚号令以一其众也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1215246_comment'></div>今聚百人之徒，具十日之粮，始可与边吏遇也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1215246_comment'></div>而彼府库发敛之资，十日之粮，岂易办哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1215246_comment'></div>富者不过椎牛飨士，一饱而奋，旦出而夕返也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1215246_comment'></div>我特清野以避其锋，使来无所获，得不偿费，彼何自苦以取憎于我乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1215246_comment'></div>独有质劫之患耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1215246_comment'></div>然考其本，则我曲而彼直。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1215246_comment'></div>父老曰：黎人之性，敦愿朴讷，无文书符契之用，刻木结绳而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1215246_comment'></div>故华人欺其愚而夺其财。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1215246_comment'></div>彼不敢诉之于吏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1215246_comment'></div>何则？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1215246_comment'></div>吏不通其语言，而胥吏责其贿赂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1215246_comment'></div>忿而无告，惟有质人而取偿耳！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1215246_comment'></div>吏足以直其忿，法足以禁其欺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1215246_comment'></div>彼若赤子之爱父母也，何惮一诉而质人也哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1215246_comment'></div>为执事计者，上策莫如自治。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1215246_comment'></div>当饬有司，严约束，市黎人物而不与其直者，岁倍偿之，且籍其家而刑其人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1215246_comment'></div>吏敢取赂者，不以常制论。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1215246_comment'></div>而守令不举者，部使者按之以闻；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1215246_comment'></div>又为之赏典，以待能吏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_98_1215246_comment'></div>如此，则能者劝，慢者惩，贪胥猾商不敢肆其奸，边自宁矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_99_1215246_comment'></div>父老又曰：异时走朱崖者，东西二道，羁旅无虞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_100_1215246_comment'></div>今七八百里悉为贼区，官吏文书商贾，往来皆道于海。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_101_1215246_comment'></div>此不可不治也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_102_1215246_comment'></div>仆以为以力胜者，兵罢而复塞；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_103_1215246_comment'></div>以利啖者，贼贪而不叛也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_104_1215246_comment'></div>朝廷若捐数官以使人，则贤于用师矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_105_1215246_comment'></div>今黎人盗边民之畜，巨室不过从十馀隶，径入其族，数其罪取之，不敢拒命者，信异其人也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_106_1215246_comment'></div>仆以为此可许以官而用矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_107_1215246_comment'></div>使赍金帛，入喻诸黎，晓以利害，惧以祸福。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_108_1215246_comment'></div>若能开复故道，使行旅无壅，则籍其众所畏服者请诸朝，假以一命，而岁与其禄，不过总十馀人，岁捐千缗耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_109_1215246_comment'></div>今朱崖屯师千人，岁不下万缗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_110_1215246_comment'></div>若取十一以为黎人之禄，可以罢千师之屯矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_111_1215246_comment'></div>且夫兵之所在，耗于国而又以启边衅也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_112_1215246_comment'></div>盖捍掫之吏，皆用武夫，而卒伍之籍，多出无赖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_113_1215246_comment'></div>所过聚落，鸡犬一空。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_114_1215246_comment'></div>来则捶暴其家人，去则坏弃其器具。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_115_1215246_comment'></div>昔日之道，未必不缘是而塞也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_116_1215246_comment'></div>仆以为戍卒可省，民兵可用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_117_1215246_comment'></div>何则？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_118_1215246_comment'></div>编户之家，家有武备，亲戚坟墓所在，人自为战，而又习其山川险阻，耐其风土瘴疠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_119_1215246_comment'></div>吏若拊循其民，岁有以赏之，则吾藩篱不可窥矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_120_1215246_comment'></div>今西北二虏，藉此以制其侵轶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_121_1215246_comment'></div>况此小丑，何足道哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_122_1215246_comment'></div>然议者本以图功名，邀爵赏，不恤长久之计，苟目前之利也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_123_1215246_comment'></div>若仆所陈，何功之有哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_124_1215246_comment'></div>然执事当先国计而后身计，则远人受赐也。</div><div id='poem_sentence_125_1215246_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1100&endYear=1100')">1100年1月1日</a>　正月初一，苏过取薤蜜作粥啖父，以养其生。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1100&endYear=1100')">1100年1月15日</a>　一月十五日，苏轼作诗，盛赞苏过夫妇笃于孝道。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1100&endYear=1100')">1100年</a>　苏过画枯木竹石，苏轼为题咏，赞其能为竹传神。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1100&endYear=1100')">1100年3月</a>　三月清明，苏过诵书朗然，父轼闻而有感，遂和陶渊明诗二首。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1100&endYear=1100')">1100年</a>　苏轼致书刘沔，赞苏过文奇，在海外为文以娱父。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1100&endYear=1100')">1100年</a>　苏轼与父论秦观、张耒才学。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1100&endYear=1100')">1100年</a>　苏轼告苏过，决不为海外人。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1100&endYear=1100')">1100年4月21日</a>　四月二十一日，朝廷命苏轼等徙内郡居住。告下，苏轼迁廉州。苏过整装，还书待发。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1100&endYear=1100')">1100年</a>　苏过与父初欲从惠州搬家来，作终老廉州计。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1100&endYear=1100')">1100年6月</a>　六月，苏过随父登舟启航，渡海离儋，儋人相送于海边。<br /></div>
-----end



-----title
合浦
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='a5e1db607ace46fab13e1fa85cd88ce2_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("a5e1db607ace46fab13e1fa85cd88ce2");'><span id='a5e1db607ace46fab13e1fa85cd88ce2_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1100&endYear=1100')">1100年</a>，29岁</div><div id='a5e1db607ace46fab13e1fa85cd88ce2' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1100&endYear=1100')">1100年7月4日</a>　七月四日，苏过与父抵廉州。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1100&endYear=1100')">1100年8月</a>　八月告下，苏轼再迁舒州团练副使，永州居住。苏过与父拟欲过中秋后离廉。苏迨已到惠州。轼令迈还书郑靖老，挈家至梧州相会。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1100&endYear=1100')">1100年8月29日</a>　八月二十九日，苏过与父离廉州。九月六日至郁林，闻秦少游死讯。<br /></div>
-----end

-----title
梧州
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='e8a94d2461f24e7fbaa7097666e130fc_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("e8a94d2461f24e7fbaa7097666e130fc");'><span id='e8a94d2461f24e7fbaa7097666e130fc_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1100&endYear=1100')">1100年</a>，29岁</div><div id='e8a94d2461f24e7fbaa7097666e130fc' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1100&endYear=1100')">1100年</a>　苏过与父至梧州，而苏迈、苏迨未到，遂顺西江赴广州，与之会合。<br /></div>
-----end



-----title
德庆
-----detail

-----end



-----title
韶关
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='bcb708fded044eb098ed72bf87993d8a_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("bcb708fded044eb098ed72bf87993d8a");'><span id='bcb708fded044eb098ed72bf87993d8a_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1100&endYear=1100')">1100年</a>，29岁</div><div id='bcb708fded044eb098ed72bf87993d8a' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1100&endYear=1100')">1100年12月</a>　十一月离廉州，十二月至韶州。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1100&endYear=1100')">1100年12月19日</a>　在韶州。十二月十九日，苏轼生日，苏过有诗相庆。作品：《大人生日》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《斜川集校注》卷二。《斜川集校注》有《大人生日》同题诗三首，此为其中之一，首句为“七年野鹤困鸡群”）</span><div id='poem_522734' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_522734' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/522734?labeling=true' target='_blank'>大人生日<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1100年12月19日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31323, "北宋", "苏过", "poem_title_522734")'>苏过</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_522734_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_522734'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_522734'>七年野鹤困鸡群，匪虎真同子在陈。<div id='poem_sentence_0_522734_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_522734'>四海澄清待今日，五朝光辅属何人。<div id='poem_sentence_1_522734_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_522734'>从来令尹元无愠，岂独原生不病贫。<div id='poem_sentence_2_522734_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_522734'>天欲斯民跻仁寿，卧龙宁许久谋身。<div id='poem_sentence_3_522734_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_522734'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_522734_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1100&endYear=1100')">1100年12月</a>　苏轼读程天侔（全父）诗，题其后付苏过。<br /></div>
-----end



-----title
大余
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='f14c5160ae6f473ba4e9a261bdbb29b8_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("f14c5160ae6f473ba4e9a261bdbb29b8");'><span id='f14c5160ae6f473ba4e9a261bdbb29b8_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1101&endYear=1101')">1101年</a>，30岁</div><div id='f14c5160ae6f473ba4e9a261bdbb29b8' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1101&endYear=1101')">1101年1月</a>　正月渡大庾岭，抵虔州。得孙志举寄书，见苏迟《赠孙志举》诗，苏过与父皆和。<br /></div>
-----end



-----title
星子
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='71e9b598f1d341acbf8b7f204e8c56cd_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("71e9b598f1d341acbf8b7f204e8c56cd");'><span id='71e9b598f1d341acbf8b7f204e8c56cd_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1101&endYear=1101')">1101年</a>，30岁</div><div id='71e9b598f1d341acbf8b7f204e8c56cd' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1101&endYear=1101')">1101年4月12日</a>　三月下旬，离虔州。四月，至南康军；十二日，苏过侍父为刘义仲题写墓表。<br /></div>
-----end



-----title
郏县
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='421bb3b5baa54ff199d344e33ed83357_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("421bb3b5baa54ff199d344e33ed83357");'><span id='421bb3b5baa54ff199d344e33ed83357_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1102&endYear=1103')">1102-1103年</a>，31-32岁</div><div id='421bb3b5baa54ff199d344e33ed83357' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1102&endYear=1102')">1102年4月</a>　春，苏过扶苏轼灵柩自淮入汴，至陈留登陆西行。四月，苏辙遣苏迈往京城迁王闰之及苏迨亡妻欧阳氏灵柩，至郏县待葬。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1102&endYear=1102')">1102年闰6月</a>　闰六月，苏过兄弟葬其亡父亡母于河南郏城小峨眉山。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1102&endYear=1102')">1102年</a>　苏迈、苏迨随叔父归许，生事萧然，苏辙鬻别业以助之。苏过与侄苏符居郏城小峨眉山守丧。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1102&endYear=1102')">1102年8月</a>　在郏县。秋八月，僧道潜（参寥子）访苏过于郏城上瑞里，将归，过作诗及叙送之。作品：《送参寥师归钱塘》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《斜川集校注》卷二。）</span>《送参寥道人南归叙》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《斜川集校注》卷八。）</span><div id='poem_522696' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_522696' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/522696?labeling=true' target='_blank'>送参寥师归钱塘</a><span class='authorDate'>（1102年8月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31323, "北宋", "苏过", "poem_title_522696")'>苏过</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_522696_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_522696'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_522696'>我先大夫东南游，六年云水穷抉搜。<div id='poem_sentence_0_522696_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_522696'>吹嘘人物到方外，伯乐未忍轻骅骝。<div id='poem_sentence_1_522696_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_522696'>老师一见心相投，气味要是同薰莸。<div id='poem_sentence_2_522696_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_522696'>尘埃岂解埋珠玉，自有宝气干斗牛。<div id='poem_sentence_3_522696_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_522696'>作诗为文尽馀事，劲节凛凛横九秋。<div id='poem_sentence_4_522696_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_522696'>俗子欲交辄掉头，我友天下第一流。<div id='poem_sentence_5_522696_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_522696'>虽遭谤骂不少避，年世久已同浮沤。<div id='poem_sentence_6_522696_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_522696'>我昨南来自炎州，师亦方解钟仪囚。<div id='poem_sentence_7_522696_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_522696'>握手流涕古汴沟，生死骨肉我未瘳。<div id='poem_sentence_8_522696_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_522696'>众人见弃谁相休，累然独处空山幽。<div id='poem_sentence_9_522696_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_522696'>忽闻剥啄师唤我，洒扫茅堂三日留。<div id='poem_sentence_10_522696_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_522696'>行行吴越有旧隐，明年当泛西湖舟。<div id='poem_sentence_11_522696_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_522696'>赠言乃是朋友义，敢效儿女空绸缪。<div id='poem_sentence_12_522696_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_522696'>夜光明月宜自收，虎文豹缬非身谋。<div id='poem_sentence_13_522696_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_522696'></div><div id='poem_sentence_14_522696_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1215250' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1215250' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1215250?labeling=true' target='_blank'>送参寥道人南归叙<span class='inlineComment2'>（崇宁元年）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1102年8月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31323, "北宋", "苏过", "poem_title_1215250")'>苏过</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1215250_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1215250'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1215250'>物有是病，必有是德也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1215250_comment'></div>药之苦口，必药之良者也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1215250_comment'></div>马之蹄齧，必马之善走者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1215250_comment'></div>君子之病曰刚与厉，隘与不逊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1215250_comment'></div>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1215250_comment'></div>此世俗之所谓病耳，何损夫君子！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1215250_comment'></div>尝以谓士之立身，宁有是病，而恶夫所谓乡原者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1215250_comment'></div>孔子曰：「吾与狂狷，狂者进取，狷者有所不为」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1215250_comment'></div>是犹可以入于君子之涂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1215250_comment'></div>而鄙夫其未得之也，患不得之；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1215250_comment'></div>既得之，患失之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1215250_comment'></div>胁肩谄笑，劳于夏畦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1215250_comment'></div>吁！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1215250_comment'></div>可哀也甚矣！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1215250_comment'></div>刚之难能也，如登高山，如挽强，如激水，不勉则不至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1215250_comment'></div>而自贬苟求之道，如走坂，如舍矢，如覆水之易也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1215250_comment'></div>故刚宁过，不失为君子；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1215250_comment'></div>少柔韦汩没，必流为鄙夫也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1215250_comment'></div>盖尝读柳子厚《佩韦赋》，陋其为人，曰：「非君子之言也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1215250_comment'></div>士惟恐不刚耳，以侧媚伾、文，求富贵以败而不复，夫岂刚之罪也哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1215250_comment'></div>使子厚蚤知所佩，则不至此也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1215250_comment'></div>《传》曰：「美者必很，恶者必婉」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1215250_comment'></div>余于交游之间信然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1215250_comment'></div>凡平日务为可喜之论，揣所乐闻，惟恐色忤人者，此必临利害，相弃如路人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1215250_comment'></div>面折人，攻其所短，若可憎者，此必与人同休戚，誓死而不去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1215250_comment'></div>浮屠中有参寥子者，年六十，性刚狷不能容物；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1215250_comment'></div>又善触忌讳，取憎于世，然亦未尝以一毫自挫也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1215250_comment'></div>余始见之于黄，今二十年，发白形瘦，而志不少变。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1215250_comment'></div>其徒语参寥子者，必曰：「是难与处」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1215250_comment'></div>士大夫语参寥子者，必曰：「是难与游」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1215250_comment'></div>然参寥子之名益高，岂非所谓有君子之病者夫！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1215250_comment'></div>使参寥子善俯仰，与世浮沈，虽人人誉之，余安用哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1215250_comment'></div>壬午岁秋八月，来自香山，见余上瑞，曰：「吾将南归，何以赠我？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1215250_comment'></div>且吾前日得奇祸几死，今未知所创，丐子一言」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1215250_comment'></div>余曰：子知屠牛坦之刀乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1215250_comment'></div>十九年若新发于硎，措刃于可游之地，而以婴不折之所也，此为善用刚矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1215250_comment'></div>子行游天下，批大郤，导大窾，愿俟知者，不汝疵也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1215250_comment'></div>不然，则善刀而藏之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1215250_comment'></div>若又能灰心槁形，澹然遗世，以从东郭顺子之游，则余他日察之，必曰：此非昔之参寥子也。</div><div id='poem_sentence_38_1215250_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1102&endYear=1102')">1102年</a>　在郏县。李廌曾来郏城卜兆葬苏轼，苏过居丧期间有诗多篇赠之。作品：《北山杂诗十首》（其九）<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《斜川集校注》卷二。北山，即指小峨眉山，位于郏县西北。）</span><div id='poem_522593' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_522593' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/522593?labeling=true' target='_blank'>北山杂诗十首<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其九 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1102年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31323, "北宋", "苏过", "poem_title_522593")'>苏过</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_522593_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_522593'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_522593'>毡裘御霜风，从人笑胡服。<div id='poem_sentence_0_522593_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_522593'>长斋似浮屠，逾月不知肉。<div id='poem_sentence_1_522593_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_522593'>东邻有病媪，发白垂鹳鹄。<div id='poem_sentence_2_522593_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_522593'>拥灶坐无衣，何曾饱脱粟。<div id='poem_sentence_3_522593_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_522593'>哀哉天民穷，寿考非其福。<div id='poem_sentence_4_522593_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_522593'>同此覆载间，我生良已足。<div id='poem_sentence_5_522593_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_522593'></div><div id='poem_sentence_6_522593_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1102&endYear=1102')">1102年</a>　在郏县。苏过、苏符于北山结茅为庐，凿墙为牖，掘地穴作炉，掘井以分甘邻里。过有诗叙其事。作品：《北山杂诗十首》（其三）<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《斜川集校注》卷二。）</span>《北山杂诗十首》（其四）<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《斜川集校注》卷二。）</span>《北山杂诗十首》（其五）<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《斜川集校注》卷二。）</span>《山居苦寒》（其一）<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《斜川集校注》卷二。山居，即指居于小峨眉山。）</span>《山居苦寒》（其二）<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《斜川集校注》卷二。）</span><div id='poem_522587' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_522587' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/522587?labeling=true' target='_blank'>北山杂诗十首<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其三 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1102年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31323, "北宋", "苏过", "poem_title_522587")'>苏过</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_522587_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_522587'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_522587'>霜馀木叶脱，浩荡风千里。<div id='poem_sentence_0_522587_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_522587'>簸摇茅屋下，布被冷如水。<div id='poem_sentence_1_522587_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_522587'>吾侪贫亦巧，纸帐陋纨绮。<div id='poem_sentence_2_522587_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_522587'>柴门任轩吼，晓梦方清美。<div id='poem_sentence_3_522587_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_522587'>墙东新凿牖，朝阳催我起。<div id='poem_sentence_4_522587_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_522587'>安眠愧耕者，陇月射牛耳。<div id='poem_sentence_0_522588'>午碗不能寐，床头井百尺。<div id='poem_sentence_0_522588_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_522588'>辘轳下长绠，铿响鸣山骨。<div id='poem_sentence_1_522588_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_522588'>分甘遍邻社，甚旱犹湍碧。<div id='poem_sentence_2_522588_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_522588'>烹茶沸小鼎，自拨寒灰白。<div id='poem_sentence_3_522588_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_522588'>默默谁与语，扣门惟木客。<div id='poem_sentence_4_522588_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_522588'>坐念鲁两生，壁间有陈迹。<div id='poem_sentence_5_522588_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_522588'></div><div id='poem_sentence_6_522588_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_522589' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_522589' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/522589?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其五 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1102年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_522589_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_522589'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_522589'>默李吾所畏，文字班马流。<div id='poem_sentence_0_522589_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_522589'>空斋锁长夜，尺渎横吞舟。<div id='poem_sentence_1_522589_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_522589'>谁令效方朔，顾盼侏儒羞。<div id='poem_sentence_2_522589_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_522589'>不如谈天李，高论隘九州。<div id='poem_sentence_3_522589_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_522589'>能为齐谐语，自许监河侯。<div id='poem_sentence_4_522589_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_content_522823'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_522823'>十里山行步步高，阴风怪穴乱呼号。<div id='poem_sentence_0_522823_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' class='authorDate'>（1102年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31323, "北宋", "苏过", "poem_title_522826")'>苏过</a></span><br id='poem_sentence_0_522826'>傍舍孤嫠八十馀，背无完絮况裙襦。<div id='poem_sentence_0_522826_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_522826'>分衣愧乏庄公惠，纸被聊将慰老臞<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_1_522826_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_522826'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_522826_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_522826'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_1_522826_0'>⑴ 自注：草堂之东南有梁妪，八十馀岁，形貌瘠伛，耳目皆废。余偶见而哀之，默谓犹子符，天寒甚，是且冻死，当制纸被与之，既而忘之。一日，忽遣其子来索纸被，其子亦不知妪安授此意，余卒与之。然聋聩老病如此，岂其神完而外游得吾之心耶，抑寒苦之极而发于梦寐也。事稍异，故记之。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_522826_comment'></div></div><br ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1102&endYear=1102')">1102年</a>　在郏县。冬雪，苏过作《小雪》诗，写贫富忧乐之状，寄穷达超脱之旨。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《斜川集校注》卷二。）</span><div id='poem_522580' class='_poem'><div class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31323, "北宋", "苏过", "poem_title_522580")'>苏过</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_522580_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_522580'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_522580'>小雪不盈寸，阴风何凛冽。<div id='poem_sentence_0_522580_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_522580'>那堪平地尺，奈此衣百结。<div id='poem_sentence_1_522580_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_522580_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_522580'>沈沈五侯居，碧瓦题目华棁。<div id='poem_sentence_4_522580_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1103&endYear=1103')">1103年</a>　春夏皆居丧于郏城，闻李廌（方叔）于颍川长社县治水磨，苏过以诗戏之。作品：《李方叔治颍川水磨作诗戏之》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《斜川集校注》卷二。）</span><div id='poem_522704' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_522704' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/522704?labeling=true' target='_blank'>李方叔治颍川水磨作诗戏之</a><span class='authorDate'>（1103年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31323, "北宋", "苏过", "poem_title_522704")'>苏过</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_522704_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_522704'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_522704'>君不见相如昔隐临邛市，文君当垆身涤器。<div id='poem_sentence_0_522704_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_522704'>未逢给札赋凌云，岂免辛勤穿犊鼻。<div id='poem_sentence_1_522704_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_522704'>又不见苏秦大困还家时，失计颇遭妻子詈。<div id='poem_sentence_2_522704_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_522704'>谁令奔走事口舌，不学周人营什二。<div id='poem_sentence_3_522704_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_522704'>李侯平生无一廛，只有便便五经笥。<div id='poem_sentence_4_522704_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_522704'>儒冠半世已误身，老欲归耕无耒耜。<div id='poem_sentence_5_522704_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_522704'>近闻颍川有瀑布，碓磨能穷溪谷利。<div id='poem_sentence_6_522704_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_522704'>酾渠凿石激清流，机动轮旋人力易。<div id='poem_sentence_7_522704_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_522704'>今年麦熟春雨足，车载斗量应有备。<div id='poem_sentence_8_522704_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_522704'>勿嫌巾袂缟纷纷，饱看溪渠鸣涖涖。<div id='poem_sentence_9_522704_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_522704'>堆盘坐想雪如山，梦中已觉钱流地。<div id='poem_sentence_10_522704_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_522704'>特君结庐秋风初，我欲叩门来上瑞。<div id='poem_sentence_11_522704_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_522704'>起搜汤饼扫飞罗，轹釜操刀定中馈。<div id='poem_sentence_12_522704_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_522704'>千金何必羡鸱夷，少有属餍而已矣。<div id='poem_sentence_13_522704_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_522704'>嵇康好锻季主卜，达人未免兹游戏。<div id='poem_sentence_14_522704_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' -----title
许昌

ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1104&endYear=1104')">1104年</a>　在长社。苏辙初得南园，作诗，苏过次其韵。作品：《和新葺南园》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《斜川集校注》卷三。苏辙次韵诗为《初得南园》，见《栾城集·栾城后集》卷三。）</span><div id='poem_522773' id='poem_sentence_4_522773_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1105&endYear=1105')">1105年</a>　在长社。仲夏，苏过观吕知止所藏唐人画马图，作跋语。作品：《题唐马》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《斜川集校注》卷八。）</span><div id='poem_1215267' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1215267' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1215267?labeling=true' target='_blank'>题唐马</a><span class='authorDate'>（1105年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31323, "北宋", "苏过", "poem_title_1215267")'>苏过</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1215267_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1215267'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1215267'>先子《赋申王马图》有「肉騣汗血尽龙种，紫袍玉带真天人」之句，见得当时不独曹纬辈画骨而不画肉，诸王留意摹写亦然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1215267_comment'></div>故后世才见画马，便指为曹纬辈作，定知诸王肆意驰骋，所见既多，下笔益高，其间造入微妙处，曹纬所不□到，其可概以画目之耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1215267_comment'></div>崇宁作噩岁仲夏吕知止家避暑，因观唐马，遂书卷末。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1215267_comment'></div>眉阳苏叔党题。</div><div id='poem_sentence_3_1215267_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1215267'><span class='label'>按：</span>《铁琴铜剑楼藏书题跋集录》卷二，上海古籍出版社一九八五年版第四二页。<br /></div><div id='poem_note_1215267_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1105&endYear=1105')">1105年</a>　泗州士人李稙（元秀）从苏过问学，岁岁往来，遂为至交。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1105&endYear=1105')">1105年</a>　在长社。范正平于颍昌西湖筑园，题名“大隐”，苏过题诗。作品：《大隐堂为范氏西田题》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《斜川集校注》卷三。）</span><div id='poem_522681' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_522681' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/522681?labeling=true' target='_blank'>大隐堂为范氏西田题</a><span class='authorDate'>（1105年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31323, "北宋", "苏过", "poem_title_522681")'>苏过</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_522681_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_522681'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_522681'>范侯作园湖之隅，缭以脩竹千芙蕖。<div id='poem_sentence_0_522681_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_522681'>鸭陂下浸波澜<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>阔，箕山西指峰峦孤。<div id='poem_sentence_1_522681_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_522681'>有堂翼然照通衢，路人尚忆华严居。<div id='poem_sentence_2_522681_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_522681'>华严初来理荒废，布衣小艇披茭蒲。<div id='poem_sentence_3_522681_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_522681'>蛙鸣不知官与私，莫来乱我夜读书。<div id='poem_sentence_4_522681_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_522681'>人怀忠直及其子，遗爱何止屋上乌。<div id='poem_sentence_5_522681_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_522681'>小范更无膏粱气，闭门一味如蠹鱼。<div id='poem_sentence_6_522681_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_522681'>肯为山林独往计，且隐市朝行坦途。<div id='poem_sentence_7_522681_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_522681'>嗟我与君涉世疏，短绠汲深尔自愚。<div id='poem_sentence_8_522681_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_522681'>行歌道上惭妻孥，坐令家无甔石储。<div id='poem_sentence_9_522681_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_522681'>欲将大隐欺谁欤，人不吾以曷早图。<div id='poem_sentence_10_522681_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_522681'>未须直学西山夫，槁项终为山泽臞。<div id='poem_sentence_11_522681_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_content_522572'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_522572'>伯祖昔为郎，出乘使者轓。<div id='poem_sentence_0_522572_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_522572_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_522572'>遂使吾蜀人，不知狱吏尊。<div id='poem_sentence_3_522572_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_522572'>收拾五车书，归扫西山坟。<div id='poem_sentence_10_522572_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_522572'>平生有家学，舍鱼取熊蹯。<div id='poem_sentence_11_522572_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_522572'>况兹甘棠俗，尚怀挟纩恩。<div id='poem_sentence_12_522572_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence'
