id='poem_sentence_16_522572'></div><div id='poem_sentence_16_522572_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1106&endYear=1106')">1106年</a>　在长社。苏过有《题<阳关图>后》文。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《斜川集校注》卷八。）</span><div id='poem_1215259' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1215259' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1215259?labeling=true' target='_blank'>题阳关图后</a><span class='authorDate'>（1106年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31323, "北宋", "苏过", "poem_title_1215259")'>苏过</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1215259_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1215259'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1215259'>山林之人，能忘富贵易；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1215259_comment'></div>轩冕之士，能处枯槁难。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1215259_comment'></div>谢安雅志东山，故于富贵如脱屣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1215259_comment'></div>山、王未能忘轩冕，故不敢数于嵇、阮间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1215259_comment'></div>大抵能脱略世故，不戚戚于贫贱者，必英伟奇特人也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1215259_comment'></div>余虽不敢执鞭从浮休公游，然先子与有一日之雅，薰莸臭味，可以不言而喻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1215259_comment'></div>公之立朝，毅然有不可犯之色；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1215259_comment'></div>退藏于家，一丘一壑，有终焉之计。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1215259_comment'></div>此其中岂无所得而然哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1215259_comment'></div>公之外孙高君，尝得浮休手书《阳关图歌》一篇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1215259_comment'></div>乃使人临画李龙眠《阳关图》置其首。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1215259_comment'></div>又得长安王正叔画浮休像：幅巾野服，坐山林间，埽弃尘累，超然物表。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1215259_comment'></div>置之卷末。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1215259_comment'></div>二人真知浮休公者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1215259_comment'></div>世人徒见其功名之心，慨然未忘，而不知今之隐几，非昔之隐几者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1215259_comment'></div>余略为之一辨。</div><div id='poem_sentence_15_1215259_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1107&endYear=1107')">1107年</a>　在长社。长兄苏迈出任嘉禾令，苏过作诗送之。作品：《送伯达兄赴嘉禾》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《斜川集校注》卷三。参舒大刚、曾枣庄《宋人年谱丛刊·苏过年谱》（四川大学出版社2002年1月版）第六册第3715页。）</span><div id='poem_522612' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_522612' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/522612?labeling=true' target='_blank'>送伯达兄赴嘉禾</a><span class='authorDate'>（1107年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31323, "北宋", "苏过", "poem_title_522612")'>苏过</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_522612_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_522612'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_522612'>我生三十馀，忧患恰半生。<div id='poem_sentence_0_522612_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_522612'>飘零万里外，偶存三弟兄。<div id='poem_sentence_1_522612_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_522612'>去去复远别，朔风催客征。<div id='poem_sentence_2_522612_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_522612'>相看各华发，岂免儿女情。<div id='poem_sentence_3_522612_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_522612'>五载卧箕颍，分甘一廛氓。<div id='poem_sentence_4_522612_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_522612'>嗟哉生理拙，口腹不解营。<div id='poem_sentence_5_522612_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_522612'>各逐升斗仕，弹冠愧渊明。<div id='poem_sentence_6_522612_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_522612'>谁知三径荒，聊代十亩耕。<div id='poem_sentence_7_522612_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_522612'>我政牛马走，君乃簿书婴。<div id='poem_sentence_8_522612_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_522612'>壮心已灰槁，焦芽不复萌。<div id='poem_sentence_9_522612_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_522612'>庄舄偶怀越，嗣宗求步兵。<div id='poem_sentence_10_522612_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_522612'>行藏本无意，簪组鸿毛轻。<div id='poem_sentence_11_522612_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_522612'>脱去西风尘，江山照人清。<div id='poem_sentence_12_522612_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_522612'>扁舟五湖月，千里为莼羹。<div id='poem_sentence_13_522612_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_522612'>行著下下考，愿辞赫赫名。<div id='poem_sentence_14_522612_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_522612'>青衫道旁吏，时哉那可争。<div id='poem_sentence_15_522612_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_522612'></div><div id='poem_sentence_16_522612_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1107&endYear=1107')">1107年</a>　在长社。堂弟苏远将监汝南酒税，将之任，苏辙、苏过皆有诗送之。作品：《送八弟赴官汝南》<span </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31323, "北宋", "苏过", "poem_title_522649")'>苏过</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_522649_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_522649'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_522649'>丈夫志四方，弹冠苦不早。<div id='poem_sentence_0_522649_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_522649'>终童来请缨，贾谊试三表。<div id='poem_sentence_1_522649_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_522649'>二子俱弱冠，功名满怀抱。<div id='poem_sentence_2_522649_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_522649'>要非江湖士，未易语枯槁。<div id='poem_sentence_3_522649_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_522649'>君年逾三十，闭门事幽讨。<div id='poem_sentence_4_522649_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_522649'>父兄逼从仕，揽辔方稍稍。<div id='poem_sentence_7_522649'>白发始为郎，定似冯唐老。<div id='poem_sentence_7_522649_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_522649'>效官曲糵间，区区营一饱。<div id='poem_sentence_8_522649_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_522649'>虽知浆馈薄，要使人无保。<div id='poem_sentence_9_522649_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_522649'>淮蔡山川类，民淳足鱼稻。<div id='poem_sentence_10_522649_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_522649'>作诗慰所思，梦绕池塘草。<div class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《斜川集校注》卷六。参舒大刚、曾枣庄《宋人年谱丛刊·苏过年谱》（四川大学出版社2002年1月版）第六册第3716页。）</span>《次韵伯充咏牡丹二首》（其二）<span id='poem_title_522787_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_522787'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_522787'>珍重谁移洛下根，玉盘径尺露花新。<div id='poem_sentence_0_522787_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_522787'>不劳铅粉强为色，自是肌肤淑且真。<div id='poem_sentence_1_522787_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_522788'>愿回春色归南亩，变作秋成玉粒匀。<div id='poem_sentence_3_522788_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_522788'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_522788_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1108&endYear=1108')">1108年</a>　苏过出示当年张方平诗草，苏辙次其韵。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1108&endYear=1108')">1108年</a>　在长社。初秋，吕本中（居仁）归颍昌，夜宿范氏盘溪，作诗，苏过次韵。作品：《和吕居仁宿盘溪》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《斜川集校注》卷三。吕本中诗为《夜宿颍昌范氏水阁》，见《东莱集》）</span><div id='poem_sentence_2_522613'>申商掩仁义，已作高阁束。<div id='poem_sentence_2_522613_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_522613'>长吟失憔悴，短缀谢烦促。<div id='poem_sentence_3_522613_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_522613'>自然四壁空，惟有三冬足。<div id='poem_sentence_4_522613_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_522613'>我怀嵩少游，已办巾一幅。<div id='poem_sentence_5_522613_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_522613'>愿言山中友，先登惟子独。<div id='poem_sentence_6_522613_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_522613'>须烦悬河辩，令我千兔秃。<div id='poem_sentence_7_522613_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_522613'>归来诗满囊，大胜富润屋。<div id='poem_sentence_8_522613_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_522613'>穷通有定分，凫胫悲所续。<div id='poem_sentence_9_522613_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_522613'>一醉盘溪堂，自取君诗读。<div id='poem_sentence_10_522613_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_522613'></div><div id='poem_sentence_11_522613_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1108&endYear=1108')">1108年</a>　在长社。苏过与吕本中、韩华国、刘知命等相与约游嵩山少室，因雨，暂未成行。十天之后，雨止，遂行，至大成岗，初见嵩少，登峻极顶，俱有诗。作品：《次韵韩华国相约游嵩少》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《斜川集校注》卷三。）</span><div id='poem_522756' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_522756' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/522756?labeling=true' id='poem_title_522693_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_522693'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_522693'>王谢风流要有种，谁比君家俱得凤。<div id='poem_sentence_0_522693_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_522693'>慈明兄弟称八龙，未易贤愚推伯仲。<div id='poem_sentence_1_522693_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_522693'>胡为从事筦库役，无乃汉阴工抱瓮。<div id='poem_sentence_5_522693_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_522693'>嗟余飘泊同闾里，一味穷愁惟子共。<div id='poem_sentence_8_522693'>平生世味似嚼蜡，丘壑暮年尤自纵。<div id='poem_sentence_8_522693_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_522693'>为君悬榻待归来，故人早破邯郸梦。<div id='poem_title_522622_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_522622'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_522622'>群芳争春风，百态工妩媚。<div id='poem_content_522842'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_522842'>轩裳定浮云，于人竟何得。<div id='poem_sentence_0_522842_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_522842'>不如饱诗书，颇似勤播植。<div id='poem_sentence_1_522842_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_522842'>丰凶纵有时，穮蓑无倦色。<div id='poem_sentence_11_522842_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_522843' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_522843' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/522843?labeling=true' ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1111&endYear=1111')">1111年3月19日</a>　在长社。三月十九日，苏过与仲兄苏迨，与客人崔遐绍、赵汉英游朱园，放生，作诗。作品：《三月十九日同仲豫兄长率崔遐绍赵汉英游朱园放鱼》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《斜川集校注》卷三。）</span><div id='poem_522596' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_522596' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/522596?labeling=true' target='_blank'>三月十九日同仲豫兄长率崔遐绍赵汉英游朱园放鱼</a><span id='poem_sentence_0_522596'>何人溃溪流，忽作瓴建屋。<div id='poem_sentence_0_522596_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_522596'>不知几鱼虾，生毙此枯渎。<div id='poem_sentence_1_522596_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_522596'>纤纤跃泥沙，濡沫曾不足。<div id='poem_sentence_2_522596_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_522596'>虽求升斗活，终困蝼蚁毒。<div id='poem_sentence_3_522596_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_522596'>眷余二三子，行春访脩竹。<div id='poem_sentence_6_522596'>汲井叩邻里，捐金劝僮仆。<div id='poem_sentence_6_522596_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_522596'>好生人所欣，稚子助揽掬。<div id='poem_sentence_16_522596_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1111&endYear=1111')">1111年</a>　在长社。苏过已得太原除书。从兄苏适赴官洛阳，过以诗送之。作品：《送仲南兄赴水南仓》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《斜川集校注》卷三。）</span><div id='poem_522699' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_522699' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/522699?labeling=true' id='poem_sentence_1_522699_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_522699'>咄嗟岁晚事大缪，翻然自许林泉役。<div id='poem_sentence_2_522699_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_522699_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_522699'>丈夫升沈何足道，竭身养志真奇特。<div id='poem_sentence_5_522699_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_522699'>闭门却求文史乐，劲气岂为穷居屈。<div id='poem_sentence_6_522699_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_522699'>信哉自有绝人处，坐使懦夫闻有立。<div id='poem_sentence_7_522699_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_522699'>迩来弹冠本非好，黾俛聊从父兄迫。<div id='poem_sentence_8_522699_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_522699'>区区试吏仓庚间，定知蜡屐何曾得。<div id='poem_sentence_9_522699_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_522699'>嗟余白发亦自笑，眷眷一官乃鸡肋。<div id='poem_sentence_10_522699_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_522699'>明年驱车走太行，政坐相如空四壁。<div id='poem_sentence_11_522699_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_522699'>秋风潩水各相送，未觉轩裳胜蓬荜。<div id='poem_sentence_12_522699_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_522699'>鹪鹩傥获一枝安，此外所忧非我力。<div id='poem_sentence_13_522699_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_522699'></div><div id='poem_sentence_14_522699_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1111&endYear=1111')">1111年</a>　在长社。苏迨赴官武昌，苏过作叙送之。作品：《送仲豫兄赴官武昌叙》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《斜川集校注》卷八。参舒大刚、曾枣庄《宋人年谱丛刊·苏过年谱》（四川大学出版社2002年1月版）第六册第3723页。苏迨时赴任武昌筦库官。）</span><div id='poem_1215249' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1215249' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1215249?labeling=true' target='_blank'>送仲豫兄赴官武昌叙</a><span class='authorDate'>（政和元年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31323, "北宋", "苏过", "poem_title_1215249")'>苏过</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1215249_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1215249'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1215249'>某生最后，不及见先君少时行事也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1215249_comment'></div>比成人，能区别，则先君历清华、典方面，既贵矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1215249_comment'></div>然窃观其退居于家，藐然陋巷，布衣粝食，寒士有所不能堪，而先君安焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1215249_comment'></div>故能糠秕富贵，而不少贬于流落。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1215249_comment'></div>所谓季文子相三君，家无衣帛之妾，厩无食粟之马，殆类是矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1215249_comment'></div>子孙虽不能髣髴其万一，然清介廉苦之风，抑有类焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1215249_comment'></div>故吾长兄年五十有三，不能俯仰于人，犹为州县吏；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1215249_comment'></div>仲兄少不乐仕进，亲戚强之，今四十有二，始为筦库官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1215249_comment'></div>又飘然远游江湖千里之外，此其中必有遗世故而轻外物者矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1215249_comment'></div>且平居里巷间，士大夫以门阀相高，炫服车马相誇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1215249_comment'></div>则吾兄敝衣缊袍，刓去圭角，乘款段马，衣野人服，与方外之士杂居而无辨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1215249_comment'></div>此得于先君子清介廉苦之风为多，余不及也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1215249_comment'></div>夫约于奉己，则求于人也薄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1215249_comment'></div>故虽小官，恬然而往。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1215249_comment'></div>进不希当世之用，退不谋三径之资。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1215249_comment'></div>则出处之间，无累于物，岂不超然自得于方寸乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1215249_comment'></div>武昌与黄冈对垒，特限一大江耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1215249_comment'></div>顷侍先君杖履往来于樊口甚数。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1215249_comment'></div>今三十年，江山宛然，而吾曹齿发如此，得不为之太息乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1215249_comment'></div>昔人感髀肉生而有功名未遂之叹，吾曹则不然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1215249_comment'></div>白首折腰，当念蚤为求田问舍之策。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1215249_comment'></div>及瓜而归，徜徉嵩少之下，以毕吾兄弟晚岁之乐，又奚恤元龙所笑哉！</div><div id='poem_sentence_21_1215249_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1111&endYear=1111')">1111年10月29日</a>　在长社。十月二十九日，雨雪，苏辙作诗咏雪，苏过次韵。作品：《次韵叔父小雪二首》（其一）<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《斜川集校注》卷三。苏辙诗为《十月二十九日雪四首》，见《栾城集·栾城第三集》卷三。）</span>《次韵叔父小雪二首》（其二）<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《斜川集校注》卷三。）</span><div id='poem_522741' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_522741' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/522741?labeling=true' target='_blank'>次韵叔父小雪二首<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1111年10月29日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31323, "北宋", "苏过", "poem_title_522741")'>苏过</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_522741_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_522741'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_522741'>屏帷夜久灰残兽，纸帐寒惊月在窗。<div id='poem_sentence_0_522741_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_522741'>似听竹声知有雪，便添酒兴欲倾缸。<div id='poem_sentence_1_522741_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_522741'>西邻正想蒲团稳，古殿遥瞻老柏双。<div id='poem_sentence_2_522741_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_522741'>自笑穷愁拙生理，不谋升斗待西江。<div id='poem_sentence_3_522741_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_522741'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_522741_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_522742' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_522742' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/522742?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1111年10月29日）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_522742_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_522742'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_522742'>夜来小雪犹凝地，睡起扶桑已著窗。<div id='poem_sentence_0_522742_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_522742'>却喜少陵时炙背，不忧北海屡空缸。<div id='poem_sentence_1_522742_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_522742'>丰年何时豚蹄祝，薄淖聊烦蜡屐双。<div id='poem_sentence_2_522742_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_522742'>试走湖边望嵩少，殆如叠嶂在烟江。<div id='poem_sentence_3_522742_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_522742'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_522742_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1111&endYear=1111')">1111年</a>　在长社。苏迈、苏迨、苏过编苏轼遗墨，成《先公手泽》。过有《书先公字后》，当作于前后。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《斜川集校注》卷八。参舒大刚、曾枣庄《宋人年谱丛刊·苏过年谱》（四川大学出版社2002年1月版）第六册第3724页。《先公手泽》，即《东坡志林》）</span><div id='poem_1215256' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1215256' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1215256?labeling=true' target='_blank'>书先公字后</a><span class='authorDate'>（1111年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31323, "北宋", "苏过", "poem_title_1215256")'>苏过</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1215256_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1215256'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1215256'>吾先君子，岂以书自名哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1215256_comment'></div>特以其至大至刚之气，发于胸中而应之于手，故不见其有刻画妩媚之工，而端章甫，若有不可犯之色。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1215256_comment'></div>知此然后可以知其书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1215256_comment'></div>然其少年喜二王书，晚乃喜颜平原，故时有二家风气。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1215256_comment'></div>俗子初不知，妄谓学徐浩，陋矣！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1215256_comment'></div>公之书，如有道之士，隐显不足以议其荣辱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1215256_comment'></div>昔之人有欲挤之于渊，则此书隐；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1215256_comment'></div>今之人以此书为进取资，则风俗靡然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1215256_comment'></div>争以多藏为誇，而逐利之夫，临摹百出，朱紫相乱，十七八矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1215256_comment'></div>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1215256_comment'></div>此皆书之不幸也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1215256_comment'></div>阳春白雪之歌出，岂容闾巷小人皆好哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1215256_comment'></div>虽然，无知者役于名，以伪为真，不足责。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1215256_comment'></div>至搢绅士大夫家为世所欺，可为太息。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1215256_comment'></div>而又有妄庸者居其间，自谓能是正其非，倔强大言，反以真为伪，其无知则一也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1215256_comment'></div>而使此书或至与玉石俱焚，是重不幸也！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1215256_comment'></div>过侍先君居夷七年，所得遗编断简皆老年字，落其华而成其实，如太羹玄酒，朱弦疏越，将取悦于妇人女子，难矣哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1215256_comment'></div>世方一律，殆未可言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1215256_comment'></div>且非独书也，斯文亦然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1215256_comment'></div>公昔为《藏经记》，初传于世，或以为非公作，其后知之者以为神奇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1215256_comment'></div>在惠州作《梅花诗》，有以为非，至有以为笑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1215256_comment'></div>此皆士大夫閒以文鸣者，其说能使人必信，其谬妄如此，乃知识《古战场文》者鲜矣，可为流俗痛哭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1215256_comment'></div>过谨书，藏于家。</div><div id='poem_sentence_22_1215256_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1111&endYear=1111')">1111年</a>　苏过编定《东坡后集》。考定东坡诗集误字。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1112&endYear=1112')">1112年2月20日</a>　在长社。二月二十日，苏辙生日，苏过作诗为庆。作品：《叔父生日》（其一）<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《斜川集校注》卷三。《斜川集校注》有（一）同题诗二首，此为其中一首，首句为“百川赴东海”）</span>《叔父生日》（其二）<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《斜川集校注》卷三。《斜川集校注》有（二）同题诗二首，此为其中一首，首句为“沟渎嗟寻常”）</span>《叔父生日》（其三）<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《斜川集校注》卷三。《斜川集校注》有（三）同题诗二首，此为其中一首，首句为“郁郁涧底松”）</span>《叔父生日》（其四）<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《斜川集校注》卷三。《斜川集校注》有（四）同题诗二首，此为其中一首，首句为“物居覆载间”）</span><div id='poem_522652' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_522652' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/522652?labeling=true' target='_blank'>叔父生日<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1112年2月20日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31323, "北宋", "苏过", "poem_title_522652")'>苏过</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_522652_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_522652'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_522652'>百川赴东海，如走万国朝。<div id='poem_sentence_0_522652_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_522652'>横岫列嵩岱，众山失岧峣。<div id='poem_sentence_1_522652_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_522652'>吾道岂不尊，凛然干云霄。<div id='poem_sentence_2_522652_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_522652'>斯文有盟主，坐制狂澜漂。<div id='poem_sentence_3_522652_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_522652'>天实相我公，高卧不知<span class='inlineComment2'>（清旧抄本作可）</span>招。<div id='poem_sentence_4_522652_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_522652'>手持文章柄，烂若北斗标。<div id='poem_sentence_5_522652_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_522652'>末学病多歧，寝令世俗浇。<div id='poem_sentence_6_522652_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_522652'>申商日充塞，仁义愈寂寥。<div id='poem_sentence_7_522652_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_522652'>造物真有意，俾公以后凋。<div id='poem_sentence_8_522652_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_522652'>群邪终放郑，正始会闻韶。<div id='poem_sentence_9_522652_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_522652'>过也匪私祝，彼苍自昭昭。<div id='poem_sentence_10_522652_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_522652'>后生方有托，未用忧箪瓢。<div id='poem_sentence_11_522652_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_522652'></div><div id='poem_sentence_12_522652_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_522653' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_522653' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/522653?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1112年2月20日）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_522653_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_522653'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_522653'>沟渎嗟寻常，固为吞舟厄。<div id='poem_sentence_0_522653_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_522653'>风无九万里，焉载垂天翼。<div id='poem_sentence_1_522653_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_522653'>老人卧箕颍，初非厌簪绂。<div id='poem_sentence_2_522653_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_522653'>时哉莫吾容，道大俗隘迫。<div id='poem_sentence_3_522653_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_522653'>虎兕歌旷野，鸾凤栖枳棘。<div id='poem_sentence_4_522653_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_522653'>苍生谩怅望，吾道何欣戚。<div id='poem_sentence_5_522653_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_522653'>卜筑殆将隐，门无翟公客。<div id='poem_sentence_6_522653_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_522653'>高踪蹑巢由，援手谢卨稷。<div id='poem_sentence_7_522653_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_522653'>我观造物意，申甫为时出。<div id='poem_sentence_8_522653_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_522653'>未应兹伟人，独不裨衮职。<div id='poem_sentence_9_522653_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_522653'>功名世所趋，富贵亦过隙。<div id='poem_sentence_10_522653_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_522653'>岂知难老福，天以寿有德。<div id='poem_sentence_11_522653_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_522653'>亭亭南涧松，不羡栋梁索。<div id='poem_sentence_12_522653_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_522653'>方兹阅寒暑，宁欲顾匠石。<div id='poem_sentence_13_522653_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_522653'>世间出世间，此得无两得。<div id='poem_sentence_14_522653_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_522653'>回首承明庐，摩挲看铜狄。<div id='poem_sentence_15_522653_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_522653'></div><div id='poem_sentence_16_522653_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_522654' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_522654' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/522654?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其三 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1112年2月20日）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_522654_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_522654'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_522654'>郁郁涧底松，千年养奇干。<div id='poem_sentence_0_522654_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_522654'>盘根入窈窕，翠盖摩霄汉。<div id='poem_sentence_1_522654_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_522654'>岩深饱霜雪，路绝窥轮奂。<div id='poem_sentence_2_522654_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_522654'>空回牛刀手，屡发匠石叹。<div id='poem_sentence_3_522654_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_522654'>物生非不逢，得天地所赞。<div id='poem_sentence_4_522654_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_522654'>虽微栋梁求，幸免斤斧难。<div id='poem_sentence_5_522654_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_522654'>我公庙堂人，端委四夷惮。<div id='poem_sentence_6_522654_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_522654'>岂惟福苍生，高风激贪懦。<div id='poem_sentence_7_522654_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_522654'>云何卧箕颍，当宁方宵旰。<div id='poem_sentence_8_522654_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_522654'>吾道久寂寥，贤愚良未判。<div id='poem_sentence_9_522654_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_522654'>汗颜与血指，袖手宁坐看。<div id='poem_sentence_10_522654_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_522654'>卷怀霖雨心，警策露电观。<div id='poem_sentence_11_522654_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_522654'>形神妙自契，眉目光璀璨。<div id='poem_sentence_12_522654_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_522654'>长松信可倚，柯叶四时贯。<div id='poem_sentence_13_522654_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_522654'>东风漫滋荣，寒雨徒零乱。<div id='poem_sentence_14_522654_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_522654'>何异楚灵椿，春秋安可算。<div id='poem_sentence_15_522654_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_522654'></div><div id='poem_sentence_16_522654_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_522655' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_522655' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/522655?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其四 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1112年2月20日）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_522655_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_522655'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_522655'>物居覆载间，阴阳为盛衰。<div id='poem_sentence_0_522655_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_522655'>我观众草木，春风不相遗。<div id='poem_sentence_1_522655_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_522655'>春风暂能荣，还有摇落时。<div id='poem_sentence_2_522655_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_522655'>区区诿消长，岁月胡能支。<div id='poem_sentence_3_522655_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_522655'>世人如草木，世态岂异兹。<div id='poem_sentence_4_522655_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_522655_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_522655'>可怜千金躯，坐困毫与釐。<div id='poem_sentence_7_522655_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_522655'>大哉孔孟志，夫子真能师。<div id='poem_sentence_8_522655_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_522655'>浩然刚在气，直养充四维。<div id='poem_sentence_9_522655_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_522655'>贫富未易动，寒暑何从窥。<div id='poem_sentence_10_522655_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_522655'>塞马无倚伏，昭琴谢成亏。<div id='poem_sentence_11_522655_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_522655'>还观傥来物，造物戏小儿。<div id='poem_sentence_12_522655_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_522655'>臞仙事吐纳，阅世犹有之。<div id='poem_sentence_13_522655_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1112&endYear=1112')">1112年</a>　在长社。居颍期间，苏过尚有《颜乐堂》诗。又有《谢公定以所藏文与可诗示其孙骥骥有诗次韵》一诗。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《斜川集校注》卷三。）</span>《谢公定以所藏文与可诗示其孙骥骥有诗次韵》<span id='poem_sentence_0_522559'>恨无阿堵君，一区今尚欠。<div id='poem_sentence_0_522559_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_522559'>且谋蔽风雨，拔草聊自苫。<div id='poem_sentence_1_522559_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_522559'>低深人易安，俭陋鬼不瞰。<div id='poem_sentence_2_522559_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_522559'>宁辞力少劳，还视家无甔。<div id='poem_sentence_3_522559_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_522559'>从来生理拙，况此岁屡歉。<div id='poem_sentence_4_522559_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_522559'>故将箪瓢心，聊作粱肉砭。<div id='poem_sentence_5_522559_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_522559'>堂前有甘井，汲取良未厌。<div id='poem_sentence_6_522559_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_522559'>堂后有药苗，一饱亦可暂。<div id='poem_sentence_7_522559_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_522559'>胡为不欢乐，何事贫忧谄。<div id='poem_sentence_8_522559_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' target='_blank'>次韵曲水泛舟四首<span class='inlineComment2'>（曲水贾文元公园）</span><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1112年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31323, "北宋", "苏过", "poem_title_522659")'>苏过</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_522659_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_522659'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_522659'>节物自催迫，意闲欢有馀。<div id='poem_sentence_0_522659_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_522659'>驾言二三子，往寻隐者居。<div id='poem_sentence_1_522659_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_522659'>城隅有乔木，人言于公闾。<div id='poem_sentence_2_522659_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_522659'>当时乞身归，买田将结庐。<div id='poem_sentence_3_522659_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_522659'>悲哉丝竹地，今为狐兔墟。<div id='poem_sentence_4_522659_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_522661_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_522661'>稍令催科帖，迤逦不到门。<div id='poem_sentence_1_522661_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_522661'>我有贤太守，手抚疮痍痕。<div id='poem_sentence_2_522661_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_522661'>未遽舍我去，寿公福祉繁。<div id='poem_sentence_3_522661_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_522661'>一饱诚难得，敢忘肉骨恩。<div id='poem_sentence_4_522661_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_title_522662_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_522662'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_522662'>性不事轩冕，敢从公卿游。<div id='poem_sentence_0_522662_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_522662'>田歌扣牛角，谁意乐府求。<div id='poem_sentence_1_522662_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_title_522558_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_522558'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_522558'>江湖半此生，老去徒见画。<div id='poem_sentence_0_522558_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_522558'>看山眼已足，涉险梦犹怕。<div id='poem_sentence_1_522558_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_522558'>老燕久黄壤，遗墨独未化。<div id='poem_sentence_2_522558_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_522558'>胸中有丘壑，故遣意匠写。<div id='poem_sentence_3_522558_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_522558'>会逢知音人，契此笔端话。<div id='poem_sentence_4_522558_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_522558_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1112&endYear=1112')">1112年</a>　在长社。蜀僧世鹏经许游嵩少，苏过作诗赠行。作品：《送乡僧世鹏游嵩少》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《斜川集校注》卷三。）</span><div id='poem_522657' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_522657' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/522657?labeling=true' target='_blank'>送乡僧世鹏游嵩少</a><span class='authorDate'>（1112年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31323, "北宋", "苏过", "poem_title_522657")'>苏过</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_522657_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_522657'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_522657'>吾蜀士尚气，凭陵以相高。<div id='poem_sentence_0_522657_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_522657'>傥无胜己友，便绝平生交。<div id='poem_sentence_1_522657_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_522657'>诗书将吾军，道艺恃所操。<div id='poem_sentence_2_522657_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_522657'>宁甘毙百战，讵肯挫一毫。<div id='poem_sentence_3_522657_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_522657'>气俗未易改，波澜到方袍。<div id='poem_sentence_4_522657_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_522657'>世鹏此其流，何止事风骚。<div id='poem_sentence_5_522657_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_522657'>我观浮屠法，成佛须我曹。<div id='poem_sentence_6_522657_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_522657'>荣枯寄梦幻，生死真鸿毛。<div id='poem_sentence_7_522657_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_522657'>恨子太孤直，崭然出蓬蒿。<div id='poem_sentence_8_522657_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_522657'>须防斤斧厄，且为声名逃。<div id='poem_sentence_9_522657_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_522657'>空山人迹少，晏坐狐狸嗥。<div id='poem_sentence_10_522657_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_522657'>三年再见子，庶其免风涛。<div id='poem_sentence_11_522657_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_522657'></div><div id='poem_sentence_12_522657_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1112&endYear=1112')">1112年</a>　在长社。蜀人杨氏芝生其墓，苏过为作记。作品：《芝堂记》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《斜川集校注》卷一〇。此文具体作时不详，姑系于此。）</span><div id='poem_1215270' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1215270' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1215270?labeling=true' target='_blank'>芝堂记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1112年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31323, "北宋", "苏过", "poem_title_1215270")'>苏过</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1215270_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1215270'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1215270'>芝之为祥草，尚矣！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1215270_comment'></div>以其兆和气而生，非封植而成，阴阳不得宰其功，雨露无所施其力，不蘖不芽，乃茎乃叶，异夫群草木，此其可贵也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1215270_comment'></div>古之君子，盖尝有感于斯，曰：「采三秀于山间」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1215270_comment'></div>非有道之士，孰可以况此！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1215270_comment'></div>神仙服饵，以五芝为长年不死之药。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1215270_comment'></div>汉以斋房九茎荐于郊庙，是以瑞名之也哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1215270_comment'></div>吾蜀有布衣杨公亮，家世好善，闻于乡里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1215270_comment'></div>为药肆以自给，不取赢馀，贫者赖之以生，不可胜计。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1215270_comment'></div>有子曰会，亦以孝谨称。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1215270_comment'></div>葬亲之三年，事死如生，朝夕必临，时物必荐，家事必告。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1215270_comment'></div>芝生其墓，或采以献。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1215270_comment'></div>乡人惊异之，曰：「此杨氏父子为善之报，彼愚夫，不知其为祥也而暴之」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1215270_comment'></div>亟往观其处，祝之使复生，已而果然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1215270_comment'></div>未几，僮仆又取以献，众大嗟惜，意其不复出矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1215270_comment'></div>不逾月，芝生如故，乡人然后知杨氏父子行必有稽于神明，何其响应弗渝，而申告者三也！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1215270_comment'></div>或曰：「为善者必有报，造物者既知之矣，胡不大其门而昌其身，而独锡之以芝也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1215270_comment'></div>寒不可以衣，饥不可以食」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1215270_comment'></div>余曰：「不然，天人之际，必谆谆然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1215270_comment'></div>表杨氏之德出于一乡，一乡之人有惩恶劝善者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1215270_comment'></div>自乡党以及州闾，推而至于四方，相勉为杨氏子，而耻其不及，其为瑞也丰矣！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1215270_comment'></div>故子皋为成宰，而成人笃其兄；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1215270_comment'></div>颍谷封人食舍肉，而庄公施其母。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1215270_comment'></div>《诗》所谓『孝子不匮，永锡尔类』，岂不谆谆然命之乎」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1215270_comment'></div>杨氏筑堂以旌之，且属里人苏某记其事，将刻石以告来者，故乐为书之。</div><div id='poem_sentence_23_1215270_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1112&endYear=1112')">1112年</a>　在长社。李文儒赴汉东教授，苏过作诗为送。作品：《送李文儒赴汉东教授》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《斜川集校注》卷三。）</span><div id='poem_522822' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_522822' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/522822?labeling=true' target='_blank'>送李文儒赴汉东教授</a><span class='authorDate'>（1112年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31323, "北宋", "苏过", "poem_title_522822")'>苏过</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_522822_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_522822'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_522822'>自欲担簦拾紫朱，谁能碌碌守吾庐。<div id='poem_sentence_0_522822_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_522822'>割鲜固已夸多获，贾勇今将试有馀。<div id='poem_sentence_1_522822_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_522822'>环堵未成三径业，束装惟载五车书。<div id='poem_sentence_2_522822_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_522822'>要令洙泗行江汉，归伴诸儒校石渠。<div id='poem_sentence_3_522822_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_522822'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_522822_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1112&endYear=1112')">1112年</a>　在长社。岑氏筑心远亭，苏过题诗。作品：《题岑氏心远亭》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《斜川集校注》卷三。岑氏，名、字未详。或即苏过之姻亲眉山人岑彦休。）</span><div id='poem_522697' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_522697' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/522697?labeling=true' target='_blank'>题岑氏心远亭</a><span class='authorDate'>（1112年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31323, "北宋", "苏过", "poem_title_522697")'>苏过</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_522697_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_522697'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_522697'>君不见郑崇门前闹如市，此心不碍如秋水。<div id='poem_sentence_0_522697_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_522697'>又不见翟公之门空设罗，翻为交情生愠喜。<div id='poem_sentence_1_522697_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_522697'>岂知靖节弃官归，五斗难堪折腰耻。<div id='poem_sentence_2_522697_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_522697'>结庐何必在山泽，方寸湛然遗远迩。<div id='poem_sentence_3_522697_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_522697'>君家小园才数亩，竹柏萧森间桃李。<div id='poem_sentence_4_522697_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_522697'>幽亭容膝审易安，不羡华堂失梓杞。<div id='poem_sentence_5_522697_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_522697'>平生少游真吾师，自欲浮沈老闾里。<div id='poem_sentence_6_522697_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_522697'>故应从事三径乐，更效子綦今隐几。<div id='poem_sentence_7_522697_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_522697'>君看六凿无天游，妇姑攘夺无穷已。<div id='poem_sentence_8_522697_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_522697'>远人无累超物表，云梦胸中吞芥子。<div id='poem_sentence_9_522697_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_522697'>纷纷朝市我无与，毂击肩摩同一轨。<div id='poem_sentence_10_522697_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_522697'>高情缥缈谢尘寰，怅望云山友黄绮。<div id='poem_sentence_11_522697_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_522697'></div><div id='poem_sentence_12_522697_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1112&endYear=1112')">1112年</a>　在长社。杭僧从信自浙经颍入都，访苏过。过作诗赠之，且招老友杭僧思聪。作品：《赠诗僧从信》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《斜川集校注》卷三。）</span><div id='poem_522656' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_522656' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/522656?labeling=true' target='_blank'>赠诗僧从信<span class='inlineComment2'>（信学诗于参寥）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1112年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31323, "北宋", "苏过", "poem_title_522656")'>苏过</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_522656_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_522656'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_522656'>吴山翠如蓝，越水碧如铜。<div id='poem_sentence_0_522656_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_522656'>山川吐奇秀，儒释俱争锋。<div id='poem_sentence_1_522656_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_522656'>接迹有禅老，提纲古宗风。<div id='poem_sentence_2_522656_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_522656'>其馀将诗律，岛可不足攻。<div id='poem_sentence_3_522656_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_522656'>我久客尘土，虽穷诗未工。<div id='poem_sentence_4_522656_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_522656'>要知笔砚废，似缺山水供。<div id='poem_sentence_5_522656_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_522656'>上人三吴来，句法乃有从。<div id='poem_sentence_6_522656_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_522656'>老潜已黄壤，弟子传清雄。<div id='poem_sentence_7_522656_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_522656'>益复访云水，高情谢樊笼。<div id='poem_sentence_8_522656_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_522656'>试草北山移，为我招琴聪<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_9_522656_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_522656'></div><div id='poem_sentence_10_522656_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_522656'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_9_522656_0'>⑴ 自注：钱塘琴僧思聪亦妙于诗文，久游京师不归。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_522656_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1112&endYear=1112')">1112年6月</a>　六月下旬，苏过出监太原府税。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='3d4233a48efe4033bbb3a815e49a0011_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("3d4233a48efe4033bbb3a815e49a0011");'><span id='3d4233a48efe4033bbb3a815e49a0011_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1112&endYear=1112')">1112年</a>，41岁</div><div id='3d4233a48efe4033bbb3a815e49a0011' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1112&endYear=1112')">1112年</a>　在长社，监太原府税任上。苏过作祭叔父苏辙文。作品：《祭叔父黄门文》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《斜川集校注》卷八。）</span><div id='poem_1215282' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1215282' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1215282?labeling=true' target='_blank'>祭叔父黄门文</a><span class='authorDate'>（1112年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31323, "北宋", "苏过", "poem_title_1215282")'>苏过</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1215282_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1215282'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1215282'>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1215282_comment'></div>天无意于世乎，曷为畀之于人？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1215282_comment'></div>夫既畀之而又夺之，理何疑于大钧？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1215282_comment'></div>昔者仲尼、孟轲周流天下，皇皇乎求君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1215282_comment'></div>盖欲拯生民于涂炭，救将丧之斯文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1215282_comment'></div>然身卒困于逆旅，志壹郁而莫信。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1215282_comment'></div>岂道大不容于世也，抑天未欲平治于斯民？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1215282_comment'></div>乌乎哀哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1215282_comment'></div>维我王父皇考，以及叔父。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1215282_comment'></div>天祚有宋，笃生良臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1215282_comment'></div>祖尧禹而陋秦汉，谈王道于一门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1215282_comment'></div>公之在庙堂也，则壬人废而蛮夷服，礼乐正而朝廷尊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1215282_comment'></div>排申、商之充塞，非仁义而莫陈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1215282_comment'></div>庶几乎虞、夏之风，反朴而还淳矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1215282_comment'></div>属世故之迫隘，乃一莸而一薰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1215282_comment'></div>横江潭之鳣鲔，岂沟渎之容身？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1215282_comment'></div>竟中道而出走，罹此邮之纷纷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1215282_comment'></div>然公之脱身南荒而归也，则澹然箕山之下，潩水之滨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1215282_comment'></div>友巢、由于千载，追松、乔于白云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1215282_comment'></div>盖与世而相忘，默渊潜而自珍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1215282_comment'></div>托《春秋》以见志，戮奸宄于灰尘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1215282_comment'></div>公虽不用也，而天下愈尊之如泰山，归之如凤麟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1215282_comment'></div>意造物之有待，使岿然而独存。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1215282_comment'></div>忽山颓而梁坏，何苍苍之不仁！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1215282_comment'></div>岂吾宗之不祐，天实祸于搢绅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1215282_comment'></div>过也昔孤，而归公于许，奉杖屦者十春。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1215282_comment'></div>维二父之笃爱，推其馀于子孙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1215282_comment'></div>痛里门之一诀，哭来讣于并汾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1215282_comment'></div>恨易箦之不见，犹及拜其冠巾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1215282_comment'></div>恍高堂其如在，疑謦咳之或闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1215282_comment'></div>誓不辱于教诲，期可见于九原。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1215282_comment'></div>倾一奠而永已，不得执绋挽公之归葬于西岷也。</div><div id='poem_sentence_31_1215282_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='da6a22b1611f496295aaca2222da3225_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("da6a22b1611f496295aaca2222da3225");'><span id='da6a22b1611f496295aaca2222da3225_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1115&endYear=1115')">1115年</a>，44岁</div><div id='da6a22b1611f496295aaca2222da3225' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1115&endYear=1115')">1115年</a>　在长社。苏过归颍，卜筑于城南，兄弟甥侄有诗为庆，作诗酬答。作品：《卜居城南二首酬兄弟甥侄》（其一）<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《斜川集校注》卷五。）</span>《卜居城南二首酬兄弟甥侄》（其二）<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《斜川集校注》卷五。）</span><div id='poem_522792' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_522792' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/522792?labeling=true' target='_blank'>卜居城南二首酬兄弟甥侄<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1115年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31323, "北宋", "苏过", "poem_title_522792")'>苏过</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_522792_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_522792'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_522792'>萧萧素发插人头，世上功名得汝求。<div id='poem_sentence_0_522792_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_522792'>神马尻舆安所税，寸田尺宅早归休。<div id='poem_sentence_1_522792_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_522792'>结茅但使才容膝，解剑还须便买牛。<div id='poem_sentence_2_522792_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_522792'>更慕少游乘下泽，不妨闾里自沈浮。<div id='poem_sentence_3_522792_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_522792'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_522792_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_522793' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_522793' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a id='poem_title_522793_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_522793'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_522793'>采椽竹屋亦天真，但喜相望北阮邻。<div id='poem_sentence_0_522793_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_522793'>等是南柯游此世，聊将传舍诳吾身。<div id='poem_sentence_1_522793_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_522727_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_522727'>平畴烟漠漠，野水碧粼粼。<div id='poem_sentence_1_522727_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_522727'>挂剑嗟吾晚，悬车叹汝伸。<div id='poem_sentence_2_522727_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_522727'>西州不忍过，朱户锁埃尘。<div class='authorDate'>（1115年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_522728_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_522728'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_522728_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_522728'>披句空遗恨，沾衣想自频。<div id='poem_sentence_2_522728_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_522728'>睹公怜友作，拟德定其伦。<div id='poem_sentence_3_522728_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_522728'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_522728_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_522729' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_522729' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/522729?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其三 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1115年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_522729_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_522729'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_522729'>引退元非病，归田却患贫。<div id='poem_sentence_0_522729_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_522729'>躬耕聊自给，知命敢言屯。<div id='poem_sentence_1_522729_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_522729'>好客还师郑，多金不羡秦。<div ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1115&endYear=1115')">1115年</a>　在长社。苏过迁居城南，与王实、史得之诸人唱酬。作品：《次韵王仲弓赠史得之》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《斜川集校注》卷五。）</span>《和王仲弓雪中怀友之什》（其一）<span showDetail'><a href='/Writing/522610?labeling=true' target='_blank'>次韵王仲弓赠史得之</a><span class='authorDate'>（1115年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a class='poemContent' id='poem_content_522610'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_522610'>春风回东皋，春雨湿田舍。<div id='poem_sentence_0_522610_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_522610'>芒鞋问脩竹，小圃条疏柘。<div id='poem_sentence_1_522610_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_522610'>史侯得此趣，十年官早谢。<div id='poem_sentence_2_522610_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_522610'>定知猿鹤怨，衣绣空行夜。<div id='poem_sentence_3_522610_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_522610'>世无摩诘手，谁见辋川画。<div id='poem_sentence_4_522610_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_522610'>且复浮沉游，款段聊叱咤。<div id='poem_sentence_5_522610_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_522610'></div><div id='poem_sentence_6_522610_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_522568' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_522568' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/522568?labeling=true' target='_blank'>和王仲弓雪中怀友之什<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1115年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31323, "北宋", "苏过", "poem_title_522568")'>苏过</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_522568_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_522568'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_522568'>出门无所之，怀刺名欲灭。<div id='poem_sentence_0_522568_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_522568'>要求我辈人，庶缓礼法设。<div id='poem_sentence_1_522568_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_522568'>城南有胜士，块坐方禅悦。<div id='poem_sentence_2_522568_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_522568'>不嫌来往频，相对餐毡雪。<div id='poem_sentence_3_522568_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_522568'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_522568_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_522569' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_522569' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/522569?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1115年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_522569_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_522569'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_522569'>我非淳于狂，君勿怖烛灭。<div id='poem_sentence_0_522569_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_522569'>时能啜少醴，谁为穆生设。<div id='poem_sentence_1_522569_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_522569'>明窗坐弈棋，聊以寄怡悦。<div id='poem_sentence_2_522569_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_522569'>胜固无所争，败亦何足雪。<div id='poem_sentence_3_522569_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_522569'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_522569_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1115&endYear=1115')">1115年</a>　在长社。芜湖人韦许筑室曰“独乐”，常安民（希古）赋诗，属苏过同赋寄之。作品：《湖阴有隐君子作轩曰独乐乡人常希古为赋诗属予同作寄之》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《斜川集校注》卷五。）</span><div id='poem_522581' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_522581' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/522581?labeling=true' target='_blank'>湖阴有隐君子作轩曰独乐乡人常希古为赋诗属予同作寄之</a><span class='authorDate'>（1115年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31323, "北宋", "苏过", "poem_title_522581")'>苏过</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_522581_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_522581'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_522581'>吾闻颜氏子，箪瓢欢有馀。<div id='poem_sentence_0_522581_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_522581'>不知外慕乐，服膺在诗书。<div id='poem_sentence_1_522581_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_522581'>君看轩冕荣，其辱与之俱。<div id='poem_sentence_2_522581_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_522581'>斯由<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>岂不遂，上蔡曾弗如。<div id='poem_sentence_3_522581_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_522581'>倚伏无已时，循环共一涂。<div id='poem_sentence_4_522581_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_522581'>贤愚但相笑，莫知改前车。<div id='poem_sentence_5_522581_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_522581'>嗟我晚闻道，一官真蘧庐。<div id='poem_sentence_6_522581_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_522581'>得之不为喜，失之分所无。<div id='poem_sentence_7_522581_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_522581'>尘垢未忘扫，冰炭久已除。<div id='poem_sentence_8_522581_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_522581'>萧然百忧释，梦觉两于于。<div id='poem_sentence_9_522581_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_522581'>江南有高士，以乐名其居。<div id='poem_sentence_10_522581_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_522581'>嗜不同众好，德则良不孤。<div id='poem_sentence_11_522581_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_522581'>磨铅事简策，校雠独勤劬。<div id='poem_sentence_12_522581_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_522581'>持此返退藏，不愿拾紫朱。<div id='poem_sentence_13_522581_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_522581'>黄卷有晤语，舍兹无与娱。<div id='poem_sentence_14_522581_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_522581'>安得乘扁舟，访君在五湖。<div id='poem_sentence_15_522581_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_522581'></div><div id='poem_sentence_16_522581_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_522581'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_3_522581_0'>⑴ 原作游，据赵本改。由乃李斯之</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_522581_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1115&endYear=1115')">1115年</a>　在长社。河东提刑崔钧降官，苏过代作谢表。作品：《代崔宪谢降官表》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《斜川集校注》卷八。）</span><div id='poem_1215221' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1215221' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1215221?labeling=true' target='_blank'>代崔宪谢降官表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1115年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31323, "北宋", "苏过", "poem_title_1215221")'>苏过</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1215221_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1215221'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1215221'>缪于刺举，以干越职之诛；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1215221_comment'></div>尚赖宽仁，止就削官之罚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1215221_comment'></div>恩深责薄，感激涕零。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1215221_comment'></div>伏念臣赋性颛愚，逢时休盛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1215221_comment'></div>虽屡膺于指使，终无补于涓埃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1215221_comment'></div>惟恐有闻，欲效鹰鹯之志；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1215221_comment'></div>自贻伊戚，不虞尸祝之讥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1215221_comment'></div>果蒙定罪以原情，聊示小惩而大戒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1215221_comment'></div>仰天知惠，抚己怀惭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1215221_comment'></div>此盖伏遇皇帝陛下躬若稽古之明，行不忍人之政。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1215221_comment'></div>祖成汤之三面，达虞舜之四聪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1215221_comment'></div>吏议难逃，盖自不安于分守；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1215221_comment'></div>天心灼见，犹许改过于将来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1215221_comment'></div>臣敢不奉以周旋，永知教戒！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1215221_comment'></div>服勤官政，期收薄效于桑榆；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1215221_comment'></div>铭刻肌肤，莫报大恩于天地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1215221_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_16_1215221_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1115&endYear=1115')">1115年8月17日</a>　在长社。七月十四日，崔钧卒。八月十七日葬，苏过作行状。作品：《河东提刑崔公行状》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《斜川集校注》卷八。）</span><div id='poem_1215276' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1215276' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1215276?labeling=true' target='_blank'>河东提刑崔公行状</a><span class='authorDate'>（政和五年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31323, "北宋", "苏过", "poem_title_1215276")'>苏过</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1215276_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1215276'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1215276'>曾祖讳裔，故赠工部侍郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1215276_comment'></div>祖讳峄，故任刑部侍郎，赠特进。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1215276_comment'></div>考讳度，故任朝散大夫，累赠宣奉大夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1215276_comment'></div>公讳钧，字元播，姓崔氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1215276_comment'></div>系出于魏相琰，至唐世有显人，为天下望族。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1215276_comment'></div>其先占籍光州，徙居开封，不知所从来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1215276_comment'></div>自特进公帅庆阳，乃家于雍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1215276_comment'></div>公以特进公荫授将仕郎，守将作监主簿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1215276_comment'></div>初任泾州酒税，积官至朝散大夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1215276_comment'></div>自泾州酒税，历迁知凤翔之扶风、瀛州之河间、磁州之武安县，签书辽州判官，通判岢岚军，知南渠、均、遂三州，领利州路转运判官，提点梓州、河东刑狱，河东路转运副使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1215276_comment'></div>初知扶风，以母忧去官，河间复丁父忧，皆不能终任。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1215276_comment'></div>知南渠州，被旨改提点大辽顿事，不赴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1215276_comment'></div>凡出仕四十有四年，终始一节。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1215276_comment'></div>公为人温厚靖深，喜愠不见于色。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1215276_comment'></div>少读书，以功名自任，不苟于吏事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1215276_comment'></div>初宰武安，州既以整办称矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1215276_comment'></div>时深、冀水潦，民流移于武安者以千数。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1215276_comment'></div>诱说豪右出粟，平其直，籍贫民，使得市，而公自临视之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1215276_comment'></div>至秋大熟，迄无殍殕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1215276_comment'></div>黄发垂髫，扶携而归，皆曰：「活我者，崔公也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1215276_comment'></div>武安之民，纪公善政，闻于朝，愿再留三年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1215276_comment'></div>诣阙下者，五百馀人，时惊异之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1215276_comment'></div>其后出守，专以清净不扰为政；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1215276_comment'></div>务在举大纲，略细故，与吏民立教，期于无犯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1215276_comment'></div>推毂士类，率先寒素。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1215276_comment'></div>掾属有故人子，诡以其父书求荐章，置金函中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1215276_comment'></div>公举之有物，笑谢而却之，然卒加荐引。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1215276_comment'></div>人以此多公，笃于故旧而能掩人之私也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1215276_comment'></div>崇宁中，有诏天下建置佛祠，榜曰「天宁万寿」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1215276_comment'></div>公时为遂宁守，奉诏矍然，曰：「此地，上始封之国，可使不先他郡乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1215276_comment'></div>然民不可劳也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1215276_comment'></div>乃因城南废寺，庀材治具，躬自督视，鼓舞吏民，不踰月而告成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1215276_comment'></div>民视轮奂之鼎新，初不知追胥之扰也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1215276_comment'></div>大观初，太行有黠盗曰李免者，聚徒山谷，时出寇掠，惊扰郡邑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1215276_comment'></div>朝廷遣将兵捕虏久无功，乃自梓州路提点刑狱移公河东，专董其事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1215276_comment'></div>公入境，以方略授诸将，按劾其逗挠疲懦、素无状者数人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1215276_comment'></div>由是人人自力，皆倍其勇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1215276_comment'></div>未几，披其党聚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1215276_comment'></div>贼穷请命，诏释之，太行以宁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1215276_comment'></div>请改转运副使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1215276_comment'></div>河东地瘠民贫，漕挽岁常不足。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1215276_comment'></div>公曰：「民不可取也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1215276_comment'></div>乃尽索诸郡贡赋、山泽之籍与廪吏养兵储边之费，计入以为出。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1215276_comment'></div>罢不急之务，讲在官之利，宽恤民力。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1215276_comment'></div>明年，储廥皆盈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1215276_comment'></div>初行均籴法，河东俗少种麦，民无以输。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1215276_comment'></div>吏恐不能塞责，公独抗疏于朝，论其不可敷办之状。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1215276_comment'></div>有旨遂罢夏籴，公私便之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1215276_comment'></div>诏天下言便民事，公在职以八事应诏：一曰议升贡，二曰重守令，三曰经漕运，四曰慎举官，五曰罢榷酤，六曰议财货，七曰罢时估，八曰重农事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1215276_comment'></div>其言皆切于世务，可以见公行己之大略矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1215276_comment'></div>久之，复除本路提刑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1215276_comment'></div>发伏擿奸，郡吏震悚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1215276_comment'></div>先是，有浮屠氏者，为狱词逮引，目以妖贼馀党，久未就捕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1215276_comment'></div>一日，获于晋州，诏公案治。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1215276_comment'></div>众谓必诛死，公独辨其非党与，谳于朝，贷之，复为浮屠如初。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1215276_comment'></div>人方知公嫉恶出于天资，而其详刑法，民自以不冤，实长者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1215276_comment'></div>公在河东凡十馀年，既倦游，慨然有归志，乃买田阳翟将老焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1215276_comment'></div>方筑室，会以事罢，乃竟请归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1215276_comment'></div>阖门不治外事，绝宾客，专以道家养生鍊气之术为意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1215276_comment'></div>无何，无甚疾而终，享年六十有六，时政和五年七月十四日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1215276_comment'></div>公兄弟二人，季曰龠，字元量，布衣从公南北，友爱未尝相舍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1215276_comment'></div>大礼，恩当任子，舍其息以先龠，朝廷不从。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1215276_comment'></div>叹谓龠曰：「吾弟未禄仕，吾无以见先君」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1215276_comment'></div>既得归，乃谢事，以恩授龠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1215276_comment'></div>命下两月而公卒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1215276_comment'></div>呜呼，可谓君子哉，若人也！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1215276_comment'></div>公娶周氏，朝请大夫宗问之女，累封宜人，先公五年卒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1215276_comment'></div>子男三人：曰琥，曰讽，皆早世；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1215276_comment'></div>曰嵩，将仕郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1215276_comment'></div>孙男二人：曰孝彦、孝纯，尚幼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1215276_comment'></div>以是年八月十七日合葬于阳翟县某原周宜人之茔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1215276_comment'></div>公平生无他嗜好，唯喜藏书，蓄古器，倾家赀以求之不惮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1215276_comment'></div>善作诗，传于士大夫之间，编集于家二十卷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1215276_comment'></div>又自取《唐史》，撰次其人物之美者，各为诗以纪之，名曰《易览》，亦藏于家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1215276_comment'></div>过昔从仕太原，公为部使者，数得以事见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1215276_comment'></div>公风姿秀整，气温而色庄，口不论臧否，言不及世故。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1215276_comment'></div>独好问长生之术，与方士内外丹之诀，熊经鸟伸、吐故纳新之说，靡不造其精微。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1215276_comment'></div>盖自弱龄从事于兹，晚岁亦专心致志焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1215276_comment'></div>曰黄金可必成，飞仙可必学，故年高而齿发不衰，颜如婴儿，殆有得于出世间法者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1215276_comment'></div>夫重于内者必轻于外，故公所至，能以身徇义，爱民利物。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1215276_comment'></div>不求赫赫之名，去而人辄思之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1215276_comment'></div>过尝辱公之知，论荐于朝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1215276_comment'></div>又与其弟元量游，复同闾里，讲公生平为详。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1215276_comment'></div>乃状其行事，以告当世君子，庶几采摭以志其墓𡑞云尔<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1215276_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_84_1215276'>知：原脱，据祠本补。</div><div id='poem_sentence_84_1215276_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1215276'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_83_1215276_0'>⑴ 《斜川集》卷五。又见《永乐大典》卷二七四四。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_1215276_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1115&endYear=1115')">1115年8月</a>　在长社。八月，赵鼎臣（承之）自京师出守邓州，过颍相访，作诗留别，苏过次韵。作品：《次韵赵承之留别》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《斜川集校注》卷五。赵鼎臣留别诗为《发颍昌留别韩次律苏叔党》，见《竹隐畸士集》卷二。）</span><div id='poem_522619' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_522619' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/522619?labeling=true' target='_blank'>次韵赵承之留别</a><span class='authorDate'>（1115年8月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31323, "北宋", "苏过", "poem_title_522619")'>苏过</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_522619_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_522619'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_522619'>出处事莫并，昔谙今则疏。<div id='poem_sentence_0_522619_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_522619'>一从畏车冕，意遂甘泥涂。<div id='poem_sentence_1_522619_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_522619'>种发日就白，衰颜宁再朱。<div id='poem_sentence_2_522619_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_522619'>壮心空万里，老病寄一区。<div id='poem_sentence_3_522619_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1115&endYear=1115')">1115年</a>　在长社。苏过有《赠远夫》诗。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《斜川集校注》卷五。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1118&endYear=1118')">1118年5月5日</a>　在长社，郾城县知县任上。五月端阳，苏过与叶梦得（少蕴）集于西湖，有诗唱酬。作品：《次韵叶守端阳日湖上宴集》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《斜川集校注》卷五。）</span><div id='poem_522753' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_522753' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/522753?labeling=true' target='_blank'>次韵叶守端阳日湖上宴集</a><span class='authorDate'>（1118年5月5日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31323, "北宋", "苏过", "poem_title_522753")'>苏过</a></span><br /><div ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1118&endYear=1118')">1118年</a>　在长社，郾城县知县任上。苏过与韩缙（君表、公表）、曾诚（存之）和陶唱酬。作品：《次韵和韩君表读渊明诗馈曾存之置酒唱酬之什》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《斜川集校注》卷五。）</span><div id='poem_522646' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_522646' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/522646?labeling=true' target='_blank'>次韵和韩君表读渊明馈曾存之酒唱酬之什</a><span /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_522646_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_522646'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_522646'>弹冠初为米，挂冠不待稔。<div id='poem_sentence_0_522646_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_522646'>人言学陶生，此举安能尽。<div id='poem_sentence_4_522646_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_522646'>曾韩轻轩冕，雅意妙无畛。<div id='poem_sentence_5_522646_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_title_522564_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_522564'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_522564'>二豪以诗鸣，优劣孰敢分。<div id='poem_sentence_0_522564_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_522564'>纵横阅万卷，何忧备三邻。<div id='poem_sentence_1_522564_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_522564'>终年发揣摩，秀句吐阳春。<div id='poem_sentence_2_522564_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_522564'>谁云不菑畬，安取三百囷。<div id='poem_sentence_3_522564_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_522564'>汝颍素多奇，世不乏孙<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>陈。<div id='poem_sentence_4_522564_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_522564'>著书效潜夫，奏赋嗤陵云。<div id='poem_sentence_5_522564_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_522564'>哀时无祁奚，丹书谁为焚。<div id='poem_sentence_6_522564_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_522564'>傥令试一割，晋盗当奔秦。<div id='poem_sentence_7_522564_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_522564'>德业閟不耀，天欲昌其身。<div id='poem_sentence_8_522564_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_522564'>定交乃余求，不贵白发新。<div id='poem_sentence_9_522564_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_522564'>从此杖屦数，为子扫榻尘。<div id='poem_sentence_10_522564_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_522564'>高谈看亹亹，挥麈落纷纷。<div id='poem_sentence_11_522564_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' 自注：避家讳，故作孙。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_522564_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_522565' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_522565' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a id='poem_title_522565_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_522565'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_522565'>逝水不可复，百年行中分。<div id='poem_sentence_2_522565'>节物谩消长，枯荄不知春。<div id='poem_sentence_2_522565_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_522565'>轩裳叹鸡肋，雀鼠盗廪囷。<div id='poem_sentence_3_522565_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_522565'>学艺晚愈拙，弹冠力难陈。<div id='poem_sentence_4_522565_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_522565'>澹然忘出处，任此无心云。<div id='poem_sentence_5_522565_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_522565'>世路羊肠险，恐遭象齿焚。<div id='poem_sentence_6_522565_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_522565'>何如老山泽，憔悴非逃秦。<div id='poem_sentence_7_522565_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_522565'>嵩少幸咫尺，云泉许容身。<div id='poem_sentence_8_522565_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_522565'>平生馀嗜好，舍旧当谋新。<div id='poem_sentence_9_522565_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_522565'>安心本无法，妙理契析尘。<div id='poem_sentence_10_522565_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_522565'>优哉真卒岁，岂复悦华纷。<div id='poem_sentence_11_522565_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_522565'></div><div id='poem_sentence_12_522565_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1120&endYear=1120')">1120年</a>　在长社。苏过有《陪郡守游西湖泛舟曲水分韵得“会”字》诗。诗。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《斜川集校注》卷五。）</span><div id='poem_522561' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_522561' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/522561?labeling=true' target='_blank'>陪郡守游西湖泛舟曲水分韵得会字</a><span class='authorDate'>（1120年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31323, "北宋", "苏过", "poem_title_522561")'>苏过</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_522561_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_522561'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_522561'>谢公志东山，杖屦未冠盖。<div id='poem_sentence_0_522561_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_522561'>兴成江湖游，意落轩冕外。<div id='poem_sentence_1_522561_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_522561'>阴阴耸百木，浏浏鸣溪濑。<div id='poem_sentence_2_522561_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_522561'>拿舟破菰荷，寻径穿萧艾。<div id='poem_sentence_3_522561_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_522561'>新亭水心见，倒影飞虹背。<div id='poem_sentence_4_522561_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_522561'>青山忽入坐，境与今意会。<div id='poem_sentence_5_522561_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_522561'>公诗如干将，游刃天宇大。<div id='poem_sentence_6_522561_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_522561'>西湖真小鲜，殊未供刀鲙。<div id='poem_sentence_7_522561_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_522561'>云烟日相劘，媚妩分晴霭。<div id='poem_sentence_8_522561_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_522648_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_522648'>前无雒洛人，后笑冯唐老。<div id='poem_sentence_1_522648_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_522648'>机云谩声价，班马空词藻。<div id='poem_sentence_2_522648_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_522648'>岂知渊源来，尚觉河汉小。<div id='poem_sentence_3_522648_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_522648'>斯文叹未坠，妙意付幽讨。<div id='poem_sentence_4_522648_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_522648'>言乘刺史藩，曾视金銮草。<div id='poem_sentence_5_522648_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_522648'>飘然香案仙，宜著蓬莱岛。<div id='poem_sentence_14_522648_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_522648'>平生林泉志，久矣轩裳藐。<div id='poem_sentence_15_522648_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1120&endYear=1120')">1120年</a>　在长社。山东潍州守修文举堂，以祀孔融，苏过题诗寄之。作品：《寄题北海文举堂》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《斜川集校注》卷六。）</span><div id='poem_522567' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_522567' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/522567?labeling=true' target='_blank'>寄题北海文举堂</a><span class='authorDate'>（1120年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span id='poem_title_522567_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_522567'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_522567'>巨君窃汉玺，如取鸿毛轻。<div id='poem_sentence_3_522567_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_522567'>忠义国所托，安危与之并。<div id='poem_sentence_4_522567_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_522567'>吾于文举见，坐折奸邪萌。<div id='poem_sentence_5_522567_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_522567'>谁能搏猛虎，乃用尺箠婴。<div id='poem_sentence_6_522567_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_522567'>义气横宇宙，不烦尺寸兵。<div id='poem_sentence_7_522567_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_522567_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1120&endYear=1120')">1120年</a>　在长社。故人从登州寄书、棋、研，苏过答书。作品：《文登帖》<span
