"poem_title_1215247")'>苏过</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1215247_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1215247'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1215247'>过再启：窃承文登信至，丈丈尊候万福，欣慰何已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1215247_comment'></div>并惠海鱼、芝藻、石研、棋子多品。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1215247_comment'></div>远物未易到此，乃蒙辍贶，何感如之！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1215247_comment'></div>区区非面谢不尽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1215247_comment'></div>过再拜。</div><div id='poem_sentence_4_1215247_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1120&endYear=1120')">1120年9月</a>　在长社。九月十二日，孙勰（志康）卒，苏过作墓志铭。作品：《孙志康墓铭》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《斜川集校注》卷九。）</span><div id='poem_1215279' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1215279' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1215279?labeling=true' target='_blank'>孙志康墓铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（1120年9月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31323, "北宋", "苏过", "poem_title_1215279")'>苏过</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1215279_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1215279'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1215279'>熙宁初，先君通守钱塘，孙君介夫使其子志康贽所业以见，愿留授经于门下，时年未弱冠也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1215279_comment'></div>先君嘉之，使与余长兄游。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1215279_comment'></div>既卒业归，自是走四方，为文章士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1215279_comment'></div>元祐间，先君知礼部贡举，志康以荐书来京师。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1215279_comment'></div>先君得其程文于黜籍中，擢寘第六人，廷试复居第六，天下然后知取之者严，而得之者固自可必也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1215279_comment'></div>志康居官不碌碌，议论劲正，有不可犯之色。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1215279_comment'></div>终身不敢畔所学。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1215279_comment'></div>以宣和二年九月十二日卒于淮宁之私第。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1215279_comment'></div>其子虬泣血以告曰：「虬先人寡所合，仕才至尚书郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1215279_comment'></div>自少至老，受国士知者，莫如东坡公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1215279_comment'></div>不得公铭其墓，得公子铭之，亦庶几矣！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1215279_comment'></div>敢以外祖黄才叔所状行事来请」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1215279_comment'></div>过惟志康父子于余家为世契，自龆龀辱与之游，曩又同宦于并门，知之最详。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1215279_comment'></div>其敢以辞力不能为解？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1215279_comment'></div>乃为泣而书之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1215279_comment'></div>公讳协，志康，其字也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1215279_comment'></div>世为虔州感化人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1215279_comment'></div>曾大父长孺，故任太子中舍，知浔州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1215279_comment'></div>大父师房，故不仕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1215279_comment'></div>父立节，即介夫也，终于桂州节度判官，赠朝散郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1215279_comment'></div>公赐进士第，授奉宁军节度推官，历冀州幕、郓州州学教授。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1215279_comment'></div>用荐者，改宣德郎、知舒州太和县。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1215279_comment'></div>八宝恩及，累迁至朝散郎，赐五品服。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1215279_comment'></div>自湖外官满，从辟高阳、太原两路安抚司机宜文字。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1215279_comment'></div>除知岳州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1215279_comment'></div>请宫祠，除提点崇福宫，归于陈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1215279_comment'></div>公有田在陈，遂为终焉计。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1215279_comment'></div>明年请老。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1215279_comment'></div>又明年，乃以疾不起。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1215279_comment'></div>享年七十一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1215279_comment'></div>公弱不戏弄，巍然有父风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1215279_comment'></div>读书无所不贯穿，尤长于《左氏春秋》。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1215279_comment'></div>文词典严，有西汉风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1215279_comment'></div>援古證今，而折衷之以己。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1215279_comment'></div>居官守正不挠，以仁厚为急，故所至辄有去思。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1215279_comment'></div>南阳张公几仲之帅高阳也，精选幕府士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1215279_comment'></div>荐绅间请行者不一，几仲独曰：「吾尝见师是黄公之婿曰孙郎者，不好面谀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1215279_comment'></div>师是有所议论，孙郎从旁辄可否之，未尝依违也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1215279_comment'></div>吾今守边，宾客中不患吾唱而无和也，特安用之？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1215279_comment'></div>若得斯人，则吾知过」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1215279_comment'></div>遂辟与俱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1215279_comment'></div>在高阳八年，宾主无间言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1215279_comment'></div>几仲移并门，又与之同往。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1215279_comment'></div>过尝见其端笏以游其庭，军府之政，必可而后有所唯诺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1215279_comment'></div>毅然见乎色，几仲为改容更张之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1215279_comment'></div>所辅益不可胜纪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1215279_comment'></div>公以文章名世，而循循然如不出诸口。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1215279_comment'></div>未尝恃己以凌物，贤愚少长，待之如一，称其善而掩其过。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1215279_comment'></div>在边之久，虽武夫悍卒，皆心服其诚，而为之尽最。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1215279_comment'></div>后守岳阳，政亦可观。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1215279_comment'></div>是时湖北开新边，调发他郡，文檄旁午于道，公私惴恐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1215279_comment'></div>公呼豪右百姓与计议于庭，曰：「君父之命不可违，吾与汝曹皆任其责」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1215279_comment'></div>出檄于怀，赋之曰：「吾不以付吏，不汝追逮，特宽为期。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1215279_comment'></div>期而不至者，罚皆倍之」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1215279_comment'></div>千里之间，民不知劳而军需告办。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1215279_comment'></div>岳阳尝经火灾，谯门两观，鞠为灰烬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1215279_comment'></div>公至之数月，登城叹曰：「昔岳阳楼观以伟丽闻天下，今乃没于丘墟草棘间，不能复前人之迹，守臣罪也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1215279_comment'></div>父老闻之，欣然有请曰：「岳人怀此久矣，非我贤守，谁当任之？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1215279_comment'></div>有无惟所命」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1215279_comment'></div>公得朝廷所赐度牒，与虞人所献山林巨植，鸠工庀徒而鼎新之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1215279_comment'></div>不踰年，壮峙如昔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1215279_comment'></div>州人扶老携幼来观，有自数百里至者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1215279_comment'></div>皆叹曰：「孙公不扰吾民，不鞭一人，而所立如斯，召父之甘棠，不在是耶」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1215279_comment'></div>故去郡之日，人挽留之，不得出郊，又维其舟，使不得去者累日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1215279_comment'></div>公治郡，专用教化，视民如家人，有争讼者，公为辩析其理，俾自屈服而去，古之循吏不是过也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1215279_comment'></div>平生无嗜好。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1215279_comment'></div>老不废书，如饥渴然；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1215279_comment'></div>善作古篆，秦汉而下不取也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1215279_comment'></div>娶黄氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1215279_comment'></div>初，东坡公奇其才，以语师是，乃以其子妻之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1215279_comment'></div>公晚得痹疾，黄夫人躬治药石，相其饮食卧起，经纪家事，不以毫发累其胸中者二年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1215279_comment'></div>公没，窀穸之事，皆夫人自任之，有古烈妇之风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1215279_comment'></div>公文集若干卷，传于世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1215279_comment'></div>呜呼，风俗之不振也久矣！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1215279_comment'></div>自义不胜利，天下之士以容悦为工，端方为拙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1215279_comment'></div>有终身为县吏，妻子至于寒饿，而天下指以为叹，又私相以为戒，风俗安得不媮乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1215279_comment'></div>而士气安得不卑也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1215279_comment'></div>此贤人君子所甚惧者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1215279_comment'></div>先君常作《刚说》一篇，为介夫而发，叹天下无其人也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1215279_comment'></div>介夫流落不遇，至死不悔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1215279_comment'></div>志康又不偶于世，抱才无所施，介夫真有子哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1215279_comment'></div>以某年月日葬于某地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1215279_comment'></div>子一人，曰虬，事亲有立，能克其家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1215279_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_83_1215279'>崆峒之山，章贡之水。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1215279_comment'></div>山川秀奇，钟于孙氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1215279_comment'></div>孙氏世儒，一经教子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1215279_comment'></div>至于志康，命世之士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1215279_comment'></div>师以道授，父以刚遗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1215279_comment'></div>处其有闻，出则或柅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1215279_comment'></div>晚游诸侯，遇其所知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1215279_comment'></div>翔而后集，夫谁敢羁？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1215279_comment'></div>抱其经术，卒不少施。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1215279_comment'></div>世无王良，骥将安之？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1215279_comment'></div>周士也贵，秦士也贱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1215279_comment'></div>义利之分，贤愚斯判。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1215279_comment'></div>斯人云亡，后生不见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1215279_comment'></div>我铭其藏，惟以永叹。</div><div id='poem_sentence_96_1215279_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1120&endYear=1120')">1120年</a>　在长社。苏过舅父王箴（元直）葬。表弟王先、王光来书，求作碑文，过为作。作品：《王元直墓碑》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《斜川集校注》卷九。）</span><div id='poem_1215278' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1215278' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1215278?labeling=true' target='_blank'>王元直墓碑</a><span class='authorDate'>（宣和二年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31323, "北宋", "苏过", "poem_title_1215278")'>苏过</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1215278_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1215278'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1215278'>西蜀有隐君子王元直者，吾母同安君之弟也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1215278_comment'></div>过生二十年，不识外家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1215278_comment'></div>侍二亲钱塘，舅氏自蜀来见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1215278_comment'></div>吾先君子相与论契阔，谈仁义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1215278_comment'></div>先君所与游，皆天下士，于舅氏有布衣交，竦然见于色。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1215278_comment'></div>留卒岁而归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1215278_comment'></div>时四方门人，争挟所能以进，丐一言为终身荣，或因之以显于世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1215278_comment'></div>而舅氏家无甔石，口未尝言贫；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1215278_comment'></div>穷居十年，口未尝言仕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1215278_comment'></div>往返万里，无一毫屈于人者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1215278_comment'></div>既不可得而亲，亦不可得而疏，于是门下士皆怅然自失。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1215278_comment'></div>过于是时始得见舅氏眉目，聆其音声，真有德君子也！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1215278_comment'></div>呜呼，岂可以世俗议哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1215278_comment'></div>舅氏之归，先君作六言诗饯之，而使诸甥皆赋其后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1215278_comment'></div>名公卿和者甚众，蜀人争传之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1215278_comment'></div>舅氏闭门不出，陈义益高，世故卒不能累其心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1215278_comment'></div>先君之迁于南也，平昔亲旧屏迹，不敢问安否者七年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1215278_comment'></div>舅氏慨然奋不顾身，曰：「公盛时在朝廷、典方面，则往见之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1215278_comment'></div>今厄穷瘴疠之地，吾等乃畏避形迹，非夫也」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1215278_comment'></div>率同往者无一人，遂独浮江而下，将自洞庭、桂岭而南。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1215278_comment'></div>会先君有诏北还，而舅氏遇疾于涂以卒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1215278_comment'></div>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1215278_comment'></div>过谓吾舅氏能行古人之事，而志不达。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1215278_comment'></div>犯患难，违众说，而竟为俗子所快，是重不幸也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1215278_comment'></div>苟不书，将何以伸于后而善风俗耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1215278_comment'></div>公讳箴，元直，字也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1215278_comment'></div>眉之眉山人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1215278_comment'></div>祖徙居青神，讳惟德者，其曾大父也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1215278_comment'></div>讳文化者，其大父也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1215278_comment'></div>讳介者，父也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1215278_comment'></div>皆隐居不仕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1215278_comment'></div>母某氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1215278_comment'></div>公九岁通经，晓解句义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1215278_comment'></div>父好赈施而患贫，无以继，乃使治息钱，取其赢以周所乏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1215278_comment'></div>公从容其旁曰：「放于利而行多怨，恐所及者鲜而取怨者多，曷若师孟子所谓仁义而已乎」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1215278_comment'></div>父大惊，取券焚之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1215278_comment'></div>弱冠，以所属文见，先君子爱之，称于贤良。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1215278_comment'></div>侯元叔时为成都学官，见而奇之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1215278_comment'></div>每与论古人，退即书数百言，如《史》、《汉》赞论者，元叔叹其有史笔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1215278_comment'></div>居丧，以哀毁见称。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1215278_comment'></div>免丧，元叔复召置门下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1215278_comment'></div>举进士，不调。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1215278_comment'></div>元叔阅其程文，曰：「尺度同于人，而中否异，是命也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1215278_comment'></div>以诗勉之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1215278_comment'></div>公遂不复事科举，专心读书，学古文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1215278_comment'></div>里中诸父耆儒皆降意与之游，为忘年交。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1215278_comment'></div>自钱塘归，得先君诗文满箧，以付其子，曰：「吾家不贫矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1215278_comment'></div>由是士大夫接迹于门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1215278_comment'></div>又以诧于里人，曰：「海内士，吾得交于黄鲁直、秦少游、王定国、刘景文之流，足矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1215278_comment'></div>元祐间，诏举经明行修，或以公名闻于部使者，荐书将上矣，力辞而免，蜀人尤称之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1215278_comment'></div>建中靖国元年春二月二十有八日，以病卒于夔州之传舍，享年五十三。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1215278_comment'></div>丧归，蜀人哀之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1215278_comment'></div>宣和二年十月二十八日，葬于青神县之玉台乡仁慎里炉头山之坞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1215278_comment'></div>公娶某氏，子男三人：遇早卒；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1215278_comment'></div>次曰先，曰光，皆举进士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1215278_comment'></div>女二人：长适杨元龟，次适杨颛县。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1215278_comment'></div>孙男四人：伯远、仲适、叔达、季逢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1215278_comment'></div>公天资仁孝，遇物以诚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1215278_comment'></div>与人子言必以孝，与兄弟言必以睦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1215278_comment'></div>缙绅间尝有不能于季孟间者，公作诗感悟之，遂相欢如初。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1215278_comment'></div>季父庆源，官于洪雅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1215278_comment'></div>以论事不合，取长官怒，忧以罪去，谋于公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1215278_comment'></div>公笑曰：「古人不肯束带见督邮，彼何人哉」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1215278_comment'></div>庆源服其语，即谢病去，为两蜀高人，公实相之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1215278_comment'></div>其闻人之善若己出，有不善者如将浼焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1215278_comment'></div>人由此多改过徙义，不敢使公知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1215278_comment'></div>此其行己大略也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1215278_comment'></div>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1215278_comment'></div>吾母与公同气也，离蜀之年，公尚幼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1215278_comment'></div>先君官于南北，不得归，吾母同安君每念外家，涕零如雨，曰：「是子有立，吾门户无忧矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1215278_comment'></div>然白首无相见期，奈何」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1215278_comment'></div>公之来钱塘也，先妣方食，惊喜失匕箸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1215278_comment'></div>起从诸甥逆公馀杭门外。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1215278_comment'></div>相持而泣，感伤行路，悲其孤而喜其至也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1215278_comment'></div>后四年先妣即世，而公之没相去无十年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1215278_comment'></div>渭阳之悲伤，无以报罔极。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1215278_comment'></div>又二十年，先与光以书来告曰：「先君隐德，未有以表而出之者，子其毋辞」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1215278_comment'></div>过矍然有感于心，泣而书之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1215278_comment'></div>先、光皆修身有立，能为诗文，公有子哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1215278_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_79_1215278'>古人有言，惟仁则荣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1215278_comment'></div>岂皆轩冕，贵为公卿？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1215278_comment'></div>礼义以载，诗书以耕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1215278_comment'></div>藏于其身，琼弁玉缨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1215278_comment'></div>人孰无死，死而不朽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1215278_comment'></div>五福有一，可传于后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1215278_comment'></div>曰攸好德，百行称首。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1215278_comment'></div>富与贵者，泯没何有？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1215278_comment'></div>我观舅氏，古之逸民。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1215278_comment'></div>躬耕乐道，以全吾真。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1215278_comment'></div>化其乡闾，训敕子孙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1215278_comment'></div>荜门圭窦，吾不曰贫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1215278_comment'></div>惟士也贵，无惭于古。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1215278_comment'></div>视其与游，户外之屦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1215278_comment'></div>青神之原，有坟其墓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1215278_comment'></div>读我铭词，以考其素。</div><div id='poem_sentence_94_1215278_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1120&endYear=1120')">1120年</a>　梁师成自河东节度使为太尉。师成自称苏轼出子，广收苏轼翰墨。是时盛传苏过依附梁师成。梁师成欲结交苏轼从孙苏元老，元老不为所动，罢中朝任，未几卒。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1120&endYear=1120')">1120年</a>　在长社。范寥（信中）以刊苏轼诗集罪，罢颍昌兵马钤辖，居颍，筑室城市，作郎官庵，雪中赋诗；苏过皆次韵。作品：《次韵范信中》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《斜川集校注》卷六。）</span>《次韵信中郎官庵》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《斜川集校注》卷六。）</span>《和范信中雪诗二首》（其一）<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《斜川集校注》卷六。）</span>《和范信中雪诗二首》（其二）<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《斜川集校注》卷六。）</span><div id='poem_522618' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_522618' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/522618?labeling=true' target='_blank'>次韵范信中</a><span class='authorDate'>（1120年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31323, "北宋", "苏过", "poem_title_522618")'>苏过</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_522618_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_522618'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_522618'>将军山林士，本无轩冕意。<div id='poem_sentence_0_522618_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_522618'>乘流亦悠悠，得坎便止止。<div id='poem_sentence_1_522618_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_522618'>平生剧孟徒，作诗建安似。<div id='poem_sentence_2_522618_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_522618'>曹刘或争先，沈谢何足拟。<div id='poem_sentence_3_522618_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_522618'>人穷语益工，天或相夫子。<div id='poem_sentence_4_522618_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_522618'>念君绿发初，四海一身耳。<div id='poem_sentence_5_522618_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_522618'>要见元鲁山，万里立自致。<div id='poem_sentence_6_522618_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_522618'>许君窥藩篱，竟以身后委。<div id='poem_sentence_7_522618_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_522618'>翩然复蹑蹻，便非昔隐几。<div id='poem_sentence_8_522618_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_522618'>功名颇见迫，终欲老云水。<div id='poem_sentence_9_522618_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_522618'>岂料小卜筑，一溪城市里。<div id='poem_sentence_10_522618_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_522618'>从兹傥来物，不足置愠喜。<div id='poem_sentence_11_522618_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_522618'>用寻巢许游，无愧汝颍士。<div id='poem_sentence_12_522618_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_522618'>我有𥝧稏田，君多樱笋美。<div id='poem_sentence_13_522618_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_522618'>杖屦日往来，风流岂不伟。<div id='poem_sentence_14_522618_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_522618'></div><div id='poem_sentence_15_522618_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_522615' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_522615' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/522615?labeling=true' target='_blank'>次韵信中郎官庵</a><span class='authorDate'>（1120年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31323, "北宋", "苏过", "poem_title_522615")'>苏过</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_522615_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_522615'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_522615'>飞流半山来，忽作长剑倚。<div id='poem_sentence_0_522615_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_522615'>吾知有奇境，何畏虎尾履。<div id='poem_sentence_1_522615_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_522615'>郎官初得名，山川虽信美。<div id='poem_sentence_2_522615_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_522615'>谁能此岩居，暂寓非终止。<div id='poem_sentence_3_522615_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_522615'>吾侪世外缘，壮心殊不已。<div id='poem_sentence_4_522615_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_522615'>每讥怀与安，同是非夫耻。<div id='poem_sentence_5_522615_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_522615'>忍饥啖藜藿，且博一笑喜。<div id='poem_sentence_6_522615_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_522615'>更寻云外人，安得助薪水。<div id='poem_sentence_7_522615_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_522615'>伶俜穿鸟道，窈窕下涧底。<div id='poem_sentence_8_522615_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_522615'>路述烟草合，欲往不得跬。<div id='poem_sentence_9_522615_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_522615'>登楼亡其梯，航海失一苇。<div id='poem_sentence_10_522615_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_522615'>仰观二三子，脚下云埃起。<div id='poem_sentence_11_522615_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_522615'>山灵若相戏，危石折屐齿。<div id='poem_sentence_12_522615_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_522615'>忧我不再来，遗恨丘壑里。<div id='poem_sentence_13_522615_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_522615'>借君谈天口，骇我未闻耳。<div id='poem_sentence_14_522615_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_522615'>秋高山更奇，后会志益伟。<div id='poem_sentence_15_522615_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_522615'>扪萝贵先登，噬脐无效此。<div id='poem_sentence_16_522615_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_522615'>与君控扶摇，赤脚踏清泚。<div id='poem_sentence_17_522615_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_522615'></div><div id='poem_sentence_18_522615_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_522578' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_522578' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/522578?labeling=true' target='_blank'>和范信中雪诗二首<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1120年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31323, "北宋", "苏过", "poem_title_522578")'>苏过</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_522578_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_522578'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_522578'>春事已稍稍，雪泥阻游观。<div id='poem_sentence_0_522578_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_522578'>壮心本无多，老境嗟易阑。<div id='poem_sentence_1_522578_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_522578'>念子功名士，早嫌怀与安。<div id='poem_sentence_2_522578_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_522578'>弃繻事远游，肯待齿发残。<div id='poem_sentence_3_522578_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_522578'>世事属餍耳，□□□□餐。<div id='poem_sentence_4_522578_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_522578'>急流成一快，勇退人独难。<div id='poem_sentence_5_522578_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_522578'>慎守林泉幽，莫辞松桂寒。<div id='poem_sentence_6_522578_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_522578'>馀龄付空寂，粗免非意干。<div id='poem_sentence_7_522578_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_522578'>愿同王翰邻，未暇贡禹弹。<div id='poem_sentence_8_522578_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_522578'>秕糠身外物，况复子所叹。<div id='poem_sentence_9_522578_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_522578'></div><div id='poem_sentence_10_522578_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_522579' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_522579' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/522579?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1120年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_522579_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_522579'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_522579'>君家寓城市，乃有山林观。<div id='poem_sentence_0_522579_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_522579'>高高复下下，卜筑殊未阑。<div id='poem_sentence_1_522579_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_522579'>昨夜三尺雪，闭门学袁安。<div id='poem_sentence_2_522579_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_522579'>且欣麦陇足，未怕红梅残。<div id='poem_sentence_3_522579_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_522579'>谁怜属国苏，取毡卧自餐。<div id='poem_sentence_4_522579_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_522579'>欲寻鸟道往，反畏屐齿难。<div id='poem_sentence_5_522579_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_522579'>凛凛溪边竹，倚空争岁寒。<div id='poem_sentence_6_522579_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_522579'>俨如十九夫，玉山方总干。<div id='poem_sentence_7_522579_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_522579'>悲风动骚屑，伴我长铗弹。<div id='poem_sentence_8_522579_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_522579'>布衾冷如水，敢效无鱼叹。<div id='poem_sentence_9_522579_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_522579'></div><div id='poem_sentence_10_522579_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1120&endYear=1120')">1120年</a>　在长社。苏过有《代人上北京留守书》，似代范寥（信中）作。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《斜川集校注》卷一〇。）</span><div id='poem_1215245' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1215245' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1215245?labeling=true' target='_blank'>代人上北京留守书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1120年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31323, "北宋", "苏过", "poem_title_1215245")'>苏过</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1215245_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1215245'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1215245'>某尝读史，见赵平原君时，有客毛遂，素不闻名于众人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1215245_comment'></div>一日，秦围邯郸，平原君患之，为求哀于楚，选门下士二十人与之俱，得十九人，而毛遂请行，平原君强听之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1215245_comment'></div>十九人者略无所施，而毛遂捧盘历阶定从于跬步之内，使赵重于九鼎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1215245_comment'></div>唐封常清、高仙芝之傔也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1215245_comment'></div>初，仙芝以其貌陋且跛，常清屡自陈，不得已置名傔中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1215245_comment'></div>军破达奚，常清于幕下潜作捷布，且记井泉次舍，克贼形势。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1215245_comment'></div>仙芝大惊，由此显名，为时良将。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1215245_comment'></div>某以为二人方陆沈自晦，辱在泥涂，不遇豪杰之士引而出之，付以事功，则不过一匹夫耳，饿死于沟渎，与草木同腐必矣，又何以表见于后世哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1215245_comment'></div>某窃不自量，结发读书，有志于古人，不肯碌碌俯仰于士大夫之间，思得豪杰之士，为之执鞭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1215245_comment'></div>念如毛遂、封常清之流，不为人知则已，倘得知己，不以众人遇我，则赴水火、蹈锋镝，不在古人后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1215245_comment'></div>今罪戾之馀不足道也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1215245_comment'></div>齿发如此，可以甘贫贱，安闾阎，不复议此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1215245_comment'></div>然区区之心，不能自默，求伸于左右者，何哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1215245_comment'></div>昔尝侍座侧，闻馀论，不以某为不肖，怜其无辜，若曰尚可教育，使不终废于世，心非木石，怀斯言而不敢忘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1215245_comment'></div>今又穷困益甚，舍左右而安所诉哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1215245_comment'></div>某一身漂零，死不足惜，有亲未葬，朝夕不敢自保；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1215245_comment'></div>妻子饥饿，不能出门户；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1215245_comment'></div>婚姻失时，言之寒心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1215245_comment'></div>可谓天之穷民也！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1215245_comment'></div>前者所犯，本非犯清议，污搢绅，不可湔洗收录之人，意谓屡更赦宥，当得复有旧物。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1215245_comment'></div>无何有司拘于文法，止叙散官，徒有被大恩之名，而卒无沾寸禄之实。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1215245_comment'></div>岂能默而不言，就死地哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1215245_comment'></div>方今之世，左右当方伯之任，荷天下之重名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1215245_comment'></div>四方之士，扫舍人之门，求为李膺之御，拾青紫、纡组绶，不知几何人矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1215245_comment'></div>怀材抱艺，不乏于使令；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1215245_comment'></div>文章翰墨，奔辏于幕府。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1215245_comment'></div>如不肖者，岂足系门下得失哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1215245_comment'></div>然左右一言，可使贫者富，穷者泰，嘘枯吹生，易如反掌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1215245_comment'></div>某困穷如此，安得不往告，而左右安得不终怜之乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1215245_comment'></div>使某得在奔走之列，感生成之遇，如毛遂、封常清，区区事业，当不辱于门下，非空言也！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1215245_comment'></div>惟执事者察之。</div><div id='poem_sentence_30_1215245_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1120&endYear=1120')">1120年</a>　在长社。岑穰（彦休）卒，苏过作文祭之。作品：《祭岑彦休文》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《斜川集校注》卷九。）</span><div id='poem_1215284' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1215284' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1215284?labeling=true' target='_blank'>祭岑彦休文</a><span class='authorDate'>（1120年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31323, "北宋", "苏过", "poem_title_1215284")'>苏过</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1215284_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1215284'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1215284'>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1215284_comment'></div>去古道远，士惟利趋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1215284_comment'></div>芥拾青紫，秕糠诗书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1215284_comment'></div>如商贾然，资舟与车。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1215284_comment'></div>得于古人，特其腐馀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1215284_comment'></div>惟彦休父，世业于儒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1215284_comment'></div>自诚而明，《六经》自娱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1215284_comment'></div>掇其英华，耻前弗如。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1215284_comment'></div>譬彼农夫，以菑以畲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1215284_comment'></div>既耕且种，且穫且储。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1215284_comment'></div>虽有水旱，孰知赢虚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1215284_comment'></div>蚤陟巍科，驰声天衢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1215284_comment'></div>金马玉堂，指日可须。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1215284_comment'></div>乃请试吏，邅回阔迂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1215284_comment'></div>弦歌两邑，古良大夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1215284_comment'></div>推其肝肺，拊妪茕孤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1215284_comment'></div>毋或伤之，同吾体肤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1215284_comment'></div>去恶勿疑，利吾耰耝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1215284_comment'></div>上党之治，益隆于初。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1215284_comment'></div>刚亦不吐，弱焉必扶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1215284_comment'></div>期月而归，遂与世疏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1215284_comment'></div>幅巾深衣，筑室端居。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1215284_comment'></div>左坟右典，东观石渠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1215284_comment'></div>邻里化之，训其稚雏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1215284_comment'></div>嗟余通家，三世乡闾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1215284_comment'></div>臭味既同，婚姻与俱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1215284_comment'></div>逾年不见，凛然清臞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1215284_comment'></div>隐几而坐，骨见衣隅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1215284_comment'></div>岂期斯人，千里半途。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1215284_comment'></div>望哭其堂，若见巾裾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1215284_comment'></div>搢绅涕洟，涂巷欷歔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1215284_comment'></div>聊陈一奠，往致生刍。</div><div id='poem_sentence_31_1215284_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1121&endYear=1121')">1121年</a>　在长社。苏过卜筑城西，营水竹可赏者数亩，慕陶渊明之为人，号小斜川，自号斜川先生。作诗以遗李行夫、范寥（信中）诸人。作品：《小斜川》（并引）<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《斜川集校注》卷六。）</span><div id='poem_522620' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_522620' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/522620?labeling=true' target='_blank'>小斜川<span class='inlineComment2'>（并引）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1121年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31323, "北宋", "苏过", "poem_title_522620")'>苏过</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_522620_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_522620'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_522620'>我老不自爱，几时真罢休。<div id='poem_sentence_0_522620_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_522620'>浮沈闾里间，漫效马少游。<div id='poem_sentence_1_522620_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_522620'>年来五十化，逝水无停流。<div id='poem_sentence_2_522620_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_522620'>胸中粗已了，浩荡欲没鸥。<div id='poem_sentence_3_522620_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_522620'>渊明我同生，共尽当一丘。<div id='poem_sentence_4_522620_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_522620'>试筑小斜川，佳名偶相俦。<div id='poem_sentence_5_522620_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_522620'>亦称辛丑岁，与公更<span class='inlineComment2'>（自注：平）</span>倡酬。<div id='poem_sentence_6_522620_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_522620'>当时二三友，得如我友不。<div id='poem_sentence_7_522620_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_522620'>赋诗俱不地，疑有湛辈忧。<div id='poem_sentence_10_522620'></div><div id='poem_sentence_10_522620_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1121&endYear=1121')">1121年</a>　在长社。李行夫迁居盘溪，苏过作诗为贺。作品：《贺李行父迁居盘溪》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《斜川集校注》卷六。）</span><div id='poem_522614' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_522614' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/522614?labeling=true' target='_blank'>驾李行父迁居盘溪</a><span class='authorDate'>（1121年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span id='poem_title_522614_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_522614'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_522614'>扬雄无儋石，而有宅一区。<div id='poem_sentence_0_522614_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_522614'>陶令官可弃，未免爱吾庐。<div id='poem_sentence_1_522614_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_522614'>古来贤达士，忘世未忘躯。<div id='poem_sentence_2_522614_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_522614'>岂知美恶间，共尽同籧篨。<div id='poem_sentence_3_522614_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_522614'>平生李居士，挈携四壁无。<div id='poem_sentence_4_522614_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_522614'>常有好颜色，直缘身世疏。<div id='poem_sentence_5_522614_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_522614'>前年家城东，一椽为有馀。<div id='poem_sentence_6_522614_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_522614'>今年家城西，隐几犹昔吾。<div id='poem_sentence_7_522614_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_522614'>此生正如此，梦觉两徐徐。<div id='poem_sentence_8_522614_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_522614'>曾何置欣戚，舍旧新是图。<div id='poem_sentence_9_522614_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_522614'>吾侪真小人，问讯填里闾。<div id='poem_sentence_10_522614_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_522614'>聊为盘溪喜，德邻良不孤。<div id='poem_sentence_11_522614_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_522614'>益知水竹深，中有山泽癯。<div id='poem_sentence_12_522614_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_522614'>虽非三宿桑，且学壶公壶。<div id='poem_sentence_13_522614_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_522614'></div><div id='poem_sentence_14_522614_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1121&endYear=1121')">1121年3月20日</a>　在长社。三月二十日，苏过为李亨伯（安正）遗文作跋。作品：《跋李防御遗文》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《斜川集校注》卷九。）</span><div id='poem_1215261' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1215261' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1215261?labeling=true' target='_blank'>跋李防御遗文</a><span class='authorDate'>（宣和三年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31323, "北宋", "苏过", "poem_title_1215261")'>苏过</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1215261_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1215261'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1215261'>防御公以儒者尉南海，设方略，破剧贼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1215261_comment'></div>进秩至苍梧太守，知名南服。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1215261_comment'></div>受代还漳江，过罗浮，为先君留十日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1215261_comment'></div>饮酒论道，商略古今，自恨相见之晚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1215261_comment'></div>过方侍行，具见其事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1215261_comment'></div>不踰年，公还朝，宰相荐换右列，付方面，盖将以功名诿焉，而公循然退避，终老于乡里，虽欲挽留而不可得。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1215261_comment'></div>非养于胸中有素，而出处进退在我，安能以清节照世乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1215261_comment'></div>读其遗文，观其字画，雍容浑厚而不迫切，君子哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1215261_comment'></div>宣和辛丑三月二十日得之于其子大忠，跋其后而归之。</div><div id='poem_sentence_8_1215261_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1121&endYear=1121')">1121年</a>　在长社。苏过有《书漳南李安正防御碑阴》文。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《斜川集校注》卷九。）</span><div id='poem_1215260' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1215260' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1215260?labeling=true' target='_blank'>书漳南李安正防御碑阴</a><span class='authorDate'>（1121年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31323, "北宋", "苏过", "poem_title_1215260")'>苏过</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1215260_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1215260'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1215260'>绍圣初，先君子谪罗浮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1215260_comment'></div>是时法令峻急，州县望风指，不敢与迁客游。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1215260_comment'></div>一夕，苍梧守李公安正，引车骑扣门，请交于衡门之下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1215260_comment'></div>先君子初不识面也，慨然论世间事，商略古今人物，下至医卜技艺，皆出人意表。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1215260_comment'></div>先君惊喜，以相见为晚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1215260_comment'></div>而公冒犯简书之畏，卒留十日而后行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1215260_comment'></div>呜呼，真天下奇男子！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1215260_comment'></div>公还朝，果为天子所知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1215260_comment'></div>擢帅邕管，蛮遁去，不敢饮马于江。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1215260_comment'></div>公尝言少时官南海，有剧贼三十馀人，出没海道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1215260_comment'></div>人不敢近，乃以计变姓名，易衣服，挟二童以往，尽缚之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1215260_comment'></div>由是显名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1215260_comment'></div>其临义勇决，蹈水火，人有不可学者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1215260_comment'></div>况于脱屣轩冕，得不优为之乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1215260_comment'></div>某于是时拜公，且与公之二子几仲、微仲游。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1215260_comment'></div>今皆有立，公为有子哉！</div><div id='poem_sentence_15_1215260_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1121&endYear=1121')">1121年</a>　在长社。苏过有《题李微叔所藏戴嵩暮雨图》诗。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《斜川集校注》卷六。）</span><div id='poem_522799' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_522799' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/522799?labeling=true' target='_blank'>题李微叔所藏戴嵩暮雨图</a><span class='authorDate'>（1121年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31323, "北宋", "苏过", "poem_title_522799")'>苏过</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_522799_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_522799'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_522799'>春云漠漠雨垂垂，水满平畴秧稻时。<div id='poem_sentence_0_522799_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_522799'>青蒻绿蓑晚归去<span class='inlineComment2'>（原校：一作青蓑蒻笠卧载归）</span>，为问市朝侬不知。<div id='poem_sentence_1_522799_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_522799'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_522799_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_522828' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/522828?labeling=true' target='_blank'>次韵王幼安哭韩君表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1121年闰5月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31323, "北宋", "苏过", "poem_title_522828")'>苏过</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_522828_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_522828'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_522828'>公子虽轩冕，山林契夙心。<div id='poem_sentence_0_522828_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_522828'>坐禅新活计，脱屣旧冠簪。<div id='poem_sentence_1_522828_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_title_1215273' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1215273?labeling=true' target='_blank'>天宁寺钟铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（1121年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span id='poem_title_1215273_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1215273'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1215273'>有宋宣和辛丑某月日，颍昌府天宁万寿禅寺住持比丘普融老，悯昔之钟坏，募人改作增大之，为铜五千斤，未期年而成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1215273_comment'></div>蜀人苏某观兹胜事，赞叹希有，而说偈言：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_1215273'>智哉大士，假幻说法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1215273_comment'></div>以大愿力，破愚痴矿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1215273_comment'></div>炽勇猛火，出智慧铜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1215273_comment'></div>戒定为模，般若为工。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1215273_comment'></div>是皆普融，成就法器。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1215273_comment'></div>置高广坐，发大音声。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1215273_comment'></div>雨风晦明，尝作佛事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1215273_comment'></div>警昧悟聋，觉迷归正。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1215273_comment'></div>以慈悲体，有扣即应。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1215273_comment'></div>随彼扣者，不入思惟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1215273_comment'></div>一切众生，烦恼灭尽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1215273_comment'></div>天宫地狱，等无高下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1215273_comment'></div>有性无性，齐成佛道。</div><div id='poem_sentence_13_1215273_comment'></div></div></div><br "poem_title_1215235")'>苏过</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1215235_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1215235'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1215235'>伏审光膺帝制，入掌水衡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1215235_comment'></div>澄清千里之畿，民无冤滥；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1215235_comment'></div>涣汗十行之诏，帝自畴咨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1215235_comment'></div>伏惟使者修撰道义储身，忠诚许国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1215235_comment'></div>谈经术以佐吏事，怀仁义以陈王前。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1215235_comment'></div>故出则俾观民风，入则缉熙庶绩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1215235_comment'></div>顾大河中国之经渎，表治乱而见于书；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1215235_comment'></div>而水官三代之虞衡，历古今而难其选。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1215235_comment'></div>将欲行其所无事，必使谋之于未然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1215235_comment'></div>宽九重宵旰之忧，慰两河生齿之望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1215235_comment'></div>循名责实，为官择人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1215235_comment'></div>果见除书，允谐旧德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1215235_comment'></div>消盗贼以安渤海，既旌报政之良；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1215235_comment'></div>临河洛而叹禹功，将继前人之美。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1215235_comment'></div>某久忝属吏，夙被仁风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1215235_comment'></div>欣太平之得贤，睹嘉猷之入告。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1215235_comment'></div>愿同燕雀，远伸贺厦之诚；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1215235_comment'></div>尚冀桑榆，晚借馀光之末。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1215235_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_18_1215235_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='25cca693b21f4e5388ed2b927b0997f5_label'><a id='poem_sentence_0_522816_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_522816'>穷似少陵无裋褐，空怀大厦庇千间。<div id='poem_sentence_1_522816_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1122&endYear=1122')">1122年</a>　或在长社。苏过有《秋蝇篇》诗。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《斜川集校注》卷六。）</span><div id='poem_522698' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_522698' id='poem_sentence_1_522698'>晨忧霜露避暗壁，晚集户牖依斜阳。<div id='poem_sentence_1_522698_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_522698'>斜阳寂寂能几许，股翼未温寒日暮。<div id='poem_sentence_2_522698_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_522698'>纵馋不敢近华筵，屏迹何须待挥麈。<div id='poem_sentence_3_522698_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_522698'>我方六月流汗时，营营聒耳缘目眉。<div id='poem_sentence_4_522698_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_522698'>盘餐旨洁未下箸，聚嘬弄吻不少迟。<div id='poem_sentence_5_522698_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_522698'>微物盛衰还有数，得意何曾念寒暑。<div id='poem_sentence_6_522698_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_522784_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_522784'>安能学稼与学圃，已得异书逢异人。<div id='poem_sentence_1_522784_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_title_522789_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_522789'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_522789'>青春过隙不多时，佳会应须日日期。<div id='poem_sentence_0_522789_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_522789'>羡子多情勤秉烛，寻芳问柳每题诗。<div id='poem_sentence_1_522789_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_522789'>洛花名字争新见，尤物东君剪刻迟。<div id='poem_sentence_2_522789_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_522789'>安得韩湘写奇句，世间铅粉谩劳施。<div ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1122&endYear=1122')">1122年</a>　在长社。欧阳晦叔建竹癖轩，苏过题诗。作品：《题欧阳晦叔竹癖轩》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《斜川集校注》卷六。）</span><div id='poem_522797' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_522797' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/522797?labeling=true' target='_blank'>题欧阳晦叔竹癖轩</a><span class='authorDate'>（1122年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span id='poem_title_522797_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_522797'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_522797'>海竹纤杉乱苇萑，君家千树独淇园。<div id='poem_sentence_0_522797_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_522797'>清阴夏簟常留客，疏影秋光共入轩。<div id='poem_sentence_1_522797_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_522797'>屐阮孰窥尘外趣，锻嵇聊与世人论。<div id='poem_sentence_2_522797_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_522797'>可怜此路今无几，桃李成蹊不待言。<div id='poem_sentence_3_522797_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_522797'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_522797_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1122&endYear=1122')">1122年</a>　在长社。某遗老建袅灠亭，苏过作《上梁文》作品：《袅灠亭上梁文》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《斜川集校注》卷九。）</span><div id='poem_1215298' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1215298' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1215298?labeling=true' target='_blank'>袅漤亭上梁文</a><span class='authorDate'>（1122年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31323, "北宋", "苏过", "poem_title_1215298")'>苏过</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1215298_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1215298'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1215298'>门外有湖，独跨一城之风景；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1215298_comment'></div>岸边无屋，难包四面之烟光。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1215298_comment'></div>虽拨棹以可航，奈牂牁之靡定。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1215298_comment'></div>用涓嘉腊，载举修梁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1215298_comment'></div>野处老人学道无成，读书粗遣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1215298_comment'></div>遭遇四朝之明主，周旋三纪之从官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1215298_comment'></div>人生七十古来稀，况邻耄齿；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1215298_comment'></div>水击三千抟而上，宁复壮心？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1215298_comment'></div>幸足迹未倦于驱驰，而眼力尚堪于登眺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1215298_comment'></div>乃眷宽闲之野，本为莽眇之区。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1215298_comment'></div>久嗟领略之太迟，敢惜经营之小费？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1215298_comment'></div>先成画舫，戛然浮漾于中流：兹创笠亭，正尔铺张于佳观。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1215298_comment'></div>值庆桥之改作，参枉渚以函通。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1215298_comment'></div>轮蹄因是以娱嬉，士女相招而和会。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1215298_comment'></div>东阡北陌，穷赋诗把酒之欢；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1215298_comment'></div>南浦西山，挹捲雨飞云之胜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1215298_comment'></div>朝游暮反，于以舒忧；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1215298_comment'></div>寒往暑来，不妨养性。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1215298_comment'></div>琼圃起前鱼之叹，云庄兴退鹢之讥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1215298_comment'></div>姑取足于鹪巢，顾何嫌于鹤怨？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1215298_comment'></div>棋坊在左，酒肆直南。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1215298_comment'></div>坐隐手谈，或留连而竟夜；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1215298_comment'></div>清明寒食，想歌舞之酣春。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1215298_comment'></div>爰代工师，戏呈韵语：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_23_1215298'>东，庆善桥虹自在通。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1215298_comment'></div>吞却玉湖成一派，细寻山色有无中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1215298_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_25_1215298'>西，筵桂高楼望却低。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1215298_comment'></div>示病维摩元不出，秋风花月使人迷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1215298_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_27_1215298'>南，亭影参差照碧潭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1215298_comment'></div>旋插柳枝三百本，他年烟雨正毵毵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1215298_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_29_1215298'>北，此去吾庐才咫尺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1215298_comment'></div>良宵正可百回来，借月留云邀夜色。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1215298_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_31_1215298'>上，缥缈丹霞千万丈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1215298_comment'></div>但知天上是神仙，不羡人间真将相。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1215298_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_33_1215298'>下，采鹤飞翔如绘画。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1215298_comment'></div>谁能拚得一生闲，来结山翁香火社。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1215298_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_35_1215298'>伏愿上梁之后，棹声不断，楫唱相闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1215298_comment'></div>留客烹茶，兼尽弈棋之兴；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1215298_comment'></div>呼童益酒，更成堕帻之欢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1215298_comment'></div>凡我同盟，共兹胜赏。</div><div id='poem_sentence_38_1215298_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1122&endYear=1122')">1122年</a>　在长社。苏过为宋景辉二子作《字说》作品：《宋景辉二子字说》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《斜川集校注》卷一〇。）</span><div id='poem_1215269' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1215269' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1215269?labeling=true' target='_blank'>宋景辉二子字说</a><span class='authorDate'>（1122年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31323, "北宋", "苏过", "poem_title_1215269")'>苏过</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1215269_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1215269'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1215269'>古人之名其子者，亦多说矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1215269_comment'></div>有获长狄侨如以喜而名其子；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1215269_comment'></div>有文在其手曰「友」，以异瑞而名其子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1215269_comment'></div>人之爱其子，莫不欲其贤且贵也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1215269_comment'></div>元宪宋公之曾孙曰肱，曰膰，余问其所以名之说。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1215269_comment'></div>其父景辉语余：「肱生而甚似其祖，必能世吾家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1215269_comment'></div>元宪以道德文章名天下，股肱元圣致太平。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1215269_comment'></div>吾所以期之如此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1215269_comment'></div>曰膰者，吾通守颍昌，释奠宣圣为亚献，膰于是日也生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1215269_comment'></div>吾惟仲尼以膰肉不至而行，夫岂为肉哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1215269_comment'></div>盖为礼也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1215269_comment'></div>士大夫生于今日，亲睹礼乐之盛，笾豆具举，此岂小小节文哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1215269_comment'></div>吾是以名之」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1215269_comment'></div>予矍然不敢以童子戏，遂字肱曰元弼，肱曰元弼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1215269_comment'></div>且著其说以授二子，勉使有立，以无废父命。</div><div id='poem_sentence_14_1215269_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1122&endYear=1122')">1122年</a>　在长社。冬，赵叔盎（伯充）招游西湖，苏过有诗。作品：《次韵赵伯充雪中见招》（其一）<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《斜川集校注》卷五。）</span>《次韵赵伯充雪中见招》（其二）<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《斜川集校注》卷五。）</span><div id='poem_522814' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_522814' class='poemTitle id='poem_sentence_0_522695_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_522695'>又不斩取楼兰王，立功万里还故乡。<div id='poem_sentence_1_522695_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_522695'>两俱茫茫空白首，车轮马迹环四方。<div id='poem_sentence_2_522695_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_522695'>忽焉投劾赋陶令，亦复近市师韩康。<div target='_blank'>谢提举玉龙万寿宫表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1122年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31323, "北宋", "苏过", "poem_title_1215224")'>苏过</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1215224_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1215224'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1215224'>备东国诸侯之长，积玷藩宣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1215224_comment'></div>赘西山散吏之员，尚縻奉稍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1215224_comment'></div>恩波浃骨，感涕交颐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1215224_comment'></div>伏念臣才不逮人，学非见道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1215224_comment'></div>雕虫篆刻，但攻无用之词章；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1215224_comment'></div>潦倒粗疏，殊乏有行之事业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1215224_comment'></div>当睿主粲惟新之化，为稽阴兴和市之恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1215224_comment'></div>猥以妄庸，误承临遣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1215224_comment'></div>萃彼八城之赋，揆于一己之平。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1215224_comment'></div>虽公尔忘私，敢效肥秦之视越；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1215224_comment'></div>然犯而聚怨，不胜众楚之咻齐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1215224_comment'></div>竟获全归，允为幸会。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1215224_comment'></div>兹盖伏遇皇帝陛下仁参高厚，圣协勋华。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1215224_comment'></div>明试以功，方厉精于政治；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1215224_comment'></div>退人以礼，每加惠于臣邻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1215224_comment'></div>岂伊朽腐之资，曲累记存之数。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1215224_comment'></div>臣杜门老矣，恋阙凄其。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1215224_comment'></div>身在江湖，怅颓龄之有几；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1215224_comment'></div>心非木石，念报德以何时？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1215224_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_19_1215224_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1123&endYear=1123')">1123年</a>　在长社。季春，苏过方践赵叔盎（伯充）之约，游曲水，分韵赋诗。作品：《同赵伯充游曲水赵氏庄分韵得“抱”字》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《斜川集校注》卷五。）</span><div id='poem_522562' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_522562' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/522562?labeling=true' target='_blank'>同赵伯充游曲水赵氏庄分韵得抱字</a><span class='authorDate'>（1123年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31323, "北宋", "苏过", "poem_title_522562")'>苏过</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_522562_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_522562'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_522562'>三春失行乐，风雨与病恼。<div id='poem_sentence_0_522562_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_522562'>忽惊节物改，树密莺声老。<div id='poem_sentence_1_522562_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_522562'>滥陪闲中客，载酒寻芳草。<div id='poem_sentence_2_522562_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_522562'>东郊纵所适，苍莽事幽讨。<div id='poem_sentence_3_522562_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_522562'>谁欤有隐居，溪谷相郁缭。<div id='poem_sentence_4_522562_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_522562'>疏篱映脩竹，叩门许径造。<div id='poem_sentence_5_522562_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_522562'>主人虽锄耰，好客自酒扫。<div id='poem_sentence_6_522562_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_522562'>结茅□□年，种木今合抱。<div id='poem_sentence_7_522562_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_522562'>飘然佳公子，忽弄松风操。<div id='poem_sentence_8_522562_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_522562'>丝桐岂能尔，妙意超物表。<div id='poem_sentence_9_522562_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_522562'>归途践危桥，月上千林缟。<div id='poem_sentence_10_522562_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_522562'>兹游非人寰，俗耳不可道。<div id='poem_sentence_11_522562_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_522562'></div><div id='poem_sentence_12_522562_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1123&endYear=1123')">1123年4月10日</a>　在长社。四月十日，苏过为海印作塔铭。作品：《安邑县寿圣寺第一代住持海印塔铭》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《斜川集校注》卷九。）</span><div id='poem_1215274' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1215274' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1215274?labeling=true' target='_blank'>安邑县寿圣寺第一代住持海印塔铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（1123年4月10日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31323, "北宋", "苏过", "poem_title_1215274")'>苏过</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1215274_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1215274'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1215274'>我先大夫卜茔于郏敖，求浮屠师使居其旁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1215274_comment'></div>义光者，自解梁来，能诵戒，讲说经论，请止留作佛事，荐冥福，众不舍去，遂建道场。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1215274_comment'></div>钟梵之音，晨夕无废。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1215274_comment'></div>光为人强力敏给，喜于事功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1215274_comment'></div>问其师承，曰：「解之安邑住持寿圣寺第一代，海印其名也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1215274_comment'></div>印寂矣，其道行有足书而未有发明之者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1215274_comment'></div>义光死有责，敢以是请」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1215274_comment'></div>某唯先茔有托于光，其何以辞？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1215274_comment'></div>师姓张氏，邑之王范村民家子也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1215274_comment'></div>生时有光烛室，人以为非常。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1215274_comment'></div>十五即出家，礼僧交青为师。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1215274_comment'></div>至政和二年乾元节，以诵经应格为沙弥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1215274_comment'></div>二十受戒具。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1215274_comment'></div>邑始建寿圣寺，师为道俗所推，使住持。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1215274_comment'></div>初未有屋一椽，不数岁，佛宇、僧舍、钟楼、经阁、山门、厨廪皆具备，而从学者翔集矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1215274_comment'></div>师持律甚严，诵经精专，自云于日星间能睹见诸天人相，岂所谓获常清净眼之报者耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1215274_comment'></div>以政和五年十一月二十二日示寂，寿八十有四，僧腊六十有五。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1215274_comment'></div>临终之日，有异香满室，远近来观，叹未曾有。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1215274_comment'></div>其徒奉其骨，塔而藏之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1215274_comment'></div>法嗣法孙凡三十一人列于碑之阴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1215274_comment'></div>苏子曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_20_1215274'>南宗北律，其自相诋訾，所从来远矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1215274_comment'></div>使吾言信然，由戒生定，定生慧，其成佛得道，岂有二哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1215274_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_22_1215274'>宣和五年四月初十日记。</div><div id='poem_sentence_22_1215274_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1123&endYear=1123')">1123年</a>　在长社。天宁寺平老升任住持，苏过作请开堂疏。作品：《请平老开堂疏》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《斜川集校注》卷九。）</span><div id='poem_1215297' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1215297' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1215297?labeling=true' target='_blank'>请平老开堂疏</a><span class='authorDate'>（1123年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31323, "北宋", "苏过", "poem_title_1215297")'>苏过</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1215297_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1215297'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1215297'>白云在天，舒卷自我。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1215297_comment'></div>明镜无垢，妍丑现前。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1215297_comment'></div>所以去来千变，卒之无心；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1215297_comment'></div>酬酢万状，本来无物。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1215297_comment'></div>今天宁长老平公，嗣真如法，传达摩衣，学道为众宗师，出众随缘利益。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1215297_comment'></div>声名藉甚，未许逃于空虚；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1215297_comment'></div>悲智兼脩，正可行之愿力。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1215297_comment'></div>重提祖令，大振宗风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1215297_comment'></div>作江海之慈航，施山川之法雨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1215297_comment'></div>妙高峰上，本为一大因缘；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1215297_comment'></div>毗耶城中，盖自两无言默。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1215297_comment'></div>鼓钟一时改观，瓦砾莫为非人。</div><div id='poem_sentence_11_1215297_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1123&endYear=1123')">1123年</a>　苏过荐李稙于向子湮（伯恭）<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1123&endYear=1123')">1123年</a>　或在长社。苏过有《上贻孙尉》文。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《斜川集校注》卷一〇。此文具体作时不详，姑系于此。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1123&endYear=1123')">1123年</a>　夏，苏过为通直郎，权通判中山府。<br /></div>

淮阳
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='2e4dbfd0d9a247f3aa7a960240f1d950_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("2e4dbfd0d9a247f3aa7a960240f1d950");'><span id='2e4dbfd0d9a247f3aa7a960240f1d950_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1106&endYear=1106')">1106年</a>，35岁</div><div id='2e4dbfd0d9a247f3aa7a960240f1d950' class='detail'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>张耒自黄州还，居陈州，苏过与吕知止造访，作诗戏之。张耒有诗奉答。<br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>同居陈州者有常安民（希古），苏过与之有唱和。<br /></div>
-----end



-----title
登封
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='87277f637d094378928b85185f475fac_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("87277f637d094378928b85185f475fac");'><span id='87277f637d094378928b85185f475fac_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1108&endYear=1108')">1108年</a>，37岁</div><div id='87277f637d094378928b85185f475fac' class='detail'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>在登封。苏过与吕本中、韩华国、刘知命等相与约游嵩山少室，因雨，暂未成行。十天之后，雨止，遂行，至大成岗，初见嵩少，登峻极顶，俱有诗。作品：《后旬日雨止遂行至大成岗初见嵩少》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《斜川集校注》卷三。）</span>《登峻极顶》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《斜川集校注》卷三。）</span><div id='poem_522757' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_522757' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/522757?labeling=true' target='_blank'>后旬日雨止遂行至大成冈初见嵩少</a><span class='authorDate'>（1108年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31323, "北宋", "苏过", "poem_title_522757")'>苏过</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_522757_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_522757'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_522757'>青山真似有情人，百里相迎列万屯。<div id='poem_sentence_0_522757_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_522757'>积翠已堪供爽气，群趋如欲避雄尊。<div id='poem_sentence_1_522757_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_522757'>少宽眼界尘埃外，却视醯鸡井陌喧。<div id='poem_sentence_2_522757_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_522757'>方信胸中有馀地，青丘云梦不劳吞。<div id='poem_sentence_3_522757_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_522757'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_522757_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_522650' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_522650' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/522650?labeling=true' id='poem_sentence_0_522650'>言登嵩高峰，结束两芒屩。<div id='poem_sentence_0_522650_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_522650'>摄衣上天梯，股栗战荦确。<div id='poem_sentence_1_522650_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_522650'>不知几流汗，跃出万仞壑。<div id='poem_sentence_2_522650_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_522650'>刚风被太虚，尘世俯下浊。<div id='poem_sentence_3_522650_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_522650'>依稀两仙童，遗我一丸药。<div id='poem_sentence_4_522650_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_522650'>平生井底蛙，未见宇宙廓。<div id='poem_sentence_5_522650_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_522650'>四维忽骞举，小知为磅礴。<div id='poem_sentence_6_522650_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_522650'>得穷恢谲眼，赖有腾趠脚。<div id='poem_sentence_7_522650_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_522650'>东观扶桑升，北瞰天河落。<div id='poem_sentence_8_522650_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_522650'>长须议雄尊，培塿眇庐霍。<div id='poem_sentence_9_522650_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_522650'></div><div id='poem_sentence_10_522650_comment'></div></div></div><br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>在登封。苏过见刘知命居士，约其卜居许下。有诗。作品：《赠知命刘居士卜居》<span id='poem_sentence_1_522841_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_522841'>眷余实畸人，雅兴世缘薄。<div id='poem_sentence_2_522841_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_522841_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_522841'>胸中横诗书，帐下馀猿鹤。<div id='poem_sentence_5_522841_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_522841_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_522841'>箕山宛在目，颍水清带郭。<div id='poem_sentence_8_522841_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' 自注：君与伯充诗，有欲卜居颍川志。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_522841_comment'></div></div><br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>在登封。游十日归，途中吕本中（居仁）作诗，苏过次韵。作品：《归途次吕居仁韵》<span -----title
宜兴
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='b3c3a39b57784b20890e48ab3acc7cba_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("b3c3a39b57784b20890e48ab3acc7cba");'><span id='b3c3a39b57784b20890e48ab3acc7cba_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1112&endYear=1112')">1112年</a>，41岁</div><div id='b3c3a39b57784b20890e48ab3acc7cba' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1112&endYear=1112')">1112年</a>　苏过尝适宜兴求食，行于横山，有诗。作品：《横山道中》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《斜川集校注》卷三。横山，在宜兴县。）</span><div id='poem_522795' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_522795' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/522795?labeling=true' target='_blank'>横山道中</a><span class='authorDate'>（1112年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31323, "北宋", "苏过", "poem_title_522795")'>苏过</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_522795_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_522795'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_522795'>物外闲人日月长，意行无复有重冈。<div id='poem_sentence_0_522795_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_522795'>林深步步衣裳湿，麦熟村村饼饵香。<div id='poem_sentence_1_522795_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_522795'>遥想云间下双舄，空怀仙子望三乡。<div id='poem_sentence_2_522795_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_522795'>欲寻好句供诗眼，旋逐东风堕眇茫。<div id='poem_sentence_3_522795_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_522795'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_522795_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
山西
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='6d9239da5fec4c6696983b5ea1964fab_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("6d9239da5fec4c6696983b5ea1964fab");'><span id='6d9239da5fec4c6696983b5ea1964fab_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1112&endYear=1112')">1112年</a>，41岁</div><div id='6d9239da5fec4c6696983b5ea1964fab' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1112&endYear=1112')">1112年</a>　监太原府税任上。苏过途经太行山，有《山行》诗。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《斜川集校注》卷四。）</span><div id='poem_522712' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_522712' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/522712?labeling=true' target='_blank'>山行</a><span class='authorDate'>（1112年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31323, "北宋", "苏过", "poem_title_522712")'>苏过</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_522712_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_522712'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_522712'>肩舆历尽黄茆冈，青山壁立耸大<span class='inlineComment2'>（疑当作太）</span>行。<div id='poem_sentence_0_522712_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_522712'>忽惊雷转山石裂，涛头千尺分钱塘。<div id='poem_sentence_1_522712_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_522712'>飞空雨雹寒崖碧，倒影垂虹射晴日。<div id='poem_sentence_2_522712_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_522712'>高岩俯瞰先目眩，杖策纵观森股慄。<div id='poem_sentence_3_522712_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_522712'>只疑天河泻地上，又恐滟滪飞山脊。<div id='poem_sentence_4_522712_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_522712'>猿猱悲鸣霜树折，虎豹震动山月黑。<div id='poem_sentence_5_522712_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_522712'>千年水石自成宝，下有蛟龙深莫测。<div id='poem_sentence_6_522712_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_522712'>明年岁旱当汝求，暴雨一声飞霹雳<span class='inlineComment2'>（以上《斜川集》卷二）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_7_522712_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_522712'></div><div id='poem_sentence_8_522712_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>

-----title
沁县
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='1f430fca004948119eb4f66609183a43_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("1f430fca004948119eb4f66609183a43");'><span id='1f430fca004948119eb4f66609183a43_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1112&endYear=1112')">1112年</a>，41岁</div><div id='1f430fca004948119eb4f66609183a43' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1112&endYear=1112')">1112年</a>　监太原府税任上。苏过行铜鞮山中，有诗。作品：《田家书事》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《斜川集校注》卷四。）</span><div id='poem_522775' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_522775' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/522775?labeling=true' target='_blank'>田家书事</a><span class='authorDate'>（1112年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31323, "北宋", "苏过", "poem_title_522775")'>苏过</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_522775_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_522775'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_522775'>路入铜鞮草木幽，不堪陇水断肠流。<div id='poem_sentence_0_522775_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_522775'>稍逢烟火人家住，似有桑麻场圃秋。<div id='poem_sentence_1_522775_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_522775'>生理艰难何所乐，石田辛苦若为收。<div id='poem_sentence_2_522775_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_522775'>天公长与丰年好，安得仁人每问牛。<div id='poem_sentence_3_522775_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_522775'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_522775_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
