-----title
太原
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='681be761d82f4a1eb18c080306ed4bb0_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("681be761d82f4a1eb18c080306ed4bb0");'><span id='681be761d82f4a1eb18c080306ed4bb0_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1112&endYear=1112')">1112年</a>，41岁</div><div id='681be761d82f4a1eb18c080306ed4bb0' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1112&endYear=1112')">1112年</a>　苏过至太原。张近（几仲）亦帅幕府到太原，赵鼎臣（承之）、孙勰（志康）、梁与可、孙海若俱为幕中客。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1112&endYear=1112')">1112年</a>　在阳曲，监太原府税。苏过代人作贺张近（几仲）启。作品：《代人贺启》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《斜川集校注》卷一〇。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1112&endYear=1112')">1112年</a>　在阳曲，监太原府税。赵鼎臣（承之）以紫岩诗相示，苏过次其韵。作品：《次韵承之紫岩长句》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《斜川集校注》卷四。）</span><div id='poem_522689' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_522689' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/522689?labeling=true' target='_blank'>次韵承之紫岩长句</a><span class='authorDate'>（1112年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31323, "北宋", "苏过", "poem_title_522689")'>苏过</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_522689_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_522689'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_522689'>乱山穷处闻鱼鼓，梵宇潭潭不知暑。<div id='poem_sentence_0_522689_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_522689'>当时麻衣此卜居，自启山林著蓝缕。<div id='poem_sentence_1_522689_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_522689'>飞空楼观惊造化，缥缈云间如帝所。<div id='poem_sentence_2_522689_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_522689'>道人疑是有道者，己不求人人自许。<div id='poem_sentence_3_522689_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_522689'>富儿争致千金多，贫者不辞筋力苦。<div id='poem_sentence_4_522689_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_522689'>若非足指按大地，荒山坐变琉璃宇。<div id='poem_sentence_5_522689_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_522689'>南阳持节奉诏归，夜上峥嵘携幕府。<div id='poem_sentence_6_522689_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_522689'>是时六月火令炽，千骑解鞍人按堵。<div id='poem_sentence_7_522689_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_522689'>登临岂为谢公赏，七子赋诗歌赵武。<div id='poem_sentence_8_522689_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_522689'>长廊月出清风生，古殿无人铃独语。<div id='poem_sentence_9_522689_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_522689'>公留三日看溪涨，白昼鱼虾落飞雨。<div id='poem_sentence_10_522689_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_522689'>我昔千里上太行，身世飘零悲逆旅。<div id='poem_sentence_11_522689_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_522689'>莫投紫岩稍自慰，欲扣僧房无可侣。<div id='poem_sentence_12_522689_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_522689'>有来野饷苜蓿饭，主人对客羞贫窭。<div id='poem_sentence_13_522689_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_522689'>何似元戎从掾吏，落日红旗照洲渚。<div id='poem_sentence_14_522689_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_522689'>椎牛酾<span class='inlineComment2'>（原误作作骊）</span>酒劳还役，号令三更传部伍。<div id='poem_sentence_15_522689_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_522689'>君能笔力记其事，句法更如山峻阻。<div id='poem_sentence_16_522689_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_522689'>一时豪放岂易得，况有幻怪供诗取。<div id='poem_sentence_17_522689_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_522689'>归来尚可诧朋友，云梦青丘俱不数。<div id='poem_sentence_18_522689_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_19_522689'>山川虽是风物殊，乐哉信美非吾土。<div id='poem_sentence_19_522689_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_20_522689'></div><div id='poem_sentence_20_522689_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1112&endYear=1112')">1112年</a>　在阳曲，监太原府税。太原府户曹参军任况之以诗相赠，苏过次韵。作品：《次韵任况之见赠》（其一）<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《斜川集校注》卷四。）</span>《次韵任况之见赠》（其二）<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《斜川集校注》卷四。）</span><div id='poem_522781' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_522781' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/522781?labeling=true' target='_blank'>次韵任况之见赠<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1112年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31323, "北宋", "苏过", "poem_title_522781")'>苏过</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_522781_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_522781'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_522781'>强辞南亩服儒冠，敢意青云便可干。<div id='poem_sentence_0_522781_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_522781'>似是马曹宜懒病，却惭鸡肋眷微官。<div id='poem_sentence_1_522781_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_522781'>眼前簿领成何用，梦里云山得暂欢。<div id='poem_sentence_2_522781_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_522781'>为问崎岖缘底事，鬓毛萧飒带围宽。<div id='poem_sentence_3_522781_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_522781'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_522781_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_522782' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_522782' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/522782?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1112年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_522782_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_522782'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_522782'>知君幼好切云冠，肯为浮名俛首干。<div id='poem_sentence_0_522782_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_522782'>应笑严徐吐唇吻，欲呼屈宋作衙官。<div id='poem_sentence_1_522782_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_522782'>地偏心远人知少，酒熟诗成我自欢。<div id='poem_sentence_2_522782_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_522782'>诗诵髯刘枯槁句，秕糠万事百忧宽。<div id='poem_sentence_3_522782_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_522782'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_522782_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1112&endYear=1112')">1112年</a>　在阳曲，监太原府税。赵鼎臣（承之）乞孙勰（志康）篆题“竹隐轩”，作诗，苏过亦次韵述志。作品：《和赵承之竹隐轩诗》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《斜川集校注》卷四。）</span><div id='poem_522623' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_522623' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/522623?labeling=true' target='_blank'>和赵承之竹隐轩诗</a><span class='authorDate'>（1112年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31323, "北宋", "苏过", "poem_title_522623")'>苏过</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_522623_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_522623'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_522623'>莫将不赀身，玩此有限年。<div id='poem_sentence_0_522623_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_522623'>心待三径足，何时赋归田。<div id='poem_sentence_1_522623_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_522623'>陶令甑无粟，阮公不言钱。<div id='poem_sentence_2_522623_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_522623'>可怜六尺躯，坐受众目怜。<div id='poem_sentence_3_522623_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_522623'>我正犯此戒，隐忧浩无边。<div id='poem_sentence_4_522623_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_522623'>幽怀祇自知，搅佩悲芳荃。<div id='poem_sentence_5_522623_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_522623'>闻君昔种竹，妙意诚超然。<div id='poem_sentence_6_522623_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_522623'>欲伴岁寒老，此计将终焉。<div id='poem_sentence_7_522623_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_522623'>郁郁环堵中，清风自招延。<div id='poem_sentence_8_522623_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_522623'>林泉有馀乐，簪组未易牵。<div id='poem_sentence_9_522623_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_522623'>早知文章累，不愿铭燕然。<div id='poem_sentence_10_522623_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_522623'>一为世所羁，遂与昔志捐。<div id='poem_sentence_11_522623_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_522623'>富贵岂不欲，孤高易隮颠。<div id='poem_sentence_12_522623_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_522623'>翻然回吾驾，造物报尔天。<div id='poem_sentence_13_522623_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_522623'>辛苦自缠缚，老蚕迷再眠。<div id='poem_sentence_14_522623_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_522623'>邯郸一梦破，怀抱良蹁跹。<div id='poem_sentence_15_522623_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_522623'>寄语山中友，信归在言前。<div id='poem_sentence_16_522623_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_522623'>耘治秋水净，扫洒春风妍。<div id='poem_sentence_17_522623_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_522623'>君言诚起余，肺腑不待镌。<div id='poem_sentence_18_522623_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_19_522623'>强颜为升斗，情态等市廛。<div id='poem_sentence_19_522623_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_20_522623'>投绂亦从此，过君请击鲜。<div id='poem_sentence_20_522623_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_21_522623'>虽微鹿门隐，不愧竹林贤。<div id='poem_sentence_21_522623_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_22_522623'>放怀绳墨外，俱作平地仙。<div id='poem_sentence_22_522623_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_23_522623'></div><div id='poem_sentence_23_522623_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1112&endYear=1112')">1112年</a>　在阳曲，监太原府税。崔钧自河东转运副使，转本路提刑，苏过代张近作贺启。作品：《代人贺启》（其一）<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《斜川集校注》卷八。《斜川集校注》有《代人贺启》（一）同题文二篇，此为其中一篇，首句为“光奉纶恩”）</span>《代人贺启》（其二）<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《斜川集校注》卷八。《斜川集校注》有《代人贺启》（二）同题文二篇，此为其中一篇，首二句为“显被明纶，升华延阁”）</span><div id='poem_1215240' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1215240' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1215240?labeling=true' target='_blank'>代人贺启<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其四 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1112年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31323, "北宋", "苏过", "poem_title_1215240")'>苏过</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1215240_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1215240'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1215240'>光奉纶恩，宠移使节。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1215240_comment'></div>辍从漕计，荣领宪司。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1215240_comment'></div>伏惟欢慰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1215240_comment'></div>恭以天子访治道于股肱，外台寄朝廷之耳目。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1215240_comment'></div>盖欲周知四方之利害，又俾黜陟一路之贤愚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1215240_comment'></div>故揽辔登车，举有澄清之志；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1215240_comment'></div>衣绣持斧，岂专逐捕之能？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1215240_comment'></div>上分宵旰之忧，旁助风行之化。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1215240_comment'></div>凡被选庸，莫非俊良。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1215240_comment'></div>谓宜推广好生之心，是以图任旧人共政。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1215240_comment'></div>某官圭璋重器，杞梓良材。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1215240_comment'></div>雅望足以镇浮，高才何止治剧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1215240_comment'></div>缓刑平狱，昔已著张廷尉之风；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1215240_comment'></div>积谷屯田，今复收赵充国之效。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1215240_comment'></div>恩还旧物，事类甘棠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1215240_comment'></div>遗爱重临，平反有待。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1215240_comment'></div>某缪膺使指，遂忝交承。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1215240_comment'></div>既忻易地之荣，又获告新之幸。</div><div id='poem_sentence_17_1215240_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_522599' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/522599?labeling=true' target='_blank'>次韵孙海见赠<span class='inlineComment2'>（用子美诗苏侯得数过，欢喜每倾倒）</span><span id='poem_title_522600_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_522600'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_522600'>神仙何渺茫，羽人想丹丘。<div id='poem_sentence_1_522602_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_522602'>夜光忽暗投，按剑惊卓荦。<div id='poem_sentence_2_522602_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_522602'></div><div id='poem_sentence_3_522602_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_522603' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_522603' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/522603?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其五 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1112年9月）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_522603_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_522603'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_522603'>自分麋鹿姿，食薇山之阿。<div id='poem_sentence_0_522603_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_522603'>不意设罗门，屡辱结驷过。<div id='poem_sentence_1_522603_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_522603'>清谈脱麈尾，奈此落月何。<div id='poem_sentence_2_522603_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_522603'></div><div id='poem_sentence_3_522603_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_522604' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_522604' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/522604?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其六 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1112年9月）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_522604_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_522604'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_522604'>仕宦才百日，邴公有馀欢。<div id='poem_sentence_0_522604_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_522604'>君今吏一邑，萧然怀抱安。<div id='poem_sentence_1_522604_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_522604'>回翔云间翮，退学鸿在磐。<div id='poem_sentence_2_522604_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_522604'></div><div id='poem_sentence_3_522604_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_522605' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_522605' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/522605?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其七 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1112年9月）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_522605_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_522605'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_522605'>簪组实外物，去来无愠喜。<div id='poem_sentence_0_522605_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_522605'>君看失马翁，倚伏寄妙理。<div id='poem_sentence_1_522605_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_522605'>顾我不亡存，斯言定非绮。<div id='poem_sentence_2_522605_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_522605'></div><div id='poem_sentence_3_522605_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_522606' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_522606' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/522606?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其八 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1112年9月）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_522606_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_522606'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_522606'>嗟余幼好奇，乘桴蹈南海。<div id='poem_sentence_0_522606_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_522606'>远游信虽美，惊梦今犹每。<div id='poem_sentence_1_522606_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_522606'>一饱类邯郸，苦乐何足骇。<div id='poem_sentence_2_522606_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_522606'></div><div id='poem_sentence_3_522606_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_522607' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_522607' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/522607?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其九 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1112年9月）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_522607_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_522607'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_522607'>居闲得三益，诗社毕此生。<div id='poem_sentence_0_522607_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_522607'>君才浩无际，可畏银河倾。<div id='poem_sentence_1_522607_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_522607'>孤军犯大敌，半夜壁屡惊。<div id='poem_sentence_2_522607_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_522607'></div><div id='poem_sentence_3_522607_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_522608' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_522608' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/522608?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其十 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1112年9月）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_522608_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_522608'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_522608'>君有中山好，严风彫塞草。<div id='poem_sentence_0_522608_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_522608'>日月遽如许，相从恨不早。<div id='poem_sentence_1_522608_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_522608'>当呼伯雅君，看子玉山倒。<div id='poem_sentence_2_522608_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_522608'></div><div id='poem_sentence_3_522608_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1112&endYear=1112')">1112年</a>　在阳曲，监太原府税。孙海若赴任，苏过作送叙，以招抚劳来民兵为嘱。作品：《送孙海若赴官河朔叙》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《斜川集校注》卷八。）</span><div id='poem_1215251' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1215251' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1215251?labeling=true' target='_blank'>送孙海若赴官河朔叙</a><span class='authorDate'>（1112年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31323, "北宋", "苏过", "poem_title_1215251")'>苏过</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1215251_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1215251'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1215251'>孟公绰为赵、魏老则优，不可为滕、薛大夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1215251_comment'></div>黄霸自二千石入为丞相，声名减于治郡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1215251_comment'></div>仆以谓此才有所短，不足以病贤者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1215251_comment'></div>子文治兵于睽，终朝而毕，不戮一人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1215251_comment'></div>子玉治兵于蔿，终日而毕，鞭七人，贯三人耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1215251_comment'></div>才则美矣，抑子文君子也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1215251_comment'></div>至于立威以举事，务杀以为能，儒者又所不为。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1215251_comment'></div>子玉真不学无术哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1215251_comment'></div>世之士大夫，少诵古人之书，盖将终身以之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1215251_comment'></div>大略出于孔、孟者，虽无能，世必称为长者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1215251_comment'></div>出于申、商，虽奇才，世必指为薄夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1215251_comment'></div>学之移人，有甚于齐、楚之咻；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1215251_comment'></div>渐摩习熟，不自知其为巫匠也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1215251_comment'></div>秦人任刀笔吏，其敝无恻隐之实。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1215251_comment'></div>故虎圈啬夫，以利口见用，则仁人君子，慨然争之，此风安可唱哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1215251_comment'></div>今国家专用儒术，政尚宽简，风俗日趋于厚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1215251_comment'></div>刑名之学，搢绅先生绝口不论。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1215251_comment'></div>以经术润饰吏事，彬彬然稍出矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1215251_comment'></div>卫人孙君海若，则其人也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1215251_comment'></div>以儒术佐忠武军幕府，官满，改中山安喜令，欣然而往。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1215251_comment'></div>或笑其抱王佐之材，不能干时取富贵，反自苦于簿书期会之间，将为乡遂里正分别曲直，不亦劳乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1215251_comment'></div>君曰：「不然，吾读书学为政也，有民有社，斯足以发吾平日之藏矣，何劳之有」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1215251_comment'></div>君之大略，温文深厚，不见喜愠，贯穿六艺，而尤长于《春秋》。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1215251_comment'></div>盖少时非孔氏、孟轲之文章，则他书不观也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1215251_comment'></div>如清庙之乐，钟磬琴瑟，锵然间作，郑卫桑濮、淫哇之声，何自作焉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1215251_comment'></div>持此而游朔方，将使犷悍木强之俗，变为礼义廉耻之风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1215251_comment'></div>仆又何言哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1215251_comment'></div>然中山府，昔吾先大夫之甘棠也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1215251_comment'></div>山川平易，控制北虏，独无关防之阻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1215251_comment'></div>先君尝论南北守盟，朝廷之德甚厚也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1215251_comment'></div>而边臣玩习无事，武备少弛，则非以称吾君委寄之意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1215251_comment'></div>边民有善骑射，耐辛苦，上下山谷，得虏之长技者，所在千百。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1215251_comment'></div>自为屯聚，以卫亲戚坟墓，其来远矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1215251_comment'></div>傥能闻诸朝，少有以镇拊劳来之，并塞精兵，坐获数万，不烦县官一粒之费，凛然有长城千里之固，则虏不敢动矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1215251_comment'></div>昔李抱真守泽、潞，教民为射，官给弓矢而蠲其徭赋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1215251_comment'></div>山东有警，昭义步兵冠天下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1215251_comment'></div>古人思患，预防有如此者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1215251_comment'></div>先君不果成而去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1215251_comment'></div>愿吾友志此言，访诸邑人之耆老，而以告夫元帅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1215251_comment'></div>有志于经远者，此太平之长策也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1215251_comment'></div>君为县令，出入阡陌，当得其详。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1215251_comment'></div>仆是以为献。</div><div id='poem_sentence_41_1215251_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1112&endYear=1112')">1112年</a>　在阳曲，监太原府税。苏过亲家常子然卒，过作文遥祭之。作品：《祭常子然文》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《斜川集校注》卷八。）</span><div id='poem_1215283' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1215283' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1215283?labeling=true' target='_blank'>祭常子然文</a><span class='authorDate'>（1112年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31323, "北宋", "苏过", "poem_title_1215283")'>苏过</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1215283_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1215283'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1215283'>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1215283_comment'></div>诗礼道丧，仅不控颐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1215283_comment'></div>以得为荣，以失为悲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1215283_comment'></div>陋矣稽古，射利乘时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1215283_comment'></div>若商贾然，垄断物宜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1215283_comment'></div>彼君子者，以心为师。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1215283_comment'></div>譬犹农夫，载耘载耔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1215283_comment'></div>虽有饥馑，吾志不移。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1215283_comment'></div>猗欤子然，信道自持。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1215283_comment'></div>抱其家学，衡吾气机。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1215283_comment'></div>如资章甫，越人何为？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1215283_comment'></div>身则不偶，论无少卑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1215283_comment'></div>白首为郎，理复何疑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1215283_comment'></div>嗟我先君，昔迁南夷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1215283_comment'></div>万里致书，公时布衣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1215283_comment'></div>同臭使然，忘其祸危。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1215283_comment'></div>先君即世，义不敢遗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1215283_comment'></div>请婚后人，不谋于龟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1215283_comment'></div>嗟我兄弟，坎𡒄无依。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1215283_comment'></div>方凿圆枘，公独见私。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1215283_comment'></div>倒其廪囷，决其藩篱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1215283_comment'></div>我倡子和，终日不违。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1215283_comment'></div>曰我有财，汝其宰之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1215283_comment'></div>岂其一别，讣音遽随。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1215283_comment'></div>委蜕而行，药不待医。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1215283_comment'></div>为仁必寿，天不吾欺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1215283_comment'></div>云何抱璞，竟不少施。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1215283_comment'></div>易箦之言，我不获知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1215283_comment'></div>两楹之奠，莫荐其归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1215283_comment'></div>惟以鄙词，致兹涕洟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1215283_comment'></div>想其音声，欬然在帷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1215283_comment'></div>庶几英灵，举此一卮。</div><div id='poem_sentence_31_1215283_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1112&endYear=1112')">1112年</a>　在阳曲，监太原府税。重九前数日，赵鼎臣（承之）作诗呈孙勰（志康）、苏过，过次其韵。作品：《次韵承之重九》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《斜川集校注》卷四。赵鼎臣所作诗为《重阳前数日夜坐不寐偶思江南塞北旧游作诗呈孙志康诸友》，见《竹隐畸士集》卷三。）</span><div id='poem_522691' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_522691' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/522691?labeling=true' target='_blank'>次韵承之重九</a><span class='authorDate'>（1112年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31323, "北宋", "苏过", "poem_title_522691")'>苏过</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_522691_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_522691'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_522691'>庾郎自诳誇重九，北海常类客无酒。<div id='poem_sentence_0_522691_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_522691'>肯教白发负黄花，不为虚名留岘首。<div id='poem_sentence_1_522691_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_522691'>人生能换几星霜，我非石心与木肠。<div id='poem_sentence_2_522691_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_522691'>乾愁漫解祇自慰，消长只系吾行藏。<div id='poem_sentence_3_522691_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_522691'>弃书学剑犹有得，西斩楼兰北疏勒。<div id='poem_sentence_4_522691_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_522691'>从军直到单于台，封侯万户何人哉。<div id='poem_sentence_5_522691_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_522691'>图形未许凌图上，草檄观君试豪放。<div id='poem_sentence_6_522691_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_522691'>山阴回时迹已陈，高阳大醉情何畅。<div id='poem_sentence_7_522691_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_522691'>为君悲歌和哀筝，请君更草丽人行。<div id='poem_sentence_8_522691_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_522691'>吴姬赵女两愁绝，一笑当时空目成。<div id='poem_sentence_9_522691_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_522691'>行行且作归装束，子云校书入天禄。<div id='poem_sentence_10_522691_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_522691'>一杯且复中圣贤，周南留滞谁我怜。<div id='poem_sentence_11_522691_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_522691'>买田早约鸱夷子，相与躬耕不计年。<div id='poem_sentence_12_522691_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_522691'></div><div id='poem_sentence_13_522691_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1112&endYear=1112')">1112年</a>　在阳曲，监太原府税。苏过有《代人贺启》文。（其四）<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《斜川集校注》卷八。此文具体作时不详，姑系于此。）</span>《代人贺启》（其五）<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《斜川集校注》卷八。此文具体作时不详，姑系于此。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1112&endYear=1112')">1112年10月</a>　十月，叔父苏辙卒，苏过奔丧于许。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='299a07e125c04b119ae0610640d39e70_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("299a07e125c04b119ae0610640d39e70");'><span id='299a07e125c04b119ae0610640d39e70_link' href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1112&endYear=1112')">1112年</a>　在阳曲，监太原府税。苏过有《代满宪谢换官表》文。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《斜川集校注》卷八。此文具体作时不详，姑系于此。）</span><div id='poem_1215220' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1215220' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1215220?labeling=true' target='_blank'>代满宪谢换官表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1112年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31323, "北宋", "苏过", "poem_title_1215220")'>苏过</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1215220_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1215220'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1215220'>伏奉告命，换授臣武功大夫者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1215220_comment'></div>官称非古，必欲正名；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1215220_comment'></div>诏命自天，遂颁新渥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1215220_comment'></div>宠以训词之温厚，允为臣子之光华。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1215220_comment'></div>抚己若惊，受恩知愧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1215220_comment'></div>恭惟先帝追三代之典，建百官之名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1215220_comment'></div>粲然虞夏之文，革去汉唐之陋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1215220_comment'></div>况大明之继照，述先志之未遑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1215220_comment'></div>亟诏有司，一刊右列。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1215220_comment'></div>致兹异数，亦及微臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1215220_comment'></div>为官择人，愧何以从士夫之后？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1215220_comment'></div>循名责实，又不能奋尺寸之功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1215220_comment'></div>徒窃宠荣，益惭尸素。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1215220_comment'></div>此盖伏遇皇帝陛下尧仁天纵，汤德日新。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1215220_comment'></div>跻大有为之心，行若稽古之政。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1215220_comment'></div>经文纬武，俾无旷职之臣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1215220_comment'></div>修废举材，下逮干城之贱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1215220_comment'></div>臣敢不服勤夙夜，祗畏简书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1215220_comment'></div>以徇义捐躯为事君，以养兵训戎为报国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1215220_comment'></div>誓益殚于犬马，庶少答于生成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1215220_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_20_1215220_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1113&endYear=1113')">1113年</a>　在阳曲，监太原府税。初春，苏过归自颍昌，任况之有诗相劳，过次其韵。作品：《自颍昌归任况之有诗次其韵》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《斜川集校注》卷四。任况之诗未详。）</span>《次韵任况之》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《斜川集校注》卷四。任况之诗未详。）</span><div id='poem_522783' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_522783' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/522783?labeling=true' target='_blank'>自颍昌归任况之有诗次其韵</a><span class='authorDate'>（1113年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a class='poemContent' id='poem_content_522783'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_522783'>暂抛彭泽故园归，趁见春山笋蕨齐。<div id='poem_sentence_0_522783_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_522783'>不谓简书诚可畏，便寻渔钓欲重携。<div id='poem_sentence_1_522783_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_522783'>故人念我勤车马，走笔题诗寄象犀。<div id='poem_content_522609'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_522609'>溪山岂远人，吏缚苦难到。<div id='poem_sentence_0_522609_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_522609'>岂惟畏简书，谁与同嗜好。<div id='poem_sentence_1_522609_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_522609'>我作汝颍行，蹉跎春事老。<div id='poem_sentence_2_522609_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_522609'>况逢怀抱恶，千里风霜冒。<div id='poem_sentence_3_522609_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_522609'>故人知我归，尺书远见劳。<div id='poem_sentence_4_522609_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_522609'>似寻西溪约，故遣一介报。<div id='poem_sentence_5_522609_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_522609'>何时脱缰锁，著我林泉帽。<div id='poem_sentence_6_522609_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_content_522790'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_522790'>春事依稀见一班，山花灼灼强施丹。<div id='poem_sentence_0_522790_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_title_522791_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_522791'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_522791'>樽馀旧压蒲萄绿，盘有南珍荔子丹。<div id='poem_sentence_0_522791_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_522791'>草草春光虽未称，人人酒令暂须宽。<div id='poem_sentence_1_522791_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_522791'>兴来勿废无何饮，老去难寻特地欢。<div id='poem_sentence_2_522791_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_522791'>慰我穷愁真待子，凭诗寄与故人看。<div ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1113&endYear=1113')">1113年</a>　在阳曲，监太原府税。苏过与任况之、贾子庄相约游西溪，子庄不至，况之有诗怨之，过次其韵。作品：《子庄约况之游西溪不至任有诗次其韵》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《斜川集校注》卷四。任况之诗未详。）</span><div id='poem_sentence_1_522621_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_522621'>念我江湖人，久负渔樵约。<div id='poem_sentence_2_522621_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_522621'>安得漫浪游，时解冠带缚。<div id='poem_sentence_3_522621_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_522621'>令尹我辈人，孤标寡然诺。<div id='poem_sentence_4_522621_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_522621'>晚逢任参军，诗思涌泉落。<div id='poem_sentence_5_522621_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_522621'>裹饭从子来，隐几访南郭。<div id='poem_sentence_6_522621_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_522621'>庶结三友欢，一笑忘杯酌。<div id='poem_sentence_7_522621_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_522621'>西溪渌已涨，渚柳风交错。<div id='poem_sentence_8_522621_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_522621'>目断君不来，孤鸿没山脚。<div id='poem_sentence_9_522621_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_522621'></div><div id='poem_sentence_10_522621_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1113&endYear=1113')">1113年</a>　在阳曲，监太原府税。任况之建樗隐轩，苏过题诗寄意。作品：《寄题任况之樗翁轩诗》<span id='poem_sentence_1_522624'>柯为直见伐，根中万乘器。<div id='poem_sentence_1_522624_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_522624'>自贻斧斤厄，信坐文章累。<div class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31323, "北宋", "苏过", "poem_title_522762")'>苏过</a></span><br /><div ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1113&endYear=1113')">1113年</a>　在阳曲，监太原府税。苏过雨中与孙勰（志康）、赵鼎臣（承之）游柳溪，捕鱼，有诗记之。作品：《雨中游柳溪呈志康诸公》<span class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/522780?labeling=true' target='_blank'>雨中游柳溪呈志康诸公</a><span class='authorDate'>（1113年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31323, "北宋", "苏过", "poem_title_522780")'>苏过</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_522780_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_522780'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_522780'>脱我芒鞋与杖藜，强随车盖著荷衣。<div id='poem_sentence_0_522780_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_522780'>青山绿水苦相唤，细雨斜风不忍归。<div id='poem_sentence_1_522780_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_522780'>幸有琉璃倾琥珀，何妨粉黛湿珠玑。<div id='poem_sentence_2_522780_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_522780'>潇湘起我江湖<span class='inlineComment2'>（原校：一作烟波）</span>兴，只恐扁舟明日非。<div id='poem_sentence_3_522780_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_522780'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_522780_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_522701' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_522701' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/522701?labeling=true' target='_blank'>志康得鱼或劝舍之诸公有诗议未判吾谁适从亦赋一篇</a><span class='authorDate'>（1113年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31323, "北宋", "苏过", "poem_title_522701")'>苏过</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_522701_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_522701'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_522701'>溪鱼有如缘木求，纵有琐细不受钩。<div id='poem_sentence_0_522701_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_522701'>我居恨不如江头，长江巨浪一苇游。<div id='poem_sentence_1_522701_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_522701'>得鱼满船鲂鲤鯈，暮归献俘烹魁酋。<div id='poem_sentence_2_522701_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_522701'>迩来越吟思命驺，斋厨空无萍藻羞。<div id='poem_sentence_3_522701_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_522701'>披抉泥沙穷涧陬，掇拾小鲜馔糗糇。<div id='poem_sentence_4_522701_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_522701'>三咽井上或可侔，先生道眼无全牛。<div id='poem_sentence_5_522701_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_522701'>虚心触物如虚舟，独未辟谷师留侯。<div id='poem_sentence_6_522701_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_522701'>手持巨饵安所投，弹铗时有冯驩忧。<div id='poem_sentence_7_522701_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_522701'>南音不变钟仪囚，朝齑暮盐意则悠。<div id='poem_sentence_8_522701_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_522701'>渠肯嗜杀对血流，欲引西江盖无由。<div id='poem_sentence_9_522701_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_522701'>升斗小惠不知赒，吾言非夸亦非媮。<div id='poem_sentence_10_522701_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_522701'>一饱等是充饥喉，暴殄天物神所不，杜陵有诗请君讴。</div><div id='poem_sentence_11_522701_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1113&endYear=1113')">1113年</a>　在阳曲，监太原府税。秋，太原府通判张仲纲（彦政）任满归京师，赵鼎臣、苏过皆有诗送别。作品：《送张倅彦政赴阙》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《斜川集校注》卷四。）</span><div id='poem_522555' id='poem_sentence_0_522555_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_522555'>太行如登天，憔悴欲谁语。<div id='poem_sentence_1_522555_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_522555'>青衫百僚底，屏气不敢吐。<div id='poem_sentence_2_522555_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_522555'>谓当哭途穷，何但折腰膂。<div id='poem_sentence_5_522555'>敢论通家旧，窃欲比文举<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_5_522555_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1113&endYear=1113')">1113年11月19日</a>　在阳曲，监太原府税。十一月十九日，大雪，赵鼎臣（承之）、梁与可访贾子庄，孙勰（志康）不得与，有诗怨之，苏过亦次韵。作品：《大雪日赵承之梁与可访贾子庄……》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《斜川集校注》卷四。）</span><div id='poem_522687' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_522687' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/522687?labeling=true' target='_blank'>大雪日赵承之梁与可访贾子庄饮爽亭孙志康不得预故有诗怨之亦次韵和一首</a><span class='authorDate'>（1113年11月19日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: id='poem_content_522687'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_522687'>三士高谈常绝席，不数汉庭人九尺。<div id='poem_sentence_0_522687_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_522687'>雪中忽到剡溪行，狂饮学髡俱一石。<div id='poem_sentence_1_522687_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_522687'>不教彭宣到后堂，只供爽气干陵冈。<div id='poem_sentence_2_522687_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_522687'>忍寒排闼计大误，夫子莫悔不得将。<div id='poem_sentence_3_522687_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_522687'>夜归过我天正黑，灯影照坐如僧房。<div id='poem_sentence_4_522687_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_522687'>峨冠切云服亦奇，胜游何不早遣知。<div id='poem_sentence_5_522687_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_522687'>风花瞥眼同一霎，欲追此欢将奈若。<div id='poem_sentence_6_522687_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_522687'>人间何往不自适，陵生且复为陵舄。<div id='poem_sentence_7_522687_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_522687'></div><div id='poem_sentence_8_522687_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1113&endYear=1113')">1113年</a>　在阳曲，监太原府税。陈观性、张子先俱有《喜雪》诗，苏过次韵。作品：《和清源陈观性喜雪》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《斜川集校注》卷四。）</span>《次韵张子先喜雪》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《斜川集校注》卷四。）</span><div id='poem_522769' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_522769' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/522769?labeling=true' target='_blank'>和清源陈观性喜雪</a><span class='authorDate'>（1113年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31323, "北宋", "苏过", "poem_title_522769")'>苏过</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_522769_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_522769'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_522769'>斗酒豚蹄语未终，飞花弄态作冲融。<div id='poem_sentence_0_522769_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_522769'>寒威尚带嘉平腊，和气争先养物风。<div id='poem_sentence_1_522769_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_522769'>爽入西山千仞色，润添南亩一犁工。<div id='poem_sentence_2_522769_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_522769'>先生休道催科拙，趁著河东岁屡<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>丰。<div id='poem_sentence_3_522769_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_522769'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_522769_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_522769'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_3_522769_0'>⑴ 原作屦，据赵本改</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_522769_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_522768' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_522768' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/522768?labeling=true' target='_blank'>次韵张子先喜雪</a><span class='authorDate'>（1113年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31323, "北宋", "苏过", "poem_title_522768")'>苏过</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_522768_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_522768'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_522768'>信道东君有化工，剪裁花雨落春风。<div id='poem_sentence_0_522768_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_522768'>忽惊区脱无馀地，变作瑶池第一宫。<div id='poem_sentence_1_522768_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_522768'>南亩麦秋先作瑞，西山玉粒未教融。<div id='poem_sentence_2_522768_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_522768'>旅人共助田夫喜，一饱遥知饼饵丰。<div id='poem_sentence_3_522768_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_522768'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_522768_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1114&endYear=1114')">1114年</a>　在阳曲，监太原府税。初春苦寒，苏过有诗呻吟。作品：《苦寒行》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《斜川集校注》卷四。）</span><div id='poem_522710' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_522710' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/522710?labeling=true' target='_blank'>苦寒行</a><span class='authorDate'>（1114年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31323, "北宋", "苏过", "poem_title_522710")'>苏过</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_522710_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_522710'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_522710'>句芒司春懦不职，纵使玄冥氧凌轹。<div id='poem_sentence_0_522710_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_522710'>三冬肃杀归尔时，长物岂容长凛慄。<div id='poem_sentence_1_522710_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_522710'>北风吹水冰成梁，急雷盖地云翻墨。<div id='poem_sentence_2_522710_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_522710'>坐令贫士高掩扃，安得重裘代絺绤。<div id='poem_sentence_3_522710_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_522710'>春泥漫漫薪不属，破灶无烟愁四壁。<div id='poem_sentence_4_522710_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_522710'>饥吟拥鼻涕流澌，皲指结衣僵欲直。<div id='poem_sentence_5_522710_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_522710'>水南水北多高士，去作达官金马客。<div id='poem_sentence_6_522710_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_522710'>朱门碧瓦照通都，耻著麻衣羡狐白。<div id='poem_sentence_7_522710_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_522710'>问余何为不录录，反老抱关守甔石。<div id='poem_sentence_8_522710_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_522710'>十日春寒何所觊，坐想朝阳生屋隙。<div id='poem_sentence_9_522710_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_522710'>愿将挟纩同斯人，杜陵大厦无由得。<div id='poem_sentence_10_522710_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_522710'>南荣炙背直万钱，燠燠此衣安且吉。<div id='poem_sentence_11_522710_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_522710'></div><div id='poem_sentence_12_522710_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1114&endYear=1114')">1114年</a>　在阳曲，监太原府税。清源县令凿池引渠，植芙蓉，建亭为娱，寄诗告苏过。过亦作诗寄之。作品：《清源大夫吴人到官之数月……》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《斜川集校注》卷四。）</span><div id='poem_522708' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_522708' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/522708?labeling=true' target='_blank'>清源大夫吴人到官之数月凿池引泉植芙蕖大变晋俗遂忘江湖之想作诗寄题芙蓉亭</a><span class='authorDate'>（1114年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31323, "北宋", "苏过", "poem_title_522708")'>苏过</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_522708_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_522708'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_522708'>先生腹有五车书，宜著天禄与石渠。<div id='poem_sentence_0_522708_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_522708'>一日不可食无鱼，何不置之于江湖。<div id='poem_sentence_1_522708_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_522708'>迩来得邑古塞隅，饮酪披毳如羌胡。<div id='poem_sentence_2_522708_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_522708'>汾水浊恶山童枯，不知先生何为娱。<div id='poem_sentence_3_522708_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_522708'>忽然寄诗遣长须，报我县圃开榛芜。<div id='poem_sentence_4_522708_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_522708'>昔为沮洳今可潴，下灌粳稻池之馀。<div id='poem_sentence_5_522708_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_522708'>清流映带红芙蕖，炯然不染先生如。<div id='poem_sentence_6_522708_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_522708'>簿书扰扰徒喧呼，不妨行吟学三闾。<div id='poem_sentence_7_522708_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_522708'>吏民已化愚溪愚，能和紫芝于蔿于。<div id='poem_sentence_8_522708_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_522708'>教条自简俗自纾，三尺不犯鞭与蒲。<div id='poem_sentence_9_522708_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_522708'>愿君越吟小踟蹰，晋楚未觉肝胆殊。<div id='poem_sentence_10_522708_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_522708'>长短莫较鹤与凫，弹铗且缓归来乎。<div id='poem_sentence_11_522708_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_522708'></div><div id='poem_sentence_12_522708_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1114&endYear=1114')">1114年</a>　在阳曲，监太原府税。太原府帅张近曾荐苏过于朝，过作启谢之。作品：《谢张帅启》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《斜川集校注》卷八。）</span><div id='poem_1215227' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1215227' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1215227?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢张帅启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1114年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31323, "北宋", "苏过", "poem_title_1215227")'>苏过</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1215227_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1215227'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1215227'>服劳关市，愧无异于稠人；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1215227_comment'></div>忽玷品题，宠实逾于华衮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1215227_comment'></div>窃以士不自重，则廉耻之风息；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1215227_comment'></div>公不灭私，则请谒之路行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1215227_comment'></div>夫惟自重而不妄登门，然后至公乐为之推毂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1215227_comment'></div>岂独求人者惟恐后，盖念知己者良亦难。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1215227_comment'></div>所取一言，故叔向以得鬷明为喜；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1215227_comment'></div>不愿万户，而太白以见荆州为荣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1215227_comment'></div>乃知分义之相投，方为取与之两得。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1215227_comment'></div>如某簪裳衰胄，樗栎散材。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1215227_comment'></div>效官米盐刀笔之间，救过簿书期会之役。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1215227_comment'></div>折腰五斗，粗安燕幕之危；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1215227_comment'></div>糊口四方，仅免牛衣之泣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1215227_comment'></div>故平居不敢以竿牍自致，而左右亦莫借齿牙先容。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1215227_comment'></div>夫何荐鹗之书，下取抱关之吏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1215227_comment'></div>增光蔀屋，改观同僚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1215227_comment'></div>重惭枯朽之馀，实费吹嘘之力。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1215227_comment'></div>此盖某官量包山薮，言重蓍龟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1215227_comment'></div>羽仪当世之公卿，绮藻一代之人物。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1215227_comment'></div>兼收并用，将嘉善而矜不能；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1215227_comment'></div>舍短取长，抑与人而不求备。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1215227_comment'></div>遂令无用，滥厕甄收。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1215227_comment'></div>若非藏垢而匿瑕，孰肯左提而右挈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1215227_comment'></div>昔晏婴取士，尚赎过于缧囚；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1215227_comment'></div>而赵武好贤，尝求人于筦库。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1215227_comment'></div>某敢不激昂衰钝，祗畏简书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1215227_comment'></div>进不负于所知，退无惭于素守。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1215227_comment'></div>以此图报，岂其敢忘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1215227_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_28_1215227_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1114&endYear=1114')">1114年</a>　在阳曲，监太原府税。河东提刑崔钧（元播）荐苏过，过有谢启。作品：《谢荐举状》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《斜川集校注》卷八。）</span><div id='poem_1215226' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1215226' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1215226?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢荐举状</a><span class='authorDate'>（1114年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31323, "北宋", "苏过", "poem_title_1215226")'>苏过</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1215226_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1215226'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1215226'>蜩鸠小技，宁有意于云霄；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1215226_comment'></div>樗栎散材，固难欺于匠石。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1215226_comment'></div>偶窃簪裳之馀胄，得齿搢绅之后尘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1215226_comment'></div>盖将糊口于四方，敢惮折腰于五斗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1215226_comment'></div>抱关击柝，已绝望于清流；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1215226_comment'></div>毁瓦画墁，尚庶几于食志。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1215226_comment'></div>然自念征商至贱，种发可羞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1215226_comment'></div>不过效米盐刀笔之勤，仅稍免簿书期会之责。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1215226_comment'></div>分甘下走，才不逾人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1215226_comment'></div>锥处囊中，虽未忘于颖脱；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1215226_comment'></div>菌蒸枯朽，实倍费于吹嘘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1215226_comment'></div>岂谓荐书，忽光蔀屋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1215226_comment'></div>顾惭名姓，辱借齿牙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1215226_comment'></div>某官德并圭璋，量包山薮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1215226_comment'></div>言足以绮藻当代，学足以羽仪清朝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1215226_comment'></div>嘉善而矜不能，出于天性；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1215226_comment'></div>举贤而赦小过，欲广人材。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1215226_comment'></div>遂令一介之微，亦预四科之选。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1215226_comment'></div>自量无用，初乏先容。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1215226_comment'></div>傥非藏垢而匿瑕，孰肯左提而右挈？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1215226_comment'></div>昔晏婴取士，尚赎过于缧囚；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1215226_comment'></div>而赵武好贤，常求人于筦库。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1215226_comment'></div>某敢不激昂驽钝，祗畏简书！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1215226_comment'></div>进不负于所知，退无惭于素守。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1215226_comment'></div>寸有长而尺有短，尽荷包荒；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1215226_comment'></div>日不足而岁有馀，益图报称。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1215226_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_26_1215226_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1114&endYear=1114')">1114年7月</a>　在阳曲，监太原府税。七月，苏过作太原兵马钤辖孙贵（和叔）墓志铭。作品：《孙团练墓志铭》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《斜川集校注》卷八。）</span><div id='poem_1215280' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1215280' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1215280?labeling=true' target='_blank'>孙团练墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（政和四年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31323, "北宋", "苏过", "poem_title_1215280")'>苏过</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1215280_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1215280'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1215280'>古者，天子置卫曰虎贲，《书》云：「有熊罴之士，不二心之臣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1215280_comment'></div>其来尚矣！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1215280_comment'></div>有宋选择天下奇才勇士，以隶亲军，号曰「诸班」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1215280_comment'></div>居则以壮国容，出则以威疆埸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1215280_comment'></div>故功名之士，多由此涂出。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1215280_comment'></div>大者赐旄钺，其次皆得称名将。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1215280_comment'></div>故太原府路兵马都钤辖孙公其人也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1215280_comment'></div>公讳贵，字和叔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1215280_comment'></div>其先赵州赞皇人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1215280_comment'></div>自大父始迁河东平定军，因家焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1215280_comment'></div>世为农。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1215280_comment'></div>公生而异于群儿，不好戏弄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1215280_comment'></div>既长，状貌颀然，智虑倜傥，里人皆异之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1215280_comment'></div>公亦稍以功名自期，志不在畎亩间也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1215280_comment'></div>会国家招置新军，公即自诣太守，请补其缺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1215280_comment'></div>太守冯公恽奇其状，以为「他日必富贵，吾所不逮」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1215280_comment'></div>乃留为钤下吏，给其衣服，俾习弓弩射艺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1215280_comment'></div>不踰年，能挽强超乘，绝于等辈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1215280_comment'></div>是时，朝廷诏下诸路，选才武以实班卫，太守即以公应诏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1215280_comment'></div>遣之日，祝曰：「富贵无相忘」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1215280_comment'></div>其爱重之如此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1215280_comment'></div>至京师，充御龙直人员。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1215280_comment'></div>每较艺，常居第一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1215280_comment'></div>入卫十年，天子亲御殿阅试诸班，以公绝伦，遂授东头供奉官，河东都总管司准备差使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1215280_comment'></div>是岁，熙宁八年也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1215280_comment'></div>丞相韩康公帅太原，夏雨不止，汾河暴溢，欲坏堤败庐舍，亟遣公护筑之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1215280_comment'></div>公昼夜庐于堤上，自执朴以巡役，人为危之而公卒不动，堤以完安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1215280_comment'></div>韩公喜曰：「全吾民者，君之力也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1215280_comment'></div>未几，除麟州横阳堡兵马监押。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1215280_comment'></div>议者请麟、府、封三州巡寨官，不宜用内郡人且无边劳者，恐缓急不足倚办，委将臣沙汰之，而用土人之有功者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1215280_comment'></div>公独以骁果勇健为军马使张公世矩所惜，留而不遣，议者不能夺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1215280_comment'></div>元祐六年，为河东第一路副将，驻横阳堡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1215280_comment'></div>时夏贼梁乙逋犯麟、府，众十五万。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1215280_comment'></div>诸寨闭壁，公独毅然不顾，数出奇兵挠击之，杀伤甚多。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1215280_comment'></div>且开门示閒暇，贼疑不敢近。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1215280_comment'></div>又遣偏裨领骑捕得贼生口，尽知其虚实，归有日矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1215280_comment'></div>乃出家赀，募死士，从閒道约麟、府诸将，告以贼退期，使设伏邀击其怠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1215280_comment'></div>诸将议不合，贼鼓行而西，莫有谁何者，士气愤沮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1215280_comment'></div>于是始服公忠勇，而惜其谋之不用也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1215280_comment'></div>公自授官，往来河西几三十年，熟知夷虏之情状，山川之险易，部落之多寡，故机不妄发。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1215280_comment'></div>及其虑胜而动，忠义所激，则常为士卒先。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1215280_comment'></div>凡与贼遇，大小十九战，未尝败北，捕获首虏以千计。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1215280_comment'></div>积功累官至昭州团练使，爵开国伯，食邑七百户。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1215280_comment'></div>崇宁之初，左右有言公姓名于上前者，有旨召诣阙陛对。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1215280_comment'></div>称旨，即除太原府路兵马钤辖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1215280_comment'></div>大观中，升都钤辖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1215280_comment'></div>公老矣，边鄙无事，乃学方士养生服饵之说。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1215280_comment'></div>无何，疡生于首。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1215280_comment'></div>公曰：「是命也，医何为哉」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1215280_comment'></div>疾遂革。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1215280_comment'></div>以政和二年六月十九日终于太原官舍，享年七十有三。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1215280_comment'></div>政和四年七月十二日，卜葬于真定府元氏县某村之新茔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1215280_comment'></div>公性沈毅有谋，驭士宽简，绝甘分少，能得人死力。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1215280_comment'></div>又好赒乡人之急，平生所得廪赐，施与略尽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1215280_comment'></div>属纩之日，家无馀赀，人为嗟叹！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1215280_comment'></div>然本起于田家子，初不知兵，猝然见奇于冯公，竟有立于世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1215280_comment'></div>昔唐李绩临事遣将，必观其人奇庞福艾者付之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1215280_comment'></div>或问其故，答曰：「薄命者不足与成功」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1215280_comment'></div>抑亦用人之一端也欤！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1215280_comment'></div>公之曾祖讳同，祖讳通，皆不仕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1215280_comment'></div>考讳诚，以公贵，至太子左卫率府率，赠官至左千牛卫大将军。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1215280_comment'></div>妣李氏，赠和义郡太君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1215280_comment'></div>公娶鲍氏，封仁寿县君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1215280_comment'></div>子二人：长曰翊，以战功至武节郎；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1215280_comment'></div>次曰靖，忠翊郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1215280_comment'></div>孙男四人：昂、炳，皆承节郎；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1215280_comment'></div>皓，承信郎；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1215280_comment'></div>季未名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1215280_comment'></div>孙女五人，尚幼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1215280_comment'></div>过始官于太原之岁也，公已病，不及见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1215280_comment'></div>既没，其子翊状公行事以来请铭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1215280_comment'></div>过惟孝子仁人，思欲扬其亲之美，其可辞焉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1215280_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_72_1215280'>虽甚盛德，谁能去兵？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1215280_comment'></div>赳赳桓桓，天实之生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1215280_comment'></div>公在内朝，王之爪牙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1215280_comment'></div>出卫社稷，能执干戈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1215280_comment'></div>以征则克，以守则固。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1215280_comment'></div>惟忠与孝，用训其旅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1215280_comment'></div>既显其亲，亦令其名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1215280_comment'></div>毕万七战，死犹有荣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1215280_comment'></div>不贪天功，边邑以宁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1215280_comment'></div>子孙绵绵，吾是以铭。</div><div id='poem_sentence_81_1215280_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1114&endYear=1114')">1114年</a>　在阳曲，监太原府税。张近（几仲）奉招还朝，其幕僚孙勰（志康）、赵鼎臣（承之）作诗送，苏过亦次韵。作品：《张几仲召还朝其幕府赵承之送行至漳水……》（其一）<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《斜川集校注》卷四。）</span>《张几仲召还朝其幕府赵承之送行至漳水……》（其二）<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《斜川集校注》卷四。）</span>《张几仲召还朝其幕府赵承之送行至漳水……》（其三）<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《斜川集校注》卷四。）</span>《张几仲召还朝其幕府赵承之送行至漳水……》（其四）<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《斜川集校注》卷四。）</span>《张几仲召还朝其幕府赵承之送行至漳水……》（其五）<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《斜川集校注》卷四。）</span>《张几仲召还朝其幕府赵承之送行至漳水……》（其六）<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《斜川集校注》卷四。）</span>《张几仲召还朝其幕府赵承之送行至漳水……》（其七）<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《斜川集校注》卷四。）</span>《张几仲召还朝其幕府赵承之送行至漳水……》（其八）<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《斜川集校注》卷四。）</span>《张几仲召还朝其幕府赵承之送行至漳水……》（其九）<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《斜川集校注》卷四。）</span>《张几仲召还朝其幕府赵承之送行至漳水……》（其十）<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《斜川集校注》卷四。）</span><div id='poem_522631' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_522631' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/522631?labeling=true' target='_blank'>张几仲被<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>①</sup>召还朝其幕府赵承之送行至漳水用杜子美诗为韵作诗十篇既还孙志康亦取其韵追送过<span class='inlineComment2'>（原误作迈）</span>方官并门因几仲之来遂得诸公相遇今幕府例罢不能无离索之意故亦用此韵见意<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1114年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31323, "北宋", "苏过", "poem_title_522631")'>苏过</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_522631_comment'></div><div class='titleComment'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_title_522631_0'>① 原封缺，据清旧抄本补</div></div></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_522631'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_522631'>元戎度量大，六二坤直方。<div id='poem_sentence_0_522631_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_522631'>好士常仄席，疾恶如探汤。<div id='poem_sentence_1_522631_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_522631'>威名在夷虏，功烈纪太常。<div id='poem_sentence_2_522631_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_522631'>臧孙自有后，何必谏如棠。<div id='poem_sentence_3_522631_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_522631'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_522631_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_522632' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_522632' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/522632?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1114年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_522632_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_522632'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_522632'>承明用儒将，那知有程李。<div id='poem_sentence_0_522632_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_522632'>坐制犬羊群，泥封一丸耳。<div id='poem_sentence_1_522632_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_522632'>平生晋公子，从者皆国士。<div id='poem_sentence_2_522632_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_522632'>谁为彀中游，狐赵何难拟。<div id='poem_sentence_3_522632_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_522632'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_522632_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_522633' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_522633' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/522633?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其三 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1114年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_522633_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_522633'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_522633'>闻公卜菟裘，欲访有鱼稻。<div id='poem_sentence_0_522633_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_522633'>䌽衣归林下，池塘共春草。<div id='poem_sentence_1_522633_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_522633'>贤者享三乐，世俗未易道。<div id='poem_sentence_2_522633_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_522633'>但恐东山心，上意还不报。<div id='poem_sentence_3_522633_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_522633'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_522633_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_522634' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_522634' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/522634?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其四 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1114年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_522634_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_522634'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_522634'>我生良多难，已安悬磬室。<div id='poem_sentence_0_522634_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_522634'>端来强敛板，诡词学造膝。<div id='poem_sentence_1_522634_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_522634'>枯荄那复春，羸兵敢借一。<div id='poem_sentence_2_522634_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_522634'>振履独商歌，知音赖师乙。<div id='poem_sentence_3_522634_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_522634'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_522634_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_522635' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_522635' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/522635?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其五 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1114年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_522635_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_522635'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_522635'>君从河朔来，言寻子桑饭。<div id='poem_sentence_0_522635_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_522635'>蹉𨇤自忘形，请交不敢惮。<div id='poem_sentence_1_522635_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_522635'>念君青云士，我是江湖散。<div id='poem_sentence_2_522635_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_522635'>共为逍遥游，未用相推挽。<div id='poem_sentence_3_522635_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_522635'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_522635_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_522636' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_522636' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/522636?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其六 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1114年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_522636_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_522636'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_522636'>与君期岁寒，穷坚老当壮。<div id='poem_sentence_0_522636_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_522636'>相从茅茨下，不羡凌烟上。<div id='poem_sentence_1_522636_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_522636'>仲由志亦陋，伤哉生无养。<div id='poem_sentence_2_522636_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_522636'>岂知众所忧，箪瓢有佳况。<div id='poem_sentence_3_522636_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_522636'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_522636_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_522637' /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_522582_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_522582'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_522582_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_522582'>君怀著云梦，尚有恢恢地。<div id='poem_sentence_2_522582_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_522582_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_522582'>满床簪笏閒，乃见山林士。<div id='poem_sentence_5_522582_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_522582_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_522582'>平生南阳馆，市骏得千里。<div id='poem_sentence_8_522582_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_522582'>我行抽手板，亦复还耒耜。<div id='poem_sentence_12_522582_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_522582'>安能久俛首，自困刀笔吏。<div ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1114&endYear=1114')">1114年</a>　在阳曲，监太原府税。冬，苏过与吴坰（子骏）之河外，大水道阻，食波菜粥，坰作诗，过和其韵。作品：《和吴子骏食波稜粥》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《斜川集校注》卷四。）</span><div id='poem_522688'
