id='poem_sentence_0_522832'>暂抛尘土扣云扉，山色空濛翠湿衣。<div id='poem_sentence_0_522832_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_522832'>涧水松风俱有恨，道人瓶钵几时归<span class='inlineComment2'>（清周在浚《晋稗》）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_1_522832_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_522832'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_522832_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1114&endYear=1114')">1114年</a>　在阳曲，监太原府税。洛阳人作抚松堂，苏过寄诗题咏。作品：《寄题抚松堂》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《斜川集校注》卷四。）</span><div id='poem_522566' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_522566' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/522566?labeling=true' target='_blank'>寄题抚松堂</a><span class='authorDate'>（1114年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31323, "北宋", "苏过", "poem_title_522566")'>苏过</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_522566_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_522566'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_522566'>胸中朝市远，何必择所居。<div id='poem_sentence_0_522566_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_522566'>门无结驷客，山林入吾庐。<div id='poem_sentence_1_522566_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_522566'>西洛有君子，筑室城之隅。<div id='poem_sentence_2_522566_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_522566'>种松在庭户，志与渊明俱。<div id='poem_sentence_3_522566_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_522566'>朝挹西山爽，暮寻南涧娱。<div id='poem_sentence_4_522566_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_522566'>霜中鹤骨瘦，雨夜龙髯疏。<div id='poem_sentence_5_522566_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_522566'>主人应相似，节抱陵云孤。<div id='poem_sentence_6_522566_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_522566'>不知寒暑迁，肯徇世俗趋。<div id='poem_sentence_7_522566_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_522566'>昔称水南北，去曳侯门裾。<div id='poem_sentence_8_522566_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_522566'>能伴松菊老，固知泾渭殊。<div id='poem_sentence_9_522566_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_522566'>我恨营口腹，敛板惭妻孥。<div id='poem_sentence_10_522566_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_522566'>三径未能归，高卧子不如。<div id='poem_sentence_11_522566_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_522566'>青衫满尘土，何时返樵渔。<div id='poem_sentence_12_522566_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_522566'>未用北山移，我来只须臾。<div id='poem_sentence_13_522566_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_522566'></div><div id='poem_sentence_14_522566_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1114&endYear=1114')">1114年</a>　在阳曲，监太原府税。苏过尚有《跋折太尉碑阴》文、《寄题折嗣益袭清阁》诗。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《斜川集校注》卷八。折太尉，为折克行。）</span><div id='poem_1215262' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1215262' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1215262?labeling=true' target='_blank'>跋折太尉碑阴</a><span class='authorDate'>（1114年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31323, "北宋", "苏过", "poem_title_1215262")'>苏过</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1215262_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1215262'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1215262'>折氏世守河西，历五季之乱，能以区区壤地保完其民人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1215262_comment'></div>封府库，籍甲兵，以归真主，抑可谓不愧窦融矣！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1215262_comment'></div>然窦氏子弟不及，融没，颇以恣纵取败于世，弗克显。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1215262_comment'></div>有茅土而折氏五世，传百有馀年，忠孝自翼，礼义自度，若出于一，则贤于窦氏远矣！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1215262_comment'></div>余于并门，始得太尉武安公之墓碑于其子嗣益。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1215262_comment'></div>读之竦然，见其制胜料敌，得士死力，有古名将之风，非特能世其家者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1215262_comment'></div>公守河西逾三十年，虏在其目中，如几上物。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1215262_comment'></div>所使偏裨部曲，如臂之使指，安得不为虏所惮？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1215262_comment'></div>昔赵以李牧守雁门，备匈奴，以便宜置吏，市租皆输幕府，为士卒费。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1215262_comment'></div>椎牛养士，士卒思奋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1215262_comment'></div>而才有寇，急入保聚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1215262_comment'></div>虏以为怯，遂举众大入。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1215262_comment'></div>牧选士出奇，破杀十馀万，匈奴卒不敢近塞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1215262_comment'></div>盖牧居边十馀岁，得虏之情状虚实详且严，以静观动，以逸待劳，则强弱固自不敌耶！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1215262_comment'></div>颇、牧不世出，岂可以常理论？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1215262_comment'></div>故余于折公亦云。</div><div id='poem_sentence_15_1215262_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1114&endYear=1114')">1114年</a>　在阳曲，监太原府税。苏过尚有《跋折太尉碑阴》、《寄题折嗣益袭庆阁》诗。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《斜川集校注》卷四。）</span><div id='poem_522684' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_522684' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/522684?labeling=true' target='_blank'>寄题折嗣益袭庆阁</a><span class='authorDate'>（1114年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31323, "北宋", "苏过", "poem_title_522684")'>苏过</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_522684_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_522684'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_522684'>帝有虎臣司北门，虚弦坐落天骄魂。<div id='poem_sentence_0_522684_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_522684'>百年不敢南牧马，草木尚有威名存。<div id='poem_sentence_1_522684_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_522684'>平生忠义身许国，不以金玉遗子孙。<div id='poem_sentence_2_522684_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_522684'>承平弓剑空在韣，惟有简编遗后昆。<div id='poem_sentence_3_522684_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_522684'>不知所活几千人，一门何止十朱轮。<div id='poem_sentence_4_522684_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_522684'>满床簪笏不足道，万石家风今复闻。<div id='poem_sentence_5_522684_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_522684'>明窗小阁卧晏温，不读孙吴看典坟。<div id='poem_sentence_6_522684_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_522684'>坐销杀气边风春，记取大冯小冯君。<div id='poem_sentence_7_522684_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_522684'></div><div id='poem_sentence_8_522684_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1114&endYear=1114')">1114年</a>　在阳曲，监太原府税。苏过又有《跋南安岩主颂》、《代人贺启（拜恩中禁）》、《代人谢启（观风全晋）》、《代人谢启（将漕逾年）》诸篇，俱作于太原，但不知确年。作品：《跋<南安岩主颂>》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《斜川集校注》卷八。此文具体作时不详，姑系于此。）</span>《代人贺启》（其三）<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《斜川集校注》卷八。此文具体作时不详，姑系于此。）</span>《代人谢启》（其一）<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《斜川集校注》卷八。《斜川集校注》有《代人谢启》（一）同题文二篇，此为其中一篇，首句为“观风全晋”此文具体作时不详，姑系于此。）</span>《代人谢启》（其二）<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《斜川集校注》卷八。《斜川集校注》有《代人谢启》（二）同题文二篇，此为其中一篇，首句为“将漕逾年”此文具体作时不详，姑系于此。）</span><div id='poem_1215263' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1215263' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1215263?labeling=true' target='_blank'>跋南安岩主颂</a><span class='authorDate'>（1114年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31323, "北宋", "苏过", "poem_title_1215263")'>苏过</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1215263_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1215263'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1215263'>佛以广大智慧、不可思议力，能于世间现种种功德，随应以求，皆使充满。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1215263_comment'></div>何也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1215263_comment'></div>佛无他缘，惟有一慈；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1215263_comment'></div>人无他术，惟有一信。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1215263_comment'></div>慈信二法，相须而行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1215263_comment'></div>故能成就无量大愿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1215263_comment'></div>昔沙门以钝根故，不能诵经。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1215263_comment'></div>其师授此南安定光岩主四句偈，诵不岁馀，日记万言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1215263_comment'></div>南徐庾氏，有子病足不能履地，金山佛鉴授以此偈，诵之数岁，两躄复伸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1215263_comment'></div>又有居士刘素，事南安像，忽得重病，祷于像前，香槃中现小青蛇，舌相纯白，举头如语。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1215263_comment'></div>后二日有人教以此偈，昼夜诵持，三日疾愈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1215263_comment'></div>此皆近岁神异。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1215263_comment'></div>如此，岂非佛子厌苦蒙昧，抱缠病恼，思脱尘劳，过于桎梏，求哀也力，起信也坚，则佛之慈悲，相应如响。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1215263_comment'></div>有是理哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1215263_comment'></div>王君师文官并门，备闻其事，赞叹希有，曰：「此偈不可不传」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1215263_comment'></div>属某书之，将镂板施人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1215263_comment'></div>某以为师文此心不忍独善其身，将使自一传二，至于千万，以信悟人，除世间苦，夫岂细事哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1215263_comment'></div>又使学道者于此观心，得究竟法，出诸生死，则何止发蒙蔽而愈膏肓乎！</div><div id='poem_sentence_17_1215263_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1215228' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1215228' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1215228?labeling=true' target='_blank'>代人谢启<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1114年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31323, "北宋", "苏过", "poem_title_1215228")'>苏过</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1215228_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1215228'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1215228'>观风全晋，缪膺刺举之司；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1215228_comment'></div>听诵舆人，敢厕荐论之列。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1215228_comment'></div>岂谓囊封之才上，遽烦华衮之见褒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1215228_comment'></div>有腼面颜，增光蔀屋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1215228_comment'></div>窃以圣朝图任，莫先旧人；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1215228_comment'></div>汉法考功，必更治郡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1215228_comment'></div>故望之试吏于冯翊，辍自九卿；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1215228_comment'></div>黄霸治最于颍川，入为丞相。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1215228_comment'></div>况此右文之世，益思共理之臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1215228_comment'></div>眷求黄发于公卿之间，用保赤子于覆载之内。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1215228_comment'></div>果闻报政，不待期年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1215228_comment'></div>某官学造渊源，才兼果艺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1215228_comment'></div>以经术润吏事，以仁义陈王前。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1215228_comment'></div>久参书殿之严，屡典侯藩之寄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1215228_comment'></div>淮阳卧治，已多长孺之风；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1215228_comment'></div>渤海政成，将被水衡之拜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1215228_comment'></div>某埽门有旧，推毂何功？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1215228_comment'></div>昔蒙一鹗之称，敢忘知遇；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1215228_comment'></div>聊采二天之誉，莫报私恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1215228_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_19_1215228_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1215229' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1215229' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1215229?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1114年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1215229_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1215229'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1215229'>将漕逾年，已愧无功于飞挽；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1215229_comment'></div>司刑一道，蔑闻有补于澄清。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1215229_comment'></div>方怀沙汰之虞，复冒转输之寄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1215229_comment'></div>自惭尸禄，空祗汗颜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1215229_comment'></div>窃惟爵禄者，待天下之有劳；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1215229_comment'></div>食货者，乃生民之先务。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1215229_comment'></div>故重选多才多艺之士，用成足食足兵之功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1215229_comment'></div>岂惟迁有无而懋化居，盖使实仓廪而知礼节。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1215229_comment'></div>矧此冀州旧壤，全晋奥区。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1215229_comment'></div>地介两河，寇临二虏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1215229_comment'></div>仰给于官者环数千里，取赋于民者逾二十州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1215229_comment'></div>责当任于赢虚，材必资于果艺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1215229_comment'></div>尽山川之曲折，虏在目中；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1215229_comment'></div>权货殖之重轻，钱流地上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1215229_comment'></div>如某者仅能寡过，初乏治称。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1215229_comment'></div>才不足以分庙堂之忧，宠已惊于逾蝼蚁之分。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1215229_comment'></div>静思忝冒，实自吹嘘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1215229_comment'></div>录其岁月之劳，借以齿牙之论。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1215229_comment'></div>此盖某官弼亮元圣，师表万民。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1215229_comment'></div>才全而德不形，任重而道愈远。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1215229_comment'></div>以求贤取士为报国，以丰财裕民付有司。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1215229_comment'></div>致此恩荣，下逮疏远。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1215229_comment'></div>谓其已试于折狱，盗贼偶宁；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1215229_comment'></div>庶几有益于理财，公私俱济。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1215229_comment'></div>某敢不激昂志节，尽瘁国家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1215229_comment'></div>上酬天地生成之恩，捐躯未已；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1215229_comment'></div>次答卵翼始终之惠，没齿难忘！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1215229_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_27_1215229_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1115&endYear=1115')">1115年</a>　苏过罢太原府监税任。<br /></div>
-----end



-----title
洛阳
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='b229c729f2114208bfd002d86caeeb77_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("b229c729f2114208bfd002d86caeeb77");'><span id='b229c729f2114208bfd002d86caeeb77_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1112&endYear=1112')">1112年</a>，41岁</div><div id='b229c729f2114208bfd002d86caeeb77' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1112&endYear=1112')">1112年</a>　在洛阳，监太原府税任上。苏过自太原归颍，途经洛阳，寓宝坛，与僧悟超游龙门，作诗别之。作品：《予寓洛阳宝坛有僧悟超……》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《斜川集校注》卷四。）</span><div id='poem_522617' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_522617' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/522617?labeling=true' target='_blank'>予寓洛阳宝坛有僧悟超类有道者与语论事能援古證今盖未祝发时读孔氏之史书涉猎大义为浮屠犹不废今老矣不复读也形骸枯槁真能遗世故而玩死生者送予至龙门陪予游东西两山作此诗别之</a><span class='authorDate'>（1098年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31323, "北宋", "苏过", "poem_title_522617")'>苏过</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_522617_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_522617'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_522617'>我生江海上，性与鱼鸟逸。<div id='poem_sentence_0_522617_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_522617'>端来入世网，竟坐形骸役。<div id='poem_sentence_1_522617_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_522617'>此心本洞然，六月遭怵迫。<div id='poem_sentence_2_522617_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_522617'>常恐忘迹熟，主人不胜客。<div id='poem_sentence_3_522617_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_522617'>道人偶相逢，宿契类畴昔。<div id='poem_sentence_4_522617_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_522617'>巉岩秀眉目，灰槁心木石。<div id='poem_sentence_5_522617_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_522617'>语我学道难，吾徒犹不力。<div id='poem_sentence_6_522617_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_522617'>纷华久风靡，外慕失阃域。<div id='poem_sentence_7_522617_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_522617'>卑之毋高论，遣去身外物。<div id='poem_sentence_8_522617_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_522617'>未能忘饥寒，衣布饭疏粝。<div id='poem_sentence_9_522617_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_522617'>此语君自味，至道在咫尺。<div id='poem_sentence_10_522617_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_522617'>阅人吾虽多，子独无荆棘。<div id='poem_sentence_11_522617_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_522617'>送行聊过溪，共蹑登山屐<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_12_522617_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_522617'></div><div id='poem_sentence_13_522617_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_522617'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_12_522617_0'>⑴ 自注：有为超作紫方袍授之，辄藏而不服，曰吾教有坏色衣，无是服也。予益高之。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_522617_comment'></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='e41e570cde084f97ad2f7c43eef1e17c_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("e41e570cde084f97ad2f7c43eef1e17c");'><span id='e41e570cde084f97ad2f7c43eef1e17c_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1117&endYear=1117')">1117年</a>，46岁</div><div id='e41e570cde084f97ad2f7c43eef1e17c' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1117&endYear=1117')">1117年</a>　在洛阳，郾城县知县任上。苏过以事至洛阳，归游龙门，作诗别同行僧超晖。作品：《仆以事至洛言还过龙门……》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《斜川集校注》卷五。）</span><div id='poem_522616' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_522616' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/522616?labeling=true' target='_blank'>仆以事至洛言还过龙门少留一宿自药寮度广化潜溪入宝应翼日过水东谒白傅祠游皇龛看经两寺登八节尤爱之复至奉先作此诗以示同行僧超晖</a><span class='authorDate'>（1117年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31323, "北宋", "苏过", "poem_title_522616")'>苏过</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_522616_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_522616'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_522616'>峥嵘两山门，共挹一水秀。<div id='poem_sentence_0_522616_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_522616'>滩声千鼓鼙，石壁万龛窦。<div id='poem_sentence_1_522616_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_522616'>何人植翠柏，幽径出尘囿。<div id='poem_sentence_2_522616_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_522616'>金银佛寺古，夜籁笙竽奏。<div id='poem_sentence_3_522616_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_522616'>僧稀梵呗少，石险松竹瘦。<div id='poem_sentence_4_522616_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_522616'>惟当效乐天，早晚弃冠绶。<div id='poem_sentence_5_522616_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_522616'></div><div id='poem_sentence_6_522616_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
郾城
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='6e559cfe425c47678f8cfd89885f7d1c_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("6e559cfe425c47678f8cfd89885f7d1c");'><span id='6e559cfe425c47678f8cfd89885f7d1c_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1116&endYear=1116')">1116年</a>，45岁</div><div id='6e559cfe425c47678f8cfd89885f7d1c' class='detail'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>在郾城，任郾城县知县。苏过出知郾城县，作《志隐跋》作品：《<志隐>跋》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《斜川集校注》卷九。苏过《志隐》一文，见《斜川集校注》卷七。）</span><div id='poem_1215219' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1215219' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1215219?labeling=true' target='_blank'>志隐赋</a><span class='authorDate'>（元符元年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31323, "北宋", "苏过", "poem_title_1215219")'>苏过</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1215219_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1215219'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1215219'>苏子居岛夷之二年，客有自许来唁，问其安否，而勉之进取。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1215219_comment'></div>曰：「天之生物，类聚群分。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1215219_comment'></div>蠢动飞走，不相夺伦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1215219_comment'></div>鱼宅于渊，兽伏于榛；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1215219_comment'></div>蚕之于冰，鼠之于焚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1215219_comment'></div>失其所则病，因其性则存。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1215219_comment'></div>且非独虫鱼然也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1215219_comment'></div>楚之橘柚不植于燕代，晋之枣栗不繁于闽越。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1215219_comment'></div>非天地之所私，繄物性之南北。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1215219_comment'></div>况于人乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1215219_comment'></div>余蜀人也，少游三晋之间矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1215219_comment'></div>秋冬之交，朔风萧条。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1215219_comment'></div>山童泽枯，堕指折胶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1215219_comment'></div>阴山之雪，三岁不消。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1215219_comment'></div>故其生实瘠而不窳，畜驷强而不乾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1215219_comment'></div>人亦刚而多勇，寿而硕坚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1215219_comment'></div>肤拆面殷，足胝手胼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1215219_comment'></div>为霜雪之所凝，凛其质之岁寒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1215219_comment'></div>而五岭之南，夷獠杂居。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1215219_comment'></div>天卑地溽，山盘水纡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1215219_comment'></div>恶溪肆流，毒雾蒸嘘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1215219_comment'></div>昼避蝮虺，夜号鼪鼯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1215219_comment'></div>草木冬花，霖潦长濡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1215219_comment'></div>星隐于气，日见于晡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1215219_comment'></div>故其民多重膇之病，寒热中肤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1215219_comment'></div>非耋而伛，非躄而扶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1215219_comment'></div>而儋耳者，又在二广之南，南溟之中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1215219_comment'></div>其民卉服鼻饮，语言不通。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1215219_comment'></div>状若禽兽，既嚚且聋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1215219_comment'></div>海气郁雺，瘴烟溟濛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1215219_comment'></div>而子安之，岂亦有道乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1215219_comment'></div>且夫君子之修身也，病没世而无闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1215219_comment'></div>故其蹑屩而取卿相，脱挽辂而□封君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1215219_comment'></div>季子从成而得印，范叔计行而专秦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1215219_comment'></div>相如进缶而赵重，毛遂奉盘而楚亲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1215219_comment'></div>或刀笔以自奋，或干戈以策勋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1215219_comment'></div>脱颖者富贵，陆沈者贱贫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1215219_comment'></div>希揄扬于鼎彝，耻湮没于埃尘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1215219_comment'></div>古人有言：『岁云暮矣，时不我与』。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1215219_comment'></div>如子之年，鸣钟鼎食者多矣，曷亦有意于世乎」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1215219_comment'></div>苏子曰：「噫！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1215219_comment'></div>若客，殆未达者耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1215219_comment'></div>大块之间，有生同之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1215219_comment'></div>喜怒哀乐，钜细不遗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1215219_comment'></div>蚁蜂之君臣，蛮触之雄雌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1215219_comment'></div>以我观之，物何足疑？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1215219_comment'></div>彭聃以寒暑为朝暮，蟪蛄以春秋为期颐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1215219_comment'></div>孰寿孰夭，孰欣孰悲？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1215219_comment'></div>况吾与子，好恶性习，一致同归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1215219_comment'></div>寓此世间，美恶几希。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1215219_comment'></div>乃欲夸三晋而陋百粤，弃远俗而鄙岛夷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1215219_comment'></div>窃为子不取也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1215219_comment'></div>子知鱼之安于水也，而鱼何择夫河汉之与江湖？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1215219_comment'></div>知兽之安于薮也，而兽何择于云梦之与孟诸？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1215219_comment'></div>松柏之后彫，萑苇之易枯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1215219_comment'></div>乃物性之自然，岂土地之能殊？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1215219_comment'></div>子乃以晋楚之产疑之，过矣！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1215219_comment'></div>虽然，瘴厉之地，子得其详也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1215219_comment'></div>仆亦择其可道者，以释子之惑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1215219_comment'></div>天地之气，冬夏一律。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1215219_comment'></div>物不凋瘁，生意靡息。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1215219_comment'></div>冬絺夏葛，稻岁再熟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1215219_comment'></div>富者寡求，贫者易足。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1215219_comment'></div>绩蕊为衣，蓺根为粮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1215219_comment'></div>铸山煮海，国以富强。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1215219_comment'></div>犀象珠玉，走于四方。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1215219_comment'></div>士独免于战争，民独勉于农桑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1215219_comment'></div>其山川则清远而秀绝，陵谷则缥缈而岪郁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1215219_comment'></div>虽龙蛇之委藏，亦神仙之所宅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1215219_comment'></div>吾盖乐游而忘返，岂特暖席之与黔突也哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1215219_comment'></div>若夫纡朱怀金，肥马轻车，固人情之所欲得也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1215219_comment'></div>而况金石之传，不朽之荣，为主上布德泽于斯民，拊四夷而宾不庭，固非独善其身，老死丘壑者所得拟也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1215219_comment'></div>然功高则身危，名重则谤生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1215219_comment'></div>枉寻者见容，方枘者必憎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1215219_comment'></div>而自古豪杰之士，有不能闾阎之穷，慨然有澄清之志，探虎穴，索骊珠，而得全者，盖无一二也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1215219_comment'></div>彼大人者，窅然观之，颦蹙远引，况以荣为乐耶！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1215219_comment'></div>世非不知得士者昌，失士者危。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1215219_comment'></div>然患难或可以共处，安逸或可以长辞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1215219_comment'></div>子胥不免于属镂，范蠡得计于鸱夷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1215219_comment'></div>萧何缧囚于患失，留侯脱屣于先知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1215219_comment'></div>敌国亡而信烹，刘氏安而勃疑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1215219_comment'></div>故介推避禄于绵田，鲁连辞赏于燕师。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1215219_comment'></div>接舆长歌于凤鸟，庄叟感慨于郊牺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1215219_comment'></div>仆无过人之才，固不足以自媒也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1215219_comment'></div>然马之羁靮，鹰之鞲绁，寒心久矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1215219_comment'></div>方长鸣于冀北，睹皂栈而知惧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1215219_comment'></div>击鲜肥于秋风，又何脔割之足顾哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1215219_comment'></div>盖尝闻养生之粗也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1215219_comment'></div>今置身于遐荒，如有物之初。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1215219_comment'></div>余逃空谷之寂寥，眷此世而愈疏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1215219_comment'></div>追赤松于渺茫，想神仙于有无。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1215219_comment'></div>此天下之至乐也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1215219_comment'></div>而子期我以世人，污我于泥涂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1215219_comment'></div>贪千仞之鷇，轻隋侯之珠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1215219_comment'></div>子以为巧，我知其愚」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1215219_comment'></div>客愧且叹曰：「吾浅之为丈夫也」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1215219_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_96_1215219'>昔余侍先君子居儋耳，丁年而往，二毛而归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1215219_comment'></div>盖尝筑室有终焉之志。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1215219_comment'></div>遂赋《志隐》一篇，效昔人《解嘲》、《宾戏》之类。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_98_1215219_comment'></div>将以混得丧，忘羁旅，非特以自广，且以为老人之娱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_99_1215219_comment'></div>先君子览之，欣然嘉焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_100_1215219_comment'></div>逮今二十年矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_101_1215219_comment'></div>政和丙申来颍水，偶发书箧，得旧稿，怅然感叹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_102_1215219_comment'></div>小儿籥在总角时，逮事先君子者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_103_1215219_comment'></div>惜此篇久亡而今存，请书其事而藏之，庶几不忘在莒云耳。</div><div id='poem_sentence_104_1215219_comment'></div></div></div><br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>在郾城，任郾城县知县。故人任况之有诗见寄，苏过和其韵。作品：《和任况之诗》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《斜川集校注》卷四。）</span><div id='poem_522844' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_522844' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/522844?labeling=true' target='_blank'>和任况之<span class='inlineComment2'>（原缺之字，径补）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1116年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31323, "北宋", "苏过", "poem_title_522844")'>苏过</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_522844_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_522844'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_522844'>簪裳如缧囚，我生三年系。<div id='poem_sentence_0_522844_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_522844'>一落罝网中，遂负山林志。<div id='poem_sentence_1_522844_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_522844'>忆故晋阳城，访古寻前事。<div id='poem_sentence_2_522844_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_522844'>萧凉麋鹿游，正坐金汤累。<div id='poem_sentence_3_522844_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_522844'>西山郁峥嵘，气势翔天际。<div id='poem_sentence_4_522844_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_522844'>因知神所托，千岁有其地。<div id='poem_sentence_5_522844_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_522844'>绵绵邑姜祠，盛德百世继。<div id='poem_sentence_6_522844_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_522844'>汾横地轴壮，泉涌山骨碎。<div id='poem_sentence_7_522844_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_522844'>我时正行役，忽此烟雨滞。<div id='poem_sentence_8_522844_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_522844'>颇遭溪谷留，使<span class='inlineComment2'>（疑应作便）</span>失乡关异。<div id='poem_sentence_9_522844_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_522844'>是时薰风初，殿阁微凉至。<div id='poem_sentence_10_522844_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_522844'>碧井照眼寒，山光湿衣翠。<div id='poem_sentence_11_522844_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_522844'>文鲂纵弱浪，野鹤下晚吹。<div id='poem_sentence_12_522844_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_522844'>平生谢公心，雅在东山醉。<div id='poem_sentence_13_522844_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_522844'>端来乞五斗，兹事复且置。<div id='poem_sentence_14_522844_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_522844'>悽悽百僚末，举首触嗔忌。<div id='poem_sentence_15_522844_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_522844'>早知折腰恶，谁敢朱云吏。<div id='poem_sentence_16_522844_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_522844'>愿君志吾言，身外皆沤寄。<div id='poem_sentence_17_522844_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_522844'>临渊休羡鱼，早决归来意。<div id='poem_sentence_18_522844_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_19_522844'>荣枯梦已破，何待邯郸记<span class='inlineComment2'>（以上清旧抄本《斜川集》）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_19_522844_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_20_522844'></div><div id='poem_sentence_20_522844_comment'></div></div></div><br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>秋，苏过徙郾城县敕书楼。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='ad6ca2d16bcd4545892cdd15cc03b707_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("ad6ca2d16bcd4545892cdd15cc03b707");'><span id='ad6ca2d16bcd4545892cdd15cc03b707_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1117&endYear=1117')">1117年</a>，46岁</div><div id='ad6ca2d16bcd4545892cdd15cc03b707' class='detail'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>在郾城，任郾城县知县。苏过卧病，儿子籥与友人置酒泛舟于郾城（左氵右隐）亭，作诗唱酬，过次韵。作品：《小子籥与其友作<（左氵右隐）亭置酒泛舟唱酬之什>予亦戏用其韵》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《斜川集校注》卷五。）</span><div id='poem_522796' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_522796' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/522796?labeling=true' target='_blank'>小子籥与其友作㶏亭置酒泛舟唱酬之什予肃戏用其韵</a><span class='authorDate'>（1117年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31323, "北宋", "苏过", "poem_title_522796")'>苏过</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_522796_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_522796'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_522796'>胜事随年阿堵中，老夫久绝马牛风。<div id='poem_sentence_0_522796_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_522796'>消磨药石一春过，寂寞樽罍万事空。<div id='poem_sentence_1_522796_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_522796'>亭下麦秋惊翠浪，山前雨脚卷晴虹。<div id='poem_sentence_2_522796_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_522796'>渡头试验丰穰意，半是村醪入颊红。<div id='poem_sentence_3_522796_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_522796'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_522796_comment'></div></div></div><br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>在郾城，任郾城县知县。襄城程彪（美中）卒，其子鼒求铭，苏过撰铭，并赋诗。作品：《襄城程先生美中墓志铭》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《斜川集校注》卷九。）</span>《次韵程秀才求作其先人埋铭》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《斜川集校注》卷五。）</span><div id='poem_1215281' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1215281' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1215281?labeling=true' target='_blank'>襄城程先生美中墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（政和七年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31323, "北宋", "苏过", "poem_title_1215281")'>苏过</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1215281_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1215281'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1215281'>古者仕而未有禄者，君有馈焉曰「献」，使焉曰「寡君」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1215281_comment'></div>虽王公不敢以其位加于匹夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1215281_comment'></div>而士亦有不见公侯，耻于鼎肉亟馈亟拜之义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1215281_comment'></div>秦汉以下，风俗不竞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1215281_comment'></div>降志辱身，惟利是趋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1215281_comment'></div>故扬子云曰：「周之士也贵，秦之士也贱」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1215281_comment'></div>有以也夫！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1215281_comment'></div>有襄城布衣之士曰程美中，素以儒术教其乡人，不汲汲于富贵，不戚戚于贫贱，独尚气节，不妄交于人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1215281_comment'></div>乡闾皆严惮之，尊之曰「先生」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1215281_comment'></div>盖尝有侍从贵臣出守颍昌，乃先生之友人也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1215281_comment'></div>或劝之俾修谒焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1215281_comment'></div>顾笑曰：「我贱彼贵，招而往，吾犹病之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1215281_comment'></div>若栖栖其门户，人其以我徼口腹而来，祗自取辱焉」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1215281_comment'></div>众大惭服。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1215281_comment'></div>邑有富人，遣其子受经于先生，既中甲乙科，乡人荣之，而先生澹然无德色。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1215281_comment'></div>其后贫甚，或强使谒之以病告，阳许诺而卒不往。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1215281_comment'></div>汝颍之士为之□□。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1215281_comment'></div>过与其子鼒游，鼒又称其处兄弟之间，有难能者，曰：「吾祖昔以财雄乡里，有子五人，先生其季也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1215281_comment'></div>伯仲皆豪放，不事生产，田园悉为嬉游费殆尽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1215281_comment'></div>而先生敝衣蔬食，杜门读书，不问有无，全兄弟之欢」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1215281_comment'></div>夫孝悌称于其家，厄穷守道称于朋友，抑亦无愧于古之士矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1215281_comment'></div>今其亡也，可不识乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1215281_comment'></div>先生讳彪，美中，其字也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1215281_comment'></div>世为开封长垣人，后徙居襄城。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1215281_comment'></div>曾大父悦，不仕；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1215281_comment'></div>大父永，赠太子中允。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1215281_comment'></div>皆隐居自晦，财豪而善施。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1215281_comment'></div>父讳初，蚤中九经第，仕屯田员外郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1215281_comment'></div>性刚直，好讥刺大臣，以故仕不甚显。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1215281_comment'></div>母李，故丞相沆之孙，侍郎师锡之女，邑封长寿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1215281_comment'></div>先生幼而警敏，好观史书，不特事科举学。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1215281_comment'></div>年甫弱冠，矫矫自立，推重于先生长者，皆自以为莫及。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1215281_comment'></div>襄城旧儒曰杨泌，未尝妄以文许人，一见之，敛衽心服，遂以女妻之，由是为襄城人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1215281_comment'></div>先生善诲人，至诚遇物，期于长育成就，学者从之如归，相踵登进士第，多有显者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1215281_comment'></div>然终其身，仅能取荐书而已，一命不沾，交游称屈，是命也夫！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1215281_comment'></div>政和七年，鼒以上舍士贡于京师，而先生亦以免解恩将同试于春官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1215281_comment'></div>未行，而以疾终于其家，享年五十有九，岁在丁酉八月二十五日也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1215281_comment'></div>子四人：曰鼒、□、阔、开。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1215281_comment'></div>女一人，适孙娱，故资政殿学士康公犹子也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1215281_comment'></div>以某年某月日，葬于某地，从祔其先。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1215281_comment'></div>鼒来请铭，铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_40_1215281'>源远而流长，立善必有自也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1215281_comment'></div>安时而处顺，秉德必有似也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1215281_comment'></div>介然乎不群于物，此其性之于己也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1215281_comment'></div>不报其人而报其德，天殆将以昌其子也。</div><div id='poem_sentence_43_1215281_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_522774' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_522774' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/522774?labeling=true' target='_blank'>次韵程秀才求作其先人埋铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（1117年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31323, "北宋", "苏过", "poem_title_522774")'>苏过</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_522774_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_522774'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_522774'>欲载扬雄老一区，清名不耀力难摹。<div id='poem_sentence_0_522774_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_522774'>但知穮蓘勤吾事，要以凶丰畀后图。<div id='poem_sentence_1_522774_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_522774'>有子人人壮门户，新诗句句琢珉瑜。<div id='poem_sentence_2_522774_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_522774'>夜光明月毋轻付，误认空空叩鄙夫。<div id='poem_sentence_3_522774_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_522774'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_522774_comment'></div></div></div><br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>在郾城，任郾城县知县。冬，敕书楼建成，又修土地庙，苏过为文祭之。作品：《郾城县迁土地祭文》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《斜川集校注》卷九。）</span><div id='poem_1215285' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1215285' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1215285?labeling=true' target='_blank'>郾城县迁土地祭文</a><span class='authorDate'>（政和七年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31323, "北宋", "苏过", "poem_title_1215285")'>苏过</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1215285_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1215285'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1215285'>谨以羊一、豕一，清酌之奠，昭告于县治土地之神。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1215285_comment'></div>某以乙未岁之冬，奉敕宰是邑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1215285_comment'></div>既至，环视公宇，垫隘圮坏十七八。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1215285_comment'></div>而外有楼，以藏敕书，欹倾将压，不可枝梧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1215285_comment'></div>吏舍半房，户外如列涂肆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1215285_comment'></div>政令之出入，不可讥禁；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1215285_comment'></div>案牍之在亡，不可考求。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1215285_comment'></div>帛币之委积，或至暴露；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1215285_comment'></div>囚徒之居处，上漏下湿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1215285_comment'></div>某窃忧之，乃请于府，量功画材，得钱八万。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1215285_comment'></div>会部使者按漕过邑，又以缮完告，得钱十万。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1215285_comment'></div>因农之隙，徙敕书楼稍南；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1215285_comment'></div>尽收吏舍官帑，列于两庑；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1215285_comment'></div>别为库以储民兵之器械；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1215285_comment'></div>又新狱之三牢，通为屋五十有五楹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1215285_comment'></div>开门而事毕睹，阖门而人知禁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1215285_comment'></div>财不费于公，力不匮于民。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1215285_comment'></div>始于丙申之秋，成于丁酉之冬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1215285_comment'></div>独令厅不改作，不敢先于奉己。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1215285_comment'></div>东西夹舍未暇者，以其苟完而止也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1215285_comment'></div>始卒两岁，雨旸以时，疾疫不作，吏亦安堵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1215285_comment'></div>意土木之兴，必有阴相之者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1215285_comment'></div>乃鸠馀材，作新斯庙，非独以答神之贶，旧庙在庖舍之后，炀灶之所熏燎，腥秽之所污黩，神傥不安其居，人亦何安焉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1215285_comment'></div>谨卜良日，奉迁神像。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1215285_comment'></div>惟神福善惩恶，保佑兹土。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1215285_comment'></div>若吏若民，永有依怙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1215285_comment'></div>顾兹威灵，其报敢忘？</div><div id='poem_sentence_26_1215285_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='cda0b10901744202b3142b484c1ceb2f_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("cda0b10901744202b3142b484c1ceb2f");'><span id='cda0b10901744202b3142b484c1ceb2f_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1117&endYear=1117')">1117年</a>，46岁</div><div id='cda0b10901744202b3142b484c1ceb2f' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1117&endYear=1117')">1117年</a>　在郾城，任郾城县知县。颍昌原天宁寺僧普融发遣南岳，苏过作诗送之。作品：《送普融老》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《斜川集校注》卷五。）</span><div id='poem_522707' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_522707' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/522707?labeling=true' target='_blank'>送普融老</a><span class='authorDate'>（1117年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31323, "北宋", "苏过", "poem_title_522707")'>苏过</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_522707_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_522707'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_522707'>孤云去来无常踪，流水曲折无定容。<div id='poem_sentence_0_522707_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_522707'>纡馀散漫随天风，流行坎止忘西东。<div id='poem_sentence_1_522707_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_522707'>南岳道人曰普融，壁立万仞疑少通。<div id='poem_sentence_2_522707_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_522707'>山林市朝能两空，未觉芥蒂于其胸。<div id='poem_sentence_3_522707_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_522707'>脱身尘埃寓高峰，澹然遗世无冥鸿。<div id='poem_sentence_4_522707_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_522707'>岂知绝物非中庸，忍饥学仙啖柏松。<div id='poem_sentence_5_522707_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_522707'>住山出山偶然中，人不吾舍吾其从。<div id='poem_sentence_6_522707_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_522707'>浆馈未足为污隆，要与后学开盲聋。<div id='poem_sentence_7_522707_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_522707'>我方处世知铅舂，自知冠冕久不工。<div id='poem_sentence_8_522707_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_522707'>愿言香火他日同，二老会当林下逢。<div id='poem_sentence_9_522707_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_522707'></div><div id='poem_sentence_10_522707_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='4590d19912e145babf72c3502a63562c_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("4590d19912e145babf72c3502a63562c");'><span id='4590d19912e145babf72c3502a63562c_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1118&endYear=1119')">1118-1119年</a>，47-48岁</div><div id='4590d19912e145babf72c3502a63562c' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1118&endYear=1118')">1118年</a>　在郾城，任郾城县知县。秋，淫雨为灾，苏过作祷文祈晴。作品：《祈祷祝文五首》（其一）<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《斜川集校注》卷九。）</span>《祈祷祝文五首》（其二）<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《斜川集校注》卷九。）</span>《祈祷祝文五首》（其三）<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《斜川集校注》卷九。）</span>《祈祷祝文五首》（其四）<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《斜川集校注》卷九。）</span><div id='poem_1215288' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1215288' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1215288?labeling=true' target='_blank'>祈祷祝文<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1118年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31323, "北宋", "苏过", "poem_title_1215288")'>苏过</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1215288_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1215288'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1215288'>涉冬不雪，常旸为灾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1215288_comment'></div>方兴嗣岁之忧，辄有望霓之请。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1215288_comment'></div>威灵如在，民欲必从。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1215288_comment'></div>瑞雪应祈，南亩沾足。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1215288_comment'></div>苏麦芽于既槁，消疠气于未萌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1215288_comment'></div>神实有功于人，吏当何以报德？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1215288_comment'></div>敢伸薄奠，以荐嘉诚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1215288_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_7_1215288_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1215289' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1215289' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1215289?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1118年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1215289_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1215289'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1215289'>吏依民而立，民恃食以生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1215289_comment'></div>岁之不登，民将告病。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1215289_comment'></div>水潦艰食，吏责安逃？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1215289_comment'></div>是用穷呼神天，并祠群望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1215289_comment'></div>救灾恤患，神则优为。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1215289_comment'></div>散沴气之滞淫，拯秋成于旦暮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1215289_comment'></div>吏民拜贶，其或敢忘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1215289_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_7_1215289_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1215290' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1215290' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1215290?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其三 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1118年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1215290_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1215290'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1215290'>淫雨为灾，欲害垂成之稼；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1215290_comment'></div>下民告病，冀回从欲之仁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1215290_comment'></div>惟神惠养于黎元，为吏难逃于忧责。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1215290_comment'></div>转阴晴于反手，变饥馑为丰年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1215290_comment'></div>眷兹默宰之功，敢怠其报；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1215290_comment'></div>惟有事神之礼，益戒无忘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1215290_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_6_1215290_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1215291' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1215291' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1215291?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其四 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1118年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1215291_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1215291'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1215291'>郾之为邑，地卑水聚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1215291_comment'></div>秋稼在野，甚畏霪雨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1215291_comment'></div>兹以病告，冀获开霁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1215291_comment'></div>曰旸而旸，神则听许？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1215291_comment'></div>拯其沟渎，实之仓庾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1215291_comment'></div>神赐则丰，我报良窭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1215291_comment'></div>荐以明诚，神其焉吐？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1215291_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_7_1215291_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1118&endYear=1118')">1118年</a>　在郾城，任郾城县知县。冬又不雪，苏过作文祈雪。作品：《祈祷祝文五首》（其五）<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《斜川集校注》卷九。）</span><div id='poem_1215292' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1215292' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1215292?labeling=true' target='_blank'>祈祷祝文<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其五 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1118年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31323, "北宋", "苏过", "poem_title_1215292")'>苏过</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1215292_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1215292'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1215292'>水潦之馀，秋成无几。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1215292_comment'></div>牟麦未种，嗣岁可忧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1215292_comment'></div>商贾告病于泥涂，穑人未终于场圃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1215292_comment'></div>而连雨不止，积潦尚多。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1215292_comment'></div>民亦何辜？吏实不德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1215292_comment'></div>惟神宰制造化，开阖阴阳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1215292_comment'></div>愿兴从欲之仁，下悯穷呼之急。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1215292_comment'></div>事神之礼，祇戒不忘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1215292_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_8_1215292_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1119&endYear=1119')">1119年</a>　在郾城，任郾城县知县。春夏皆旱，苏过祷雨龙潭，有祝文。作品：《祷雨孚济龙潭祝文》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《斜川集校注》卷九。）</span>《送圣水还孚济龙潭祝文》<span
