href='/Writing/1215295?labeling=true' target='_blank'>祷雨孚济龙潭祝文</a><span class='authorDate'>（1119年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31323, "北宋", "苏过", "poem_title_1215295")'>苏过</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1215295_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1215295'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1215295'>窃以人穷则呼，莫急于死生之际；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1215295_comment'></div>旱既太甚，盖将有沟壑之忧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1215295_comment'></div>爰自去岁之冬，迄此季春之月，时雨未降，常旸为灾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1215295_comment'></div>念祷祠山川之勤，本州县守令之职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1215295_comment'></div>恐精诚之未格，致德意之或违。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1215295_comment'></div>眷言畎亩之人，何负神天之谴？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1215295_comment'></div>麦禾告病，农末俱忧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1215295_comment'></div>糇粮将绝于咽喉，饥馑继之以盗贼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1215295_comment'></div>赋敛有常而无损，死亡必至而何逃？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1215295_comment'></div>此岂上天好生之仁，亦非龙神庙食之福。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1215295_comment'></div>恭惟孚济之号，祀典所尊，合于天心，实司霈泽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1215295_comment'></div>栖神灵于潭洞，凛号令为风雷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1215295_comment'></div>变化出于须臾，丰凶在其可否。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1215295_comment'></div>傥遂一夫之私请，敢勤十日之来临。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1215295_comment'></div>分涓滴于瓶罂，遍膏泽于田野。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1215295_comment'></div>救此流离之厄，尽归肉骨之恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1215295_comment'></div>当以佛乘，仰答灵贶。</div><div id='poem_sentence_16_1215295_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1215293' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1215293' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1215293?labeling=true' target='_blank'>送圣水还孚济龙潭祝文</a><span class='authorDate'>（1119年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31323, "北宋", "苏过", "poem_title_1215293")'>苏过</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1215293_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1215293'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1215293'>伏以千里之灾，抑有徵于度数；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1215293_comment'></div>再三之渎，敢失信于神明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1215293_comment'></div>眷言岁旱之哀号，辄勤风驭之至止。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1215293_comment'></div>微衷莫达，德意未敷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1215293_comment'></div>殆一方罪戾之所招，虽十日穷呼而靡获。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1215293_comment'></div>谨遵首志，躬饯归途。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1215293_comment'></div>罄佛事以酬初心，沥丹诚以祈后效。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1215293_comment'></div>伏愿神踪反旆，灵液回川。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1215293_comment'></div>尚怜涸辙之氓，无废为霖之志。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1215293_comment'></div>请命上帝，速敕雷师。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1215293_comment'></div>转凶祸为丰年，域斯民于仁寿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1215293_comment'></div>当恳求于爵号，庶少答于生成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1215293_comment'></div>尚飨。</div><div id='poem_sentence_12_1215293_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1215296' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1215296' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1215296?labeling=true' target='_blank'>祷雨忏文</a><span class='authorDate'>（1119年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31323, "北宋", "苏过", "poem_title_1215296")'>苏过</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1215296_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1215296'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1215296'>今为亢阳不雨，害于麦禾，迎请龙王，未获感应。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1215296_comment'></div>辄自思惟，谁执其咎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1215296_comment'></div>此皆阎浮众生，造罪深重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1215296_comment'></div>身口意业，及贪嗔痴；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1215296_comment'></div>包藏祸心，损人利己。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1215296_comment'></div>不忠不孝，欺天欺神。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1215296_comment'></div>昧其本心，造成重罪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1215296_comment'></div>降鉴不远，何以召和气之祥；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1215296_comment'></div>积恶所薰，自然致天灾之报。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1215296_comment'></div>膏泽未降，农末俱忧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1215296_comment'></div>饥馑将兴，死亡必至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1215296_comment'></div>谨发诚心，恭请法师寅公诵戒忏悔；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1215296_comment'></div>又请长老演公为作證明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1215296_comment'></div>投诚佛前，求哀作礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1215296_comment'></div>重念人有自新之路，佛开忏悔之文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1215296_comment'></div>傥能易虑而洗心，尚可赦过而宥罪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1215296_comment'></div>一意悔过，更无他辞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1215296_comment'></div>已造未来，今悉自忏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1215296_comment'></div>愿垂慈悯，副此祷祈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1215296_comment'></div>变罪垢为福田，施法水为甘雨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1215296_comment'></div>救此焦枯之厄，庶免流离之灾。</div><div id='poem_sentence_20_1215296_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1119&endYear=1119')">1119年</a>　在郾城，任郾城县知县。颍昌州佐范元礼将官太常协律郎，苏过作叙送之。作品：《送范元礼序》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《斜川集校注》卷九。）</span><div id='poem_1215252' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1215252' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1215252?labeling=true' target='_blank'>送范元礼序</a><span class='authorDate'>（宣和元年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31323, "北宋", "苏过", "poem_title_1215252")'>苏过</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1215252_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1215252'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1215252'>高平范元礼，始仕筦库，三迁为州佐，皆治颍昌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1215252_comment'></div>余以占籍闾里，得从之游将十年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1215252_comment'></div>每见使人忘其鄙吝，虽更仆而语不厌，愈扣而德愈丰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1215252_comment'></div>岁在己亥，京师以协律召。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1215252_comment'></div>将行，语余：「古有赠言，子曷赋之」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1215252_comment'></div>余惟朋友之义，子于我求其所谓益者欤？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1215252_comment'></div>抑损者欤？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1215252_comment'></div>多闻直谅，则余岂敢；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1215252_comment'></div>善柔便佞，子又饫闻而不取也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1215252_comment'></div>使余何言哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1215252_comment'></div>且求子之失而不可得，将箴而无所从，则余何言哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1215252_comment'></div>古人韦弦之佩，盖扶所长而救所短也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1215252_comment'></div>和羹之喻，献其可而替其否也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1215252_comment'></div>如医者焉，岂有攻其所未病者哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1215252_comment'></div>然子以好词来，余安所拒之？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1215252_comment'></div>吾闻鲁臧孙有言：「季孙之爱我，疾疢也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1215252_comment'></div>孟孙之恶我，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_16_1215252", 1215252, "Clauses/38/Comments/0")'>药石</span>也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1215252_comment'></div>美疢不如恶石，石犹生我，疢之美者，其毒滋多」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1215252_comment'></div>诚哉，是言也！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1215252_comment'></div>余于临患难、共祸福之际，则见其人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1215252_comment'></div>吾乡有史夫子，读书不仕，闭门养亲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1215252_comment'></div>不妄与人交，人亦寡与之合。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1215252_comment'></div>面折人之短，而为人谋则忠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1215252_comment'></div>盖乡人之不善者恶之云尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1215252_comment'></div>元礼独与之厚善，久而弥信。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1215252_comment'></div>以是知子畏美疢而喜<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_25_1215252", 1215252, "Clauses/57/Comments/0")'>药石</span>也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1215252_comment'></div>余可终无言哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1215252_comment'></div>天下之患生于豫怠，而狃于宴安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1215252_comment'></div>贵之移人，有所不期而疾于影响。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1215252_comment'></div>子以妙龄而取贵仕，舍参佐而游朝廷，论思献纳，行有日矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1215252_comment'></div>然富而能贫，贵而能贱，从古所难。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1215252_comment'></div>以其安于习俗也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1215252_comment'></div>自此而往，当与天下豪杰者处，翱翔翰墨，驰骛功名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1215252_comment'></div>为之乏少，而布衣穷阎之士，有不可得而致者矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1215252_comment'></div>日闻所不闻，一唱而百和，称于前而述于后，适于心而悦于耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1215252_comment'></div>为之乏少，而朋友剀切之言，有不可得而闻者矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1215252_comment'></div>则好恶习俗，或与俱迁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1215252_comment'></div>余窃私忧而过计之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1215252_comment'></div>故于其行，敢以是告。</div><div id='poem_sentence_38_1215252_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1119&endYear=1119')">1119年</a>　在郾城，任郾城县知县。友人赵仪之赴官汝阴，苏过作诗送行。作品：《送赵仪之丞汝阴》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《斜川集校注》卷五。）</span><div id='poem_522647' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_522647' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/522647?labeling=true' target='_blank'>送赵仪之丞汝阴</a><span class='authorDate'>（1119年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31323, "北宋", "苏过", "poem_title_522647")'>苏过</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_522647_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_522647'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_522647'>先师诏后人，学优仕有馀。<div id='poem_sentence_0_522647_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_522647'>治身犹农功，勤惰报亦如。<div id='poem_sentence_1_522647_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_522647'>公子生华屋，翛然山泽癯。<div id='poem_sentence_2_522647_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_522647'>胸中一丘壑，结发谈诗书。<div id='poem_sentence_3_522647_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_522647'>闲平风流在，自与常人殊。<div id='poem_sentence_4_522647_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_522647'>清华通帝籍，簪受辉里闾。<div id='poem_sentence_5_522647_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_522647'>我独求试吏，十室聊卷舒。<div id='poem_sentence_6_522647_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_522647'>未起青云心，且与黄卷娱。<div id='poem_sentence_7_522647_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_522647'>淮壖留荐饥，待子活焦枯。<div id='poem_sentence_8_522647_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_522647'>前贤迹相踵，咏歌载西湖。<div id='poem_sentence_9_522647_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_522647'>麦秋未可期，往哺当勤劬。<div id='poem_sentence_10_522647_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_522647'>作诗聊祖道，请以书邻虚<span class='inlineComment2'>（自注：仪之自名其室曰邻虚。）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_11_522647_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_522647'></div><div id='poem_sentence_12_522647_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1119&endYear=1119')">1119年</a>　在郾城，任郾城县知县。祷祈不应，苏过作文讼之。作品：《讼风伯》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《斜川集校注》卷五。）</span><div id='poem_522663' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_522663' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/522663?labeling=true' target='_blank'>讼风伯</a><span class='authorDate'>（1119年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31323, "北宋", "苏过", "poem_title_522663")'>苏过</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_522663_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_522663'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_522663'>天胡久不雨，我欲讼之天。<div id='poem_sentence_0_522663_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_522663'>二麦槁欲死，骄阳犹炽然。<div id='poem_sentence_1_522663_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_522663'>重阴数布野，雨意来无边。<div id='poem_sentence_2_522663_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_522663'>未许一濡地，辄遇四风颠。<div id='poem_sentence_3_522663_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_522663'>摆摇涧谷响，宁复留云烟。<div id='poem_sentence_4_522663_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_522663'>雨师良已勤，风伯殆未悛。<div id='poem_sentence_5_522663_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_522663'>天公纵此为，忍使暴我田。<div id='poem_sentence_6_522663_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_522663'>默诉若有答，不待巫史传。<div id='poem_sentence_7_522663_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_522663'>昨者六七月，屋溜如绳悬。<div id='poem_sentence_8_522663_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_522663'>淋漓逮十日，奔突溃百川。<div id='poem_sentence_9_522663_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_522663'>行旅已断道，闾阎欲通船。<div id='poem_sentence_10_522663_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_522663'>不藉屏翳功，日星几变迁。<div id='poem_sentence_11_522663_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_522663'>我请酌民情，血诚通帝渊。<div id='poem_sentence_12_522663_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_522663'>风雨要有时，乃不为咎愆。<div id='poem_sentence_13_522663_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_522663'>赤子仰粒食，云何绝其烟。<div id='poem_sentence_14_522663_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_522663'>徒闵负贩劳，不忧稼穑先。<div id='poem_sentence_15_522663_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_522663'>怨讟满南亩，欢忻为市廛。<div id='poem_sentence_16_522663_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_522663'>谩说昏垫害，欲誇扫除贤。<div id='poem_sentence_17_522663_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_522663'>何曾补日月，空祇留饥年。<div id='poem_sentence_18_522663_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_19_522663'>区区讼风伯，聊赓退之篇。<div id='poem_sentence_19_522663_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_20_522663'></div><div id='poem_sentence_20_522663_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='99c8ad9d1e3249a2994504581df21dae_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("99c8ad9d1e3249a2994504581df21dae");'><span id='99c8ad9d1e3249a2994504581df21dae_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1119&endYear=1119')">1119年</a>，48岁</div><div id='99c8ad9d1e3249a2994504581df21dae' class='detail'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>在郾城，任郾城县知县。秋，祷雨获应，苏过作诗为庆。惊喜之下，不觉沉疴为之一扫。作品：《郡守祷雨获应》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《斜川集校注》卷五。）</span>《再和》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《斜川集校注》卷五。）</span><div id='poem_522556' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_522556' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/522556?labeling=true' target='_blank'>郡守祷雨获应</a><span class='authorDate'>（1119年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31323, "北宋", "苏过", "poem_title_522556")'>苏过</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_522556_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_522556'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_522556'>秋阳六十日，闵闵岁可惧。<div id='poem_sentence_0_522556_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_522556'>原田龟坼块，城市尘没屦。<div id='poem_sentence_1_522556_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_522556'>谁欤悲若人，活彼于旦暮。<div id='poem_sentence_2_522556_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_522556'>精禋发仁恻，诚意辄上诉。<div id='poem_sentence_3_522556_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_522556'>神山閟灵湫，水旱天所付。<div id='poem_sentence_4_522556_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_522556'>潜虬懒废职，暴虎往斗怒。<div id='poem_sentence_5_522556_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_522556'>抑无东海冤，又岂桑羊蠹。<div id='poem_sentence_6_522556_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_522556'>天心自响答，民语酌道路。<div id='poem_sentence_7_522556_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_522556'>嗟予生理拙，饥饱共农圃。<div id='poem_sentence_8_522556_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_522556'>披衣夜不眠，听此檐间语。<div id='poem_sentence_9_522556_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_522556'>沉疴忽去体，黄壤流膏乳。<div id='poem_sentence_10_522556_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_522556'>少宽县令责，尽复南亩故。<div id='poem_sentence_11_522556_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_522556'>呼儿酌我酒，欲写无佳句。<div id='poem_sentence_12_522556_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_522556'>聊同千里谣，非公谁与哺。<div id='poem_sentence_13_522556_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_522556'></div><div id='poem_sentence_14_522556_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_522557' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_522557' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/522557?labeling=true' target='_blank'>再和</a><span class='authorDate'>（1119年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31323, "北宋", "苏过", "poem_title_522557")'>苏过</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_522557_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_522557'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_522557'>吾君如汤仁，常为无灾惧。<div id='poem_sentence_0_522557_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_522557'>一夫恐不获，贸贸悲辑屦。<div id='poem_sentence_1_522557_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_522557'>二斗东南忧，诏书走晨暮。<div id='poem_sentence_2_522557_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_522557'>陈陈发囷廪，粒食不待诉。<div id='poem_sentence_3_522557_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_522557'>知公经纶手，故以民社付。<div id='poem_sentence_4_522557_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_522557'>汪然叔度陂，不见伟节怒。<div id='poem_sentence_5_522557_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_522557'>德星所临次，民瘼消朽蠹。<div id='poem_sentence_6_522557_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_522557'>祝祠往无愧，飞雨来半路。<div id='poem_sentence_7_522557_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_522557'>耕犁及二麦，浸灌休老圃。<div id='poem_sentence_8_522557_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_522557'>何人执笔书，为瑞非虚语。<div id='poem_sentence_9_522557_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_522557'>应言颍川凤，未要猫相乳。<div id='poem_sentence_10_522557_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_522557'>益欣狱讼少，三尺略细故。<div id='poem_sentence_11_522557_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_522557'>丞掾从歌呼，讴谣入章句。<div id='poem_sentence_12_522557_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_522557'>谢公未赋归，赤子犹待哺。<div id='poem_sentence_13_522557_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_522557'></div><div id='poem_sentence_14_522557_comment'></div></div></div><br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>在郾城，任郾城县知县。习贡以徽猷阁待制知成都，苏过代作谢表。作品：《代习帅谢除徽猷阁待制知成都表》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《斜川集校注》卷九。）</span>《代成都帅到任谢上表》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《斜川集校注》卷九。）</span><div id='poem_1215222' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1215222' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1215222?labeling=true' target='_blank'>代席帅谢除徽猷阁待制知成都表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1119年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31323, "北宋", "苏过", "poem_title_1215222")'>苏过</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1215222_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1215222'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1215222'>起于琳馆，付以名邦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1215222_comment'></div>复玷除书，荐膺谋帅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1215222_comment'></div>宠以禁严之职，畀增方面之崇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1215222_comment'></div>误恩曲加，抚躬知愧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1215222_comment'></div>伏以陈力就列，臣子所以委质而事君；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1215222_comment'></div>为官择人，朝廷盖将砺世而磨钝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1215222_comment'></div>自昔祖宗之故事，必由侍从而进身。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1215222_comment'></div>况内阁之华资，待天下之名士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1215222_comment'></div>掌星躔之宝训，近日月之清光。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1215222_comment'></div>岂特搢绅之荣，实高儒学之选。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1215222_comment'></div>而臣赋材鄙野，备问空虚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1215222_comment'></div>福盈每惧于灾生，器小不堪于大用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1215222_comment'></div>弟兄持橐，愧先后于一门；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1215222_comment'></div>铜竹请符，盖屡穷于五技。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1215222_comment'></div>独荷渊衷之眷，辱收閒废之馀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1215222_comment'></div>雨露所加，乾坤莫报。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1215222_comment'></div>此盖伏遇皇帝陛下圣神广运，睿知有临。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1215222_comment'></div>法天地之自然，一道德而同俗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1215222_comment'></div>长辔远驭，轻爵禄以兴事功；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1215222_comment'></div>左戚右贤，惜名器而彰淑慝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1215222_comment'></div>察臣乏先容于左右，谓臣尝尽瘁于使令。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1215222_comment'></div>致此恩荣，下及孱陋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1215222_comment'></div>策其驽钝，誓永坚于一心；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1215222_comment'></div>志在糜躯，庶用酬于千载。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1215222_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_24_1215222_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1215223' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1215223' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1215223?labeling=true' target='_blank'>代成都帅到任谢上表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1119年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31323, "北宋", "苏过", "poem_title_1215223")'>苏过</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1215223_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1215223'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1215223'>西南都会，古称巴蜀之雄；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1215223_comment'></div>表里山川，国本蚕丛之旧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1215223_comment'></div>士风厚善，民讼简稀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1215223_comment'></div>宣布诏条，告谕父老。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1215223_comment'></div>咸悉朝廷之意，曾不鄙夷其民。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1215223_comment'></div>故择宗臣，以安远俗<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1215223_comment'></div>伏念臣斗筲小器，朴簌凡材。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1215223_comment'></div>生逢日月之明，得遂箕裘之志。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1215223_comment'></div>夤缘一仕，寖被使令。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1215223_comment'></div>盖尝试之于边陲，又复宠之以延阁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1215223_comment'></div>略无毫发之补报，徒窃天地之恩私。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1215223_comment'></div>眷此坤维，号称锦里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1215223_comment'></div>其民务本而力穑，其士好学而有文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1215223_comment'></div>组绣被于中原，富饶甲于天下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1215223_comment'></div>历观祖宗之遣帅，率皆廊庙之伟人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1215223_comment'></div>顾委任之非轻，知拊循之有自。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1215223_comment'></div>三刀见梦，著史策以为荣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1215223_comment'></div>两使占星，候天文而协应。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1215223_comment'></div>如臣才能无取，闻望素轻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1215223_comment'></div>叨冒宠光，有腼面目。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1215223_comment'></div>兹盖伏遇皇帝陛下则尧之大，法禹之勤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1215223_comment'></div>建六官而代天工，操八柄以驭臣下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1215223_comment'></div>坐念五十州之远，特轸渊衷；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1215223_comment'></div>必求二千石之良，主宣德意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1215223_comment'></div>知臣忠孝粗守，筋力未衰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1215223_comment'></div>使之察吏而督奸，岂贵邀功而生事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1215223_comment'></div>边鄙不耸，庶几魏绛之能；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1215223_comment'></div>狱市兼容，远师曹参之治。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1215223_comment'></div>臣敢不益坚素节，图报睿知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1215223_comment'></div>上宽宵旰之忧，次答生成之造。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1215223_comment'></div>奉天威之咫尺，若临渊冰；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1215223_comment'></div>承王命于春秋，敢忘夙夜？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1215223_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_32_1215223_comment'></div></div></div><br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>在郾城，任郾城县知县。冬，叶梦得（少蕴）移竹于贾文元园，作诗，苏过次韵。作品：《次韵少蕴移竹于贾文元园二首》（其一）<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《斜川集校注》卷五。）</span>《次韵少蕴移竹于贾文元园二首》（其二）<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《斜川集校注》卷五。）</span><div id='poem_522570' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_522570' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/522570?labeling=true' target='_blank'>次韵少蕴移竹于贾文元园二首<span class='inlineComment2'>（时倅车乃文元裔孙）</span><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1119年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31323, "北宋", "苏过", "poem_title_522570")'>苏过</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_522570_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_522570'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_522570'>猗欤丞相园，中有岁寒根。<div id='poem_sentence_0_522570_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_522570'>千夫屹冠剑，坐阅云来孙。<div id='poem_sentence_1_522570_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_522570'>当年拥节旄，雅志在淇园。<div id='poem_sentence_2_522570_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_522570'>琅玕映城郭，琴筑鸣潺湲。<div id='poem_sentence_3_522570_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_522570'>春笋半出林，横鞭争触藩。<div id='poem_sentence_4_522570_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_522570'>坐陵霜雪气，高压桃李繁。<div id='poem_sentence_5_522570_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_522570'>年来王子猷，来乘刺史轩。<div id='poem_sentence_6_522570_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_522570'>请分一亩阴，自访三家村。<div id='poem_sentence_7_522570_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_522570'>赋诗属公考，益遣交情敦。<div id='poem_sentence_8_522570_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_522570'>一雨饱生意，莫嫌池水浑。<div id='poem_sentence_9_522570_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_522570'></div><div id='poem_sentence_10_522570_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_522571' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_522571' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/522571?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1119年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_522571_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_522571'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_522571'>我公经纶手，胡为试盘根。<div id='poem_sentence_0_522571_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_522571'>忠言与嘉绩，有后期臧孙。<div id='poem_sentence_1_522571_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_522571'>胸中五千卷，三岁不窥园。<div id='poem_sentence_2_522571_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_522571'>种德如川增，源深自潺湲。<div id='poem_sentence_3_522571_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_522571'>遽辞承明庐，出备诸侯藩。<div id='poem_sentence_4_522571_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_522571'>仁风被草木，已觉棠阴繁。<div id='poem_sentence_5_522571_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_522571'>此君况手植，伴公读书轩。<div id='poem_sentence_6_522571_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_522571'>未须劳越吟，寓目聊江村。<div id='poem_sentence_7_522571_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_522571'>群豪争吐奇，和诗相劝敦。<div id='poem_sentence_8_522571_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_522571'>愧无峥嵘句，往继火陆浑。<div id='poem_sentence_9_522571_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_522571'></div><div id='poem_sentence_10_522571_comment'></div></div></div><br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>在郾城，任郾城县知县。范季远作止斋，苏过题诗。作品：《范季远作止斋求诗以此寄之》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《斜川集校注》卷五。）</span><div id='poem_522686' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_522686' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/522686?labeling=true' target='_blank'>范季远作止斋求诗以此寄之</a><span class='authorDate'>（1119年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31323, "北宋", "苏过", "poem_title_522686")'>苏过</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_522686_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_522686'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_522686'>急流勇退真难事，要取荣枯君自味。<div id='poem_sentence_0_522686_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_522686'>世间轩冕如嚼蜡，自觉山川天下贵。<div id='poem_sentence_1_522686_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_522686'>君如八骏方服辀，帝闲正欲求千里。<div id='poem_sentence_2_522686_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_522686'>刷燕秣越非所愿，放浪烟霞蹑云水。<div id='poem_sentence_3_522686_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_522686'>萧然筑室在人境，身与此心俱欲止。<div id='poem_sentence_4_522686_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_522686'>倦飞偶学陶彭泽，示疾还同老居士。<div id='poem_sentence_5_522686_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_522686'>政忧功名来未免，吾驾不回谁与柅。<div id='poem_sentence_6_522686_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_522686'>古来索价累高人，少室终南应所鄙。<div id='poem_sentence_7_522686_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_522686'></div><div id='poem_sentence_8_522686_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='585ec456bd04496a86d5cdf0686ec8ed_label'><a href='javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1120&endYear=1120')">1120年</a>　苏过罢郾城任。<br /></div>

-----title
邯郸
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='7daf10c9d6fe4ecaa24f8fe734193a3e_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("7daf10c9d6fe4ecaa24f8fe734193a3e");'><span id='7daf10c9d6fe4ecaa24f8fe734193a3e_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1123&endYear=1123')">1123年</a>，52岁</div><div id='7daf10c9d6fe4ecaa24f8fe734193a3e' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1123&endYear=1123')">1123年</a>　权通判中山府任上。行经邯郸，苏过赋诗吊古。作品：《丛台》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《斜川集校注》卷六。）</span><div id='poem_522817' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_522817' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/522817?labeling=true' target='_blank'>丛台</a><span class='authorDate'>（1123年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31323, "北宋", "苏过", "poem_title_522817")'>苏过</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_522817_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_522817'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_522817'>百尺危台高入云，欲将罗绮炫强秦。<div id='poem_sentence_0_522817_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_522817'>长平一战坑俱满，台上应无豪杰人。<div id='poem_sentence_1_522817_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_522817'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_522817_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
唐县
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='353424af0fcc4542b8296202f928d93e_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("353424af0fcc4542b8296202f928d93e");'><span id='353424af0fcc4542b8296202f928d93e_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1123&endYear=1123')">1123年</a>，52岁</div><div id='353424af0fcc4542b8296202f928d93e' class='detail'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>在唐县，权通判中山府任上。苏过行于军城，有诗。作品：《行军城道中》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《斜川集校注》卷六。军城，砦名，在属中山府，在今河北唐县西北。）</span><div id='poem_522821' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_522821' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/522821?labeling=true' target='_blank'>行军城道中</a><span class='authorDate'>（1123年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31323, "北宋", "苏过", "poem_title_522821")'>苏过</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_522821_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_522821'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_522821'>北望青山几百重，秋来翠色欲摩空。<div id='poem_sentence_0_522821_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_522821'>犬戎绝漠今无几，鸟道营粮力已穷。<div id='poem_sentence_1_522821_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_522821'>岩谷有田空琐细，旌旗何日卷殷红。<div id='poem_sentence_2_522821_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_522821'>此行岂得功名事，聊欲探奇访葛洪<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_3_522821_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_522821'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_522821_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_522821'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_3_522821_0'>⑴ 自注：军城北葛洪山甚奇，是夜宿葛川驿。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_522821_comment'></div></div><br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>或在唐县，权通判中山府任上。苏过有《道中买得草屦》诗。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《斜川集校注》卷六。）</span><div id='poem_522808' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_522808' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/522808?labeling=true' target='_blank'>道中买得草屦</a><span class='authorDate'>（1123年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(31323, "北宋", "苏过", "poem_title_522808")'>苏过</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_522808_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_522808'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_522808'>买得芒鞋拄杖挑，心先向足蹑云霄。<div id='poem_sentence_0_522808_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_522808'>山林本是吾归处，不待移文辱见招。<div id='poem_sentence_1_522808_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_522808'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_522808_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end
